Yesu Oku Nɛ Mɛ Gɛ Ede Kɛdɔ ŋuŋlɔmɛ lu nɛ Yesu Kristo Daviti yɛ Eyi gɛ enu Abraham yɛ Eyi nɛ shu: Abraham yɛ edzi Isak yɛ aka, Isak yɛ edzi Yakɔb yɛ aka, Yakɔb yɛ edzi Yuɖa anɛ yɛadzyalɛ nɛ aka, Yuɖa yɛ edzi Pɛrɛz anɛ Zera balɛ aka, gɛ balɛ eni edzi Tamar, Pɛrɛz yɛ edzi Hɛzrɔn yɛ aka, Hɛzrɔn yɛ edzi Ram yɛ aka, Ram yɛ edzi Amminadab yɛ aka, Amminadab yɛ edzi Nashɔn yɛ aka, Nashɔn yɛ edzi Salmɔn yɛ aka, Salmɔn yɛ edzi Boaz yɛ aka, gɛ yɛ eni edzi Rahab, Boaz yɛ edzi Obeti yɛ aka, gɛ yɛ eni edzi Ruth, Obeti yɛ edzi Yesse yɛ aka, Klɛ Yesse ebe dzi Ekusi Daviti yɛ aka.
Daviti yɛ edzi Salomonɛ yɛ aka, gɛ yɛ eni edzi Yuriah yɛedzini aba fla, Salomonɛ yɛ edzi Rehoboam yɛ aka, Rehoboam yɛ edzi Abiya yɛ aka.
Abiya yɛ edzi Asa yɛ aka, Asa yɛ edzi Yehoshafɛt yɛ aka, Yehoshafɛt yɛ edzi Yehoram yɛ aka, Yehoram yɛ edzi Uzzia yɛ aka, Uzzia yɛ edzi Yotam yɛ aka, Yotam yɛ edzi Ahaz yɛ aka, Ahaz yɛ edzi Hezekia yɛ aka, Hezekia yɛ edzi Manase yɛ aka, Manase yɛ edzi Amɔn yɛ aka, Amɔn yɛ edzi Yosia yɛ aka, klɛ Yosia yɛ edzi Yekonia anɛ yɛadzyalɛ balɛ aka, nɛ kibelɛ nɛ gɛ keyu ebe vua lɛ avɛnɔ Babilɔn.
Nɛ Babilɔn tɛzɛza beke mɛ, Yekonia yɛ edzi Shealtiɛl yɛ aka, Shealtiɛl yɛ edzi Zerubabɛl yɛ aka, Zerubabɛl, Abiud yɛ aka, Abiud yɛ edzi Eliakim yɛ aka, Eliakim yɛ edzi Azɔ yɛ aka, Azɔ yɛ edzi Zadɔk yɛ aka, Zadɔk yɛ edzi Akim yɛ aka, Akim yɛ edzi Eliud yɛ aka, Eliud yɛ edzi Eleaza yɛ aka, Eleaza yɛ edzi Matan yɛ aka, Matan yɛ edzi Yakɔb yɛ aka, klɛ Yakɔb yɛ enu Yosɛfu yɛ aka, Maria yɛ enyine gɛ ba mɔ Yesu akɔ, gɛ be klu asɛ Kristo.
So tɛmumɔm lɔfɔntialɛ̃ petee klɛ za denɔ Abraham ɔbɔ nanɔ Daviti yɛa bha, tɛmumɔm lɔfɔntialɛ̃ denɔ Daviti yɛa bha ɔdɔ nanɔ tɛtutu vɛ Babilɔn, klɛ kɛfɔntialɛ̃ za denɔ tɛtutu nɛ ɔdɔ nanɔ Kristo.
Yesu Kristo Tɛmumɔ Kana mɛ Yesu Kristo tɛmumɔ nɛ ga pɛ kɛba: Ba kpɛ yɛeni Maria bunuwã akɔ Yosɛfu sɛ tɛ aba gbanɔ, pɔ flogo tɛ la ba zanɛ aglɔ nɛɛ kɛba wɛ̃ sɛ Maria eti munɔ ɛya ganɔ Ɔfufɔɛ Dzyɔgo nɛa bha.
Alasɛ Yosɛfu gɛ edzi Maria yɛenyine nɛ enu anɔ dzyɔgo so nɛɛ, adɛ pɛɛ sɛ tɛ akpɛ Maria kɛwɛ̃ so, atrɔ nɛ kɛtɔkpum asɛ aba shɛnahwɛ Maria shu kɛdzyɛɛ.
Pɔ kɛlɛede gɛ akpɛ kɛtɔkpum ana nɛɛ, Kpaya axwɛdɛ ebe bu ishu akasɛ yɛ nɛ bulɛla mɛ asɛ, “Yosɛfu Daviti yɛeyi, tɛ si kifu nɛ Maria tɛgbɛgbanɔ vɛnɔ bupa mɛ ansɛ wedzini ana nɛ shu, alasɛ ɛya nɛ gɛ ɛlɛ yɛ shu nɛɛ lɛ de Ɔfufɔɛ Dzyɔgo nɛ ɔkɔ.
Aba mɔ eyianyɛ, gɛ kɛlɛ sɛ tɛ ɔkɔ yɛ nyi sɛ Yesu, alasɛ yɛ ebe bu yɛ banɔ nɛ edenɔ balɛ buzizi mɛ.” Ebuia nɛ petee la ba kɛlɛ mɛ sɛ tɛ ba yɛkɔ mɔ Apalete nɛ ebui nɛ gɛ aɖɔ ganɔ atɔnu nɛa bha na asɛ: “Kebite nɛ kebe munɔ ɛya klɛ ka ba mɔ eyianyɛ, klɛ le be kulu yɛ asɛ Yimanuɛlɛ” gɛ kɛlɛesi nu sɛ, “Kpaya alɛ plɛnɔ lɔ.” Gɛ Yosɛfu anyɛmɛ denɔ tra nɛ mɛ, abhɛtɛ ansɛ gɛ Kpaya axwɛdɛ nɛ etsre yɛ klɛ agbanɔ Maria avɛnɔ bupa mɛ ansɛ yɛedzini ana.
Pɔ yɛ anɛ Maria ba dɛ za tɛnyɛ anɛ tɛdzɛ mɛ ɔdɔ nanɔ yɛ eyianyɛ nɛ tɛmumɔ.
Klɛ akɔ yɛ kinyi asɛ Yesu.
Bebuinyi Teli Ede Kiwiɔyɛkɔ Ebe Di Yesu Kɛlɛede gɛ ba mɔ Yesu beke nɛ Betlehem anɛ Yuɖia, anɛ Ekusi Heroɖesɛ kibe, bebuiti teli be de kiwiɔyɛkɔ aba Yerusalɛm klɛ le be bisi asɛ, “Fakɔ eyi nɛ gɛ ba mɔ anasɛ Yuɖanɛ ekusi nɛ alɛ?
Bumɔ yɛ nɛ kiwiɔyɛkɔ klɛ lɔ ba sɛ tɛ buba kpɛ kɛtɔkpuesi kɔ yɛ.” Gɛ Ekusi Heroɖesɛ enu sɛ kana, kɛ kpɛ yɛ bunuhu, klɛ Yerusalɛm petee aza plɛnɔ yɛ.
Gɛ ekulu yɛ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ gbla anɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ nɛ petee ebe xogo, ebisi alɛ ɔkɛlɛ gɛ ba ɖɔ sɛ ba baa mɔ Kristo.
Be bu kɛlɛ nu etsrea sɛ, “Nɛ Betlehem nɛ Yuɖia,” alasɛ kana atɔnu nɛ aŋlɔmɛ elu asɛ: “ ‘Pɔ wɔ, Betlehem, nɛ Yuɖia kesukpa nɛa bha, odinu ebhliyi nɛ bagɛ baa ŋɛabha nɛ shi nɛ Yuɖia, alasɛ wɔ mɛ agɛ aba ŋa anɔabha nɛ ebee de yɛ ebe dzi agbɛgbanɔ kɔ mɛ Izraɛlanɛ.’ ” Ɔkɛlɛ Heroɖesɛ ekulu kiwiɔyɛkɔ bebuiti nɛ tɛkpukpum klɛ ebisi alɛ ɔɖa nɔɔ nɛ mɛ pɔtɛɛ gɛ kɛwũwɔɛ nɛ wɛ̃ kɔa lɛ.
Asɛsɛ balɛ nɛ Betlehem klɛ asɛ, “Nɔ vɛ tɛ nɔ dɔ pɛ anuvɔ nɛ mɔmɔ.
Kibe lɛ gɛ nɔɔ mɔ yɛ, nɔ ba tɛ nɔ bɔ kɔ mɛ ti, sɛ tɛ mɛ tsyɛ ɛda kpɛ kɛtɔkpuesi kɔ yɛ.” Gɛ be nu ekusi nɛ kibui nɛ beke, ba vɛ balɛ kidzoa bha, klɛ kɛwũwɔɛ nɛ gɛ bamɔ nɛ kiwiɔyɛkɔ nɛ putɔ kɔa lɛ ɔdɔnanɔ kɛlɛ tɛdzudzrɔ nɛ ɔklɛ gɛ anuvɔ nɛ alɛ.
Gɛ ba mɔ kɛwũwɔɛ same ekua lɛ adɔ kidzo afla.
Gɛ be de ku bupa nɛ mɛ, ba mɔ ŋɛvuvɔ anɛ yeni Maria, klɛ be zhiakpla klɛ ba kpɛ kɛtɔkpuesi akɔ yɛ.
Ɔkɛlɛ ba danɛ balɛ ɔkpɛtɛ klɛ be bu kɛdɔkukɔ ansɛ, elifi anɛ sɛkadzɛdzã anɛ babɔhuhu akɔ yɛ.
Klɛ gɛ beti bu akasɛ alɛ nɛ bulɛla mɛ sɛ be tee tsodzi avɛ Heroɖesɛ ɔkɔ so, ba da ga kidzo bhlatɔ avɛ balɛe pi.
Tɛsisi Vɛ Egipte Gɛ kiwiɔyɛkɔ bebuiti na shɛ beke, Apalete nɛ axwɛdɛ nɛ ada wɛ̃ nɛ Yosɛfu bulɛlam klɛ etsrea sɛ, “Lɔ, yɛkɔ ŋɛvuvɔ anɛ yeni tɛ osi vɛ Egibte.
Za ɔkɛlɛ ɔdɔ nanɔ kibe lɛ gɛ eba tsre wɔ, alasɛ Heroɖesɛ abaa pɛ anuvɔ na sɛ tɛ eyi.” So evu alɔ, ayɛkɔ ŋɛvuvɔ anɛ yeni nɛ elishim klɛ ashɛ̃ avɛ Edzyibite, ɔkɛlɛ aza ɔdɔ nanɔ kibe lɛ gɛ Heroɖesɛ ebe tsi.
Klɛ kɛ ba kɛlɛm anasɛ gɛ Apalete nɛ aɖɔ ganɔ atɔnu nɛa bha sɛ, “Nɛ Edzyibite mɛ ɛba kulu mɛ eyianyɛ nɛ denɔ.” Kibe lɛ gɛ Heroɖesɛ aba mɔ sɛ kiwiɔyɛkɔ bebuiti nɛ be ti bui adɛ yɛ, obulo oku yɛ, klɛ akɔ ɔshã sɛ be yi eyianyɛnuvɔ kanyaka nɛ Betlehem anɛ yɛ kɛdɔ nɛm petee, denɔ agɔ tabha ɔmɛnaesi, anasɛ gɛ enu denɔ kiwiɔyɛkɔ bebuiti nɛ ɔkɔ.
Ɔkɛlɛ kibui nɛ gɛ ba ɖɔ lu ganɔ atɔnu Yeremia bha nɛ ba kɛlɛ mɛ sɛ: “Be nu ogugu toli kɛdɔ nɛ Rama, anɛ iyuyo anɛ awɔ̃hũdzɛdzã, Rashɛ̃l ebi kɔ yeyialɛ klɛ ataa dɛmɛ sɛ tɛ ba yɔ yɛ idzyi, alasɛ ba va ma.” Tɛ Tsitsodzi Vɛ Nazarɛtɛ Kɛlɛe de gɛ Heroɖesɛ etsi, Apalete nɛ axwɛdɛ aba wɛ̃ nɛ Yosɛfu bulɛlam nɛ Edzyibite klɛ asɛ, “Vu ɔlɔ, yɛkɔ anuvɔ anɛ yɛeni tɛ nɔ shɛ vɛ Izraɛl kesukpam, alasɛ bagɛ ba pɛɛ anuvɔ nɛ asɛ tɛ be yi nɛ eti tsi.” So evu alɔ, klɛ ayɛkɔ anuvɔ anɛ yɛeni nɛ avɛnɔ Izraɛl kesukpam.
Pɔ gɛ enu asɛ Heroɖesɛ yeyi Atsyɛlausɛ yɛ aŋa bukusi nɛ yɛaka kinyi mɛ nɛ Yuɖia nɛɛ, kifu kui sɛ tɛ avɛ ɔkɛlɛ.
Gɛ batɛ kpɛ yɛ ɔshã nɛ bulɛla mɛ so, etsodzi ɔkɛlɛ klɛ ada fla vɛ Galelia kɛdɔ nɛm, klɛ ada za ɔma toli gɛ bee kulu asɛ Nazarɛtɛ nɛm.
Kana kɛda ba kɛlɛm anasɛ gɛ ba ɖɔɛ lɛ aganɔ batɔmu nɛa bha asɛ: “Be be kulu yɛ asɛ Nazarɛtɛeyi.”
Yohanɛsɛ Enikpɛ Nɛ Kidzo Gɛgamɛ Nɛ ewia lɛlɛ nɛ mɛ Yohanɛsɛ Enikpɛ nɛ aba, nɛ kibui nɛ tɛɖuɖɔ nɛ Yuɖea Ayakpam, klɛ aaɖɔ asɛ, “Tsyinaɛtem, alasɛ owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ otsobunɔ.” Yɛ enu agɛ yɛ bui ba ɖɔ ganɔ Yezaya atɔnu nɛa bha: “Anɔ olim toli gɛ okulu nɛ ayakpamɛ, ‘Gamɛ kidzo nɛ olu kɔ Apalete, bu edzo dzyudzyɔ kɔ yɛ.’ ” Yohanɛsɛ kɛdɔnyunyumu kipuaga tɛka la bhɛtɛ lɛ nɔ, klɛ kazaplukpa ɔdzadi ɔkana yɛa shɛ.
Yɛ kɛdɔŋɛŋa klɛ dzi ahwaye anɛ betsiuni.
Banɔ be koeyi edenɔ Yerusalɛm anɛ Yuɖea petee anɛ Yɔɖan kɛdɔ nɛm petee atɔnɔ yɛ.
Be bu balɛ buzizi nɛ aɖɔ, klɛ akpɛ buni akɔa lɛ nɛ Yɔɖan Keni nɛm.
Pɔ gɛ amɔ Farisianɛ anɛ Sarusianɛ gɛ baa ba ɔkɛlɛ gɛ aakpɛ buni, etsre alɛ asɛ, “Wɔnɔ atagblashã yam banɔ!
Anee ye tsre nɔ sɛ no si ɔlɔ butɔ nɛ gɛɛ ba?
No yu eyuyu anɛ kitemtsyitsyina nyɛnyɛna vunɔm.
Klɛ nɔ tɛ bhɛtɛ kɛtɔkpum sɛ nɔ bɔ na wɔnɔ shu ɖɔ tsre sɛ, ‘Abraham alɛ bulɔ ahwɛ ansɛ aka.’ Itsre wɔnɔ sɛ denɔ aklãgbua nɛ mɛ Kpaya aba na beyi bu kɔ Abraham.
Kawɛ nɛɛ ke tsri isigu nɛa bha kukuu ku, klɛ osi kanyaka gɛ ɔtɛ bo yu eyuyu dzyɔgo be be tẽ ɔlɛ ebho klɛ la ba yɛkɔ atɛ̃a kpɛ kifum.
“Ɛɛkpɛuni kɔ wɔnɔ nɛ buni kɔ kite mɛ tsyitsyina.
Pɔ mɛede anɔ nɛ gɛ alɛ kemi adɛ mɛ aba ba, yɛ butsrukpɔaklɔ tsyɛ ɛdɛ na gɛ ɛba vunɔ.
Yɛ aba kpɛuni kɔ nɔ nɛ Ɔfufɔɛ Dzyɔgo anɛ kifu.
Yɛ, kawɛ̃sa nɛ kalɛ yɛ ahwɛmɛ, klɛ ebe ŋuse yɛ kedzripi, aba yalɛ yɛ agɔnɛ nɛ ada kpɛ owulem klɛ aba pɔɛ tɛhwɛ nɛ kifu gɛ tɛ ba ni di mɛ.” Bunikpɛkpɛ Kɔ Yesu Ɔkɛlɛ Yesu aba denɔ Galelia ebe ku Yɔɖan sɛ tɛ Yohanɛsɛ akpɛuni kɔ yɛ.
Pɔ Yohanɛsɛ edi asɛ tɛ aplɛ yɛ, aaɖɔ asɛ, “Mɛ kɛlɛ sɛ tɛ ɔkpɛuni ɔkɔ, klɛ mɛ ɔkɔ ɔba?” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Kɔ kɛ za na ɔtsɔ̃; kɛbɔ sɛ tɛ bubhɛtɛ ana sɛ tɛ kɛ na nɛ tɛzɛza dzyɔgo mɛ petee.” Klɛ Yohanɛsɛ ayɛkɛ lɛ.
Gɛ banya kpɛuni nɛ akɔ Yesu beke ko, klɛ ewu ekoeyi nɛ buni nɛm.
Nɛ kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ owũsise nɛ ɔdanɛ, klɛ amɔ Kpaya Ɔfufɔɛ nɛ gɛ ozhi ɔɔba anasɛ gɔgɔwi anɛ kifuɔmɔɛ nɛ ɔza yɛa bha.
Klɛ oli toli mɛ ode owũsise sɛ, “Meyi naa, gɛ ɛdɛmɛnɔ; yɛm mɛ mɔ awɔ̃kuku mɔmɔ.”
Yesu Tɛfifekedi Ɔkɛlɛ Ɔfufɔɛ nɛ ɔbɔ gbanɛ Yesu ɔvɛnɔ ayakpam kɔ ɔfufɔɛkpã sɛ tɛ lo feke yɛ odi.
Gɛ anya onugbu ewi afɛtalɛ̃ anɛ elishi afɛtalɛ̃ nɛ beke, bubhɛ ba yi yɛ.
Ɔfufɔɛkpã nɛ ɔba yɛ ɔbha klɛ lɔ ɖɔ sɛ, “Onu gɛ onu Kpaya Yeyi, klɛ tɛ otsre aklãgbua nɛ tɛ le tsyina dzi kɛŋɛŋa.” Yesu etsre ɔlɛ asɛ, “Kɛ ŋlɔmɛ li sɛ, ‘anɛ kɛŋɛŋa shu ko Anɔdzyrame aba za nɛ ɛkpã, pɔ kibui kanyaka gɛ de Kpaya onugbum koeyi.’ ” Ɔkɛlɛ ɔfufɔɛkpã nɛ ɔyɛkɔ yɛ ɔvɛnɔ ishubhubhui ɔmagbla nɛm klɛ lɔ kɔa lɔ busɔlɛvu nɛ ɔɖɛɖamakɔdɛ.
Lɔ sɛ, “Onu gɛ onu Kpaya Yeyi,” tɛ ɔtɛ̃ɛ ɔdɔ dɔ kesukpa.
Alasɛ kɛ ŋlɔmɛ li sɛ: “ ‘Kpaya aba kɔ yɛ baxwɛdɛ na za nɛ awɔ̃ nɛ wɔshu, klɛ la ba sɔlɛ wɔ akpɛ balɛ ahwɛmɛ, sɛ tɛ ɔtɛ yɛkɔ wɔ katsrukpɔ obo hu kɛklãgbu.’ ” Yesu ebui lɛ nu etsre asɛ, “Kɛ ŋlɔmɛ li tsyɛ sɛ: ‘Tɛ feke Apalete wɔ Kpaya nɛ odi.’ ” Ɔfufɔɛkpã ɔzɔ gbanɔ Yesu ɔvɛnɔ butu ɖɛɖama tulia bha klɛ lɔ yɛkɔ kanɔm bukusiɛŋakɔ nɛ petee nɛ bulɛ mɛ tɛpupudi nɛ akasɛ yɛ.
Klɛ lɔ ɖɔ sɛ, “Kɛdɔɛ nɛ petee ɛba yɛkɔ kɔ wɔ,” “onu gɛ obo zhikpla ɔkpɛ kɛtɔkpuesi kɔ mɛ.” Yesu etsre yɛ asɛ, “Tsuɔvɛ nɛ mɛ ɔbha, Satana!
Alasɛ kɛ ŋlɔmɛ li sɛ, ‘Kpɛ kɛtɔkpuesi kɔ Apalete wɔ Kpaya, tɛ ɔdɛ yɛ tite koe xwɛ.’ ” Ɔkɛlɛ ɔfufɔɛkpã nɛ ɔshɛ nɛ yɛɔbha, klɛ kpaya baxwɛdɛ aba ebe di yɛ ɔkɔ.
Yesu Akpɛ Kpayɛbui Nɛ Tɛɖuɖɔesi Gɛ Yesu enu asɛ bevu Yohanɛsɛ akpɛ buvu, etsodzi avɛ Galelia.
Gɛ ashɛ̃ nɛ Nazarɛtɛ, avɛ ada za Kapenuam, gɛ alɛ kɛvɔ nɔ bha nɛ Zebulunɛ nɛ Naftali kibee, sɛ tɛ kibui nɛ gɛ ba ɖɔ ganɔ Yezaya atɔnu nɛa bha nɛ kɛ na: “Zebulɔnɛ kesukpa anɛ Naftali kesukpa, kidzo nɛ gɛ vɛ aƒu nɛ shu, Yɔɖanɛ nɛ shu, Bagɛ be di nu Yuɖanɛ nɛ Galelia— banɔ nɛ ga kpasɛ otumu mɛ ba mɔ kifu piim; nɛ baga lɛ butsi buyi kesukpa nɛ mɛ kifu deke.” Denɔ kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ ɔvɛnɔ klɛ Yesu etenɔ Kpayɛbui nɛ ɖɔ, “Tsyinɛtem, alasɛ owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ tɛ tsu ba.” Badɔkpasɛ Tutɔpu Nɛ Tɛkuklu Gɛ Yesu aaga nɛ Galelia aƒu nɛ shu, amɔ badzya tɛabha, Simɔnɛ gɛ be kulu asɛ Petro anɛ yadzya Andrɛasɛ.
Be dzi aza da kenimdzikle kɛvɔ nɛ mɛ alasɛ benu banɔ gɛ bee bu kenimɛdzya.
Yesu asɛ, “Nɔ ba, zamɛe de mɔ,” “klɛ ɛba bhɛtɛ wɔnɔ banɔ gɛ be bu banɔ.” Ɔkɛlɛ nɛ ko, bagbla shɛnahwɛ kenimdzikle nɛ shu elu, klɛ la lɛ yɛe de.
Denɔ ɔkɛlɛ ɔlɛ nɛ ɔvɛnɔ, amɔ badzya tɛabha teli, Yakobo gɛ enu Zebeɖi yɛeyi anɛ yɛadzya Yohanɛsɛ.
Ba za keniabha opupu mɛ nɛ balɛ aka Zebeɖi, gɛ ewũse balɛ kenimdzikle.
Yesu eklua lɛ, klɛ begble koeyi ashɛ̃ alɔ opupu nɛ balɛ aka klɛ ba tɔnɔ yɛ.
Yesu Ebeke Banyɛnya Nɛ Banya Yesu aga nyɔ ekoeyi nɛ Galelia, anɛ kɛdɔkɛkasɛ nɛ balɛ oxogokɔevu nɛm, kibui dzyɔgo nɛ tɛɖuɖɔ denɔ bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ shu, klɛ ebeke banya nyaanya nɛ banɔ mɛ.
Be nu yɛ dɔ akana Siria petee, klɛ banɔa gbanɔ balɛ banyɛnya edidedi amɛna yɛ, banɔ teli nɛ ishutɛtã, beteli ɛfufɔɛkpã vua lɛ, beteli baa wɔlɛ ebho, klɛ beteli bagba klɛ ebeke balɛ banya nɛ petee.
Banɔɛza gbla denɔ Galelia, Dekapolisɛ Yerusalɛm, Yuɖia anɛ Yɔɖanɛ kɛdɔ nɛ mɛ petee ba za yɛe de.
Ayulabui Gɛ Yesu amɔ banɔɛza, ewu butu nɛa bha klɛ azaesi.
Yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ aba yɛ ɔbha, klɛ etenɔ balɛ kɛdɔ kasɛ pɛ aɖɔ sɛ, “Ba yula bagɛ ba dɔɛtsyui nɛ ɔfufɔɛ mɛ, alasɛ balɛ yɛ kɛlɛ nu bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ owũsise.
Ba yula bagɛ balɛ akpasɛ awɔ̃hũdzɛdza mɛ, alasɛ balɛ kite le be vu idzyi akpɛ.
Ba yula bagɛ enu banɔ yuyɔ, alasɛ balɛ aba ŋa kesukpa.
Ba yula bagɛ bubhɛ anɛ oniwɛ ɔɔta nɛ tɛzɛzam dzyɔgo shu so, alasɛ balɛ ebe xui.
Ba yula bagɛ balɛ edi eshutukubui, alasɛ balɛ le be di eshutukubui.
Ba yula bagɛ balɛ idzyi mɛ ebhui, alasɛ balɛ aba mɔ Kpaya.
Ba yula beboevu, alasɛ balɛ le be kulu asɛ Kpaya yeyialɛ.
Ba yula bagɛ ba kpatɔnɔ akpɛ tɛzɛza dzyɔgo so, alasɛ balɛ yɛ kɛlɛ nu bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ owũsise.
“Ba yula wɔnɔ bagɛ banɔa kula, pɛ bakpatɔnɔ klɛ baa ɖɔ ebuikpã edidedi petee nɛ wɔnɔ shu akpɛ mɛ so.
Nɔ mɔ same tɛ nɔ wɔ, alasɛ wɔnɔɛ bhɛ tri nɛ owũsise, alasɛ kidzoe lɛ nɛ dia bha ke la ga pɛ ba kpatɔnɔ batɔnu nɛ gɛ eputɔ kɔ nɔ.
Bɔmɔɛ Anɛ Kifu “Wɔnɔ nu kanɔ nɛ mɛ bɔmɔɛ.
Pɔ onu gɛ bɔmɔɛ lɛla bulɛ ɔdzyɛ, kɛlɛ bu zɛ ba dzi bɔmɔɛ?
Bɔ tia pɛ kɔ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ, ɔyɛkɔ dɛ sɛ tɛ ba yɛkɔ bulɛ atɛɛ elu kɔ banɔ la ga. “Wɔnɔ nu kanɔ nɛ mɛ kanɛgbɛ.
Ɔmagbla nɔɔ gɛ otsri butua bha ba tɛ ba na ɔlɛ kpu.
Banɔ eti deke kanɛgbɛ pɛ baa yɛkɔ akpɛ kɛdɔesi.
Yɛ osia bha baa yɛkɔ atrɔ, pɛ aakɔ anɔnyanɔ kifu.
Kana kidzoɛ lɛ nɛa bha ke, nɔ kɔ wɔnɔ kifu nɛ deke nɛ banɔa mɛ, sɛ tɛ bamɔ wɔnɔ kibuigba bhɛbhɛtɛ klɛ tɛ ba kpɛ wɔnɔ Aka nɛa bha nɛ owũsise.
Ɔshã Nɛabha Tɛbhɛbhɛtɛ “Nɔ tɛ bhɛtɛ tɔkpum ɔsɛ ɛba Ɔshã nɛ oxule kɔ ɔdɔgɔsɛ Batɔnu, ɛdɛ ba ɛlɛ oxule kɔ, pɔ ɛlɛa bha tɛbhɛbhɛtɛ.
Itsre nɔ kɛgba, ɔdɔnanɔ kibe lɛ gɛ owũsise anɛ kesukpa kaa lɛla, kɛdɔ ŋuŋlɔmɛ bhli dɛ, kɛdɔŋlɔmɛshi kɛdɔfuflɔ̃ bhli, ganɔ kidzo nyɛdzoa bha nɛ tɛ baa lɛla nɛ Ɔshã nɛm ɔdɔnanɔ kibe lɛ gɛ kibuinyɛbui kɛ bɛɛ lɛm beke.
Anɔnyanɔ gɛ ebule ɔshã nɛ obhliyi ɔkɔ toli klɛ akasɛ banɔ bhlatɔ tsyɛ asɛ ba bhɛtɛ ana, be be kulu yɛ ebhliyia dɛ nɛ bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛm nɛ owũsise, pɔ aanɔ nɛ gɛ aabhɛtɛ klɛ aakasɛ ɛshãɛ nɛɛ, be be kulu yɛ asɛ agbɛgbla nɛ owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ.
Alasɛ itsre wɔnɔ sɛ odi nu sɛ wɔnɔ tɛzɛzadzyɔgo nɛ pɛ̃ dɛ Farisianɛ anɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ nɛɛ, kɛlɛ lɛm sɛ nɔ tɛ bo tsoku owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛm.
Kɛdɔkɛkasɛ Nɛ Anɔ Yiyi Shu “Wɔnɔ no ti nu sɛ baɖɔ kukuuku etsre banɔ nɛ asɛ, ‘Tiyi anɔ, klɛ anɔnyanɔ gɛ eyi anɔ be be kulu kebhui nɛ yɛ.’ Pɔ itsre nɔ sɛ, anɔnyanɔ gɛ amɔ oblo nɛ yɛadzya be be kulu kebhui nɛ yɛ.
Ɔyɛkɔplɛnɔ anɔnyanɔ gɛ ebe tsre yadzya sɛ, ‘Ɔmɛtã kɔ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ,’ ebe bu shu nu nɛ Bebhuiklu naa mɛ.
Pɔ anɔ nɛ gɛ aaɖɔ sɛ, ‘Wɔ agã onu!’ ebe tsoku butɔm anɛ kifu mabeke mabekem.
“So nɛɛ, onu gɛ ɔvɛnɔ kɛdɔ kukɔ nɛ busɔlɛvumokpo nɛa bha pɛ ɔbaka sɛ wadzya evunɔɛ bui tili nɛ wɔ, shɛnahwɛ kɛdɔ nɛ shu olu ɔkɛlɛ nɛ busɔlɛvumokpo nɛ otugba tɛ ɔshɛ̃.
Putɔnɔ nɛɛ vɛ tɛ ɔdɔ bhɛtɛ terikpo anɛ wadzya; tɛ otsio tsodzi ɔba tɛ ɔbɔ kɔ wɔɛ dɔ.
“Wũse wɔnɔ nɛ bagɛ ba yɛkɔɛ bui nɛ wɔ nɛe bhui nɛ shi zia.
Bhɛtɛ kishi wũwũse nɛ kibe lɛ gɛ wɔnɔ nɛ yɛ oko tsri dzoa bha, flogo tɛ aba yɛkɔ wɔa kɔ ebhuiklu, tɛ ebhuiklu nɛ aba yɛkɔ wɔa kpɛ ahwɛ kɔ ɔshãelete, klɛ aba yɛkɔ wɔ ada tɛ̃a kpɛ vu.
Itsre wɔ kɛgba sɛ, ɔtɛ bo koeyi ɔdɔ nanɛ kibe lɛ gɛ ɔbuya kaple gɔgɔɛ.
Kɛdɔkɛkasɛ Nɛ Ɔmamdɛdɛ Shu “No ti nu gɛ baɖɔ asɛ, ‘Tɛ dɛ ɔmam.’ Pɔ itsre wɔnɔ sɛ anɔnyanɔ gɛ ebe di adzɛ teli wɔ̃mɛ atɛ pɛɛ yɛ nɛ yɛ idzyi mɛ.
Onu gɛ wɔ kɛŋamɛ wɔ̃hũ nɛ kɔ sɛ ɔbhɛtɛ buzizi, kpɛɛ lɛ obu tɛ ɔyɛkɔ tɛɛ̃.
Kɛpɛ kɔ wɔ sɛ tɛ wɔ shu nɛ ɔkɔ toli ɔpɔ tɛ̃ dɛ sɛ tɛ ba yɛkɔ wɔ anɔosi nɛ petee ada tɛ̃a kpɛ kifu gɛ tɛ baa ni di mɛ.
Klɛ onu wɔ kɛŋahwɛ nɔɔ kɔ sɛ ɔbhɛtɛ buzizi, bhui ɔlɛ tɛ ɔyɛkɔ tɛ̃.
Apɛ kɔ wɔ sɛ tɛ wɔ shu nɛ ɔkɔ toli ɔtɛ za dɛ sɛ tɛ wɔ anɔosi nɛ petee ɔdɔ vɛ kifu gɛ tɛ baa ni di mɛ.
Anyɛ Nɛ Adzɛ Aglɔshu Shɛshɛ̃nahwɛ “Ba tɛ ɖɔɛ lɛ asɛ, ‘Anɔnyanɔ gɛ aba shɛ̃nahwɛ yedzini shu, alasɛ tɛ akɔ yɛ keplukpa nɛ lɛa bha.’ Pɔ itsre wɔnɔ sɛ anɔnyanɔ gɛ ashɛ̃nahwɛ yedzini shu, gɛ odi nu sɛ adɛ ɔma mɛ so, akɔ sɛ adzɛ nɛ aba tɛ bhɛtɛ aglɔbui, klɛ anɔnyanɔ gɛ aaba tɛ gbanɔ adzɛ alɛlɛ nɛɛ abhɛtɛ aglɔbui.
Batabu Shu Kɛdɔkɛkasɛ “Ɔyɛkɔplɛnɔ, no ti nu sɛ, ba ɖɔɛ lɛ tsre banɔ kibe dzidze sɛ, ‘Nɔ tɛ tu wɔnɔ atabu, pɔ nɔ nyɛna wɔnɔ batabu nɛ mɛ ovunɔ gɛ nɔ ka kɔ Apalete.’ Pɔ itsre wɔnɔ sɛ, Nɔ tɔɔ tanɔ kɛdɔ, eedzi sɛ owuũsise nɔɔ tanɔ tsyɛ o, alasɛ ɔlɛ onu Kpaya kegbu, ɔdɔgɔsɛ ɔtanɔ kesukpa nɛo, alasɛ kalɛ nu Kpaya ɔtsrɛegbu, ɔflɔ ɔdɔgɔsɛ ɔtanɔ Yerusalɛm o, alasɛ yɛenu Ekusi nɛ ɔmagbla.
Klɛ nɔ tɛ tanɔ wɔnɔ kɛtɔkpu, alasɛ ɔtɛ bɔ na tɛka tirikpo bhɛtɛ tɛ kidzi kitutu ɔdɔgɔsɛ kifufu.
Kplitaa nɛ, kɔ wɔ ‘Xee’ nɛ edzi ‘Xee,’ tɛ wɔ ‘Owo’ nɛ edzi ‘Owo’, kibui nyɛbui di gɛ kɛɛ zɛ dɛ kana nɛ kide ɔfufɔɛkpã nɛ ɔkɔ.
Kɛwɔ̃hũ Nɛ Kɛwɔ̃hũ Ɔzakɔ “No ti nu gɛ ba ɖɔ asɛ, ‘Kɛwɔ̃hũ nɛ kɛwɔ̃hũ ɔzakɔ, klɛ kile nɛ kile ɔzakɔ.’ Pɔ itsre wɔnɔ sɛ, Nɔ tɛ wɔ̃lãkɛ kibui nɛ anɔ kpã.
Onu gɛ anɔ teli abɔ wɔ kɛdɔ nɛ kɛŋa ɔgla, tsyina kɛbɛtɛkpɛ mɛ ɔyɛ tsyɛ ɔkɔ yɛ tɛ abɔ.
Klɛ onu gɛ anɔ teli asama wɔ akɔ wɔ kesi awi nɛ, yɛkɔ kabha yɛ nɛ tsyɛ ɔta kɔ yɛ.
Anɔ teli atrɔ wɔa bha sɛ ɔgbanɛ yɛ kidzo kekplo tierikpo, ga bukplo tɔbha nɛ yɛ.
Kɔ anɔ nɛ gɛ eebisi wɔɛ dɔ, klɛ tɛ tsyina kede ɔkpɛ anɔ nɛ gɛ asa pa kɛdɔ tili nɛ wɔ ahwɛ.
Tɛɖuɖɔ Kɔ Bagɛ Ba Dɛ Pɛɛ Wɔ “No ti nu sɛ ba ɖɔ asɛ, ‘Pɛɛ wɔhaɛ kibui, tɛ ogu anɔ gɛ ata pɛɛ wɔ.’ Pɔ itsre nɔ sɛ, nɔ ɖɔ bagɛ ba taa pɛɛ wɔnɔ, tɛ no bisi kɛdzyɔgo kɔ bagɛ ba kpatɔnɔ wɔnɔ, sɛ tɛ nɔ bo dzi beyi kɔ wɔnɔ Aka nɛ owũsise.
Yɛ akɔ sɛ yɛ kiwi nɛ yɛɛ kɔ ezizi nɛ adzyɔgo, klɛ aakɔ sɛ subha adɔ abalɛ adzyɔgo nɛ ezizi nɛa bha.
Onu gɛ ɔɔɖɔ bagɛ baa ɖɔ wɔ, kide ɔbɔ mɔ nɛ kɛlɛ mɛ?
Sɛ badɔdzyɔ nɛ tsyɛ baa bhɛtɛ ana?
Klɛ onu gɛ ɔɔsɛnɔ wadzyalɛ tite ko, kide kinu sɛ ɔɔbhɛtɛ dɛ bagɔgɔɛ?
Sɛ bagɛ ba kpɛ kɛtɔkpuesi kɔ kɛdɔ bhlatɔ nɛ tsyɛ baa bhɛtɛ kana?
Nɔ za nɛ tɛnɛna mɛ, ansɛ gɛ wɔnɔ Owũsise Aka nɛ alɛ nɛ tɛnɛna mɛ.
Kɛdɔkɛkasɛ Nɛ Kɛdɔkukɔ Shu “Dii mɔ sɛ ɔtɛ ‘bhɛtɛ wɔ ebuidzyɔgo’ nɛ banɔa mɛ, sɛ tɛ ba mɔ wɔ.
Onu gɛ ɔbhɛtɛ ana, ɔtɛ bɔ yɛkɛ kɛbhɛnyɛbhɛ denɔ wɔ Aka nɛ Owũsise nɛ ɔkɔ.
“So onu gɛ ɔɔkɔ etsyutsyuini dɔ, tɛ kpɛ kɛlɛ ogugu ganɔ buxulɔ̃ɛ bubɔ mɛ, ansɛ gɛ itroelete nɛ baa bhɛtɛ nɛ ixogokɔevu nɛ mɛ nɛ edzogbla nɛa bha, sɛ tɛ be ku anɔ awɔ̃.
Itsre wɔnɔ kɛgba sɛ, bagɛ baa bhɛtɛ ana ba tɛ yɛkɛ balɛ ahwɛhuhu nɛ petee.
Pɔ onu gɛ ɔɔkɔ anɔɔ nɛ gɛ alɛasɛ ba kɔ kɛdɔ, tɛ kɔ wɔ kɛbɛtɛkpɛ ɔhwɛ nɛ oti kɛdɔnɔ nɛ gɛ kɛŋa ɔhwɛ nɛ ɔɔbhɛtɛ, sɛ tɛ wɔ kɛdɔ kukɔ nɛ za tikpukpu mɛ.
Klɛ mɛ ko Wɔaka, nɛ gɛ aamɔ kɛdɔ nɛ tɛkpukpu mɛ nɛ aba buya kɛlɛ kɛbhɛ akɔ wɔ.
Kpayakuklu “Klɛ kibe nɔɔ nɛ gɛ ɔsɛ okulukpaya, tɛbhɛtɛ ansɛ gɛ itroelete nɛ baa bhɛtɛ, alasɛ balɛ nɛɛ ba pɛɛa sɛ tɛ ba za kititi nɛ oxogokɔevu nɛm, anɛ edzogbla nɛa bha sɛ tɛ banɔ ba mɔ balɛ.
Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, balɛ nɛɛ di na tɛ yɛkɛ balɛ ahwɛhuhu nɛ petee.
Pɔ onu gɛ no bo kulu Kpaya, no tsoku wɔnɔ bee vu nɛ mɛ, tɛ nɔ da opupu tɛ no kulu wɔnɔ Aka nɛ gɛ ba taa mɔ.
Klɛ wɔnɔ Aka, gɛ aamɔ kibuinyɛbui gɛ ba bhɛtɛ nɛ tikpukpu mɛ, aba buya kɛlɛ kɛbhɛ akɔ nɔ.
Klɛ kibe nɔɔ nɛ gɛ ókulukpaya, nɔ tɔɔ zɔ kpɛ igugu anɛ kaɖɔ ɖuɖɔ gelee ansɛ bagɛ ba dɛ sɔlɛ, alasɛ balɛ bee di asɛ ganɔ kana mɛ tɛ be nu balɛɛ dɔ.
Nɔ tɛ za ansɛ balɛ, alasɛ wɔnɔ Aka enyi kɛgɛ nɔɔ pɛɛ flogo pɛ nɔ bɔ ɖɔ sɛ obisi yɛ.
“Ɔtsɔ̃, kanii, alɛ asɛ tɛ no zo klukpaya: “ ‘Bulɔ Aka nɛ owũsise, wɔɛ nyi la ba kpɛ nɛ abha, Kɔ wɔ bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ ɔba, wɔ tɛpɛpɛɛ lɔ ba bhɛtɛ nɛ kesukpa nɛabha, ansɛ gɛ kɛlɛ nɛ owũsise.
Kɔ lɔ obo nɛ kɛŋɛŋa.
Yɛkɔ bulɔ buzizi nɛ otsye lɔ, ansɛ gɛ bulɔ tsyɛ bu yɛkɔ buzizi tsye bagɛ ba bhɛtɛ buzizi amɛna bulɔ kɔ.
Klɛ tɛ gbanɔ lɔ kpɛ tɛfifekedi mɛ, pɔ bu lɔ odenɔ ezizi nɛ ahwɛ mɛ.’ Alasɛ onu gɛ ɔyɛkɔ tsye bagɛ ba bhɛtɛ buzizi amɛna wɔ kɔ, wɔ Owũsise Aka nɛ tsyɛ aba yɛkɔ etsye wɔ.
Pɔ onu gɛ ɔɔtɛ yɛkɔ buzizi otsye anɔ, wɔ Aka nɛ tsyɛ atɛ ba yɛkɔ etsye wɔ.
Kɛdɔkɛkasɛ Nɛ Onugbu Nyɛnya Shu “Onu gɛ nɔɔ sɛ tɛ nɔ nya onugbu, nɔ tɔɔ bhɛtɛ ishu ansɛ butɔ mɛ nɔ kpasɛ, ansɛ gɛɛ betroni na bhɛtɛ, alasɛ balɛ bee ɖuɖu amɛ nɛm sɛ tɛ ba wɛ̃ ansɛ banɔ gɛ baa nya inugbu.
Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, batɛ yɛkɛ bala abhɛ nɛ petee.
Pɔ onu gɛ nɔɔ sɛ tɛ nɔ nya onugbu, nɔ kpɛ bubɔ nɛ adamɛ tɛ no plu amɛ, sɛ tɛ atɛ wɛ̃ kɔ banɔ ansɛ onugbu nɔɔ nya, pɔ kɔ wɔnɔ Aka nɛ gɛ nɔ tɔɔ mɔ, gɛ yɛ aamɔ kɛkanyaka gɛ kɛɛ bhɛtɛ nɛ tɛkpukpu mɛ, aba buya kɛbhɛ akɔ nɔ.
Kɛdɔ Bɛbala Lu Nɛ Owũsise “Nɔ tɛ bala wɔnɔ kɛkesrɔdɔ nɛ kesukpa nɛa bha, gɛ babɔ nɛ budzyewule lɛ gɛ ba zi kɛ lɛ, bezi tsyɛ be be zuruɛ kɛ lɛ.
Pɔ nɔ bala wɔnɔ kɛkesrɔdɔ nɛ owũsise kɔ ishu, ɔkɛlɛ bugɛ anɛ budzyewule ma gɛ ba zi kɛ lɛ, bezi tsyɛa tɛ be tsoku ɔkɛlɛ pɛ be be zuru.
Alasɛ ɔkɛlɛ gɛ anɔ kɛdɔ dzyɔgo kɛɛ lɛ ɔkɛlɛ yɛ idzyi nɛ aaza.
“Kɛwɔ̃hũ kɛ lɛ nu kanɛgbɛ kɔ anɔosi.
Onu gɛ wɔ awɔ̃hũ nɛ abɔ, wɔ anɔ nɛ petee obo yuku nɛ kifu gɛ kɛɛ tã.
Pɔ onu wɔ awɔ̃hũ nɛ amɛtã, wɔ anɔɔ nɛ petee obo yuku nɛ otumu.
So, onu gɛ kifu nɛ gɛ lɛ wɔ mɛ nɛ nu otumu kpɛkpa, kɛlɛ otumu ɔɔlɛlɛ nɛ obo tri!
“Anɔnyanɔ atɛ ba na axwɛ dɛ kɔ baka tɛabha.
Aba ɖɔ teli adɛ teli, klɛ aba mɔ ɔhwɛ kɔ teli adɛ teli.
Ɔtɛ bɔɔ na axwɛ dɛ kɔ Kpaya anɛ Ehoeyi.
Tɛ Ganɛ Awɔ̃ “So, itsre nɔ, nɔ tɛ ga nɛ awɔ̃ nɛ wɔnɔ ɛkpãm, kɛ gɛ nɔ bɔ ŋa pɛ nɔ bɔ wɛ̃, ɔdɔgɔsɛ kɛpɔtɛ gɛ no bo nyumu nɛ shu.
Ɛkpã nɛ dɛ zhã dɛ kɛŋɛŋa, klɛ anɔosi nɛ tsyɛ ɔdɛ zhã dɛ kɛpɔtɛ?
Di kɛlɛɛ mɛ buzhuɔɛ, butɛ ɖa kɛdɔ, butɛ bu kɛdɔ nɛ buya mɛ akpɛ iwule mɛ, tsyɛ wɔnɔ Owũsise Aka nɛ aanyunɔ bulɛ.
Sɛ nɔ lɛ otugba kɔ lɛ?
Anee gɛ alɛ wɔnɔ mɛ pɛ yɛ awɔ̃ gɛganɔ nɛ aba na ɔɖa tɛta torikpo ayɛkɔ ata yɛ ɛkpã?
“Klɛ kide so pɛ nɔɔ ganɛ awɔ̃ nɛ kɛdɔ nyunyumu shu?
Di kana gɛ kpɔkɔɛ nɛ ayakpam nɛ eeshe.
Ba taa wa kɛxwɛ pɛ ɔdɔgɔsɛ bee tro oɖoti.
Pɔ itsre nɔ sɛ, Salomo anɛ yɛ ehoeyidɔ nyunyumu mɛ petee tsyɛ adɛ pudi ansɛ kpɔkɔɛ.
Onu gɛ kana Kpaya eenyumuɛ dɔ kɔ tɛwa nɛ ayakpa mɛ, gɛ kɛ lɛ ɔkɛ̃ nɛ oboo klɛ kivu pɛ ba ba yɛkɔ atɛ̃a kpɛ kifu mɛ, kide so pɛ Kpaya etee nyumu kɛdɔ kɔ nɔ adɛ, O tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa bhli anɔ?
So nɔ tɔɔ ganɛ awɔ̃, tɛ nɔ zɔɔ ɖɔ sɛ, ‘Kide lɔ ba ŋa?’ ɔdɔgɔsɛ ‘Kide lɔ ba wɛ̃?’ pɛ ‘Kide lɔ ba nyumu?’ Alasɛ bagɛ ba dɛ yɛkɛ Kpayɛa bha ŋa balɛ akpatɔnɔ kɛdɔɛ nɛɛ di petee, klɛ wɔnɔ Owũsise Aka nɛ enyi asɛ kɛdɔɛ nɛ petee zhã wɔnɔ.
Pɔ pɛɛ yɛ bukusi ɔŋakɔ nɛ yɛ tɛnɛnamɛzɛza nɛ oputɔnɔ, klɛ la ba yɛkɔ kɛdɔɛ nɛ petee tsyɛ ata kɔ nɔ.
So tɛ ganɛ awɔ̃ nɛ kivu shu, alasɛ kivu nahwɛ ba ganɛ kɛlɛ shu awɔ̃.
Kiwinyɛɛwi kɛ lɛ nɛ kɛlɛ nahwɛ tibui.
Kebhui Kukulu Nɛ Ɔhayɛ “Tɛ kuluebhui nɛ anɔ, tɛ le be kulu nɛ wɔ tsyɛ.
Alasɛ kana gɛ okuluebhui nɛ banɔ, kana le be kulu nɛ wɔ tsyɛ, klɛ kedzyidzyi nɔɔ nɛ gɛ ɔyɛkɔ odzyidzyi kɔ anɔ, kalɛ la ba yɛkɔ edzyidzyi kɔ wɔ tsyɛ.
“Kide pɛ odoo di kishi bhli nɛ gɛ kpasɛ wɔhaɛ nɛ kɛwɔ̃hũ nɛ mɛ ɔkɔ, pɛ ɔshɛnahwɛ kesukpogunu nɛ gɛ ka kpasɛ wɔɛ yɛ nɛ mɛ nɛ shu?
Kɛlɛ obo tsre wadzya sɛ, ‘Kɔ mɛ bu kishi nɛ kɛwɔhũ nɛ mɛ kɔ wɔ,’ nɛ kibe lɛ gɛ kesukpogunu alɛ wɔɛyɛ nɛ mɛ kibenyɛbe?
Wɔ etroni, bu kesukpogunu nɛ wɔ kɛwɔ̃hũ nɛ mɛ, tɛ ɔmɔ mɔmɔ kɔ wadzya nɛ yɛ tɛbubu.
“Tɛ yɛkɔ kɛdɔnɔɔ nɛ gɛ kɛlɛ shu bhui nɛ ɔkɔ bukudzɔgɛ, tɛ yɛkɔ wɔ kɛdɔ ŋɛŋaedzi nɛ ɔtɛɛ kpɛ kɔ bahɛ.
Onu gɛ ɔbhɛtɛ ana, ba ba ga kɛlɛa bha nɛ balɛ ɛtsrɛ, klɛ le be tsyina atɔ wɔ klɛ la ba tswɛ wɔ mɛ akpɛ bupɛ pɛɛpɛ.
Bisi, Pɛɛ, Bho Opupu “Bisi tɛ ba kɔ wɔ, pɛɛ tɛ ɔmɔ, bho opupu tɛ ba danɛ akɔ wɔ.
Alasɛ, anɔnyanɔ gɛ eebisi ayɛkɛ; agɛ apɛɛ kɛdɔ amɔɛ dɔ, klɛ agɛ eebho opupu ba danɛ akɔ yɛ.
“Anee gɛ yeyi ebe bisi yɛ gbɛgbɛvu pɛ aba yɛkɔ kɛklãgbu akɔ yɛ?
Ɔdɔgɔsɛ ebisi kɛkpã pɛ aba yɛkɔ eblidzya akɔ yɛ?
Onu wɔnɔ, kɛlɛ lɛm sɛ nɔ tsɔmɔ pɔ, no ti kana gɛ nɔ bɔ yɛkɔ kɛdɔ dzyɔgo ɔkɔ wɔnɔ bunuvɔɛ, kɛlɛ ɔyɛkɔ dɛ wɔnɔ Aka nɛ owũsise nɛ ataa yɛkɔ kɛdɔ dzyɔgo akɔ bagɛ bee bisi yɛ!
So, nɛ kibuinyɛbui mɛ, bhɛtɛ kibui ɔvɛnɔ anɔbhlatɔ kɔ ansɛ gɛ ɔpɛɛ sɛ babhɛtɛ amɛna wɔ kɔ, alasɛ kɛɛnɛ kɛlɛ xogo bhɛtɛ Ɔshã anɛ Batɔnu.
Budunu Shuɛ Nɛ Bunɛnɛ “Ga kidzo shuɛ nɛ otsoku.
Alasɛ, kedunu nɛnɛ nɛ kidzo nɛnɛ kɛlɛ da yi buzizi mɛ, klɛ be gelee baa ga kɛlɛ etsoku.
Pɔ kedunu bhli nɛ kidzo shuɛ kɛlɛ tɔnɔ vɛ ɛkpã mɛ, klɛ banɔ bhli teli ko ba la mɔɛ lɛ.
Osi Nɛ Ɔlɛ Eyuyu “No lu awɔ̃ nɛ itro batɔnu.
Baa ba wɔnɔ amɛ nɛ ibhoshi buplukpa kɛdɔnyunyumu mɛ, pɔ nɛ kɛmɛ, be nu ayakpam bukudzɔgɛ tsutsɔmɔ.
Ganɔ balɛ eyuyu nɛ mɛ nɔ bɔ yɛkɔ ɔkpɛ balɛ kɛxawũ.
Ba gɔ omumɔɛ edenɔ magɔsim pɛ ɔdɔgɔsɛ ɔgɔ denɔ buli mɛ?
Kana osi dzyɔgo kanyaka ooyu eyuyu dzyɔgo, pɔ osi kpã eyuyu kpã loo yu.
Osi dzyɔgo ɔtɛ bo yu eyuyu kpã, klɛ osi kpã ɔtɛ bo yu eyuyu dzyɔgo.
Osi kanyaka gɛ otoo yu eyuyu dzyɔgo be te ɔlɛ ebho klɛ baa yɛkɔ atɛ̃ akpɛ kifum.
Kɛlɛ so, ganɔ balɛ eyuyu nɛ mɛ ɔbɔ yɛkɔ ɔkpɛ balɛ kɛxawũ.
“Ganɛ anɔnyanɔ gɛ eekulu mɛ asɛ, ‘Apalete, Apalete,’ yɛ ebe tsoku bukusi ɔŋakɔ nɛ owũsise, pɔ aanɔ nɛ gɛ aabhɛtɛ atrɔ mɛ Aka nɛ gɛ alɛ owũsise nɛ tɛpɛpɛa bha.
Bee gelee aba ɖɔ etsre mɛ nɛ kiwi lɛ nɛa bha sɛ, ‘Apalete, Apalete ganɛ wɔɛ nyi mɛ lɔɔ ɖɔ ebui lu, klɛ lɔ kɛka ɛfufɔɛkpã bu klɛ bu bhɛtɛ ebui gɛ eyinɔ anɔ gelee?’ Kɛlɛ mɛ ɛba tsre alɛ wee sɛ, ‘Itinyi nɔ.
Nɔ tsuvɛ nɛ mɛ ɔbha, wɔnɔ ebuikpã bhɛbhɛtɛ elete!’ Ebuinyi Nɛ Agã Bevudzu “Kɛlɛ so anɔnyanɔ gɛ enu mɛ ebuia nɛ, klɛ ayɛkɔ alɛ akpɛ tɛbhɛbhɛtɛ mɛ asɔnɔ anɔ nyinyibui gɛ edzu buvu atrɔ kɛklãgbua bha.
Subha aba dɔ, nɛ budekeni, klɛ kɛlɛɛ ba fu hunɔ buvu; tsyɛ bɔdɛ kpa, alasɛ buvu nɛ bu denɔ bɔlɛ kesikpɛkpɛ nɛ kɛklãgbua bha.
Pɔ anɔnyanɔ gɛ enu mɛ ebuia klɛ adɛ yɛkɔ kpɛ tɛbhɛbhɛtɛ mɛ asɔnɔ agã gɛ edzu buvu atrɔ anyɛsɛa bha.
Subha aba dɔ, nɛ budekeni, klɛ kɛlɛɛ nɛ ba fu hunɔ buvu klɛ butsra.” Gɛ Yesu aɖɔ ebuia nɛ beke, yɛ kɛdɔkɛkasɛ nɛ bhɛtɛ banɔɛza nɛ bi, alasɛ akasɛ kɛdɔ ansɛ anɔ gɛ kabhaŋɛŋa ka lɛ yɛ ahwɛ, klɛ ganɛ ansɛ balɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ.
Anyɛ Nɛ Bunyadzɛdzã Gɛ Yesu ede Butu nɛa bha aba, banɔɛza za yɛe de.
Anyɛ teli gɛ anya bunyadzɛdzã ebe dzu ekuisie si akɔ yɛ asɛ, “Apalete, onu gɛ ɔbɔ dɛmɛ, tɛ oplu mɛ shu.” Yesu ebu yɛ ɔhwɛ klɛ ehunɔ anyɛ.
Klɛ aɖɔ asɛ, “Ɛdɛmɛ.
Kɔ wɔshu bhui!” Ko klɛ anyɛ nɛ bunya dzɛdzã nɛ beke kɔ yɛ.
Klɛ Yesu etsre yɛ asɛ, “Di kɛlɛ ɔkɔ sɛ odi tsre anɔnyanɔ.
Pɔ vɛ, tɛ ɔdɔ yɛkɔ wɔ ishu nɛ ɔkasɛ kpayanɔ tɛ ɔbhɛtɛ kɛdɔ kukɔ ansɛ gɛ Mosesɛ aɖɔ, tɛ kidzi kibuimɔɖɔ kɔ banɔ.” Keyutugbani Aka Teli Tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa Kibe lɛ gɛ Yesu etsoku Kapenaum nɛɛ, keyutugbani teli atɔnɛ yɛ aba ebe bisi tɛpɛplɛnɔ.
Asɛ, “Apalete, mɛ axwɛdɛ teli awɔlɛdɔ klɛ agba eli mɛ bupa nɛm klɛ akpasɛ butɔm gɛganɛɛ.” Yesu etsre yɛ asɛ, “Ɛba vɛ tɛ ɛda beke yɛ bunya.” Keyutugbani nɛ ebu kɛlɛ nu asɛ, “Apalete, ɛdɛ dzyenɔ sɛ tɛ ɔba mɛ ovutɔe si.
Pɔ ɖɔ kibui nɛ ko, tɛ mɛ axwɛdɛ nɛ bunya nɛ bubeke.
Alasɛ mɛnahwɛ inu anɔ gɛ ɛkpasɛ ɔshãe si, gɛ keyutugbani ba lɛ mɛe si.
Itsre anɔ sɛ ‘Vɛ,’ ko aavɛ, ‘Ba,’ ko anɔ aaba.
Itsre mɛ axwɛdɛ sɛ, ‘Bhɛtɛ kɛdɔɛ’ nɛ ko, klɛ aabhɛtɛ kɛ lɛ.” Gɛ Yesu enu ebuia nɛ, le yinɔ yɛ klɛ aɖɔ etsre bagɛ ba lɛ yɛede nɛ asɛ, “Itsre wɔnɔ kɛgba sɛ, ɛka mɔ anyɛnyanyɛ ana di nɛ Izraɛl gɛ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa gbɛgbla nɛɛ di lɛ yɛ ahwɛ.
Itsre nɔ sɛ banɔ gelee ebe de owuwu anɛ ozhizhi, klɛ la ba za balɛ ɛzakɔ nɛ kɛdɔŋakɔ nɛ Abraham, Isakɛ anɛ Yakɔb nɛ owũsisɛ bukusi nɛ mɛ.
Pɔ ba ba yɛkɔ bagɛ ba kpasɛ bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛesi nɛ atɛa kpɛ ɔtɔ, nɛ otumu mɛ, nɛ ɔkɛlɛ gɛ iyuyo nɛ eletɛtã aba za.” Klɛ Yesu etsre keyutugbani aka nɛ asɛ, “Vɛ!
Kɛ ba bhɛtɛ ansɛ gɛ ɔyɛkɛ klɛa bha ŋa.” Klɛ yɛ axwɛdɛ nɛ bunya nɛ bu beke nɛ ɔɖa ɔɔlɛlɛ nɛm.
Yesu Ebeke Banɔ Gelee Banya Gɛ Yesu ebe ku Petro bupa nɛ mɛ, amɔ Petro yandze nɛ gɛ elie si nɛ buwuiunya.
Yesu ehunɔ yɛ ɔhwɛ nɛ ko klɛ buwui nɛ beke, klɛ evua lɔ klɛ akpa yɛa bha di.
Gɛ owulago ɔna, ba yɛkɔ banɔ gelee gɛ ɛfufɔɛkpã za balɛa bha nɛ amɛna Yesu, klɛ akɛka ɛfufɔɛ nɛ ebu nɛ kibui tirikpo ko tɛɖuɖɔ klɛ ebeke banɔ nɛ petee banya.
Kibui kɛ ba kɛlɛ mɛ sɛ tɛ ba yɛkɔ amɔ kɛgɛ baɖɔ aganɔ atɔnu Yezaya bha sɛ: “Ayɛkɔ bulɔ maza mazamɔ klɛ etuku bulɔ banya.” Yesu Kedezɛza Kedziŋɛŋa Gɛ Yesu amɔ banɔɛza nɛ yɛ ɔbha, akɔ sɛ ba tsɔkɛ kɛvɔ nɛ avɛ ogbigbe bhla nɛa bha.
Klɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ teli aba ebe tsre yɛ asɛ, “Adɔkasɛ, ɛba za wɔe de vɛ ɔkɔnyɔkɔ gɛ ɔɔvɛ.” Yesu ebu lɛ nu sɛ, “Ayakpamkudzɔgɛ nɛ mɔ ɛlɛ okukɔ klɛ kɛlɛɛm buzhuɔɛ nɛ tsyɛ mɔ bulɛ evu, pɔ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ aka mɔ ɔkɛlɛ gɛ ebe lu yɛ tɔkpu.” Adɔkpasɛ teli tsyɛ etsre yɛ asɛ, “Apalete, putɔnɔ kɔ mɛ vɛ tɛ ɛda vubɔ maka.” Pɔ Yesu etsre yɛ asɛ, “Za mɛe de, tɛ ɔkɔ betsitsi nɛ ba vubɔ balɛ anɔtsitsi.” Yesu Adzrɔ Kɛlɛgɛganɛ Klɛ etsoku opupu nɛ mɛ klɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ ba tɔnɔ yɛe de.
Nɛ mati mati mɛ kɛlɛgbla tili ba kpaa fu gɛganɛɛ nɛ kɛvɔ nɛa bha, gɛ akɔsɛ kɛlɛ nɛ buni nɛ wu ga opupu nɛa bha.
Pɔ Yesu yɛ eli azaa dɔ tra.
Badɔkpasɛ nɛ ba vɛ ada nyɛmɛ yɛ, klɛ la ɖɔ asɛ, “Apalete, bu lɔ!
Bu baa dɔe ni!” Klɛ etsre alɛ sɛ, “wɔnɔ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa bhli elete, kide so pɛ noo si kifu ana?” Klɛ evualɔ klɛ akpɛ ɔshã kɔ kɛlɛɛ anɛ buni, klɛ ɔkɔnyɔkɔ dɔ sɛ̃ɛ.
Kibui nɛ bhɛtɛ banɔ nɛ bi klɛ be bisi asɛ, “Anyɛ ɖuweɖui di naa?
Gɛ kɛlɛ anɛ buni tsyɛ ta yɛ batɔ!” Ɛfufɔɛkpã Banyɛ Tɛabha Banya Tɛbibeke Gɛɛ ede ku kedea pɛ nɛ Gadarenisɛ kɛdɔ nɛ mɛ, ɛfufɔɛkpã banyɛ tiabha teli be koeyi denɔ idzre nɛ shi aba tsyanɛ yɛ.
Baa nyagba nɛ anɔ nɛ ɔkɛlɛ gɛ kɛkɔ sɛ anɔnyanɔ ataa naa fla nɛ ɔkɛlɛ.
Ɛfufɔɛkpã elete nɛ ba kpɛ ogugu asɛ, “Kidee wɔ ɔɔpɛ denɔ bulɔ kɔ, Kpaya yɛ Eyi?” “Ɔba ɔkɛ̃ sɛ tɛ ɔbɔ nyama bulɔ flogo tɛ bulɔ ɔɖa nɛ mɛ ɔbɔ na dza?” Nɛ balɛ ɔbha nɛɛ be, bahɛha tili dzi zɛ ŋa kɛdɔ.
Ɛfufɔɛkpã nɛ kɔ Yesu kɛtɔkpu sɛ, “Onu gɛ ɔbɔ kɛka lɔ obu, klɛ tɛ ɔyɛkɔ lɔ ɔkpɛ bahɛ nɛ gɛ beli ɔkɛlɛ nɛ mɛ.” Etsre alɛ asɛ, “Nɔ vɛ!” Klɛ lɛ koeyi da tsoku bahɛ nɛ mɛ, klɛ bahɛha nɛ petee si da dɔ ku kɛvɔ nɛ mɛ klɛ be tsi eku buni nɛ mɛ.
Bagɛ balɛ agbanɛ bahɛha nɛ si ashɛ̃ avɛ ɔma nɛ mɛ ada ɖɔ kana gɛ ebui nɛ aba za kɔ ɛfufɔɛkpã elete.
Klɛ ɔma mɛ banɔ nɛ petee koeyi avɛ sɛ tɛ ba da tsyanɛ Yesu.
Klɛ gɛɛ ba mɔ yɛ, ba kɔ yɛ tɔkpu asɛ ashɛ̃ nɛ balɛ bee.
Yesu Ebeke Anɔgbɛgba Bunya Yesu atɛɛ ku kenia bha opupu toli mɛ, klɛa tsɔkɛ avɛ yɛ nahwɛ ɔma nɛ mɛ.
Banɔ teli be tuku anɔgbɛgba nɛ oputsoa bha ebe lu.
Gɛ Yesu amɔ bagɛ ba mɛna anɔ nɛ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa, etsre anɔgbɛgba nɛ asɛ, “Kpɛɛ te, meyi; ba yɛkɔ wɔ buzizi nɛ etsye wɔ.” Nɛ kɛɛ anɛ nɛ shu, ɛshãdɔkasɛ nɛ ba kpa ɖɔ nɛ aglɔ mɛ asɛ, “Anyaa nɛɛ aabhɛtɛ ebusobui!” Gɛ Yesu atɛ mɔ balɛ atɔkpu nɛ mɛ so, aɖɔ asɛ, “Kide so pɛɛ nɔ nyɛna atɔkpumkpã ebui ɔkpɛ wɔnɔ idzyi mɛ ana?
Kiɖue gɛ lɛ bubɔɛbɔɛ dɛ: sɛ tɛ baɖɔ asɛ, ‘Ba yɛkɔ wɔ buzizi nɛ etsye wɔ,’ pɛnɔɔ sɛ tɛ baɖɔ asɛ, ‘Lɔ tɛ ɔga’?
Pɔ sɛ tɛ no ti sɛ Anɔdzyrame Yeyi nɛɛ kabhaŋɛŋa ka lɛ yɛahwɛ nɛ kesukpa nɛa bha sɛ tɛ ayɛkɔ buzizi etsye.” Klɛ aɖɔ etsre anɔgbɛgba nɛ asɛ, “Lɔ, yɛkɔ wɔ oputso tɛ ɔga vɛ bupa mɛ.” Klɛ anyɛ nɛ alɔ klɛ ashɛ̃ avɛ bupa mɛ.
Gɛ banɔɛza nɛ ba mɔ ebuia nɛɛ, kɛ bhɛtɛ balɛ bi, klɛ ba kpɛ Kpaya nɛa bha, agɛ yɛ akɔ banɔ kabhaŋɛŋɛa nɛɛ di.
Mateo Tɛ Kukulu Gɛ Yesu aba shɛ edenɔ ɔkɛlɛ, amɔ anɔ teli gɛ be kulu asɛ Mateo gɛ ezhedzi badɔdzyɔ kɛkpako nɛ mɛ.
Yesu etsre yɛ asɛ, “Za mɛe de,” klɛ Mateo evualɔ klɛ atɔnɔ yɛ.
Gɛ Yesu edzi aŋa kɛdɔ nɛ Mateo bupa mɛ, badɔdzyɔ gelee nɛ “bezizi” nɛ ba ba ŋa kɛdɔ nɛ aplɛnɔ yɛ anɛ badɔkpasɛ.
Gɛ Farisianɛ na mɔa na, be bisi yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ, “Kide so pɛɛ wɔnɔ Adɔkasɛ nɛ xũ nɛ aaŋa kɛdɔ nɛ badɔdzyɔ anɛ ‘bezizi’?” Gɛ enu balɛ tibibisi, Yesu etsre alɛ asɛ, “Ganɛ agɛ ataa nya nɛ yɛ ebisi awani, anyɛnya yɛ alɛ kɔ awani.
Pɔ nɔ vɛ tɛ nɔ dɔ pɛɛ kibui nɛe si onu: ‘Ɛpɛɛ eshutukubui didi, ganɛ busoyiyi.’ Alasɛ ɛdɛ ba kɔ badzyɔgo nɛ tɛkukulu, pɔ kɔ bezizi.” Be Bisi Yesu Ebui Nɛ́ Onugbu Nyɛnya Shu Klɛ Yohanɛsɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ ba klɛ be bisi Yesu asɛ, “Kide so pɛɛ bulɔ anɛ Farisianɛ nɛ bunya onugbu pɛɛ, wɔnɔ nɛ wɔ badɔkpasɛ nɛ xũ nɔ tɔɔ nya onugbu?” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Klɛ adzɛenyine befu ebe ze bi yɛ nɛ kibe lɛ gɛ alɛ balɛ ɔbha?
Kibe tili baa ba gɛ ba ba nyɛna adzɛenyine nɛ agbanɔ ashɛ̃nɔ nɛ balɛ ɔbha, ka ba nya onugbue.
“Anɔnyanɔ atɛ yɛkɔ kɛpɔtɛ gɛ ka dzi kɛkuku akamɛ atsa nɛ kɛvuvɔ, alasɛ ɔkamɛkɔ nɛ ɔbɔ tsyɔɛ koeyi nɛ kɛpɔtɛ nɛ shu, gɛ kɛ ba kɔ sɛ tɛtsyutsyɔɛ nɛ tsɔmɔ dɛa na.
Kana ke anɔ atɛ yɛkɔ bulu vuvɔ akpɛ keluplui kuku mɛ.
Onu gɛ baa bhɛtɛ ana, keluplui nɛ ka ba yɛɛ, klɛ bulu nɛ ba balɛ zi.
Owo, bulu vuvɔ nɛɛ kelutsukpu vuvɔ mɛ la kpɛ bulɛ ka editabha na za mɔmɔe.” Yesu Anyɛmɛ Adzɛnuvɔɛ Tsitsi Klɛ Ebeke Adzɛ Teli Bunya Kibe lɛ gɛ edzi aɖɔ ebuia nɛ, ekusi teli aba edzu ekuisie si akɔ yɛ klɛ aɖɔ asɛ, “Meyiadzɛ nuvɔɛ nɛ etsi ɔtsɔtsiɔ̃.
Pɔ bɔ trɔ ahwɛ nɛ yɛa bha tɛ anyɛmɛ.” Yesu alɔ klɛ aza anyɛ nɛe de avɛ, klɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ tsyɛ atɔnɔ yɛ.
Nɛ kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ adzɛ teli gɛ dzyosu eekoeyi nɛ yɛ shu agɔ lɔfɔntubha nyɔɔ, aga yɛede klɛ ebe hunɔ yɛ awi nɛ butɔ.
Adzɛ nɛ aɖɔ etsre yɛ shu asɛ, “Onu gɛ ɛhunɔ yɛ awi nɛ butɔ nɛ ko, mɛ bunya nɛ ba beke.” Yesu etsyina edi adzɛ.
Klɛ aɖɔ asɛ, “Kpɛɛ te, eyiadzɛ,” “wɔ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa nɛ tɛ beke wɔ bunya.” Klɛ adzɛ nɛ bunya nɛ gbla beke kɔ yɛ denɔ ɔɖɔ lɛ nɛ mɛ.
Gɛ Yesu etsoku agɛ aaŋɛabha nɛ bupa nɛ mɛ amɔ bagɛ baa bɔ ezhue anɛ banɔɛza anɛ igugu kpɛkpɛ, klɛ asɛ, “Nɔ shɛ nɛ ɔklɛ.
Adzɛnuvɔɛ nɛ edi tsi pɔ tra yɛa dɔ.” Pɔ banɔ nɛ amɔɛ yɛ.
Gɛ be bu banɔɛza nɛ eyinɔ beke, Yesu etsoku atɔnɔ adzɛnuvɔɛ klɛ ada nyɛna yɛ ɔhwɛ klɛ evu alɔ.
Yɛ tɛnyɛnyɛmɛ nɛ yi kana nɛ kibee lɛ nɛ petee.
Yesu Ebeke Anhũpu Nɛ Omumuu Banya Gɛ Yesu ashɛ̃ aavɛ denɔ ɔkɛlɛ, awɔ̃hũ pupuelete tɛabha ba za yɛe de, nɛ yɛ tɛ kukulu sɛ, “Di bulɔ eshutukubui, Daviti Yeyi!” Kibe lɛ nɛ gɛ etsoku buvu nɛ mɛ beke, awɔ̃hũ pupuelete tɛabha ba tɔnɔ yɛ avɛ, klɛ ebisi balɛ asɛ, “Nɔ yɛkɛ ɔŋa sɛ ɛba na kibui nɛ bubhɛtɛ?” Be bui lɛ nu asɛ, “Ee, Apalete.” Ɔkɛlɛ Yesu ehunɔ balɛ awɔ̃hũ nɛ klɛ aɖɔ asɛ, “Nɛ wɔnɔ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa nɛ nu kɛ ba kɛlɛ mɛ kɔnɔ”, klɛ balɛ awɔ̃hũ nɛ adanɛ.
Yesu akpɛ balɛ ɔshã gɛganɛɛ asɛ, “Nɔ dii lɛ ɔkɔ sɛ anɔnyanɔ eti ti kibuinyɛbui edenɔ kibui nɛ shu.” Pɔ ba shɛ avɛ ada kaka kibui nɛ akpɛ kibe lɛlɛ nɛ mɛ petee.
Gɛ bee koeyi nɛ ɔkɔlɛ, ba yɛkɔ anyɛ teli gɛ ɔfufɔɛkpã otsri yɛa bha pɛɛ ataa na kaɖɔ ɖɔ nɛ amɛna Yesu.
Klɛ gɛ akɛka ɔfufɔɛ nɛ ebu beke anyɛ nɛ akpa kaɖɔ ɖɔ.
Kibui nɛ bhɛtɛ banɔɛza nɛ bi klɛ ba ɖɔ asɛ, “Kibuinyɛbui ana ka ba kɛlɛ mɛ di nɛ Izraɛl.” Pɔ Farisianɛ na asɛ, “Ɔfufɔɛkpã ekusi nɛa bha aaga pɛ aakɛka ɛfufɔɛkpã nɛ ebu.” Baxwɛwa Nɛ Be Di Kpe Yesu aga ɛma anɛ ɛmabhli nɛ petee mɛ, aakasɛ dɔ nɛ ixogokɔevu nɛ mɛ, klɛ aaɖɔ kibui dzyɔgo nɛ edenɔ bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ shu klɛ eebeke banyanyanya nɛ banɔ mɛ.
Gɛ amɔ banɔɛza, eshutukubui eku yɛ nɛ balɛ, alasɛ ba kpɛ balɛ bunuhu klɛ tɛpɛplɛnɔ kɛma kɔa lɛ, ansɛ ibhoshi gɛ agbɛgbanɔ ama kɔ ɛlɛ.
Klɛ etsre yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ, “Kɛdɔbubu nɛ lɛ kpi pɔ baxwɛwa nɛ ba dɛ na tɛashɛ̃.
No bisi Kɛxwɛaka sɛ tɛ asɛsɛ baxwɛwa nɛ buya nɛ mɛ.”
Yesu Akpɛ Yɛ Banɔ Lɔfɔntɛabha Yesu ekulu yɛ badɔkpasɛ lɔfɔntɛabha nɛ amɛna yɛ ɔbha klɛ akɔ balɛ kabhaŋɛŋa sɛ tɛ ba yɛkɔ akɛka ɛfufɔɛkpã ebu tɛ be beke banyanyanyɛ di.
Banɔkpɛkpɛ lɔfɔntɛabha nɛ enyi naa: putɔnɔ, Simɔnɛ (gɛ bee kulu asɛ Petro) anɛ yadzya Andrɛasɛ, Yakobo Zebeɖi yɛ eyi, anɛ yɛadzya Yohanɛsɛ, Filipo anɛ Batelemeo, Tomasɛ anɛ Mateo gɛ enu adɔdzyɔ, Yakobo Alfeosɛ yɛ eyi, anɛ Tadeosɛ, Simɔnɛ Zelɔtɛ anɔ anɛ Yuɖasɛ Iskarɔtɛ nɛ, gɛ akpɛ Yesu ahwɛ.
Banɔ lɔfɔntɛabha nɛ gɛ Yesu akpɛ asɛsɛ anɛ ɛshãɛ nɛ asɛ: “Nɔ tɛ ga nɛ bagɛ ba dɛ ayɛkɛ Kpaya abha aŋa ɔdɔgɔsɛ tɛ no do tsoku Samarianɛ ɔma nyɔma mɛ.
Nɔ vɛ Izraɛlanɛ ibhoshi nɛ gɛ lɛla nɛ ɔkɔ.
Onu gɛ nɔɔ vɛ, nɔ ɖɔ kibui nɛ ɔsɛ, ‘Owũsise bukusi nɛ tɛ tsuba.’ No beke banyɛnya nɛ banya, nɔ nyɛmɛ betsitsi, no xule bagɛ baa nya bunyadzɛdzã nɛ shu, nɔ kɛka ɛfufɔɛkpã obu.
Fãa nɔ yɛkɛ, fãa nɔ kɔɛ dɔ.
Nɔ tɛ yɛkɔ sɛkadzɛdzã pɛ sɛkafufu ɔdɔgɔsɛ sɛkahẽhẽ ɔkpɛ wɔnɔ ɔdzadi mɛ, nɔ tɛ yɛkɔ ɔkpɛtɛ kɔ wɔnɔ kidzo gɛga, ɔdɔgɔsɛ kabhawi pɛ ɔtsrɛklɔ nɛ ovusi, alasɛ axwɛwa alɛ kɔ kɛbhɛ yɛyɛkɛ.
“Ɔmanyɔma ɔdɔgɔsɛ obhliyi kanyaka mɛ gɛ noo tsoku, nɔ pɛɛ anɔ dzyɔgo teli ɔkɔ tɛ nɔ za ɔdɔ nanɔ kibe nɔɔ nɛ mɛ gɛ nɔ bɔ shɛ.
Onu gɛ noo tsoku bupa tuli mɛ, nɔ kɔ aye.
Bupa nɔɔ nɛ gɛ bɔɔ yɛkɛ nɔ, nɔ kɔ wɔnɔ ishuyuyɔ nɛ za plɛnɔ bulɛ, kɛɛ ma ana, nɔ kɔ wɔnɔ ishuyuyɔ nɛ tsodzi ba nɔ kɔ.
Onu gɛ anɔ teli atɛ ba yɛkɛ wɔnɔ pɛ ɔdɔgɔsɛ ataa nɔ kibui nɛ atɔ, no xule wɔnɔ butsrukpɔ osumududu nɛ olu bupa ɔdɔgɔsɛ ɔma nɔɔ nɛ mɛ onu gɛ nɔɔ shɛ.
Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, kɛ ba za bubɔɛbɔɛ kɔ Sorom anɛ Gomora nɛ kebhuikluwi nɛa bha ɔyɛkɔ dɛ ɔma nɔɔ lɛlɛ.
Ɛɛsɛsɛ wɔnɔ ansɛ ibhoshi nɛ ayakpam bukudzɔgɛ shi.
So nɔ bhɛtɛ bushɛ ansɛ eblidzya tɛ wɔnɔ shu ibhui ansɛ gɔgɔwii.
“Nɔ lu awɔ̃ nɛ banɔdzyrame, be be vu nɔ ayɛkɔ akpɛ ahwɛ kɔ bamani klɛ ba ba mɛna nɔɛ dɔ nɛ balɛ ixogokɔevu nɛ mɛ.
Nɛ mɛ tɔkpu so ba ba gbanɔ nɔ avɛnɔ baga ŋɛabha anɛ bekusigbla nɛ ɔkɔ ansɛ bebuimɔɖɔ kɔ balɛ anɛ bagɛ be di nu Yuɖanɛ.
Pɔ onu gɛ bee vu nɔ, nɔ tɛ ga nɛ awɔ̃ nɛ kibui nɔ nɛ gɛ nɔ bɔ ɖɔ ɔdɔgɔsɛ kana gɛ nɔ bɔ ɖɔɛ lɛ.
Ɔɖɔ lɛlɛ nɛ mɛ ba ba kɔ nɔ kibui nɔ nɛ gɛ nɔ bɔ ɖɔ, alasɛ kɛ tɛ ba dzi sɛ wɔnɔ ɖɔ kaɖɔ, pɔ wɔnɔ Aka nɛ Ɔfufɔɛ nɛ ɔlɛ ɔbɔ ɖɔ kaɖɔ nɛ ɔganɔ wɔnɔa bha.
“Adzya aba ga yadzya esi ayɛkɔ ada kpɛ butsi mɛ, klɛ aka tsyɛ aba bhɛtɛ ana nɛ yeyi, beyi ba ba lɔ kititi nɛ balɛ eni anɛ aka shu klɛ ba ba yɛkɔ balɛ ada kpɛ butsi mɛ.
Banɔ petee ba tɛ ba dɛmɛ wɔnɔɛ bui akpɛ mɛ so, pɔ aanɔ nɛ gɛ aza mɔmɔ ɔdɔ nanɔ obekekɔ be be bu yɛ.
Kibe lɛ gɛ bakpatɔnɔ nɔ nɛ ɔkɔtoli, no si ɔvɛ ɔkɔ bhlatɔ.
Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, nɔ tɛ bɔ ga Izraɛl ɛma nɛ mɛ beke flogo pɛ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ aba ba.
“Adɔkpasɛ adɛ ɖama dɛ yɛ adɔkasɛ, pɛɛ ɔdɔgɔsɛ axwɛdɛ yɛ aba dɛ yɛ apalete.
Abɔ kɔ adɔkpasɛ sɛ tɛ aza ansɛ yɛ adɔkasɛ, tɛ axwɛdɛ tsyɛ aza anasɛ yɛ apalete.
Onu gɛ bee kulu apaka nɛ asɛ Ɔfufɔɛkpã ekusi, klɛ le be kulu yɛ bupa mɛanɛ!
“So no too si balɛ fu.
Kɛdɔnyɛdɔ ma gɛ ba dɛ lɛ dɔ pɛ ba tɛ ba danɛ dɔ nɛ klɛa bha, ɔdɔgɔsɛ be kpui lɛ pɛ ba tɛ be bui lɛ eyinɔ sɛ be ti.
Kɛgɛ itsre nɔ nɛ otumu mɛ, nɔ ɖɔɛ lɛ nɛ kelizɛzam, kɛgɛ bee tsre nɔ hunihuni, nɔ kpɛ lɛ igugu nɛ buvu aɖam.
No ti si fu nɛ bagɛ be be yi nɔ pɛ ba tɛ ba na kɛtɔwi nɛ buyi.
Pɔ no si fu nɛ agɛ aba na wɔ ɔfufɔɛ anɛ ishuidzya nu yi nɛ fu gɛ tɛ ba ni di mɛ.
Anɛ buyɛ̃kpakpɛ tɔbha ba dɛ kaple ko?
Tsyɛ pɛ tierikpo nɛ bulɛ shi atɛ ba wɔlɛ adɔ kesukpa gɛ odi nu Aka nɛ tɛ pɛpɛɛ.
Klɛ wɔnɔ kɛtɔkputɛka nɛ ada mɛ tsyɛ lɛ tɛkɛkla mɛ.
So no ti si fu, nɔ lɛ kedziŋɛŋa mɛ ɔdɛ buyɛ̃kpakpɛ gelee.
“Anɔnyanɔ gɛ aabaka mɛ bui nɛ banɔdzyrame amɛ, mɛ tsyɛ ba baka yɛ bui nɛ Maka nɛ gɛ alɛ owũsise nɛ amɛ.
Pɔ aanɔ nɛ gɛ ashɛ̃nahwɛ mɛ shu nɛ banɔ amɛ, mɛ tsyɛ ba shɛnahwɛ yɛ shu nɛ Maka nɛ gɛ alɛ Owũsise nɛ amɛ.
“No ti di lɛ ɔsɛ ɛba sɛ tɛ ɛmɛna ishuyuyɔ nɛ kesukpa nɛa bha, ganɛ ishuyuyɔ mɛ mɛna, pɔ keyu.
Alasɛ ɛba sɛ tɛ ɛba tsyina “ ‘eyianyɛ kɔ kititi lulɔ nɛ yaka shu, eyiadzɛ kɔ kititi lulɔ nɛ yeni shu, eyinidze kɔ kititi lulɔ nɛ yandze shu banɔ nɛ gɛ ba dɛ pɛɛ anɔ teli bui be de yɛ bupa mɛ.’ “Anɔnyanɔ gɛ aɖɔ yaka anɛ yeni adɛ mɛ klɛ adɛ na kɔ mayɛ tɛdzidzi, anɔnyanɔ gɛ aɖɔ yɛ eyianyɛ anɛ yɛ eyiadzɛ adɛ mɛ klɛ adɛ na kɔ mayɛ tɛdzidzi, klɛ anɔnyanɔ gɛ adɛ yɛkɔ yɛnahwɛ butsiosi pɛ aaza mɛe de adɛ na kɔ mayɛ tɛdzidzi.
Anɔnyanɔ gɛ aaba pɛɛ yɛ ɛkpã aba lɛla ɛlɛ, klɛ anɔnyanɔ gɛ aaba lɛla yɛ ɛkpã akpɛ mɛ so aba mɔɛ lɛ.
Aanɔ nɛ gɛ aayɛkɛ wɔnɔ mɛ ayɛkɛ, klɛ agɛ aayɛkɛ mɛ ayɛkɛ anɔ nɛ gɛ akpɛ mɛ.
Anɔnyanɔ gɛ aayɛkɛ atɔnu sɛ enu atɔnu so, aba yɛkɛ atɔnui bhɛ, klɛ anɔnyanɔ gɛ aayɛkɛ anɔnɛna sɛ enu anɔnɛna so aba yɛkɛ anɔnɛna kɛbhɛ.
Klɛ onu gɛ anɔ teli aakɔ beyibhlianɛ ɔmayɛ teli buni yuyɔ kantse sɛ enu mɛ adɔkpasɛ so, itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, yɛ tsyɛ atɛ ba lɛla yɛ kɛbhɛ.”
Yesu Nɛ Yohanɛsɛ Enikpɛ Gɛ Yesu aɖɔaɖɔ kɔ yɛ badɔkpasɛ lɔfɔntɛabha nɛ beke, ashɛ̃ nɛ ɔkɛlɛ atɔnɔ avɛ Galelia ɛma nɛ mɛ ada kasɛ dɔ anɛ kibui nɛ tɛɖuɖɔ.
Kibe lɛ gɛ Yohanɛsɛ akpasɛ buvu enu kɛdɔnɔ nɛ gɛ Kristo edzia bhɛtɛ, akpɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ, tɛ be bisi yɛ asɛ, “Wɔ onu agɛ ba sɛ aba ba, pɛnɔɔ bu di anɔ bhlatɔɛ dzoenu?” Yesu ebu klɛ nu asɛ, “No tsodzi ɔvɛ tɛ no do tsre Yohanɛsɛ kɛdɔnɔ nɛ gɛ no nu pɛ nɔɔ mɔ: awɔ̃hũ pupuelete nɛ ba kpaa mɔ, akpatanɛ alɔa ga, bunya dzɛdzãelete nɛ banya nɛ ba shɛ, batɔpu nɛ ba kpa nu, betsitsi nɛ ba nyɛmɛ, klɛ ba ɖɔ kibui dzyɔgo nɛ etsre betsyutsyuini.
Ba yula aanɔ nɛ gɛ ataa wɔlɛ ekoeyi akpɛ mɛ so.” Gɛ Yohanɛsɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ baa shɛ, Yesu akpa kaɖɔ ɖɔ tsre banɔɛza nɛ Yohanɛsɛ shu asɛ: “Kidee no koeyi ɔvɛ ɔdɔ mɔ nɛ ayakpa nɛ mɛ?
Ɔsɔɔ gɛ odzi ofu kɛlɛɛ?
Onu ganɛa na, klɛ kide okoeyi ɔvɛ ɔdɔ mɔ?
Anɔ gɛ enyumu kɛdɔ pupudi?
Ao, banɔ nɛ gɛ bee nyumu kɛdɔ pupudi nɛ balɛ bekusi nɛ bapa mɛ.
Kɛlɛ kide okoeyi ɔvɛ ɔdɔ mɔ?
Atɔnu ɔdɔ mɔ?
Ee, mɛ itsre wɔ, klɛ kɛ dɛ atɔnu tsyɛ.
Anɔa nɛ shu ba ŋlɔmɛ ebuia nɛ asɛ: “ ‘Ɛba kpɛ mɛ axwɛdɛ putɔnɔ kɔ nɔ, yɛ ebe wũse wɔ kidzo nɛ akpɛ otugba kɔ nɔ.’ Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ: Nɛ banɔ nɛ gɛ badzɛ ba mɔ nɛ mɛ akanyaka aka vɛ otugba pɛ agbɛgbla dɛ Yohanɛsɛ Enikpɛ; pɔ agɛ enu ebhliyi nɛ owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ agbɛgbla dɛ yɛ.
Denɔ Yohanɛsɛ Enikpɛ nɛ kibe ɔbɔ nanɔ ɔtsɔ̃ nɛɛ, owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ yɛkɔ amɛgɛganɛ vɛ otugba, klɛ banɔ amɛgɛganɛ ba nyɛna bulɛ evunɔ.
Alasɛ batɔnu anɛ Ɛshã nɛ aɖɔɛ lɛ lu flogo pɛ Yohanɛsɛ.
Klɛ onu gɛ ɔpɛɛ sɛ tɛ ɔyɛkɛ lɛ, yɛ enu Eliya nɛ gɛ aba ba.
Anɔɔ nɛ gɛ batɔ alɛ yɛ, tɛ enu.
“Kide mɛ ɛba yɛkɔ tɛmumɔɛ nɛ mɛ ɛsɔnɔ?
Be dzi ansɛ bunuvɔɛ gɛ be zhiedzi budzi nɛ mɛ pɛ bee kulu bagɔgɔɛ nɛ asɛsɛ asɛ: “ ‘Bu bɔ kizhoe nɛ kɔ nɔ, klɛ no di yu, bu zha iyuyodzɛ klɛ no di bi.’ Alasɛ Yohanɛsɛ aba nɛ maŋa maŋa ɔdɔgɔsɛ awɛ̃ dɔ, klɛ baa ɖɔ asɛ, ‘Evunɔ ɔfufɔɛkpã.’ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ aba nɛ kɛdɔŋɛŋa nɛ kɛdɔwɛ̃wɛ̃, klɛ baa ɖɔ asɛ, ‘Adɔŋagbla anɛ eluwɛ̃ naa, badɔdzyɔ anɛ buziziabhɛtɛ nɛ ɔbhɛa.’ Pɔ kibuinyinyi bu kasɛ nɛ yɛ axwɛwɛwa nɛ mɛ.” Butɔ Kɔ Ɛmagbla Nɛ Gɛ Dɛ Tsyina Kitem Ɔkɛlɛ Yesu ebu ɛmagbla nɛ mɛ gɛ aba bhɛtɛ yɛ ebuiyiyinɔ anɔ nɛa bha agɔ, alasɛ lɛ di tsyina kitem.
“Butɔ kɔ wɔ, Korazin!
Butɔ kɔ wɔ, Bɛtsaɛda!
Otɔsɛ Taɛre anɛ Sidɔn ɛma mɛ ba bhɛtɛ ebuiyiyinɔ anɔa nɛɛ, anlo ɛlɛ xũ nɛ tɛ tsyina etem kukuuku nɛ kpekpeawim zɛza anɛ butɔ sɛsra shu.
Pɔ itsre nɔ sɛ, kɛ ba za bubɔɛbɔɛ kɔ Taɛre anɛ Sidɔn nɛ kebhuiwi nɛa bha dɛ wɔnɔ.
Klɛ wɔ, Kapenaum, be be feke wɔ ewunɔ akpɛ kɛlɛɛ mɛ dza?
Ao, obo zhi okue si ɔyɛkɔ vɛnɔ odzudzukɔ.
Otɔsɛ ebui yiyinɔanɔ gɛ babhɛtɛ nɛ wɔ mɛ edzi asɛ Sodom la bhɛtɛ alɛ, la ta wɔ ɔkɛlɛ ɔbɔ nanɔ oboe wi.
Pɔ itsre nɔ sɛ, kɛba za bubɔɛbɔɛ kɔ Sodom nɛ kebhuiwi nɛa bha ɔyɛkɔ dɛ wɔ.” Bumuene Kɔ Bagɛ Baa Tɔɔ Nɛ kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ Yesu aɖɔ asɛ, “Ɛkpɛ wɔ, nɛabha, mɛ Aka, owũsise nɛ kesukpa Apalete, alasɛ ɔyɛkɔ ebuia nɛ okpu bebuinyi anɛ badɔkpasɛ, klɛ obua lɛ ɔkasɛ bunuvɔɛ bhli.
Ee, Aka, alasɛ kɛnɛ nɛ nu wɔ tɛpɛpɛɛ dzyɔgo.
“Ebui nɛ petee mɛ Aka nɛ atɛ yɛkɔ akpɛ mɛ ahwɛ.
Anɔnyanɔ etinyi Eyi gɛ odinu sɛ Aka, klɛ anɔ nyanɔ etinyi Aka gɛ odinu sɛ Eyi nɛ banɔ nɛ gɛ Eyi nɛ apɛa sɛ tɛ ebu yɛ akasɛ.
“Nɔ ba mɛ ɔkɔ, wɔnɔ ba gɛ nɔɔ tɔ klɛ ebui nɛ adɛ nɔ, tɛ ɛkɔ nɔ bumuene.
Nɔ yɛkɔ mɛ ɔkpakasi nɛ ɔtrɔ shu tɛ nɔ kpasɛ kɛdɔ denɔ mɛ ɔkɔ, alasɛ ɛyɔ klɛ mɛ dɔfɔ̃ɔ nɛ idzyi mɛ, klɛ nɔ bɔ mɔ omuenekɔ kɔ wɔnɔ atɔwi.
Alasɛ mɛ ɔkpakasi nɛ ɔlɛ bubɔɛbɔɛ klɛ mɛ kituku nɛ dzi fukuu.”
Apalete Kɔ Kimuenewi Nɛ kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ Yesu aga nikpe buya tuli mɛ aafla nɛ kimuenewi nɛa bha.
Bubhɛ buu yi yɛ badɔkpasɛ klɛ ba kpa nikpe nu dzyini tã.
Gɛ Farisianɛ na mɔ ana, klɛ be tsre Yesu asɛ, “Di!
Wɔ badɔkpasɛ naa bhɛtɛ kɛgɛ ba tɛ bhɛtɛ nɛ Kimuenewi nɛa bha.” Yesu ebui lɛ bunu asɛ, “Nɔ kɔ kla onu di kɛgɛ Daviti abhɛtɛ gɛɛ bubhɛ yi yɛ anɛ yeshopoa lɛ?
Etsoku Kpaya buvu nɛ mɛ, klɛ yɛ anɛ yeshopoa lɛ nɛ ada tã gbɛgbɛvu yuyula, gɛ kinu ɔshã dɛda kɔa lɛ sɛ tɛ ba bhɛtɛ ana, alasɛ gbɛgbɛvu kɛ lɛ kɔ kpayanɔ nɛ tite tɛtɛtã.
Pɛnɔɔ nɔ kɔ kla mɔ nɛ Ɔshã nɛ mɛ sɛ nɛ Kimuenewi nɛa bha, kpayanɔ anɛ busɔlɛevu nɛ mɛ tsyɛ ba da ɔshã ɔlɛ nɛ flogo tsyɛ pɛɛ kɛpɔnyɛpɔ dɛ za balɛ shu dza?
Itsre nɔ sɛ, agɛ agbɛgbla dɛ kpayavu nɛ alɛ ɔkɛ̃.
Otɔsɛ no nu ebuia nɛ kesi, ‘Ɛlɛ kɔ eshutukubui, ganɛ kɛdɔ kukɔ,’ anlo nɔ gɛ tɔ bu bagɛ kɛpɔ ma balɛ shu nɛ kɛpɔ flogo.
Alasɛ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ yɛ enu Apalete kɔ Kimuenewi.” Gɛ alɔ nɛ ɔkɛlɛ, ashɛ̃ avɛ ede tsoku balɛ oxogokɔvu nɛ mɛ, klɛ anyɛ ɔhwɛ tsitsi toli ɔza ɔklɛ.
Gɛ baa pɛɛ kibui nɔɔ nɛ gɛ ba ba yɛkɔ ebhui Yesu nu nɔ so, be bisi yɛ asɛ, “Kɛ lɛ ɔshã mɛ sɛ tɛ be beke bunya nɛ Kimuenewi nɛa bha dza?” Yesu ebui lɛ bunu asɛ, “Onu gɛ wɔnɔ ɔmɛayɛ teli obhoshi ɔwɔlɛku ozi mɛ nɛ Kimuenewi nɛa bha etee ti bu ɔlɛ dza?
Klɛɛ ŋa anɔ adɛ ŋa kedzi adɛ obhoshi!
So kɛlɛ ɔshã sɛ tɛ ba bhɛtɛ kibui dzyɔgo nɛ Kimuenewi nɛa bha.” Ɔkɛlɛ aɖɔ etsre anyɛ nɛ asɛ, “Bu wɔ ɔhwɛ nɛ ɔmɛna.” So anyɛ nɛ ebu ɔhwɛ nɛ amɛna klɛ ɔhwɛ nɛ otsodzi oku ɔlɛɛ ku, mɔmɔ ansɛ gɛ ɔbhla nɛ ɔlɛ.
Pɔ Farisianɛ nɛ be koeyi avɛ klɛ ba da nya kana gɛ ba ba ga pɛɛ be be yi Yesu.
Kpaya Axwɛwa Nɛ Gɛ Ebu Ansɛ gɛ kɛ lɛ tɛtiti mɛ kɔ yɛ, Yesu etsoekoeyi nɛ ɔklɛ.
Banɔ gelee ba za yɛe de, klɛ ebeke balɛ banya, klɛ akpɛ ɔshã kɔ balɛ asɛ ba tɛ ɖɔ anɔ di gɛ enu.
Kɛɛ nɛ kɛ lɛ sɛ tɛ kɛbhɛtɛ ansɛ gɛ ba ɖɔ ganɔ atɔnu Yezaya bha sɛ: “Mɛ axwɛwa nɛ gɛ ibu nɛ naa, agɛ yɛ mɛ ɛɖɔ, yɛmɛ mɛ mɔ same, ɛba yɛkɔ mɛ Ɔfufɔɛ nɛ kpɛ yɛm, klɛ ebe bu kɛdzyudzyɔ nɛ akasɛ amadi nɛ petee.
Atɛ ba pɛɛ ebla ɔdɔgɔsɛ akpɛ ogugu, anɔnyanɔ eti be nu yɛ olim nɛ edzo nɛa bha.
Tɛwa yɛyɛkɛ kɛpɔ kanyaka eti be dzyini, klɛ kanɛgbɛ keputakpa tɛtã kanyaka eti be wulu kalɛ atɛ̃, ɔdɔ nanɔ kibe lɛ gɛ agbanɔ kɛdzyudzyɔ avɛnɔ kabhaŋɛŋam.
Yɛ kinyi nɛ mɛ amadi nɛ aba yɛkɔ balɛ kidzoenu didi nɛ atrɔ.” Yesu Anɛ Ɔfufɔɛkpãekusi Ɔkɛlɛ ba gbanɔ anyɛ teli gɛ ɛfufɔɛkpã tsri yɛa bha gɛ akɔ sɛ eku omumu klɛ epu awɔ̃hũ tsyɛ amɛna yɛ, klɛ Yesu ebeke yɛ banya, pɛ akpa kaɖɔɔ ɖɔ klɛ akpa mɔ tsyɛ.
Kibui nɛ bhɛtɛ banɔ nɛ petee bi klɛ ba ɖɔ asɛ, “Anyaa nɛɛ ebe dzi Daviti Yeyi nɛa?” Pɔ gɛ Farisianɛ be nu ana, ba ɖɔ asɛ, “Ganɔ ɛfufɔɛkpã ekusieyi nɛa bha anɔa nɛ aakɛka ɛfufɔɛkpã nɛ ebu.” Yesu enyi balɛ atɔkpu nɛ mɛ so etsre alɛ asɛ, “Bukusiɔŋakɔ kanyaka gɛ bu ma kpɛ bupɛ tubha mɛ bu ba yɛɛ, klɛ ɔmagbla nɛ bupa kanyaka gɛ bu pɔɛhle nɛ aglɔ shu bu tɛ ba naa za.
Onu gɛ Satana akɛka Satana, kɛlɛ alɛ apɔɛhle nɛ yɛnahwɛshu nɛ shu.
Kɛlɛ klɛ yɛ bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ ɔbɔ za kititi?
Klɛ onu gɛ ɛkɛka ɛfufɔɛkpã ganɔ ɛfufɔɛkpãkusia bha, anea bha wɔnɔ banɔ nɛ xũ na ga kɛka ɛlɛ obu?
So ɔtsɔ̃, balɛ ebe dzi wɔnɔ bebhuikulu.
Pɔ onu gɛ mɛ ɛkɛka ɛfufɔɛkpã ganɔ Kpaya Ɔfufɔɛ nɛa bha, kɛlɛ alɛ Kpaya bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ ɔba wɔnɔa bha naa lɛlɛ.
“Ɔyɛkɔ plɛnɔ, kɛlɛ anɔ teli ebe tsoku anɔ gɛganɛ bupa mɛ ko pɛ aba yalɛ yɛ kɛnɔmɛdɔ ashɛ̃nɔ gɛ odinu sɛ ebhuso anɔ gɛganɛ nɛ nu nya lu?
Kɛlɛ flogo pɛ aba na zuru nɛ bupa nɛ mɛ.
“Anɔɔ nɛ gɛ ama plɛnɔ mɛ enu anɔ gɛ alɔ kititi nɛ mɛ shu, klɛ anɔɔ nɛ gɛ eti be xogo nɛ mɛ aba pɔɛehle.
Klɛ so itsre nɔ, buzizi kanyaka anɛ kibusobui kanyaka ba ba yɛkɔɛ kɛlɛ etsye anɔ, pɔ buzizi kanyaka nɛ Ɔfufɔɛ nɛ shu ba tɛ ba yɛkɔ etsye.
Anɔnyanɔ gɛ aba ɖɔ kaɖɔkpã nɛ Anɔdzyrame Yeyi nɛ shu ba ba yɛkɔ etsye yɛ, pɔ anɔ nɛ gɛ aba ɖɔ kaɖɔ kpã nɛ Ɔfufɔɛ Dzyɔgo nɛ shu ba tɛ ba yɛkɔ etsye, eze dzi nɛ tɛmumɔɛ nɛ mɛo kɛ gɛ tɛ ba nɛ mɛo.
“Dzu osi dzyɔgo, klɛ ɔlɛ eyuyu nɛ tsyɛ ebe dzi adzyɔgo, tɛ dzu osi kpã, klɛ ɔlɛ eyuyu nɛ tsyɛ ebe dzi akpã, alasɛ osi ɔlɛ eyuyu nɛ la ba yɛkɔ akpɛ ɔlɛ kɛxawũ nɔ.
Wɔnɔ atagblashã tɛzɛzam banɔ, kɛlɛ wɔnɔ banɔ nɛ gɛ ɔtsɔmɔ nɔ bɔ ɖɔ kibui dzyɔgo tii li?
Alasɛ kibui nɛ kɛɛ dɛ idzyi klɛ onugbu nɛ ɔɔɖɔaɖɔ.
Anɔ dzyɔgo ebu ebui dzyɔgo edenɔ yɛ ebui dzyɔgo nɛ gɛ abala nɛ yɛ mɛ, klɛ anɔkpã edenɔ yɛ ebuikpã nɛ gɛ abala nɛ yɛ mɛ.
Pɔ itsre nɔ sɛ, kɛ ba bisi sɛ banɔ ba ɖɔ balɛ tɛzɛzam akasɛ nɛ kebhuiwi nɛa bha nɛ balɛ kibui gɛ ma kibuinyɛbuim gɛ ki koeyi denɔ balɛ onugbu mɛ.
Alasɛ ganɔ wɔ ebuiɖuɖɔ nɛm le be bu wɔ butsya, klɛ ganɔ wɔ ebuiɖuɖɔ nɛm le be bu wɔ kɛpɔ.” Ebui Yiyinɔanɔ Tɛpɛpɛ Ɔkɛlɛ Farisianɛ anɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ na ɖɔ etsre yɛ asɛ, “Adɔkasɛ, bu pɛɛ sɛ tɛ bu mɔ kibui yiyinɔanɔ tili denɔ wɔ kɔ.” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Atɔkpum gɛganɛ anɛ ɔmamdɛdɛ banɔ nɛ obonobo kanɔa nɛ mɛ bee bisi asɛ tɛ ba mɔ kibui yiyinɔanɔ!
Pɔ ba tɛ ba kɔ anɔnyanɔ kɛkanyaka, Yona atɔnu na yɛ ko.
Alasɛ kana gɛ Yona aza kɛkpãgbla nɛ ɛya mɛ ewi tata nɛ itumu tɛta, kana Anɔdzyrame Yeyi nɛ tsyɛ aba za tisim ewi tata nɛ itumu tɛta.
Niniveanɛ na ba lɔɔ titi nɛ kebhuim nɛ ɔtsɔ̃ nɛ tɛmumɔɛ nɛm banɔ klɛ be be bui lɛ pɔ; alasɛ be tsyina kitem nɛ Yona kibuiɖuɖɔ nɛ mɛ, klɛ ɔtsɔ̃ agɛ adɛ Yona nɛ ya lɛ ɔkɛ̃ naa.
Ozhizhi Adzɛeni nɛ aba lɔ kititi nɛ kebhuim nɛ tɛmumɔɛ nɛm banɔ klɛ ebe bui lɛ kɛpɔ; alasɛ alɔ edenɔ kanɔ nɛ obekekɔ sɛ ta aba tatɔ nɛ Salomo kibuinyinyi, klɛ ɔtsɔ̃ agɛ yɛ adɛ Salomo nɛ yalɛ ɔkɛ̃ naa.
“Kibe lɛ gɛ ɔfufɔɛkpã ookoeyi nɛ anɔ mɛ, lɔ dɔɔ ga nyɔ busukpa kpɛkpã mɛ ɔpɛɛ omuenekɔ klɛ lɔ tɛ mɔ.
Ɔkɛlɛ lɔɔ ɖɔ sɛ, ‘Ɛba tsodzi vɛ bupa nɛ mɛ gɛ ɛtɛ shɛ.’ Kibe lɛ gɛ loo do ku, pɛ lɔɔ mɔ sɛ anɔnyanɔ ama bulɛ mɛ, ba gba bulɛ mɛ klɛ ba bhɛtɛ bulɛ mɛ elu mɔmɔ.
Ɔkɛlɛ ɔfufɔɛ nɛ ootsodzi ɔvɛ ɔdɔ gbanɔ tigene bhlatɔ gɛ tsɔmɔ dɛ ɔlɛ nahwɛ nɛ ata shu, klɛ lɛ ba tsoku da za ɔkɛlɛ.
Klɛ anɔ yɛ tɛzɛza mɛ ba tsodzi tsɔmɔ dɛa na gɛ aza putɔnɔ.
Kana kɛ ba za kɔ kɛtɔkpum gɛganɛ tɛmumɔɛ nɛm banɔ.” Yesu Yɛ Eni Anɛ Yɛadzyalɛ Nɛ kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ gɛ Yesu eke dzi aɖɔ kaɖɔ akɔ banɔɛza nɛɛ, yeni anɛ yadzyalɛ na za ɔtɔ, baa pɛ asɛ tɛ ba ɖɔ kaɖɔ nɛ yɛ.
Anɔ teli ebe tsre Yesu asɛ, “Weni anɛ wɔadzyalɛ nɛ beli ɔtɔ, baa pɛɛ asɛ tɛ ba ɖɔ kaɖɔ nɛ wɔ.” Yesu etsre anɔ nɛ asɛ, “Anee yɛ enu meni klɛ anee yenu madzyalɛ?
Ebu ɔhwɛ akpɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ ɔkɔ asɛ, “Meni anɛ madzyalɛ naa.
Alasɛ ananyanɔ gɛ abhɛtɛ Maka nɛ owũsise nɛ tɛpɛpɛɛ yɛ enu badzya, mada anɛ meni.”
Kɛkpalɛ Nɛ Adɔhwɛ Teli Shu Kiwi lɛlɛ nɛ ke Yesu ekoeyi ada za kɛvɔ nɛ butɔ.
Banɔaza lɛlɛ nɛɛ di na ba kana yɛ atsya klɛ ede tsoku keniabha opupu tolim ezhedzi, nɛ kibe lɛ gɛ banɔ nɛ petee ba kana kɛvɔ nu tɔ atsya.
Klɛ etenɔ kaɖɔ ɖɔ tsre banɔ nɛ akpalɛ mɛ asɛ, “Ayadɛ teli ekoeyi avɛ kɛdɔ ɔhwɛ kɔ.
Kibe lɛ gɛ ahwɛ kɛdɔ nɛɛ, eteli awɔlɛ adɔ kidzo nɛ shu, klɛ buzhuɔɛ ba tɔkɛ alɛ amunɔ.
Eteli awɔlɛ dɔ aklãgbum, gɛ la dɛ mɔ tisi mɔmɔ.
Le yi zia, alasɛ tisi nɛ dɛ do nɛ ɔklɛ.
Pɔ gɛ buwui nɛ ba tã, eyii nɛ gɛ eyi la tayɛ̃ alasɛ la dɛ kpɛ igu.
Eyii nɛ teli awɔlɛ adɔ ewim, gɛ ewi nɛ ebe she ada lɛ.
Kana ke eyii nɛ teli adɔ kesukpa dzyɔgoa bha, gɛ akɔ sɛ le yu, nɛ kɛfɔɛfɔmɛ, anɛ afɛtehlomɛ, anɛ afata mɛ ɔyɛkɔ dɛ agɛ ba ɖa.
Anɔ nɛ gɛ batɔ alɛ yɛ, tɛ enu.” Badɔkpasɛ na tɔnɔ yɛ aba klɛ le bisi yɛ asɛ, “Kide so pɛ ɔɖɔ kaɖɔ otsre banɔ nɛ akpalɛ mɛ?” Ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Ba tɛ yɛkɔ ebui kpukpu nɛ owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ tɛtiti akɔ nɔ, pɔ ganɛ kɔ balɛ.
Aanɔ nɛ gɛ kɛdɔ lɛ yahwɛ bazia kɔ yɛ ata, klɛ kɛdɔ ba za yɛ ahwɛ gelee.
Aanɔ nɛ gɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ ma yahwɛ, kibhliyi nɔɔ gɛ lɛ yɛ ahwɛ tsyɛ ba ba yɛkɛ kɛlɛ nɛ yahwɛ.
Kibui nɛ so pɛ ɛɖɔ kaɖɔ nɛ akpalɛ mɛ kɔa lɛ, “Bee di, pɔ ba ta mɔ, bee nu, pɔ bete nu kɛlɛe si.
Nɛ balɛ mɛ ba tɛ mɔ Yezaya atɔnu nɛ ebui nɛ mɛ asɛ: “ ‘No bo zo nu xũi, pɔ nɔ tɛ bo nu kɛlɛ esi di, no bo zo di kɛdɔ xũi, pɔ nɔ tɛ bɔ zɔɔ mɔɛ lɛ mɛ.
Alasɛ banɔa nɛ idzyi mɛ aba agɛganɛ; agɛganɛ kɔa lɛ sɛ tɛ benu nɛ balɛ batɔ, klɛ ba da balɛ awɔ̃hũ.
Otɔ sɛ anɛ kana bata za mɔ nɛ balɛ awɔ̃hũ, be nu nɛ balɛ batɔ, be nu kibuiesi nɛ balɛ idzyi, klɛ tɛ betsyina, klɛ mɛ ba beke balɛ banya.’ “Pɔ ba yula wɔnɔ awɔ̃hũ alasɛ laa mɔ, wɔnɔ batɔ alasɛ lee nu.
Kɛlɛ so nɛ itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, batɔnu gelee nɛ banɔ dzyɔgo teli ba pɛɛ sɛ tɛ ba mɔ kɛ gɛ nɔ mɔ, pɔ ba dɛ mɔ kɛlɛ, klɛ tɛ be nu kɛ gɛ no nu pɔ be di nuɛ lɛ.
“Nɔ tatɔ tɛ no nu adɔhwɛ kɛkpalɛ nɛe si, Kibe lɛ gɛ anɔ teli enu bukusiɔŋakɔ kibui pɛ edi nu klɛe si, ɔfufɔɛkpã nɛ ɔbɔ ba ɔbɔ bhɛ kɛ gɛ ba tɛ ɖa kpɛ idzyi nɛ mɛ nɛ obu.
Kɛlɛ nu eyii nɛ gɛ awɔlɛ adɔ kidzo nɛ shu.
Eyii nɛ gɛ adɔ aklãgbu nɛ mɛ alɛ nu anɔ nɛ gɛ enu kibui klɛ ayɛkɛ lɛ nɛ same.
Pɔ gɛ kibui nɛ dɛ kpɛ igu nɛ yɛ mɛ so adɛ nyɛna kibui nɛm dzroɖoɖo.
So onu gɛ bunuhu ɔdɔgɔsɛ tɛkpɛkpatɔnɔ tili nya ba nɛ kibui nɛ shu ko awɔlɛ ekoeyi.
Eyii nɛ gɛ adɔ ewi mɛ alɛ nu anɔ gɛ enu kibui, pɔ ɛkpã nɛ mɛ butɔ nɛ kɛnɔmɛdɔ anɔwuwɔɛ eshe ada yɛ so kibui nɛ dɛ yu eyuyu nɛ yɛ mɛ.
Pɔ eyii nɛ gɛ adɔ kesukpa dzyɔgo nɛa bha, alɛ nu anɔ gɛ enu kibui klɛ enu kɛlɛe si.
Klɛ kibui nɛ ba yu eyuyu gelee nɛ kɛfɔɛfɔm, nɛ ɛzakɔ afɛtehlo, afata mɛ ɔyɛkɔ dɛ eyi nɛ gɛ ba ɖa.” Kɛkpalɛ Nɛ Tɛwa Shu Yesu aza kpɛ kɛkpalɛ bhlatɔ akɔa lɛ asɛ: “Owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ ɔsɔnɔ ansɛ anɔ gɛ avɛ yɛ buya mɛ klɛ ada hwɛ kɛdɔeyi dzyɔgo.
Pɔ kibe lɛ gɛ anɔnyanɔ avɛnɔ tra, agɛ adɛ ɖɔ yɛ na vɛ ada hwɛ tɛwaeyi akpɛ amɔ nɛshi, klɛ ashɛ̃.
Gɛ amɔ nɛ eyi pɛ le she, klɛ tɛwa nɛ tsyɛ yi koeyi.
“Ayadɛ nɛ baxwɛdɛ na ba tɔnɔ yɛ asɛ, ‘Aka, anɛ eyi dzyɔgo ɔhwɛ nɛ buya nɛ mɛ dza?
Klɛ fakɔ tɛwa nɛ de?’ Ebu kɛlɛ nu asɛ, “ ‘Anɔ nɛ gɛ adɛ ɖɔ mɛ nɛ yɛ ada wa kɛxwɛ lɛlɛ.’ “Baxwɛdɛ nɛ be bisi yɛ asɛ, ‘Ɔpɛ sɛ tɛ buvɛ da kpa tɛwa nɛ bu dza?’ Ebu kɛlɛ nu asɛ, “ ‘Oo,’ alasɛ onu gɛ nɔ vɛ tɛwa nɛ ɔkpabu kɔ, kɛ ba ba kɛlɛ mɛ sɛ nɔ bɔ kpa amɔ nɛ ɔta.
Nɔ kɔ kɛlɛ nɛ tɛwa nɛ petee she ketsu ɔdɔ na nɔ alɛ ɔpɔkɔ.
Nɛ kibe lɛ mɛ ɛba tsre baxwɛwa nɛ sɛ: Putɔnɔ no xogo tɛwa tɛ nɔ nya kɛlɛ kɔ tɛ pupɔɛ, klɛ tɛ no xogo amɔ nɛ tsyɛ ɔyɛkɔ bɔ kpɛ mɛ owule nɛ mɛ.’ ” Akpalɛ Nɛ Eyixwɛtsɛ Anɛ Bunayekedɔ Shu Yesu aza kpɛ kɛkpalɛ bhlatɔ asɛ: “Owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ odzi ansɛ eyixwɛtsɛ, gɛ anɔ teli ada ɖa nɛ yɛ buya mɛ.
Kɛnya lɛ kɛlɛ mɛ sɛ alɛ enu eyibliyii adɛ nɛ wɔ eyinyeyi shi, pɔ onu gɛ ki she, kɛ ba dzi kevudeya osi gbɛgbla dɛ, gɛ kɛ ba kɔ sɛ kɛlɛm buzhuɔɛ bu ba ba dɔ ɔlɛ ɛshɛ nɛ mɛ.” Aza kpɛ kɛkpalɛ bhlatɔ kɔ balɛ asɛ, “Owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ odzi ansɛ bunayekedɔ gɛ anɔdzɛ aayɛkɔ akpɛ buna gelee mɛ kɔ tɛ yiyeke nɛ tɛ pipe.” Yesu aɖɔ ebuia nɛ petee nɛ akpalɛ mɛ etsre banɔɛza, adɛ ɖɔ kibuinyɛbui etsrea lɛ gɛ odinu sɛ ganɔ kɛkpalɛm.
So kana ebui nɛ gɛ baɖɔ aganɔ atɔnu nɛa bha nɛ aba ba kɛlɛ mɛ asɛ: “Ɛba danɛ mɛ onugbu nɛ akpalɛ, Ɛba ɖɔ ebui kpukpu nɛ gɛ ekpu denɔ kanɔ nɛ kesi kpɛkpɛ.” Tɛwa Akpalɛ Nɛ Kesibubu Ɔkɛlɛ ashɛ̃ lɔ banɔɛza nɛ avɛ bupa mɛ.
Yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ ba tɔnɔ yɛ aba klɛ la ɖɔ asɛ, “Bu buya mɛ tɛwa nɛɛ kpalɛ nɛesi kɔ lɔ.” Ebu kɛlɛ nu asɛ, “Anɔ nɛ gɛ aɖa eyi dzyɔgo nɛ yɛ enu Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi.
Buya nɛ mɛ bulɛ nu kanɔ nɛ mɛ, klɛ eyi dzyɔgo nɛ alɛ nu bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ mɛ bee yi.
Tɛwa nɛ klɛ nu ezizi nɛ yeyialɛ, klɛ anɔkpã nɛ gɛ aɖa lɛ nɛ yɛ enu ɔfufɔɛkpã.
Kɛdɔ yɛyɛkɔ kibe nɛ kɛlɛ nu kanɔ nɛ obekekɔ, klɛ badɔyɛkɔ nɛ balɛ enu Kpaya baxwɛdɛ.
“Kana gɛ ba kpa tɛwa pɛ ba pɔɛ lɛ nɛ kifu mɛ, kana kɛ ba za nɛ kanɔ nɛ obekekɔ.
Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ aba kpɛ yɛ baxwɛdɛ nɛ asɛsɛ, klɛ le be bu kizizi kanyaka nɛ yɛ bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ mɛ gɛ kɔ buzizi nɛ bagɛ ba bhɛtɛ butsutsɔmɔ.
Ba ba yɛkɔ balɛ ada tɛɛ̃ akpɛ kifu gɛganɛm, ɔkɛlɛ gɛ iyuyo nɛ eletɛtã aba za.
Klɛ badzyɔgo nɛ ba ba tã ansɛ kiwi nɛ balɛ Aka nɛ bukusiɔŋakɔ.
Anɔɔ nɛ gɛ batɔ alɛ yɛ, tɛ enu.
Akpalɛ Nɛ Kɛkesrɔdɔ Kpukpu Nɛ Kɛklãgbu Yɛŋaedzi Shu “Owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ odzi ansɛ kɛkesrɔdɔ tili gɛ bekpu nɛ ayakpam.
Gɛ anɔ teli emunɔɛ lɛ, etsodzini kɛlɛ ekpu, klɛ nɛ yɛ same mumɔ mɛ nɛ ada yɛkɔ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ gɛ lɛ yahwɛ nɛ adɛ klɛ avɛ ede dzi kesukpɛa lɛlɛ.
“Kana, owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ odzi ansɛ edziniga gɛ avɛ ada pɛɛ aklãgbu ŋɛŋaedzi dzyɔgo.
Gɛ avɛ ede munɔ kɛŋɛŋaedzi tili, ashɛ̃ avɛ ada yɛkɔ yɛ kɛdɔ kanyaka gɛ kɛlɛ yahwɛ nɛ adɛ klɛ ede dzia lɛ.
Kɛkpalɛ Nɛ Dzikle Shu Kana ke, owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ odzi ansɛ kenimdzikle gɛ ba tɛa kpɛ kɛvɔm pɛ ebu akpã edidedi.
Kibe lɛ gɛ kenimdzikle nɛ eyuku, ba gɛ be bu kenimɛdzya nɛ be he yɛ amɛna ogbigbe nɛa bha.
Klɛ be zhiaza kesi klɛ la tɔkɛ kenimɛdzya dzyɔgo nɛ akpɛ bushɔ mɛ, pɔ ba yɛkɔ atsutsɔmɔ nɛ atɛ̃.
Kana kɛba za nɛ kibe bibeke nɛ mɛ.
Kpaya baxwɛdɛ na ba ba klɛ le be bu atɔkpum gɛganɛ elete nɛ badzyɔgo nɛ shi klɛ la ba yɛkɔ balɛ atɛ̃akpɛ kifu gɛganɛ nɛ mɛ, ɔkɛlɛ gɛ iyuyo nɛ eletɛtã aba za.
Yesu ebisi balɛ asɛ, “Sɛ no nu ebuia nɛ petee mɛ?” Be bu klɛ nu asɛ, “Ee.” Aɖɔ etsre alɛ asɛ, “Kɛlɛ so ɔshãdɔkasɛ kanyaka gɛ ba kasɛ dɔ edenɔ owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ shu asɔnɔ ansɛ apalete gɛ ebu yɛ kɛkesrɔdɔ vuvɔ nɛ kɛkuku nɛ edenɔ yɛ kɛdɔ ɔbalakɔ.” Atɔnu Gɛ Ama Kinyi Gɛ Yesu akpɛ akpalɛa nɛ beke, avɛ yɛ kidzo gɛga nɛa bha denɔ ɔkɛlɛ.
Gɛ ebe ku yɛ kepiɔma nɛ mɛ, akpa kɛdɔ kasɛ banɔ nɛ balɛ oxogokɔvu nɛ mɛ, klɛ kɛbhɛtɛ balɛ bi.
Be bisi asɛ, “Fakɔ anyɛa nɛ edenɔ kibuinyinyi nɛ ebui yiyinɔ anɔ kemia nɛ di?” “Ganɛ adɔfatɛ nɛ yeyi nɛ naa?
Ganɛ yeni nɛ bee kulu asɛ Maria, klɛ anɛ yadzyalɛ balɛ nu Yakobo, Yosɛfu, Simɔnɛ anɛ Yuɖasɛ?
Sɛ yadalɛ nɛ petee balɛ bulɔ ɔbha?
Klɛ fakɔ anyɛa nɛ edenɔ ebuia nɛ petee?” Klɛ ba mɔ obulo nɛ yɛ.
Pɔ Yesu etsre alɛ asɛ, “Atɔnu nɛ yɛ kepiɔma nɛ yɛ bupa mɛ ba tɛ yɛkɛ yɛ bui.” Klɛ adɛ bhɛtɛ ebui yiyinɔanɔ gelee nɛ ɔkɛlɛ, alasɛ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa ma balɛ mɛ.
Be Bhui Yohanɛsɛ Enikpɛ Nɛ Kɛtɔkpu Nɛ kibe lɛ gɛ Heroɖesɛ kɛtɔkpum gɛganɛ elete nɛ enu Yesui dɔ, klɛ etsre yɛ bagɛ bee di yɛ ɔkɔ nɛ asɛ, “Yohanɛsɛ Enikpɛ nɛ naa, alɔ edenɔ bekpum!
Klɛ so pɛ ebui yiyinɔanɔ kemia nɛ di ka wa kɛxwɛ nɛ yɛ mɛ.” Ɔtsɔ̃ nɛɛ Heroɖesɛ eti vu Yohanɛsɛ anya kpɛ vu akpɛ Heroɖiasɛ, yadzya Filipo yɛedzini nɛ so, alasɛ Yohanɛsɛ aganɔ yɛ ɔshã kpɛ asɛ: “Ɔshã ɔdɛ kɔ kidzo sɛ tɛ ɔpɛɛ adzɛ alɛlɛ.” Heroɖesɛ atrɔ sɛ tɛ eyi Yohanɛsɛ, pɔ eesi banɔ nɛ fu, alasɛ ba mɔ Yohanɛsɛ ansɛ atɔnu.
Nɛ Heroɖesɛ kɛmɔwi nɛa bha Heroɖiasɛ yɛeyiadzɛ nɛ ebe yu kivu gɛ kɛnyɛna Heroɖesɛ idzyi, gɛ kɛkɔ sɛ akatabu asɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ gɛ adzɛnuvɔɛ nɛ ebe bisi, yɛ Heroɖesɛ aba bhɛtɛ lɛ akɔ yɛ.
Nɛ adzɛnuvɔɛ nɛ yeni nɛ tɛpɛpɛ nu, aɖɔ asɛ, “Bhui Yohanɛsɛ Enikpɛ nɛ tɔkpu ɔtrɔ kɛtɛa bha kɔ mɛ nɛ ɔkɛ̃.” Kibui nɛ trɔ ekusi nɛa bha, pɔ nɛ yɛ batabu nɛ nu nɛ yɛ befu gli nɛ amɛ so, akɔ asɛ ba bhɛtɛ ansɛ gɛ adzɛnuvɔɛ nɛ ebisi, klɛ akɔ sɛ be bhui Yohanɛsɛ tɔkpu nɛ buvu.
Ba yɛkɔ kɛtɔkpu nɛ atrɔ kɛtɛa bha amɛna, klɛ ba yɛkɔ akɔ anuvɔ, klɛ yɛ evunɔɛ lɛ avɛnɔ yɛeni.
Yohanɛsɛ badɔkpasɛ na ba yɛkɔ yɛ etsitsi nɛ ada vubɔ.
Ɔkɛlɛ ba shɛ avɛ ede tsre Yesu.
Yesu Anyunɔ Banɔ Akpã Teti Gɛ Yesu enu kɛgɛ ba kɛlɛ mɛ, ekoeyi nɛ ɔkɛlɛ aza keniabha opupu mɛ avɛ okpukpukɔ.
Gɛ be nu kibui nɛɛ, banɔɛza na ga butsrukpɔ aza yɛe de edenɔ ɛma nɛ mɛ.
Kibe lɛ gɛ Yesu ezhi aba kesukpa pɛ amɔ banɔɛza, be ku yɛ eshutukubui klɛ ebeke balɛ banya.
Gɛ owulago nɛ ɔɔna, badɔkpasɛ na ba yɛ ɔbha klɛ ba ɖɔ asɛ, “Okpukpukɔ nɔɔ, klɛ keli tsyɛ fli bele.
Kpɛ banɔɛza nɛɛ dzo, sɛ tɛ ba vɛ ɛmabhli nɛ mɛ tɛ be de dzi kɛŋɛŋa tili akɔ shu.” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Kɛ ka za sɛ ba shɛ.
Wɔnɔ nɔ pɛɛ kɛdɔ tili ɔkɔa lɛ tɛ ba ŋa.” Be bui lɛ nu asɛ, “Gbɛgbɛvu ɛgbaa titi anɛ keni mɛ adzya tabha ko ala lɛ bulɔ ahwɛ nɛ ɔkɛ̃.” Asɛ, “Nɔ yɛkɔa lɛ ɔmɛna mɛ nɛ ɔkɛ̃.” Klɛ akɔ sɛ banɔ nɛ be zhi aza kesi nɛ tɛwa nɛa bha.
Gɛ ayɛkɔ gbɛgbɛvu ɛgba titi anɛ keni mɛ adzya tabha klɛ ebu amɛ akpɛ owũsise, ehu ahwɛ klɛ edzyini gbɛgbɛvu nɛ mɛ.
Ɔkɛlɛ ayɛkɔ kpɛ ahwɛ kɔ badɔkpasɛ, klɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ tsyɛ ayɛkɔ akɔ banɔɛza.
Balɛ petee ba ŋa klɛ be xui, klɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ atɔkɛ kesukpayɛ wiliwili nɛ ashuɛ lɔfɔntabha.
Banɔ nɛ gɛ ba ŋa kɛdɔ nɛ kiwii lɛ nɛ ana ansɛ banɔnyɛ akpã teti, badzɛ nɛ bunuvɔɛ ma zɛ lɛ mɛ.
Yesu Aga Kenia Bha Nɛ kibe mazimazi mɛ Yesu akɔ sɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ be ku kenia bha opupu tɛ be putɔ akɔɛ avɛ keni nɛa pɛ bhla, tɛ yɛ akpɛ banɔɛza nɛ dzo.
Gɛ akpɛ balɛ dzo beke, yɛnahwɛ ashɛ̃ ewu avɛ butu tuli shu sɛ tɛ ede kulukpaya.
Gɛ owulago nɛ ɔna, yɛ terikpo agɔ nɛ ɔkɛlɛ, pɔ keniabha opupu nɛ ɔtɛ vɛ odzidzekɔɛ bɔɛ nɛ ogbigbe nɛ shu, buni giglebe nɛ tɛ tiɔ lɛ alasɛ kɛlɛɛ nɛ fu ɔlɛ.
Nɛ olizatɔ eɖɔ tɛlɛ̃ mɛ Yesu ekoeyi ága nɛ keni nɛa bha atɔnɔa lɛ.
Kibe lɛ gɛ yɛ badɔkɛpasɛ nɛ amɔɛ gɛ aaga keni nɛa bha, kifu kua lɛ tsutsɔmɔ tsɔmɔ.
Ba ɖɔ asɛ, “Ekpu.” klɛ ba kpɛ ogugu nɛ kifum.
Pɔ Yesu etsre balɛ zia asɛ, “Nɔ kpɛ te!
Mɛ nɔɔ mɔ.
No ti si fu.” Petro ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Apalete, onu wɔ, tsre mɛ ɔsɛ ɛba wɔ bha nɛ keni nɛa bha.” Yesu asɛ, “Gaba.” Ɔkɛlɛ Petro ezhi ekoeyi nɛ opupu nɛ mɛ, aga keni nɛa bha atɔnɔ Yesu aavɛ.
Pɔ gɛ amɔ kɛlɛɛ, kifu ku yɛ, klɛ akpa buni nɛ mɛ zhiku, akpɛ ogugu asɛ, “Apalete, bu mɛ!” Ɔkɛlɛ nɛ ko, Yesu ebu ɔhwɛ klɛ anyɛna yɛ.
Aɖɔ asɛ, “Wɔ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa bhli anɔ, kide so pɛ ɔdɛ yɛkɛ ɔŋa!” Klɛ gɛ be wueku opupu nɛ mɛ, kɛlɛɛ nɛ zukɔ lɔ.
Ɔkɛlɛ bagɛ ba kpasɛ opupu nɛ mɛ na kpɛ atɔkpuesi kɔ yɛ, aaɖɔ sɛ, “Kɛgbɛagba wɔ onu Kpaya yɛ Eyi.” Kibe lɛ gɛ ba tsɔkɛ, ba da dzrɔ nɛ Genesarɛtɛ.
Klɛ gɛ banɔ nɛ ɔklɛ nɛ ba kpɛ yɛ kɛxawũ sɛ Yesu, ba kpɛ odu asɛsɛ ɛma nɛ gɛ kana kibe lɛ nɛm petee.
Banɔ ba yɛkɔ balɛ banyɛnya nɛ petee amɛna yɛ klɛ ba kɔ yɛ tɔkpu asɛ akɔ banyɛnya nɛ be hunɔ yɛ awidzidze nɛ tɔ tite, klɛ bagɛ be hunɔ yɛ nɛ petee balɛ banya nɛ beke.
Bubhubhui Nɛ Bu Mabhui Mabhui Ɔkɛlɛ Farisianɛ anɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ nɛ de Yerusalɛm aba tɔnɔ Yesu klɛ le bisi asɛ, “Kide so pɛ wɔ badɔkpasɛ nɛ xũ na ta bhɛtɛ atrɔ beshishe anɛ kepiegu nɛa bha?
Be tee plu ahwɛ flogo pɛ baa ŋa kɛdɔ!” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Klɛ kide so pɛ nɔɔ ta Kpaya ɛshã nɛe si akpɛ wɔnɔ kepiegu nɛ so?
Alasɛ Kpaya ɖɔ asɛ, ‘Kpɛ kɛtɔkpuesi ɔkɔ wɔaka nɛ weni’ klɛ ‘Anɔnyanɔ gɛ aba ɖɔ kibui akpɛ yɛaka ɔdɔgɔsɛ yɛeni edzyenɔ sɛ be yi yɛ.’ Pɔ ɔɔɖɔ sɛ onu gɛ anɔ teli aɖɔ tsre yɛaka ɔdɔgɔsɛ yɛeni sɛ, ‘Tɛpɛplɛnɔ kanyakaɛ di gɛ ɔbɔ mɔ denɔ mɛ ɔkɔ nɛ nu kɛdɔ kukɔ gɛ ba bhɛtɛ kɔ Kpaya,’ ganɛ sɛ ayɛkɔ ‘akpɛ yɛaka nɛabha’ nɔ.
Ki nu sɛ nɔ oxule Kpaya kibui akpɛ wɔnɔ kepiegu nɛ so.
Wɔnɔ betroni!
Yezaya kɛbui dzyɔ gɛ amɔɖɔ nɛ wɔnɔ shu asɛ: “ ‘Banɔa na kpɛm nɛa bha nɛ balɛ inugbu, pɔ balɛ idzyi nɛ alɛ odzidzekɔ nɛ mɛ shu.
Baa kpɛ kɛtɔkpuesi akɔm nɛ kɛlɛɛ mɛ, balɛ kɛdɔkɛkasɛ nɛ nu ɛshã gɛ banɔa kasɛ.’ ” Yesu ekulu banɔɛza nɛ amɛna yɛ ɔbha klɛ aɖɔ asɛ, “Nɔ ta batɔ tɛ no nuibuiesi.
Kɛdɔnɔ nɛ gɛ kɛ ga onugbu mɛ tsoku anɔ mɛ ‘ki ti tutru yɛ,’ pɔ kɛ gɛ ga anɔ onugbu mɛ koeyi kɛlɛ kɔ sɛ ‘etutru.’ ” Ɔkɛlɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ aba yɛ ɔbha klɛ be bisi asɛ, “No nyi sɛ gɛ Farisianɛ nɛ enu kibui nɛ kɛ lɔɛ titi nɛ balɛ shu xãa?” Ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Osi kanyaka gɛ mɛ owũsise Aka nɛ edi dzu ba ba nyɛna ɔlɛ ehe akpa nɛ igu.
Shɛnahwɛ balɛ shu; be nu awɔ̃hũpuelete gɛ agbanɔ anɔ.
Onu gɛ awɔ̃hũpuelete agbanɔ awɔ̃hũpuelete, balɛ petee ba ba tɛ wɔlɛ eku ozi mɛ.” Petro asɛ, “Bu kɛkpalɛ nɛesi kɔ lɔ.” Yesu ebisi balɛ asɛ, “Nɔ kɔ lɛ mũguũ ana?” “Nɔ tɔɔ mɔ sɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ gɛ tsoku onugbu mɛ kɛɛ vɛ ɛyam pɛ kɛ daa koeyi nɛ ishu nɛ mɛ?
Pɔ ebui nɛ gɛ aaga onugbu mɛ ekoeyi le de idzyi nɛ mɛ, klɛ alɛ ‘tutru’ anɔ.
Alasɛ idzyi nɛ mɛ atɔkpum kpã, gɛ enu anɔyiyi, aglɔbui, azhuzhɔlɛbui, buzi, otro ebuimɔɖɔ, anɔshuzizi ede.
Ebuia nɛ ala bhɛtɛ anɔ pɛ ‘etuturu’, pɔ kɛdɔ ŋɛŋa nɛ ahwɛ maplumaplu atɛ bhɛtɛ anɔ pɛ ‘etuturu.’ ” Kananaɛtɛ Dzi Tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa Gɛ ba shɛ nɛ ɔkɛlɛ, Yesu ekoeyi avɛ Taɛre anɛ Sidɔnɛ kɛdɔ nɛ mɛ.
Kananaɛtɛ dzi teli gɛ ede kibé lɛ nɛ aba yɛ ɔkɔ, nɛ iyuyo asɛ, “Apalete, Daviti yɛ Eyi, di mɛ eshutukubui!
Mɛ eyiadzɛ aatɔ tsutsɔmɔ tsɔmɔ nɛ ɔfufɔɛkpã gɛ otsri yɛa bha nɛ mɛ.” Yesu adɛ ɖɔ kibuinyɛbui.
Kɛlɛ so yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ ba tɔnɔ yɛ avɛ klɛ be de tsre yɛ asɛ, “Kpɛ adzɛ nɛ dzo, alasɛ ganɛ obo eze bi iyuyo alɛ lɔe de.” Yesu ebui lɛ nu etsre alɛ asɛ, “Izraɛl ibhoshi nɛ gɛ lɛla nɛ tite ɔkɔ la kpɛ mɛ.” Adzɛ nɛ alɔ ebe dzu ekuisiesi nɛ yɛ otugba.
Klɛ aɖɔ asɛ, “Apalete, plɛnɔ mɛ!” Ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Kɛ ma sɛ tɛ ba yɛkɔ bunuvɔɛ nɛ kɛŋɛŋa atɛɛ elu kɔ balɛ bukudzɔgɛ.” Adzɛ nɛ asɛ, “Ee, Apalete,” “pɔ bukudzɔgɛ nɛ tsyɛ tɔkɛ kiwiliwili nɛ gɛ wɔlɛ denɔ bulɛ apalete alɛ nɛ ɔkplɔ̃ nɛa bha nɛ xũ aŋa.” Ɔkɛlɛ Yesu bui lɛ nu asɛ, “Adzɛ, wɔ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa gbla lɛ wɔahwɛ!
Ba yɛkɛ wɔ tɛbibisi.” Klɛ adzɛ nɛ yɛyiadzɛ nɛ bunya nɛ gbla beke nɛ ɔɖɔ lɛlɛ nɛ mɛ.
Yesu Anyunɔ Banɔ Akpã Talɛ Yesu ashɛ̃ nɛ ɔkɛlɛ avɛ Galelia Aƒu nɛ shu.
Ɔkɛlɛ ewu avɛ butu tuli shu klɛ ede dzi kesi si.
Banɔɛza gbla tɔnɔ yɛ aba, banɔ gɛ bata ga, awɔ̃hũpu, akpata, imumu anɛ banɔ gelee bhlatɔ, klɛ ba yɛkɔ ebe lu yɛ butsrukpɔ nu; klɛ ebeke balɛ banya.
Kɛ bhɛtɛ banɔ nɛ bi sɛ, ba mɔ imumu gɛ kpa kaɖɔ ɖɔ, ba bhɛtɛ akpatanɛ la dzyɔ, bagɛ ba taa ga na kpaa ga klɛ awɔ̃hũpu nɛ akpaa mɔ.
Klɛ ba kpɛ Izraɛl Kpaya nɛa bha.
Yesu ekulu yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ amɛna klɛ etsre alɛ asɛ, “Eshutukubui didi alɛ mɛ mɛ nɛ banɔa; ba tɛ za mɛ ɔbha ewi tata klɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ ma gɛ ba ba ŋa.
Ɛdɛ pɛɛ sɛ tɛ ɛkpɛ balɛ dzo nɛ bubhɛ, odi bhi ba ba tɛ tsra nɛ dzo mɛ.” Yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Fakɔ lɔ ba denɔ gbɛgbɛvu kɔ banɔ kplumua nɛ okpukpu kɔɔ nɛ?” Yesu ebisi asɛ, “ɛgbaa tɛshɛ ɛlɛ lɛ wɔnɔ ahwɛ?” Ba sɛ, “Tigene, anɛ kenimɛdzya bhli.” Etsre banɔɛza nɛ asɛ baza kesi.
Ɔkɛlɛ ayɛkɔ ɛgbaa tigene anɛ kenimɛdzya bhli, klɛ gɛ ehu ahwɛ, aya ɛlɛmɛ klɛ ayɛkɔ akpɛ ahwɛ kɔ badɔkpasɛ, klɛ balɛ tsyɛ ayɛkɔ akpɛ ahwɛ kɔ banɔ.
Balɛ petee ba ŋa klɛ be xui.
Kɛlɛe de badɔkpasɛ nɛ ba tɔkɛ ewiliwili nɛ gɛ awɔlɛ ashuɔɛ tegene.
Banɔ nɛ gɛ ba ŋa kɛdɔ na lɛ akpã talɛ, badzɛ nɛ bunuvɔ ba mɛɛlɛ mɛ.
Gɛ Yesu akpɛ banɔɛza nɛ dzo beke, ede tsoku keniabha opupu nɛ mɛ klɛ ashɛ̃ avɛ Magadanɛ be.
Kɛdɔmumɔ Pɛpɛɛ Denɔ Yesu Ɔkɔ Farisianɛ anɛ Sarusianɛ na tɔnɔ Yesu aba klɛ le be feke yɛ edi ganɔ tibibisim sɛ abhɛtɛ kɛdɔmumɔ tili gɛ kide owũsise tɛ be di.
Ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Kibe lɛ gɛ owulago ɔɔna, nɔ sɛ, ‘Kanɔ nɛ mɛ ka ba pɛ̃, alasɛ owũsise nɛ ɔdzã,’ klɛ nɛ kɛvulɔ mɛ, ‘Obo kɛlɛ ba fu, alasɛ owũsise nɛ ɔdzã klɛ lɔ da gblo.’ No nyi kana gɛ nɔ bɔ kla owũsise nɛ obu ɔlɛe si, pɔ nɔ tɛ ɔna kibe nɛ mɛ kɛdɔmumɔ nɛe si bu.
Atɔkpum gɛganɛ anɛ aglɔbui bhɛbhɛtɛ kanɔa nɛ mɛ banɔ naa pɛɛ ebui yiyinɔanɔɛ dɔmumɔ, pɔ ba tɛ ba kɔ akanyaka odu nu sɛ Yona kɛdɔmumɔ.” Ɔkɛlɛ Yesu ashɛ̃ nɛ balɛ ɔbha klɛ ada fla shɛ.
Farisianɛ Anɛ Sarusianɛ Nɛ Bunayekedɔ Kibe lɛ gɛ ba tsɔkɛ kɛvɔ, badɔkpasɛ nɛ ba dzɛkɛ ba dɛ yɛkɔ kɛŋɛŋa kanyaka.
Yesu etsre balɛ asɛ, “No dii mɔ.” “No lu awɔ̃ nɛ Farisianɛ anɛ Zaɖusianɛ anɛ bunayekedɔ nɛ shu.” Ba nyɛna kibui nɛ edi nɛ aglɔm asɛ, “Alasɛ bɔ dɛ mɛna kɛŋɛŋa kanyaka so.” Gɛ enyi kibui nɔɔ nɛ gɛ baa nyɛna so, Yesu ebisi asɛ, “Wɔnɔ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa bhli banɔ, kide pɛɛ kɛŋɛŋa maza maza wɔnɔ ahwɛ bui nɔɔ ɖɔ?
Kɛlɛ so no too nu kibue si di?
Nɔ tɔɔ baka egba titi kɔ banɔ akpã teti, anɛ ashuɔɛ tashɛ̃ nɔɔ nɛ gɛ nɔ yalɛ?
Ɔdɔgɔsɛ egba tigene kɔ banɔ akpã talɛ, anɛ ashuɔɛ tashɛ̃ nɔɔ nɛ gɛ nɔ yalɛ?
Kɛlɛ ki dzi so pɛ no too nu kɛlɛe si sɛ ganɛ kɛŋɛŋa shui bui mɛ ɛɖɔ tsre wɔnɔ?
Pɔ nɔ za nɛ awɔ̃ nɛ Farisianɛ anɛ Zaɖusianɛ anɛ bunayekedɔ nɛ shu.” Ɔkɛlɛ be nu kɛlɛe si sɛ ganɛ bunayekedɔ nɛ gɛ ba kpɛ gbɛgbɛvu buna nɛ mɛ bui aaɖɔ, pɔ Farisianɛ anɛ Sarusianɛ kɛdɔkɛkasɛ nɛ shu ya alɔ kititi.
Petro Adanɛ Kristo Shu Kibe lɛ gɛ Yesu ebe ku Sizeria Filipi bee, ebisi yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ, “Anee banɔa ɖɔ sɛ yɛ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ enu?” Be bu klɛ nu asɛ, “Banɔ teli asɛ Yohanɛsɛ Enikpɛ, be teli asɛ Eliya, klɛ babhlatɔ tsyɛ asɛ, Yeremia nɛ obhi batɔnu nɛ ɔmayɛ teli.” Yesu ebisi balɛ asɛ, “Pɔ wɔnɔ xɔ̃?” “Anee nɔ sɛ yɛ mɛ inu?” Simɔnɛ Petro ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Wɔ nu Kristo, ɛkpã Kpaya nɛ yɛ Eyi.” Yesu ebu lɛ nu asɛ, “Ba yula wɔ, Simɔnɛ Yona yɛeyi, alasɛ ganɛ anɔdzyrame yɛ bu kibui nɛ akasɛ wɔ, pɔ mɛ Aka nɛ owũsise yɛ bui lɛ akasɛ wɔ.
Klɛ mɛ itsre wɔ sɛ wonu Petro, klɛ nɛ kɛklãgbui nɛa bha mɛ ba bhɔ mɛ busɔlɛɔha nɛ ɛtrɔ, klɛ butsi tsyɛ tɛ ba ŋa ɔlɛa bha.
Ɛba yɛkɔ owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ buvuaɖɛ nɛ kɔ wɔ, kɛdɔnyɛdɔ gɛ nɔ nya nɛ kesukpa nɛa bha ba ba nya kɛlɛ nɛ owũsise, klɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ gɛ no bule nɛ kesukpa be be bule kɛlɛ nɛ owũsise.” Ɔkɛlɛ akpɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ ɔshã sɛ ba tɛ ɖɔ tsre anɔnyanɔ sɛ yɛ enu Kristo.
Yesu Aɖɔ Yɛ Titsitsi Nɛ Elu Denɔ kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ Yesu etenɔ ebuie si bu kɔ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ alasɛ tɛ avɛ Yerusalɛm tɛ ada tɔ nɛ ebui gelee mɛ nɛ beshishe nɛ ahwɛ mɛ, kpayaɔzakɔanɔ anɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ, klɛ kɛ ba za sɛ tɛ be yi yɛ klɛ nɛ kiwi tramɛ ebe tsodzi anyɛmɛ aba ɛkpãm.
Petro agbanɛ yɛ eyinɔɛ de klɛ ada kpa yɛ.
Ɔkɛlɛ Petro aɖɔ asɛ, “Ao, Apalete!” “Kibui nɛ tɛ ba ba wɔa bha!” Yesu etsyina klɛ etsre Petro asɛ, “Fla nɛ mɔ bha, Satana!
Onu kɛklãgbu gɛ ɔkpatanɛ mɛ; Kpaya ebui nɛ ama wɔ kɛtɔkpu mɛ, banɔdzyrame ayɛ ala lɛ.” Ɔkɛlɛ Yesu etsre yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ, “Onu gɛ anɔ teli asɛ aba za mɛe de, alasɛ tɛ ashɛ̃nahwɛ yɛshu nɛ shu tɛ ayɛkɔ yɛ butsiosi (atitsoga) tɛ aza mɛe de.
Alasɛ aanɔ gɛ apɛa sɛ tɛ ebu yɛ ɛkpã aba lɛla ɛlɛ, pɔ aanɔ gɛ aba lɛla yɛ ɛkpã nɛ akpɛ mɛ so aba mɔɛ lɛ.
Kibui dzyɔgo ɖueɖu kɛ ba dzi kɔ anɔ sɛ tɛ kanɔ nɛ petee kedzi yɛa yɛ, tɛ yɛ ɔfufɔɛ nɛ ɔdɔ lɛla?
Ɔdɔgɔsɛ kidee anɔ aba naa yɛkɔ atsrakɛ yɛ kɛtɔwi nɛ nɔ?
Alasɛ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ aba ba nɛ Yaka ishu bhubhui mɛ nɛ yɛ baxwɛdɛ, klɛ aba buya kɛbhɛ kɔ anɔnyanɔ nɛ kana gɛ awa kɛxwɛ nɛ nu.
Itsre nɔ kɛgba, banɔ teli gɛ be lii titi nɛ ɔkɛ̃ be ti be mini butsi flogo pɛ ba ba mɔ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ aaba nɛ yɛ bukusi mɛ.”
Yesu Ishutsyitsyina Nɛ ewi tehloe de Yesu agbanɔ Petro, Yakobo anɛ Yohanɛsɛ Yakobo yadzya, klɛ avɛnɔ balɛ nɛ butu ɖɛɖama tulia bha nɛ balɛ nahwɛ ishua hwɛ.
Ɔkɛlɛ Yesu etsyina shu nɛ balɛ amɛ.
Yamɛ nɛ mɛ atã nasɛ kiwi, klɛ yɛ bawi nɛ be fuli ansɛ kifu.
Ɔkɛlɛ nɛ ko Mose anɛ Eliya ba wɛ̃ nɛ balɛ amɛ pɛ bedza ɖɔaɖɔ nɛ Yesu.
Petro etsre Yesu sɛ, “Apalete, kɛpɛ kɔlɔ sɛ bulɛ ɔkɛ̃.
Onu gɛ ɔbɔ pɛɛ lɛ ana, ɛba dzu bugba tɔta, tierikpo kɔ wɔ, tierikpo kɔ Mose anɛ tierikpo kɔ Eliya.” Nɛ kibe lɛ gɛ Petro ekedza ɖɔ kaɖɔ, ɔmunɔ fufu toli ɔbɔ kana balɛ ɔtsya, klɛ olim toli oyi denɔ ɔlɛ mɛ sɛ, “Meyi naa, gɛ ɛdɛmɛ yɛ bui; yɛmɛ mɛ mɔ amɛ zhizhiesi.
Nɔta yɛa tɔ!” Kibe lɛ gɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ nu ana, ba wɔlɛ adɔ klɛ le kumu amɛesi, nɛ kifu sisi.
Pɔ Yesu aba klɛ ebe hunɔ alɛ.
Kɛlɛa sɛ, “Nɔ lɔ,” “No to si kifu.” Kibe lɛ gɛ bebu amɛ ewunɔ ba da mɔ anɔnyanɔ ɔyɛkɔdɛ Yesu.
Gɛ be zhi butu nɛ aaba, Yesu akpɛ alɛ ɔshã sɛ, “Nɔ tɛ ɖɔ tɛ anɔnyanɔ enu kɛdɔnɔ gɛ nɔ dɔ mɔ, ɔdɔ nanɔ kibe lɛ gɛ be feke Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ edenɔ bekpum.” Badɔkpasɛ nɛ bisi yɛ asɛ, “Kɛlɛ kide so pɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ nɛ baa ɖɔ asɛ, kɛlɛ sɛ tɛ Eliya eputɔ aba?” Yesu ebu kɛlɛ nu asɛ, “Tɛ nɔ yɛkɛ ɔŋa, Eliya aba ba klɛ ebe tsodzini kɛdɔnyɛdɔ elu klɛ ɔzakɔ.
Pɔ itsre nɔ, Eliya atɛ ba kukuuku, klɛ ba dɛ kpɛ yɛ xaŋũ, pɔ ba bhɛtɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ gɛ ba pɛɛ nɛ yɛ.
Kana Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ tsyɛ abaa tɔ nɛ balɛ tɛhwɛm.” Ɔkɛlɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ enu kɛlɛesi asɛ Yohanɛsɛ Enikpɛ nɛ aaɖɔ.
Ɔfufɔɛkpã Eyi Teli Bunya Tibibeke Kibe lɛ gɛ ba ba tɔnɔ banɔɛza, anyɛ teli aba tɔnɔ Yesu klɛ edzu ekuisie si kɔ yɛ.
Klɛ aɖɔ asɛ, “Apalete, di mɛeyi nɛ eshutukubui.” “Aawɔlɛ ebho klɛ aatɔ tsutsɔmɔ tsɔmɔ.
Ebe gelee adɔ ku kifu mɛ nɛ buni mɛ.
Ɛyɛkɔ yɛ ɛmɛna wɔ badɔkpasɛ, pɔ ba dɛ na yɛ bunya nu beke.” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Ao banɔ gɛ ba dɛ pɛ̃ klɛ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa ma nɔ ahwɛ,” “kɛlɛ za mɛ ɛba za wɔnɔ bha ɔdɔnanɔ?
Kɛlɛ za mɛ ɛba za plɛnɔ wɔnɔ ɔdɔnanɔ?
Yɛkɔ anuvɔ nɛ ɔmɛna mɛ nɛ ɔkɛ̃.” Yesu anyɛna nɛ ɔfufɔɛkpã nɛa bha, klɛ lɔ fla okoeyi nɛ anuvɔ nɛ mɛ, klɛ yɛ bunya nɛ beke nɛ ɔɖɔ lɛlɛ nɛ mɛ.
Ɔkɛlɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ ba tɔnɔ Yesu nɛ tikpukpum klɛ be bisi yɛ asɛ, “Kide so pɛɛ bulɔ xũ nɛ dɛ na ɔlɛ kɛka bu?” Yesu asɛ, “Alasɛ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa bhli ko kɛlɛ lɛ wɔnɔ ahwɛ.
Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, onu gɛ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa bhli ansɛ ɔyurɔpɔɛyi kɛɛ lɛ wɔnɔ ahwɛ, nɔ bɔ na butu nɛ tsre sɛ, ‘Shɛ nɛ ɔkɛ̃ tɛ ɔvɛ ɔkɛ̃,’ klɛ bu ba vɛ.
Kɛdɔnyɛdɔ ma gɛ nɔ tɛ bɔ naa bhɛtɛ.” Pɔ ɔfufɔɛ ɔnɛ nɛɛ di ɔtɛ boo koeyi odinu ganɔ kpayakuklu nɛ onugbunyɛnya mɛ.
Kibe lɛ gɛ be be xogo nɛ Galelia, etsre alɛ asɛ, “Ba ba ga Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛe si akpɛ banɔ ahwɛ.
Be be yi yɛ, klɛ nɛ kiwi tramɛ nɛa bha ebe tsodzi alɔ aba ɛkpãm.” Klɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ be yuku nɛ same mamɔmamɔ.
Busɔlɛvu Mɛ Kɛdɔkukɔ Gɛ Yesu nɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ ede ku Kapenaumɛ beke, badɔdzyɔ nɛ gɛ ba yɛkɛ kadzyɔ na ba tɔnɔ Petro klɛ be bisi yɛ asɛ, “Wɔnɔ adɔkasɛ nɛ xũ ataa kɔ busɔlɛvu mɛ kadzyɔ?” Ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Ee, aakɔ,” Kibe lɛ gɛ Petro ebe tsoku bupa nɛ mɛ, Yesu yɛ eputɔ aɖɔa ɖɔ.
Ebisi asɛ, “Simɔnɛ wɔ kɛtɔkpum sɛ kɛlɛɛ?” “Ba ne ahwɛ kesukpa bha bekusi nɛ ba yɛkɛ kadzyɔ nɛ ɖutɛɛ—balɛ naɛhwɛ beyi pɛnɔɔ banɔ bhlatɔ ahwɛ?” Petro ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Denɔ banɔ bhlatɔ ahwɛ.” Yesu etsre yɛa sɛ, “Kɛlɛ alɛ be bu balɛ beyi nɛ xũ nɛ kɛlɛ mɛ.” “Pɔ sɛ tɛ bu tɛ da nɛ balɛa bha, vɛ kɛvɔ nɛ mɛ tɛ ɔdɔ kpɛ wɔ ɖaɖuwɛ.
Yɛkɔ kɛkpã tutɔpu nɛ gɛ obo bu, yaka kɛlɛ onugbu nɛ mɛ klɛ ɔbɔ mɔ kɔba tɛalɛ̃ kihoeyi tili.
Yɛkɔɛ lɛ tɛ ɔdɔ kɔ kadzyɔ nɛ mɛ nɛ wɔnɔ nu.”
Agbɛgbladɛ Nɛ Owũsise Bukusi Nɛm Nɛ kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ Badɔkpasɛ nɛ ba tɔnɔ Yesu aba klɛ be bisia sɛ, “Anee ya dɛ nɛ owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ mɛ?” Ekulu anuvɔ bhli teli klɛ akɔ yɛ alɔ kititi nɛ balɛ shi.
Klɛ aɖɔ asɛ: Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, odɛ nu sɛ no tsyina klɛ nodzi ansɛ banuvɔ bhli, nɔ tɛ bɔ na owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ mɛ tsoku odi.
Kɛlɛ so, anɔnyanɔ gɛ anyɛna shu ansɛ anuvɔ bhlia nɛɛ yɛ enu agbɛgbladɛ nɛ owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ mɛ.
“Klɛ anɔnyanɔ gɛ aba yɛkɛ anuvɔ bhlia nɛ akpɛ etem nɛ mɛ kinyi mɛ, ayɛkɛ mɛ.
Pɔ onu gɛ anɔ teli aba kɔ sɛ beyi bhlia nɛ di gɛ ba yɛkɛ mɛa bha ŋa nɛ be de ku buzizi mɛ, aba pɛ kɔ yɛ adɛ onu gɛ ba yɛkɔ buhɔ gbla tsa kpɛ yɛ oli pɛ ba yɛkɔ ada tɛ̃ akpɛ aƒu odzudzukɔ.
“Butɔ kɔ kanɔ alasɛ ebui nɛ gɛ alɛ ka lɛ mɛ gɛ etii banɔ akpɛ buzizi mɛ nɛ so!
Ebui alɛlɛ nɛ di alasɛ tɛ la ba, pɔ butɔ kɔ anɔɔ nɛa bha gɛ la ba ga aba!
Onu gɛ wɔ ɔhwɛ ɔdɔgɔsɛ wɔ ɔtsrɛ ɔbɔ kɔ sɛ odo ku buzizi mɛ, bhui ɔlɛ ɔtɛ̃.
Aba pɛ kɔ wɔ sɛ tɛ otsoku ɛkpãm nɛ ɔtsrɛ bhubhui anɛ ɔhwɛ bhuibhui ɔkɔ dɛ sɛ ba yɛkɔ wɔ ada tɛ̃ akpɛ kifu manimani mɛ nɛ ɛhwɛ tɛbha anɛ ɛtsrɛ tɛbha.
Klɛ onu gɛ wɔ kɛwɔ̃hũ tili kɔ sɛ tɛ odo ku buzizi mɛ, kpa kɛlɛ ɔtɛ̃.
Aba pɛ̃ kɔ wɔ adɛ sɛ tɛ otsoku ɛkpãm nɛ kɛwɔhũ tirikpo, ɔyɛkɔ dɛ sɛ tɛ ba yɛkɔ wɔ ada tɛ̃ akpɛ kifu manimani mɛ nɛ awɔ̃hũ tabha.
Kɛkpalɛ Nɛ Obhoshi Lɛlɛla Shu “Di kɛlɛ ɔkɔ sɛ no ti di bunuvɔɛ bhlia nɛ ɔmɛayɛ kanyaka bhliyii.
Alasɛ itsre nɔ sɛ balɛ baxwɛdɛ nɛ owũsise naa mɔ mɛ Aka nɛ owũsise nɛ amɛ kibenyɛbe.
Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ aba sɛ tɛ ebe bu kɛdɔ nɛ gɛ kɛ lɛla.
“Wɔ kɛtɔkpu nɛ mɛ sɛ kɛ lɛɛ?
Onu ibhoshi kɛfɔɛfɔ lɛ anyɛ teli ahwɛ, klɛ toli ɔlɛla, ataa shɛnahwɛ afɛtezhita nɛ tiezhita nɛ shu elu avɛ ada pɛɛ ɔgɛ ɔlɛla?
Klɛ onu gɛ aamɔ ɔlɛ, kɔ mɛ tsre nɔ kɛgba, aba mɔ same nɛ ɔlɛ shu ɔyɛkɔ dɛ afɛtezhita nɛ tiezhita nɛ gɛ ɛdɛ lɛla.
Kana wɔnɔ Aka nɛ owũsise tsyɛ atɛ ba pɛɛ asɛ tɛ banuvɔ bhlia nɛ kanyaka alɛla.
Adzya Nɛ Gɛ Abhɛtɛ Buzizi Amɛna Wɔkɔ “Onu gɛ wadzya abhɛtɛ buzizi amɛna wɔkɔ, vɛ tɛ odo bu buzizi nɛ ɔkasɛ yɛ, nɛ wɔnɔ nɛ yɛ tɛa bha shi ko.
Onu gɛ enu kɛlɛesi akɔ wɔ, klɛ wɔnɔ nɛ yɛ no bo tsodzi ɔza terikpo.
Pɔ onu gɛ eti be nu wɔesi, yɛkɔ anɔ terikpo tɛabha ɔta shu, sɛ tɛ ‘kibuinyɛbui mɛ ba danɛ ganɔ bebuimɔɖɔ tɛabha tɛata amɛ.’ Onu gɛ adɛ ta balɛ tsyɛ batɔ, yɛkɔ kibui nɛ ɔkɔ busɔlɛɔha, klɛ onu gɛ adɛ ta ɔha nɛ tsyɛ atɔ, klɛ tɛ ɔyɛkɔ yɛ ansɛ anɔ gɛ adɛ sɔlɛ klɛ enu ansɛ adɔdzyɔ gɛ edzyini anɔa kpɛ.
“Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, kɛkanyaka gɛ nɔ nya nɛ kesukpa nɛa bha kɛ ba za tɛnyɛnyam nɛ owũsise, klɛ kɛgɛ no bule nɛ kesukpa nɛa bha, be be bule kɛlɛ nɛ owũsise.
“Ɛkaa ɖɔ sɛ, onu wɔnɔ tɛabha teli nɛ kesukpa nɛa bha nɔ dɛmɛ ɔtrɔ kɛdɔnyɛdɔa bha pɛ no bisi, mɛ Aka nɛ owũsise aba bhɛtɛ kɛlɛ akɔ nɔ.
Alasɛ ɔkɛlɛ gɛ banɔ tɛabha tɛata be xogo nɛ mɛ kinyi mɛ, ɛlɛ balɛɛ shi.” Kɛkpalɛ Nɛ Axwɛdɛ Gɛ Etee Di Eshutukubui Shu Ɔkɛlɛ Petro atɔnɔ Yesu aba klɛ ebisi yɛ asɛ, “Apalete, etsye tashɛ̃ mɛ ɛba yɛkɔ itsye madzya gɛ abhɛtɛ kibui kpã amɛna mɛ ɔkɔ?
Ɔdɔ nanɔ etsye tegene dza?” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Itsre wɔ, ganɛ etsye tegene, etsye afɛtegene edi tegene.
“Kɛlɛ so, owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ lo dzi ansɛ ekusi gɛ apɛa sɛ tɛ aga yɛ kɔba ebuim nɛ yɛ baxwɛdɛ.
Gɛ akpɛ ebuim gɛga nɛesi, ba gbanɔ anyɛ teli gɛ adɔ yɛ bhɛ gblagbla amɛna yɛ.
Gɛ anyɛ nɛ adɛ mɔ kɔba nɛ abuya so, apalete nɛ akɔ sɛ ba yɛkɔ anyɛ anɛ yɛedzini anɛ yɛeyialɛ anɛ yɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ gɛ lɛ yahwɛ nɛ adɛ, tɛ ba yɛkɔ abuya kɛbhɛ nɛ nɔ.
“Axwɛdɛ nɛ ezhi adɔ ekuisia bha kɔ apalete.
Akɔ kɛtɔkpu asɛ, ‘Dɔfɔɔ̃ kɔ mɛ,’ ‘tɛ ɛba buya kɛbhɛ nɛ petee kɔ wɔ.’ Apalete nɛ di axwɛdɛ nɛ eshutukubui, klɛ ayɛkɔ kɛbhɛ nɛ etsye yɛ, klɛ akɔ asɛ aga vɛ.
“Pɔ gɛ axwɛdɛ alɛlɛ nɛ ekoeyi avɛ, ada tsyanɔ yɛabhla teli gɛ yɛ tsyɛ adɔ kɛbhɛ bhli tili nɛ yɛ shu.
Anyɛna yɛ klɛ atasɔlɛ yɛ kɛhali.
Klɛ asɛ, ‘Buya kɛbhɛ nɛ gɛ ɔdɔ nɛ mɛ shu nɛ ɔkɔm!’ “Yɛ ɔhaɛ axwɛdɛ nɛ ezhidɔ ekuisia bha klɛ akɔ yɛ kɛtɔkpu asɛ, ‘Dɔfɔɔ̃ nɛ mɛ, klɛ ɛba buya kɛbhɛ nɛ kɔ wɔ.’ “Pɔ adɛ dɛmɛ.
Aga kɛlɛ shu ayɛkɔ anyɛ nɛ ada kpɛ buvu ɔdɔnanɔ kibe lɛ gɛ abuya kɛbhɛ.
Kibe lɛ gɛ baxwɛdɛ gɔgɔɛ nɛ ba mɔ kana gɛ kibui nɛ vɛ, kɛtrɔ balɛa bha klɛ ba tɔnɔ balɛ apalete nɛ avɛ klɛ ba da ɖɔ kibuinyɛbui gɛ vɛ kabha nɛ etsre yɛ.
“Ɔkɛlɛ apalete nɛ ekulu axwɛdɛ nɛ amɛna, klɛ etsre ya sɛ, ‘Wɔ kɛtɔkpum gɛganɛ axwɛdɛ,’ ‘Mɛ ɛtsa odi kpɛ wɔ kɛbhɛnyɛbhɛ mɛ alasɛ ɔkɔ kɛtɔkpu so.
So kɛma sɛ odi wɔhaɛ axwɛdɛ nɛ eshutukubui ansɛ gɛ idi wɔ?’ Nɛ obulo mɛ, apalete nɛ etsodzini yɛ evu akɔ bevupo sɛ ba vɔɛ ɔdɔnanɔ kibe lɛ gɛ aba buya kɛbhɛ nɛ petee gɛ adɔ nɛ yɛ shu.
“Kana mɛ owũsise Aka nɛ aba bhɛtɛ nɛ wɔnɔ mɛayɛ kanyaka gɛ atɛ ba yɛkɔ kibui etsye yɛadzya edenɔ yɛ idzyi mɛ.”
Yesu Akasɛdɔ Nɛ Aglɔshu Shɛshɛ̃nahwɛ Kibe lɛ gɛ Yesu aɖɔ ebuia nɛ beke, ashɛ̃ nɛ Galelia klɛ avɛ Yuɖia kɛdɔ nɛm nɛ Yɔɖanɛ kapɛ bhla.
Banɔɛza gbla ba tɔnɔ yɛ, klɛ ebeke balɛ banya nɛ ɔklɛ.
Farisianɛ teli aba sɛ tɛ be be feke yɛ edi.
Be bisi yɛ asɛ, “Kɛ lɛ ɔshã sɛ tɛ anyɛ ashɛ̃nahwɛ yɛedzini shu nɛ kibui tili anɛ kibuinyɛbui shu dza?” Yesu ebu kɛlɛ nu asɛ, “Nɔ kɔ kla di sɛ nɛ kesikpɛkpɛ Adɔbhɛtɛ ‘abhɛtɛ balɛ anyɛ nɛ adzɛ,’ klɛ asɛ, ‘Kana so, anyɛ aba shɛ alɔ yɛaka anɛ yɛeni ada bhɛtɛ terikpo nɛ yɛedzini, klɛ batɛa bha nɛ be dzi ishuidzya tirikpo.’ So be tie dzi tɛabha, bedzi terikpo.
So nɛɛ, kedɔnɔ gɛ Kpaya anyɛna atsa, tɛ kɔ anɔ ebule kɛlɛ.” Be bisi asɛ, “Kɛlɛ kide so pɛɛ Mose akɔ kidzo sɛ anyɛ abhɛtɛ keplukpa tɛ ayɛkɔ ashɛ̃nahwɛ yedzini shu tɛ akpɛ yɛ dzo?” Yesu ebu kɛlɛ nu asɛ, “Mose akɔ nɔ kidzo sɛ nɔ shɛnahwɛ adzɛ shu alasɛ wɔnɔ idzyi nɛ mɛ agɛganɛ.
Pɔ ganɛ kana kɛ za denɔ kesikpɛkpɛ.
Itsre nɔ sɛ, anɔnyanɔ gɛ ashɛ̃nahwɛ yɛedzini shu, pɛ odinu sɛ adɛ ɔma mɛ so, klɛ aza da gbanɔ adzɛ bhlatɔ asɔnɔ sɛ ɔdɛ ɔma mɛ.” Badɔkpasɛ nɛ tsre yɛ asɛ, “Onu kana kɛɛ lɛ kɔ anyɛ anɛ adzɛ, klɛ apɛ adɛ sɛ tɛ aglɔgbɛgbanɔ atɛ za.” Yesu ebu kɛlɛ nu asɛ, “Ganɛ anɔnyanɔ ko ya ba yɛkɛ kibui nɛ, pɔ ba gɛ balɛ ba kɔɛ lɛ nɛ ko.
Alasɛ banɔ teli ba ma anyɛmɛ ba mɔa lɛ ana; be teli banɔ ba la bhɛtɛ alɛ ana; klɛ be teli ba dɛ pɛɛ adzɛ tɛgbɛgbanɔ akpɛ owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ so.
Aanɔ nɛ gɛ aba yɛkɛ kibui nɛɛ tɛ ayɛkɛ lɛ.” Banuvɔ Bhli Anɛ Yesu Ɔkɛlɛ la gbanɔ bunuvɔɛ bhli tuli amɛna Yesu sɛ tɛ atrɔ ahwɛ nɛ balɛa bha tɛ eklukpaya nɛ balɛ tɔkpu.
Pɔ badɔkpasɛ na dɛ kɔ bagɛ ba gbanɔ alɛ mɛna nɛ amɛ.
Yesu asɛ, “Nɔ kɔ bunuvɔɛ bhli na ba mɔkɔ, nɔ tɛ kɔ sɛ ba tɛ ba, alasɛ owũsise bukusi nɛ nu baa lɛ nɛɛ di nu yɛ.” Kibe lɛ gɛ atrɔ ahwɛ nɛ balɛa bha beke, avɛ yɛ kidzo nɛa bha denɔ ɔklɛ.
Anyɛsɔ Ehueielete Teli Ɔtsɔ̃ nɛɛ anyɛ teli aba tɔnɔ Yesu klɛ ebisi asɛ, “Adɔkasɛ, kibui dzyɔgo ɖueɖu kɛlɛ lɛ sɛ ɛbhɛtɛ tɛ ɛmɔ ɛkpã gɛ ɛtɛba beke di?” Yesu ebisi yɛ asɛ, “Kide so pɛ obisi mɛ kibui nɔɔ nɛ gɛ ki nu kɛdzyɔgo?” “Kpaya terikpo ko yɛ enu adzyɔgo.
Onu gɛ ɔpɛ sɛ tɛ ɔmɔ ɛkpã, klɛ bhɛtɛ ɔtrɔ ɛshã nɛa bha.” Anyɛ nɛ ebisi asɛ, “Ɛshã iɖueɖu?” Yesu ebuɛ lɛ nu asɛ, “ ‘Ti yi anɔ, tɛdɛ ɔmam, tɛ zuru, tɛ hu otro ɔmɔɛ bui ɔɖɔ, ta waka nɛ weni atɔ,’ tɛ ‘ɔdɛmɛ wɔhaɛ bui ansɛ gɛ ɔdɛmɛ wɔshui bui.’ ” Anyɛnuvɔɛ nɛ asɛ “ebuia nɛ petee ɛbhɛtɛ alɛa bha.” “Kiɖueɖu kɛlɛ gɔ?” Yesu asɛ, “Onu gɛ ɔpɛɛ sɛ tɛ ɔna, vɛ dɔ dɛ wɔ kɛnɔmɛdɔ nɛ gɛ lɛ wɔ ahwɛ tɛ ɔyɛkɔ ehoeyi nɛ ɔkɔ betsyutsyuini, klɛ kɛnɔmɛdɔ ba za wɔahwɛ nɛ owũsise.
Tɛ otsodzi ɔba tɛ ɔbɔ za mɛe de.” Kibe lɛ gɛ anyɛnuvɔɛ nɛ enu ebuia nɛ, amɔ obulo klɛ ashɛ̃, alasɛ ehoeyi gelee alɛ yahwɛ.
Ɔkɛlɛ Yesu etsre yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ, “Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, aba gɛganɛ kɔ ehoeyielete sɛ tɛ etsoku owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ mɛ, Ɛkaa tsre nɔ sɛ, kɛ lɛ bubɔɛbɔɛ kɔ kipuaga sɛ tɛ aga kɛtsa ozim ɔyɛkɔ dɛ sɛ tɛ ehoeyielete etsoku Kpaya bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ mɛ.” Kibe lɛ gɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ be nu ebuia nɛɛ, la bhɛtɛ balɛ bi tsutsɔmɔtsɔmɔ klɛ be bisi yɛ asɛ, “Kɛlɛ anee ya ba mɔ tɛbubu?” Yesu edi alɛ klɛ asɛ, “Nɛ anɔdzyrame kapɛ mɛ, kɛ tɛ ba za bubɔɛbɔɛ, pɔ nɛ Kpaya kɔ, kibuinyɛbui lɛ bubɔɛbɔɛ.” Petro etsre yɛ asɛ, “Bu tɛ shɛnahwɛ bulɔ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ shu sɛ tɛ bu za wɔe de!
Kide gɛ zɛ ba za kɔ lɔ?” Yesu etsrea la sɛ, “Itsre nɔ kɛgba nɛ sɛ, nɛ kibe lɛ gɛ bebe tsodzini kɛdɔnyɛdɔ abhɛtɛ kɛ vuvɔ, gɛ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ ebe zhi aza yɛ bukusiegbu gɛ kalɛ shu adanɛ nɛa bha, Wɔnɔa gɛ ɔlɛ mɛe de tsyɛ obo za bukusigbu lɔfɔnɛtubha nɛa bha, ozo klu bubhui nɛ Izraɛl amadi lɔfɔntabha.
Klɛ anɔnyanɔ gɛ atɛ shɛ alɔ bapa, yɛadzyalɛ, yɛadalɛ, yɛaka, yɛeni, yɛeyialɛ, yɛ kaya akpɛ mɛ so, aba yɛkɛ kɛdɔɛ lɛ nɛ ɛzakɔ kɛfɔɛfɔ klɛ aba mɔ ɛkpã gɛ ɛtɛ ba beke.
Pɔ banɔ tutɔpu gelee be be dzi gɔgɔɛ, klɛ be gelee gɛ bagbɛde ne be dzi batutɔpu.
Kɛkpalɛ Nɛ Baxwɛwa Nɛ Vãyɛ̃ Buya Shu Yesu avɛ kɛlɛa bha sɛ, “Alasɛ owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ ɔlɛ ansɛ kesukpaelete teli gɛ alɔ kɛvulɔ pinii avɛ sɛ tɛ ada pɛɛ banɔ tɛ ba da wa kɛxwɛ kɔ yɛ nɛ buya mɛ.
Adɛmɛ asɛ aba bua kiwi zɛzɛ kɛbhɛ gɛ nu dinario akɔa lɛ, klɛ asɛsɛ balɛ nɛ buya nɛ mɛ.
“Nɛ kɛvulɔ ɛɖɔ tizhita mɛ ana, ekoeyi ada mɔ banɔ nɛ teli gɛ be li titi nɛ kedzi mɛ gɛ ba taa bhɛtɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ.
Klɛ etsre balɛ asɛ, ‘Wɔnɔ tsyɛ nɔ vɛ tɛ nɔ dɔ wa kɛxwɛ nɛ mɛ buya nɛ mɛ, tɛ ɛba buya kɛbhɛ nɔɔ nɛ gɛ dzyenɔ nɛ ɛkɔ nɔ.’ Kɛlɛ so ba vɛ.
“Anyɛ nɛ eze koeyi nasɛ kemuze ɛɖɔ lɔfɔntɛbha nɛ ɛɖɔ tɛta mɛ ana klɛ aza da bhɛtɛ ana.
Anasɛ owulago ɛɖɔ titi mɛ ana eze koeyi avɛ ada mɔ banɔ teli gɛ be ke li akana.
Ebisi balɛ asɛ, ‘Kide no li ɔkɛ̃ nɛ ɔbhɛtɛ kiwi nɛ mɛ petee kɛxwɛnyɛxwɛ mawamawa?’ Be bui lɛ nu asɛ, “ ‘Alasɛ anɔnyanɔ adɛ ba yɛkɔ lɔ.’ “Ɔkɛlɛ etsre alɛ asɛ, ‘Wɔnɔ tsyɛ nɔ vɛ tɛ nɔ dɔ wa kɛxwɛ nɛ mɛ vãyɛ̃ buya nɛ mɛ.’ “Gɛ owulago nɛ ɔna, ayalete nɛ etsre yɛ baxwɛwa otugbanɔ nɛ asɛ, ‘Kulu baxwɛwa tɛ ɔbuya balɛ abhɛ nɛ ɔkɔ alɛ, tɛ ɔkpɛe si denɔ banɔ gugɔɛ nɛ gɛ ɔyɛkɔ nɛa bha ɔdɔ nanɔ ba tutɔpu.’ “Baxwɛwa nɛ gɛ ba yɛkɔ nɛ ɛɖɔ titi mɛ na ba klɛ akanyaka ayɛkɛ dinario terikpo.
So ba gɛ be bhuso yɛkɔ nee di kidzoenu sɛ balɛ kɛbhɛ nɛ ba vɛ otugba dɛ.
Pɔ balɛ tsyɛ dinario terikpo ko la kɔa lɛ.
Gɛ ba yɛkɛ kɛbhɛ nɛ beke, bakpa kaɖɔ ɖɔ nɛ ayaelete nɛ shu.
Baa ɖɔ asɛ, ‘banɔ nɛ gɛ ba yɛkɔ gɔgɔɛ ɔɖɔ torikpo ko la yɛkɔ awa kɛxwɛ,’ ‘klɛ ɔbhɛtɛ balɛ la sɔnɔ lɔ gɛ wa kɛxwɛ nɛ ɔgbɛgbla kɔ nɛ buwui nɛa bha kiwi zɛzɛ petee.’ “Pɔ ebui lɛ nu etsre terikpo asɛ, ‘Ɔbhɛa, nɛ sɛ ɛtɛɛ bhɛtɛ wɔ mɔmɔ.
Anɛ kiwi zɛzɛ bhɛ gɛ nu dinario terikpo ɔdɛmɛ sɛ ɔbɔ wa kɛxwɛ nɛ ɔkɔ?
Yɛkɛ wɔ kɛbhɛ tɛ ɔshɛ.
Ɛpɛɛ sɛ tɛ ɛbua kɛbhɛ kɔ anɔ gɔgɔɛ nɛ gɛ ɛyɛkɔ ansɛ gɛ ɛkɔ wɔnɔ.
Kidzo ma mahwɛ sɛ tɛ ɛbhɛtɛ kɛdɔnɔ nɛ gɛ ɛpɛɛ nɛ mɛnahwɛ ehoeyi nɛ dza?
Ɔɔkpɛ mɛ awɔ̃ alasɛ mɛ ɛyamɛ yɔ so dza?
“So agugɔɛ nɛ ebe dzi atutɔpu, klɛ atutɔpu nɛ ebe dzi agugɔɛ.” Yesu Aza Ɖɔ Kaɖɔ Nɛ Yɛ Butsi Nɛ Shu Elu Gɛ Yesu ashɛ̃ aavɛ Yerusalɛm, agbanɔ badɔkpasɛ lɔfɔntɛabha nɛ eyinɔɛ de klɛ etsre balɛ asɛ, “Bu shɛɛ vɛ Yerusalɛm, klɛ ba ba ga Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛesi akɔ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ anɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ.
Be be bu yɛ butsipɔ, klɛ ba ba yɛkɔ yɛ akpɛ bagɛ be di nu Yuɖanɛ nahwɛ gɛ la ba kpɛ butsɔ klɛ be be tu yɛ klɛ la ba kplayɛasɔ butsiosi shu.
Nɛ kiwi tramɛ nɛa bha be be tsodzini yɛ anyɛmɛ amɛna ɛkpã mɛ!” Eni Kɛdɔpɛpɛɛ Ɔkɛlɛ Zebeɖi yeyianyɛalɛ anɛ balɛeni nɛ aba Yesu ɔbha anɛ yɛ beyianyɛ klɛ, gɛ edzu ekuisiesi, ebisi eshutukubui didi denɔ yɛ ɔkɔ.
Ebisi asɛ, “Kide ɔsɛ ɔpɛɛ?” Klɛ adzɛ nɛ asɛ, “Trɔ ahwɛ kɛlɛa bha sɛ tɛ meyianyɛ tɛabha nɛ ɔmayɛ teli aza wɔ kɛŋa mɛ tɛ abhla nɛ aza wɔ kɛbɛtɛkpɛ mɛ nɛ wɔ bukusiɔŋakɔ.” Yesu etsre yɛ asɛ, “Oti nyi kɛdɔnɔ nɛ gɛ oobisi.” “Ɔbɔ na buniatse nɛ gɛ ɛba wɛ̃ nɛ ɔwɛ̃ xãa?” Be bu kɛlɛ nu asɛ, “Buba na.” Yesu etsre alɛ asɛ, “Nɔ bɔ na kantse nu wɛ̃ kɛgba, pɔ mɛ kɛŋa mɛ anɛ kɛbɛtɛkpɛ mɛ zɛza ganɛ mɛ ba kɔ kɛlɛ.
Ɛzakɔɛ lɛ nɛ lɛ kɔ bagɛ mɛ Aka abala elu kɔ ɔklɛ.” Kibe lɛ gɛ banɔ lɔfɔ nɛ nu kibui nɛɛ, ba mɔ obulo nɛ badzya tɛabha.
Yesu eklua lɛ exogo klɛ asɛ, “No nyi sɛ ba gɛ be di nu Yuɖanɛ ba ŋa balɛ ɔkɔayɛ nɛa bha, klɛ balɛ banɔgbla na wa kabhaŋɛŋa shuixwɛ nɛ balɛa bha.
Kɛ ma kɔ wɔnɔ kana.
Nɛ klɛ shu, aanɔ nɛ gɛ apɛɛ sɛ tɛ edzi agbɛgbla nɛ wɔnɔɛ shi ala sɛ tɛ edzi wɔnɔ axwɛdɛ, klɛ aanɔ nɛ gɛ apɛa sɛ tɛ edzi atutɔpu, alasɛ tɛ edzi wɔnɔ axwɛdɛ, anasɛ gɛ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ adɛ ba sɛ tɛ ba dɛ axwɛ akɔ yɛ, pɔ aba sɛ tɛ aba dɛ axwɛ, tɛ ayɛkɔ yɛ ɛkpã nɛ abuya anasɛ kɛbhɛ nɛ banɔɛ tɔkpu.” Bawɔ̃hũpu Tɛabha Ba Mɔ Anhũ Dɛdanɛ Gɛ Yesu nɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ baa shɛ nɛ Yeriko, banɔɛza piim za yɛe de.
