Bawɔ̃hũpu tɛabha teli ba za kidzo nu tɔ, klɛ gɛ be nu asɛ Yesu aafla, ba kpɛ ogugu asɛ, “Apalete, Daviti yɛ Eyi, di lɔ eshutukubui!” Banɔɛza na kpɛ ogugu nɛ balɛa bha sɛ badɔ sɛɛ̃, pɔ ba za kpɛ ogugu nɛ gɛganɛɛ adɛa na, “Apalete, Daviti yɛ Eyi, di lɔ eshutukubui!” Yesu adzrɔ klɛ ekulua lɛ.
Ebisi alɛ asɛ, “Kide nɔ sɛ ɛbhɛtɛ kɔ nɔ?” Be bui lɛ nu asɛ, “Apalete, bu pɛɛ sɛ mɔ.” Yesu edi alɛ eshutukubui klɛ ehunɔa lɛ awɔ̃hũ.
Klɛ ba gbla kpaa mɔ klɛ la lɔ alɛ yɛe de.
Yesu Etsoku Yerusalɛm Nɛ Same Mumɔ Gɛ bee tsobunɔ Yerusalɛm pɛ be be ku Betfage nɛ Olivɛ Butu nɛa bha, Yesu akpɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ tɛabha, etsre alɛ asɛ, “Nɔ vɛ ɔmabhli nɛ gɛ ɔlɛ wɔnɔ otugba, nɔ bɔ mɔ kitukuaga teli gɛ akpasɛ ohuim, gɛ yeyi eli yɛ ɔbha.
No bule balɛ tɛ nɔ gbanɔa lɛ ɔmɛna mɛ.
Onu gɛ anɔ teli aɖɔɛ bui tili no tsre yɛ ɔsɛ Apalete nɛ ya pɛa lɛ, ko ba ba shɛnahwɛ balɛ shu asɛsɛ.” Kibui nɛ kɛba klɛm sɛ tɛ ba yɛkɔ amɔ ebui nɛ gɛ ba ɖɔ ganɔ batɔnu nɛa bha sɛ: “Tsre Zayɔnɛ Adzɛnuvɔɛ nɔ sɛ, ‘Di, wɔ ekusi na ba wɔbha, adɔfɔɔ̃ klɛ etsri kitukuaga nɛa bha, nɛ agaeyi nɛa bha, gɛ enu kitukuagaeyi.’ ” Badɔkpasɛ na vɛ ada bhɛtɛ ansɛ gɛ Yesu ashrɔa lɛ.
Ba mɛna kitukuaga nɛ yeyi, ba yɛkɔ balɛ apɔtɛ nɛ ada kɔa lɛ, klɛ Yesu aza alɛa bha.
Banɔɛza gelee bule balɛ apɔtɛ elu kidzo nɛm, klɛ be teli edzyini isishɛ elu kidzo nɛa bha.
Banɔɛza nɛ gɛ putɔ kɔ yɛ nɛ bagɛ ba za yɛe de na kpɛ igugu asɛ, “Hosiana kɔ Daviti yɛ Eyi!” “Ba yula anɔ nɛ gɛ aaba nɛ Apalete nɛ kinyim!” “Hosiana nɛ ɔɖɛɖamakɔ dɛ!” Gɛ Yesu etsoku Yerusalɛm, ɔmagbla nɛ petee oshuku klɛ le bisi asɛ, “Ane naa?” Banɔɛza nɛ asɛ, “Yesu naa, atɔnu gɛ ede Nazarɛtɛ nɛ Galelia.” Yesu Nɛ Busɔlɛvu Nɛm Yesu etsoku busɔlɛvu nɛ kɛma nɛ mɛ klɛ akɛka bagɛ bee dzi kɛdɔ pɛ baa dɛ kɛdɔ nɛ ɔkɛlɛ.
Akaka bagɛ baa tsrakɛ ehoeyi anɛ bagɛ baa dɛ bagɔgɔwi nɛ bakplɔ̃ nɛ petee.
Etsre balɛ asɛ, “Ba ŋlɔmɛ elu sɛ, ” “ ‘Mɛ bupa be be kulu lɛ asɛ kpayakuklu bupa,’ pɔ nɔ yɛkɔ bulɛ ɔɔbhɛtɛ ‘bezi ɔzakɔ.’ ” Awɔ̃hũpu anɛ akpata atɔnɔ yɛ aba busɔlɛvu nɛ mɛ klɛ ebeke balɛ banya.
Pɔ gɛ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ anɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ na mɔ ebui nɛ di gɛ Yesu abhɛtɛ nɛ bunuvɔɛ nɛ igugu nɛ gɛ baa kpɛ nɛ busɔlɛvu nɛ ɔbha be nɛ asɛ, “Hosiana kɔ Daviti yɛ Eyi, ” kɛ kua lɛ obulo.
Bee bisi yɛ asɛ “No nu ebui nɛ gɛ bunuvɔɛa nɛ baa ɖɔ?” Yesu ebui lɛ nu sɛ, “Ee,” nɔ kɔ kla, “ ‘Denɔ beyi anɛ bunuvɔɛ bhli nɛ inugbu mɛ nɔ tɛ trɔahwɛ kabhakpɛkpɛ nɛa bha.’ ” Klɛ ashɛ̃ alɔ balɛ klɛ ekoeyi nɛ ɔmagbla nɛm avɛ Betani, ɔkɛlɛ gɛ ada za.
Kabhɔ Tsitsi Nɛ kɛvulɔ nɛ pinii, gɛ etsri yɛ kidzoa bha etsodzi avɛ ɔmagbla nɛ mɛ, bubhɛ yi yɛ.
Gɛ amɔ kabhɔosi nɛ kidzo nɛ tɔ, ebunɔ ɔlɛ pɔ adɛ mɔ eyuyu kanyaka nɛ ɔlɛm ɔkɔ dɛ awulakpa kpɛkpa.
Ɔkɛlɛ etsre osi nɛ asɛ, “Wɔ otio yu eyuyu nɛ kanɔ mɛ kiwinyɛwi!” Nɛ ɔkɛlɛ osi nɛ ɔgblɔ wɔlɛawa.
Gɛ badɔkpasɛ na mɔa na kɛ bhɛtɛ alɛ bi.
Be bisi asɛ, “Kɛlɛ lɛ za pɛɛ kabhɔosi nɛ ogblo tsi ki tsi tili ana?” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, onu gɛ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa lɛ wɔahwɛ, ganɛ kɛ gɛ ba bhɛtɛ osi nɛ ko ɔbɔ na bhɛtɛ, ɔbɔ na butu nɛ otsre sɛ, ‘Vɛ, yɛkɔ wɔ shu ɔdɔ tɛ̃ kpɛ aƒu mɛ,’ klɛ kɛ ba bhɛtɛ.
Onu gɛ ɔyɛkɛŋa, ɔbɔ yɛkɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ gɛ obisi ganɔ kpayakuklu mɛ.” Ebuibibisi Nɛ Yesu Kabhaŋɛŋa Nɛ Shu Yesu etsoku busɔlɛvu nɛ kibee, klɛ, gɛ aza kasɛ dɔ, kpayaɔzakɔanɔ anɛ beshishe kɔ banɔ nɛ ba tɔnɔ yɛ aba.
Be bisi asɛ, “Kabhaŋɛŋa ɖueɖu mɛ ɔɔbhɛtɛ ebuia nɛ petee?” “Klɛ anee gɛ akɔ wɔ kabhaŋɛŋɛa nɛɛ di?” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Mɛ tsyɛ ba bisi nɔ kibui tirikpo.
Onu gɛ noo bui lɛ nu ɔkɔ mɛ, ɛba tsre nɔ kabhaŋɛŋa nɔɔ nɛ mɛ gɛ ɛbhɛtɛ ebuia nɛɛ.
Yohanɛsɛ bunikpɛkpɛ— fakɔ lu de?
Owũsise lu de pɛnɔɔ banɔ kɔ?” Ba kpa kibui nu nyɛnadi nɛ aglɔm klɛ la ɖɔ asɛ, “Onu buɖɔ sɛ, ‘Bu de owũsise,’ ebe bisi lɔ asɛ, ‘Klɛ kide so pɛ bu dɛ yɛkɛ yɛa bha ŋa dza?’ Pɔ onu buɖɔ sɛ, ‘Bu de banɔ kɔ,’ klɛ buu si banɔ nɛ kifu, alsɛ balɛ petee ba yɛkɛ kɛlɛ asɛ Yohanɛsɛ nɛɛ edzi atɔnu.” So, be bui lɛ etsre Yesu asɛ, “Bu ti nyi.” Klɛ Yesu asɛ, “Klɛ mɛ tsyɛ tɛ ba tsre nɔ kabhaŋɛŋa nɔɔ nɛ shu gɛ ɛga pɛ ɛbhɛtɛ ebuia nɛ.” Kɛkpalɛ Nɛ Beyianyɛ Tɛabha Shu “Wɔnɔ kɛtɔkpu nɛ mɛ sɛ kɛlɛ?
Anyɛ teli aza gɛ beyianyɛ tɛabha za yɛahwɛ.
Atɔnɔ atutɔpu nɛ avɛ asɛ, ‘Eyi, vɛ tɛ ɔdɔ wa kɛxwɛ nɛ vãyɛ̃ buya nɛ mɛ obo.’ Eyi nɛ asɛ, ‘Ɛtɛɛ vɛ,’ pɔ kɛlɛe de mɛ ebe tsyina yɛ kɛtɔkpum klɛ avɛ.
“Ɔkɛlɛ aka nɛ atɔnɔ eyi bhla nɛ avɛ klɛ ede tsre yɛ tsyɛ kibui lɛ.
Yɛ tsyɛ asɛ, ‘Ɛba vɛ, aka,’ pɔ adɛ vɛ.
“Nɛ beyi tɛabha nɛ shi, eɖueɖu ya bhɛtɛ aka nɛ tɛ pɛpɛɛ?” Be bui lɛ nu asɛ, “Eyi tutɔpu.” Yesu etsre alɛ asɛ, “Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, badɔdzyɔ anɛ badzɛ zhuzhɔlɛ nee tsoku kpyakusiɔŋakɔ nɛ mɛ aalɔ nɔ.
Alasɛ Yohanɛsɛ aba kasɛ nɔ tɛnɛnamɛzɛza, klɛ nɔ dɛ yɛkɛ yɛa bha ŋa, pɔ badɔdzyɔ anɛ badzɛ zhuzhɔlɛ nɛ xũ ba yɛkɛ aŋa.
Klɛ nɛ klɛe de gɛ nɔɔ mɔ kɛɛ nɛɛ tsyɛ, no di tsyina kitem pɛ ɔyɛkɛ yɛa bha ŋa.
Kɛkpalɛ Nɛ Badɔwa Shu “Nɔ tatɔ nɛ kɛkpalɛ bhlatɔɛ nɛ tsyɛ: Kesukpaelete teli aza gɛ adɛ vãyɛ̃ buya.
Abhɔ kidri akana buya, ebu wãyɛ̃ kizi nɛ bɔlɛ mɛ klɛ edzu opokɔvu nɛ buya nɛ mɛ.
Klɛ ayɛkɔ buya nɛ akpɛ ahwɛ kɔ bayadɛ teli klɛ aga ɛdzo.
Gɛ kɛdɔ nɛ bu be nɛɛ na, akpɛ yɛ baxwɛdɛ nɛ asɛsɛ bagɛ bee di buya nɛa bha na sɛ ba yɛkɛ yɛ ɔŋakɔ nɛ amɛna yɛ.
Bagɛ bee di buya nɛa bha nɛ vu baxwɛdɛ, be tu terikpo, be yi abhla, klɛ be hu atramɛ nɛ aklãgbu.
Klɛ anyɛ nɛ aza kpɛ baxwɛdɛ bhlatɔ asɛsɛ balɛ, gɛ balɛ tɛkɛklam vɛ otugba dɛ batutɔpu, klɛ bagɛ alɛ buya nɛa bha na za bhɛtɛ balɛ tsyɛ ana.
Gugɔɛ gugɔɛ nɛɛ, anyɛ na ba kpɛ yɛeyianyɛ nɛ asɛsɛ alɛ.
Anyɛ na sɛ, ‘Be be di mɛ eyianyɛ nɛ xũ ɔkɔ.’ Pɔ gɛ bamɔ yɛ eyianyɛ, klɛ la ɖɔ nɛ aglɔm asɛ, ‘Agɛ abaa za aka nɛ ɔzakɔ nɛ naa.
Nɔ ba, kɔ lɔ yiyɛ tɛ buyɛkɛ yɛ ɔŋakɔ.’ Kɛlɛ so bevu anyɛ nɛ yɛ eyianyɛ na tɛɛ̃ ebu nɛ buya nɛ mɛ klɛ le de yi yɛ.
So onu gɛ ayalete nɛ aba ba, kidee aba bhɛtɛ nɛ bagɛ tsri buya nɛa bha?” Be bui lɛ nu sɛ, “Aba yɛkɔ batsutsɔmɔa lɛlɛ nɛ akpɛ ɔtsutsɔmɔkɔ, klɛ aba yɛkɔ buya na kpɛ ahwɛ kɔ bayadɛ bhlatɔ, gɛ ba ba ma kɛdɔ nɛ pɛ ba ba yɛkɔ yɛ ɔŋakɔ nɛ akɔ yɛ onu gɛ be bui dɔ.” Yesu etsre banɔ nɛ asɛ, “Nɔ kɔ kla mɔ nɛ Kpayɛbuieplukpa nɛ mɛ odi sɛ: “ ‘Kɛklãgbu nɛ gɛ bevubhɔ nɛ be gbe, kɛba dzi buvu nɛ ɔxãkɔɛklãgbu; Apalete nɛ ya bhɛtɛ kɛɛ nɛɛ, klɛ kɛbhɛtɛ bulɔɛ bi.’ Kɛlɛ so itsre nɔ sɛ ba ba nyɛna Kpaya bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ ayɛkɛ nɛ wɔnɔ ahwɛ ayɛkɔ ada kɔ banɔ nɛ gɛ be yu ɔkɛlɛ eyuyu.
Anɔ nɛ gɛ aba wɔlɛ adɔ kɛklãgbui nɛa bha ebe dzyini eku bupɛ pɛɛpɛ mɛ, pɔ anɔ nɛ gɛ yɛa bha kɛɛ ba wɔlɛ dɔ aba yɛɛ.” Gɛ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ anɛ Farisianɛ nɛ be nu Yesu akpalɛa nɛ, be ti sɛ balɛ aaɖɔ.
Ba pɛɛ kidzo nɔɔ nɛa bha gɛ ba ba ga pɛ be be vui pɛ be be yi yɛ, pɔ be si banɔɛza nɛ fu alasɛ banɔ nɛ ba yɛkɔ yɛ ansɛ atɔnu.
Kɛkpalɛ Nɛ Adzɛ Ɔgbanɔkɔ Shu Yesu aza ɖɔ kaɖɔ nɛ kɛkpalɛ mɛ etsre balɛ asɛ, “Owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ odzi ansɛ gɛ ekusi abala adzɛ ɔgbanɔkɔ akɔ yɛ eyianyɛ.
Akpɛ yɛ baxwɛdɛ nɛ bagɛ ekulu akɔ adzɛgbɛgbanɔɛ wi nɛe si asɛ ba ga ba, pɔ ba dɛ dɛmɛ aba.
“Ɔkɛlɛ aza kpɛ baxwɛdɛ gelee adɛa na klɛ asɛ, ‘Tsre bagɛ ikulu nɛ sɛ ɛtɛ bala mɛ kɛŋɛŋa, Ɛtɛ yi mɛ nɛtsyɔɛnye gɛ elu bubɔ, klɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ lɛ kɛlɛ ɔzakɔ.
Nɔ ga ba adzɛ ɔgbanɔ kɔ.’ “Pɔ ba dɛ yɛkɔ nɛ kɛlɛ mɛ klɛ ba shɛ, teli ashɛ̃ avɛ yɛ ayakpam, klɛ teli tsyɛ ashɛ̃ avɛ yɛ axwɛ mɛ.
Bagɔgɔɛ nɛ be vu yɛ baxwɛdɛ, ba dɛ bhɛtɛ alɛ mɔmɔ klɛ be yi alɛ.
Ekusi nɛ amɔ obulo.
Klɛ akpɛ yɛ keyutugbani ovulo klɛ le be yi bebudzyi alɛlɛ klɛ la pɔɛ balɛ ɔmagbla.
“Ɔkɛlɛ etsre yɛ baxwɛdɛ nɛ asɛ, ‘Batɛ bala adzɛ ɔgbanɔkɔ nɛ beke, pɔ bagɛ ikulu nɛ adɛ na kɔ ɔkɛlɛ tɛbɛba.
Nɔ vɛ kidzo nɛa bha tɛ nɔ gbanɔ anɔnyanɔ gɛ nɔɔ mɔ nɛ ɔmɛna adzɛ ɔgbanɔkɔ.’ Kɛlɛ so baxwɛdɛ ba vɛ klɛ ba da gbanɔ anɔnyanɔ gɛ ba mɔ, ba dzyɔgo anɛ be zizi, klɛ adzɛ nɛ ɔgbanɔkɔ obo yuku nɛ befu.
“Pɔ gɛ Ekusi nɛ ebe ku ɔkɛlɛ sɛ tɛ amɔ befu, evu awɔ̃hũ nɛ anɔ teli asɛ yɛ adɛ kpɛ adzɛ ɔgbanɔkɔ awi.
Ebisi asɛ, ‘Ɔbhɛa,’ ‘kɛlɛ ɔbhɛtɛ pɛ otsoku ɔkɛ̃ gɛ ɔdɛ kpɛ adzɛ ɔgbanɔkɔ bawi?’ Anɔ nɛ adɛ ɖɔ kaɖɔnyɛaɖɔ.
“Ɔkɛlɛ Ekusi nɛ etsre bagɛ ba dɛ axwɛ nɛ asɛ, ‘Nɔ nya yɛ ɛtsrɛ anɛ ɛhwɛ, tɛ nɔ yɛkɔ yɛ ɔtɛ̃ɛ kpɛ ɔtɔ, nɛ otumu nɛ mɛ, ɔkɛlɛ gɛ iyuyo nɛ eletɛtã aba za.’ “Alasɛ be kulu banɔ gelee, pɔ tɛashɛ̃ ko be bu nɛ balɛ mɛ.” Kadzyɔ Kɔ Kaɛza Ɔkɛlɛ Farisianɛ ne koeyi avɛ ada nya nɛ yɛ shu kana gɛ ba ba ga pɛ be be vu yɛ ganɔ yɛnahwɛ ebui ɖuɖɔ mɛ.
Ba kpɛ balɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ aplɛnɔ Heroɖesɛanɛ nɛ yɛ ɔkɔ.
Ba ɖɔa sɛ, “Adɔkasɛ, ” “bunyi sɛ onu anɔ gɛ ɔbhɛtɛ ebui nɛ alɛ ɔzakɔ klɛ ɔkasɛ dɔ nɛ Kpaya dzo nɛ kɛgba nɛ nu.
Banɔdzyrame ataa hwanɛ wɔ, alasɛ oto di balɛ ɔkɔ sɛ banee di be nu dza.
Tsre lɔ ɔtsɔ̃, kidee gɛ nu wɔɛ yɛ?
Kɛbɔ sɛ ba dzyɔ kɛdɔ kɔ Kaɛza pɛnɔɔ kɛmɛtã?” Pɔ gɛ Yesu enyi butsutsɔmɔ nɔ gɛ kpasɛ balɛ kɛtɔkpum so, etsre balɛ asɛ, “Wɔnɔ betroni, kide pɛ nɔ pɛ mɛ sɛ tɛ no bu nɛ kɛgbam?
Nɔ kasɛ mɛ ehoeyi nɛ gɛ nɔɔ dzyɔ kɛdɔ nɛ nɔ.” Ba yɛkɔ kihueyi gɛ nu denarosɛ terikpo amɛna yɛ, klɛ Yesu ebisi balɛ asɛ, “Ane tɛtɛta nɛɛ?
Klɛ anee dɔ ŋuŋlɔmɛ?” Be bui lɛ nu asɛ, “Kaɛza yɛ.” Ɔkɛlɛ etsre alɛ asɛ, “Yɛkɔ kɛgɛ nu Kaɛza yɛ nɛ ɔkɔ Kaɛza, tɛ ɔyɛkɔ kɛgɛ nu Kpaya yɛ nɛ ɔkɔ Kpaya.” Gɛ be nu kibui nɛɛ, kɛ bhɛtɛ alɛ bi.
So ba shɛnahwɛ yɛ shu klɛ ba shɛ.
Adzɛ Gbɛgbanɔ Nɛ Kɛlɔwia Bha Nɛ kiwi lɛlɛ nɛ tutuutu Sarusianɛ, gɛ baa ɖɔ sɛ tɛ nyɛnyɛmɛ denɔ butsi mɛ ma, ba ba tɔnɔ Yesu nɛ tɛbibisi.
Ba sɛ, “Adɔkasɛ, ” “Mosesɛ etsre lɔ sɛ onu gɛ anyɛ etsi pɛ kɛɛ lɛ sɛ adɛ mɔ beyi, kɛ lɛ sɛ tɛ yɛadzya nɔɔ gɛ alɛ nɛ ayɛkɔ yɛedzini nɛ agbanɔ tɛ amɔ beyi akɔ yɛ.
Ɔtsɔ̃ nɛɛ badzya tiegene teli ba za bulɔ mɛ.
Atutɔpu nɛ agbanɔ adzɛ klɛ etsi alɔ yɛ, klɛ gɛ adɛ mɔ beyi nɛ yɛ shu so, ashɛ̃lɔ yɛedzini nɛ akɔ yɛadzya.
Kana kɛ za kɔ adzya bhla anɛ atramɛ, ɔdɔ nanɔ egigenemi nɛa bha.
Gugɔɛ nɛɛ, adzɛ nɛ ebe tsi.
Ɔtsɔ̃, nɛ tɛnyɛnyɛmɛ kiwi nɛa bha, eɖueɖu yɛedzini yɛ ebe dzi nɛ tɛegene nɛ shi, gɛ balɛ petee ba tɛ gbanɔ yɛ edi?” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Nɔɔ ga kito alasɛ no ti nyi Kpayɛbui ɔdɔgɔsɛ yɛ kemi.
Nɛ kɛlɔwi nɛa bha banɔ batɛa gbanɔ aglɔ ɔdɔgɔsɛ ba yɛkɔ anɔ akɔ sɛ bagbanɔ, ba ba za ko ansɛ baxwɛdɛ nɛ owũsise.
Pɔ nɛ betsitsi nɛ tɛlulɔ shu, nɔ kɔ kla onu kɛdɔnɔ nɛ gɛ Kpaya aɖɔ tsre nɔ asɛ, ‘Mɛ nu Abraham Kpaya, Isaka Kpaya, anɛ Yakɔpu Kpaya’?
Edi nu betsitsi nɛ Kpaya, Belulu na yɛ enu.” Gɛ banɔɛza nɛ nu kibui nɛɛ, yɛ kɛdɔkɛkasɛ nɛ bhɛtɛ balɛ bi.
Ɔshã Gbɛgbladɛ Gɛ Farisianɛ nɛ be nu asɛ Yesu ehu Sarusianɛ nɛesi, be de xogo.
Balɛ ɔmɛayɛ teli, gɛ enyi ɔshã ebe feke yɛ edi nɛ tɛbibisi nɛ asɛ: “Adɔkasɛ, Ɔshã oɖueɖu ɔlɛ onu ɔgbɛgbladɛ nɛ Ɔshã nɛm?” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ: “ ‘Ɖɔ Apalete wɔ Kpaya nɛ wɔ idzyi nɛ wɔ ɔfufɔɛ nɛ wɔ kɛtɔkpum petee.’ Ɔshã nɛ ɔlɛ onu ɔtutɔpu nɛ ɔgbɛgbladɛ petee.
Klɛ ɔbhla nɛ tsyɛ odzi ansɛ ɔlɛ: ‘Ɖɔ wɔhaɛ ansɛ gɛ ɔɖɔ wɔ shu.’ Ɛshã anɛ Batɔnu nɛ petee ba sɔmɛ ɛshã tɛbhɛ nɛ shu.” Anee Yɛ Eyi Yɛ Enu Kristo Gɛ Farisianɛ nɛ be xogo, Yesu ebisi alɛ asɛ, “Kide gɛ nu wɔnɔ kɛtɔkpu mɛ nɛ Kristo shu?
Anee yeyi enu?” “Be bui lɛ nu asɛ, “Daviti yɛ Eyi.” Yesu etsre balɛ asɛ, “Kɛlɛ kɛ za so pɛɛ Daviti, nɛ yɛ kaɖɔ ɖuɖɔ nɛ Ɔfufɔɛ nɛ shu, pɛɛ ekulu yɛ asɛ ‘Apalete’?
Alasɛ aɖɔ asɛ, “ ‘Apalete nɛ tsre mɛ Apalete nɛ asɛ: “Za mɛ kɛŋam ɔdɔnanɔ kibe lɛ gɛ ɛyɛkɔ wɔ bagɛ ba dɛ pɛɛ wɔ nɛ ɛkpɛ wɔ butrukpɔe si.” ’ Kɛlɛ onu gɛ Daviti ekulu yɛ asɛ, ‘Apalete,’ klɛ eze be dzi yɛ eyi?” Anɔnyanɔ ada na kibuinyɛbui ɖɔ ayɛkɔ ebu yɛ bui nɛ nu, klɛ denɔ kiwi lɛ nɛ vɛnɔ anɔnyanɔ adɛ bhɛtɛ edi asɛ eze be bisi yɛ ebuinyɛbui ɔdɛ kana.
Batɔ Tiegene Yesu etsre banɔɛza nɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ, “Ɛshãdɔkasɛ anɛ Farisianɛ ne woku Mose kegbu nɛa bha.
So alasɛ tɛ nɔ ta balɛ atɔ tɛ nɔ zɔɔ bhɛtɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ gɛ be tsre nɔ.
Pɔ nɔ tɛ bhɛtɛ kɛ gɛ baa bhɛtɛ, alasɛ ba taa bhɛtɛ kɛgɛ baa kasɛ.
Ba nya etukugbla klɛ ba yɛkɔ atrɔ banɔ bundɔ, pɔ balɛ nahwɛ na ta pɛɛ sɛ tɛ ba yɛkɔ balɛ kɛwɔɛ tirikpo tsyɛ ehunɔ etuku nɛ.
“Kɛdɔnyɛdɔ gɛ ba bhɛtɛ nɛɛ, ba bhɛtɛ kɛlɛ sɛ tɛ banɔ amɔ, Ba bhɛtɛ balɛ besebe nɛ gɛ ba ta shu nɛ bhlɛlɛlɛ klɛ balɛ bawi nɛ butɔ ihui nɛ dze dzroɖoɖo, ba pɛɛ ɛzakɔgbla nɛ bakplɔ̃ shu klɛ ba dɛmɛ bugbugbla mɛ zɛza nɛ ixogokɔevu nɛ mɛ, ba pɛɛ tɛsɛsɛnɔ denɔ banɔ ɔkɔ nɛ budzi mɛ tɛ beze kulua lɛ asɛ ‘Adɔkasɛ.’ “Pɔ ama sɛ be kulu nɔ asɛ ‘Adɔkasɛ,’ alasɛ Apalete terikpo ko yɛ alɛ wɔnɔ ahwɛ klɛ wɔnɔ petee no nu badzya.
Klɛ no ti kulu anɔnyanɔ nɛ kesukpa nɛa bha sɛ, ‘aka,’ alasɛ Aka terikpo yɛ alɛ nɔ ahwɛ, klɛ yɛ alɛ owũsise.
Ɔdɔgɔsɛ kɛ za sɛ tɛ be kulu wɔ asɛ ‘adɔkasɛ,’ alasɛ Adɔkasɛ terikpo yɛ alɛ wɔnɔ ahwɛ, gɛ enu Kristo.
Agbɛgbladɛ nɛ wɔnɔ mɛ nɛ yɛ ebe dzi wɔnɔ axwɛdɛ.
Alasɛ anɔɔ nɛ gɛ ebe feke yɛ shu be be zhinɔ yɛ, klɛ anɔɔ nɛ gɛ ebe zhinɔ yɛ shu be be feke yɛ ewunɔ.
“Butɔ kɔ wɔnɔ, ɛshãdɔkasɛ anɛ Farisianɛ, wɔnɔ betroni!
Nɔ da owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ ɔkpɛ banɔa.
Wɔnɔ nahwɛ no to tsoku, klɛ nɔ tɔ kɔ bagɛ ba pɛa sɛ be tsoku nɛ tsyɛ etsoku.
Butɔ kɔnɔ, ɛshãdɔkasɛ anɛ Farisianɛ, wɔnɔ betroni!
Nɔ yɛɛ banyɛtsi nɛ be vu klɛ kɔ ishu kɛkasɛ so ba ɖɔ ebui dzidze nɛ kpaya kukulu mɛ.
Kɛlɛ so ba ba tɛta nɔ batɔ gɛganɛ adɛa na.
“Butɔ kɔ wɔnɔ, ɛshãdɔkasɛ anɛ Farisianɛ, wɔnɔ betroni!
Nɔɔ ga kidzo nɛ kesukpa anɛ aƒu abha sɛ tɛ no tsyina anɔ terikpo, klɛ onu gɛ eedzi wɔnɔ mɛayɛ teli beke, nɔ bɔ bhɛtɛ yɛ aba tsɔmɔ ɛzakɔ tɛbha dɛ ansɛ kifu mabeke mabeke mɛ eyi nɛ gɛ no nu.
“Butɔ kɔ wɔnɔ, awɔ̃hũpu gaa gbanɔ banɔ!
Nɔ sɛ, ‘Onu gɛ anɔ teli atanɔ busɔlɛvu, ki di nu kibuinyɛbui, pɔ onu gɛ anɔ teli atanɔ busɔlɛvu mɛ sɛkadzɛdzã nɛɛ, yɛ xũ yɛ atabu nɛ anya yɛ.’ wɔnɔ bagã awɔ̃hũpu!
Kiɖue gɛ gbɛgbla dɛ, sɛkadzɛdzã nɛ pɛnɔɔ, busɔlɛvu nɛ gɛ bhɛtɛ sɛka dzɛdzã pɛ yɛ shu bhui?
Nɔɔ ɖɔ tsyɛ ɔsɛ, ‘Onu gɛ anɔ teli aka busɔlɛvumokpo nɛ atabu, kɛdɛ kasɛ kibuinyɛbui, pɔ onu gɛ anɔ teli aka kɛdɔkukɔ nɛ gɛ tsri busɔlɛvumokpo nɛa bha nɛ atabu, yɛ atabu nɛ xũ nɛ anya yɛ.’ wɔnɔ banɔ gɛ no pu awɔ̃hũ!
Kiɖue klɛ gbɛgbla dɛ, kɛdɔ kukɔ nɛ pɛnɔɔ, busɔlɛvumokpo nɛ gɛ obhɛtɛ kɛdɔ nɛ pɛ klɛ shu bhui?
Kɛlɛ so, anɔɔ nɛ gɛ atanɔ busɔlɛvumokpo nɛɛ atanɔ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ gɛ tsri ɔlɛa bha tsyɛ.
Klɛ anɔɔ nɛ gɛ atanɔ busɔlɛvu atanɔ buvu anɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ gɛ lɛ buvu nɛ mɛ.
Klɛ anɔɔ nɛ gɛ atanɔ owũsise nɛɛ, atanɔ Kpaya kegbu anɛ anɔ nɛ gɛ edzi kalɛa bha.
“Butɔ kɔ wɔnɔ, ɛshãdɔkasɛ anɛ Farisianɛ, wɔnɔ betroni!
Nɔɔ kɔ wɔnɔ kɛdɔ huhuhu tirikpo nɛ kɛfɔ mɛ—aduve, dzakanɛ anɛ ɔsã.
Pɔ nɔ shɛnahwɛ ɔshã anɛ ebui gɛganɛ nɛ mɛ—tɛnɛna, eshutukubui didi nɛ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa.
Nɔ tɔ bhɛtɛ kidegba yɛ, klɛ nɔ gɛ tɔ shɛnahwɛ kɛku nɛ tsyɛ shu.
wɔnɔ awɔ̃hũpu elete gɛ baa gbanɔ anɔ!
No pi kagɛbhli ɔtɛ̃ɛ pɔ nɔɔ munɔ kipuaga.
“Butɔ kɔ nɔ, ɛshãdɔkasɛ nɛ Farisianɛ, wɔnɔ betroni!
Noo tsi kantse nɛ kesugba nɛ kede, pɔ nɛ kɛmɛ be yuku nɛ kɛdɔgbɛgbla ŋɛŋa anɛ ishuiyɛ tɛpɛpɛ.
Farisianɛ awɔ̃hũpu elete!
No bhuso kantse anɛ kesugba nɛ mɛ butsi ko kede nɛ tsyɛ ebe bhui.
“Butɔ kɔ wɔnɔ, ɛshãdɔkasɛ anɛ Farisianɛ, wɔnɔ betroni!
No dzi ansɛ idzre gɛ ba la ɛlɛ buwa fufu, gɛ pudi nɛ ɔtɔɔ pɔ kɛmɛ nɛ mɛ yuku nɛ banɔ tsitsi axwa klɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ shu dɛbhui.
Kana ke, nɛ ɔtɔɔ nɔ wɛ̃ ansɛ banɔ dzyɔgo, pɔ wɔnɔ kɛmɛ nɛ mɛ yuku nɛ buzizi anɛ itrohuhu.
“Butɔ kɔ nɔ, ɛshãdɔkasɛ anɛ Farisianɛ, wɔnɔ betroni!
No bu idzre ɔkɔ batɔnu klɛ nɔ wũse banɛna nɛ ɔvubɔkɔ.
Klɛ nɔ ɖɔ sɛ, ‘Otɔsɛ bu za lɔ za nɛ baka shishe nɛɛ be, bu gɛ ta plɛnɔa lɛ nɛ batɔnu nɛ dzyosu bɛ balɛe si mɛ.’ Kɛlɛ so no bu ishuipɔ wɔnɔ sɛ no nu bagɛ be yi batɔnu nɛ ɛyameyia lɛ.
Kɛlɛ alɛ, nɔ kpɛ wɔnɔ bakakuku nɛ buzizi anɛ butɔtɛtɛta nɛ oyukue!
“Wɔnɔ beblidzya!
Wɔnɔ atagblashã ɛyamɛeyi!
Kɛlɛ nɔ bɔ na sii lɔ kifumani manim zɛza kɛpɔ?
Kɛlɛ so ɛsɛsɛ nɔ batɔnu anɛ bebuinyi anɛ badɔkasɛ.
Balɛmɛayɛ teli no bo yia lɛ klɛ nɔ bɔ kplalɛɔsɔ; be teli nɔ bɔ tua lɛ nɛ wɔnɔ ixogokɔevu nɛ mɛ klɛ nɔ bɔ kpatɔnɔ alɛ denɔ ɔmam ɔvɛnɔ ɔmam.
Klɛ so wɔnɔa bha nɛna nɛ petee gɛ ba balɛ nɛesi nɛa bha aba ba, denɔ Abɛl dzyosu nɛna ɔdɔ nanɔ Zakaria Berekia yeyi nɛ dzyosu, gɛ no yi nɛ busɔlɛvu anɛ busɔlɛvumokpo nɛa tsya.
Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, ebuia nɛ petee aba ba tɛmumɔɛ nɛ mɛ banɔa nɛa bha.
“O Yerusalɛm, Yerusalɛm, wɔ gɛ oyi batɔnu klɛ ohu bagɛ ba sɛsɛ wɔ nɛ aklãgbu, klɛ pɛɛ mɛ ɛdɛ pɛɛ sɛ tɛ ɛxogo weyialɛ, ansɛ gɛ ɔkukɔni oxogo akukɔɛyi akpɛ ɔlɛ busɛ mɛ, pɔ nɔ dɔɔ dɛmɛ.
Di, ba shɛ̃nahwɛ wɔ bupa nɛ akpɛkpa akpɛ wɔ ahwɛ.
Alasɛ itsre nɔ sɛ, nɔ tɛɔ mɔ mɛ ɔdɔ nanɔ kibe lɛ gɛ nɔ bɔ ɖɔ sɛ, ‘Ba yula anɔɔ nɛ gɛ aaba nɛ Apalete nɛɛ nyi mɛ.’ ”
Kɛdɔmumɔ Nɛ Kibe Nɛ Obekekɔ Yesu ashɛ̃ nɛ busɔlɛvu nɛm pɛ agaa vɛ klɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ na ba tɔnɔ yɛ klɛ ba baka yɛ buvu nɛ bui.
Ebisi asɛ, “Nɔɔ mɔ ebuia nɛ petee xãa?” “Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, ba tɛ ba shɛnahwɛ kɛklãgbu kanyaka atrɔ klɛ ɔhaɛa bha, ba ba tsɛ kɛkanyaka ebho.” Gɛ Yesu ezhidzi Olivɛ butu nɛa bha, yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ aba yɛ ɔbha nɛ tɛkpukpum.
Klɛ ba ɖɔ asɛ, “Tsre lɔ, ” “kibe ɖueɖu mɛ kibui nɛ ba ba kɛlɛ mɛ, klɛ kide gɛ ba dzi wɔ tɛbɛba nɛ kɛdɔmumɔ nɛ kibe nɛ tibibeke mɛ?” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “No lu awɔ̃ sɛ tɛ anɔnyanɔ atɛ ba wɛɛ nɔ.
Alasɛ banɔ gelee ba baa ba nɛ mɛ kinyi mɛ, aza ɖɔ asɛ, ‘mɛ nu Kristo,’ klɛ ba baa wɛɛ banɔ gelee.
No bo nu buyu anɛ buyutɛta kɛdɔ, pɔ no di klɛ ɔkɔ sɛ kɛtɛ hwanɛ nɔ.
Alasɛ tɛ ebuia nɛ aba kɛlɛ mɛ, pɔ tɛbibeke nɛ mɛ lɛ gɛ baa ba.
Amadi aba lɔ kititi nɛ amadi shu, klɛ bukusiɔŋakɔ ba lɔ kititi nɛ bukusiɔŋakɔ shu.
Bubhɛ ba dɔ klɛ busukpa ba hwa nɛ ɛzakɔ gelee.
Anɛ nɛ petee le nu ansɛ eyimumɔ ɛyamtɛtã kesikpɛkpɛ.
“Ɔkɛlɛ la ba yɛkɔ wɔnɔ akpɛ ahwɛ kɔ sɛ ba kpatɔnɔ klɛ be be yi nɔ, klɛ amadi nɛ petee atɛ ba pɛɛ wɔnɔɛ bui akpɛ mɛ so.
Nɛ kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ banɔ gelee ba ba shɛnahwɛ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa nɛ shu klɛ la ba ga aglɔ esi klɛ la tɛa dɛmɛ aglɔɛbui, klɛ itro batɔnu gelee ba baa wɛ̃ klɛ la ba wɛɛ banɔ gelee.
Nɛ kɛtɔkpum gɛganɛ kabha wuwu, banɔ gelee ɔhaglɔ ɖuɖɔ na ba yɔ, pɔ anɔɔ nɛ gɛ aza gɛganɛɛ be be bu yɛ.
Klɛ ba ba ɖɔ bukusiɔŋakɔ kibui nɛ akana kanɔ nɛ mɛ petee ansɛ kibuimɔɖɔ kɔ amadi nɛ petee, klɛ flogo pɛ obekekɔ nɛ ɔbɔ ba.
“Kɛlɛ so onu gɛ no li ɔzakɔ bhubhui pɛ nɔ mɔ ‘ebusobui nɛ gɛ akɔ butsyrɔ,’ gɛ alɛ bui la ɖɔ ganɔ atɔnu Daniɛlɛa bha nɛɛ—kɔ adɔkla nɛ enu klɛesi— kɛlɛ tɛ nɔ kɔ bagɛ alɛ Yuɖia nɛ be si avɛ betu nɛa bha.
Tɛ kɔ anɔnyanɔ gɛ etsri yɛ ovutɔ ada mɛ ezhi ba kesi sɛ aba yɛkɔ yɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ nɛ buvu nɛ mɛ.
Tɛ kɔ anɔnyanɔ gɛ alɛ ayakpa mɛ nɛ etsodzi avɛ sɛ atɛ yɛkɔ yɛ kabhawi.
Kɛlɛ za lɛ ba za gɛganɛɛ kɔ bayamunɔ anɛ bamumɔ vuvɔ nɛ ewia lɛlɛ nɛ mɛ!
No kulukpaya sɛ tɛ wɔnɔ kisi be nɛ tɛ dzi bublɔɛ be ɔdɔgɔsɛ nɛ kimuenewi nɛa bha.
Alasɛ kibe lɛ nɛɛ butɔ piim ba za, gɛ bu dɛ sɔnɔ bukanyaka denɔ kanɔ nɛ mɛ kesikpɛkpɛ ɔbɔ nanɔ ɔtsɔ̃—klɛ butɛa fla sɔnɔ bukanyaka di.
Otɔsɛ ganɛ bubhui le bhui ewi alɛ nɛa bha agɔ, anɔnyanɔ agɛ ta fla gɔ, pɔ nɛ agɛ be ti bu kɔ lɔ nɛ so, ewi alɛlɛ nɛa bha aba tsɛ.
Nɛ kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ onu gɛ anɔ teli etsre wɔa sɛ, ‘Di, Kristo nɛ naa!’ ɔdɔgɔsɛ, ‘Yɛ eli ɔkɛ̃ naa!’ tɛ yɛkɛ lɛa bha ɔŋa.
Alasɛ itro be Kristo nɛ itro batɔnu nɛ ba ba wɛ̃ klɛ ba ba bhɛtɛ kɛdɔmumɔ gbɛgbla nɛ ebui gɛ abhɛtɛ bi sɛ tɛ ba yɛkɔ awɛɛ bagɛ be klu nɛ tsyɛ—onu gɛ kɛ ba kɛlɛ mɛ ana.
Di, ɛtɛ tsre nɔ kpɛ otugba.
“Kɛlɛ so onu gɛ anɔ teli etsre nɔ asɛ, ‘Yɛ naa, gɛ ede ayakpam ekoeyi,’ no ti koeyi ɔtɔ, ɔdɔgɔsɛ, ‘Yɛ eli ɔkɛ̃ naa, nɛ kɛmɛ bevu nɛ mɛ,’ nɔ tɛ yɛkɛ klɛa bha ɔŋa.
Alasɛ ansɛ gɛ subhaɛfu nɛ kii de kiwiɔyɛkɔ pɛɛ kɛɛ wɛŋ nɛ kiwiɔdɔkɔ, kana Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ tɛbɛba nɛ baa za.
Ɔkɛlɛ gɛ kɛdɔtsitsi lɛɛ, ɔkɛlɛ eshishi nɛ ebe xogo.
“Nɛ ewi tsutsɔmɔa lɛ nɛe de ko, “ ‘kiwi nɛ ba dɔ otumu, klɛ wele nɛ atɛa tã; awɛ̃wɛ̃ nɛ aba wɔlɛ denɔ kɛlɛɛ mɛ, klɛ owũsise banɔ nɛ aba hwa.’ “Nɛ kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ kɛdɔmumɔ nɛ ba wɛ̃ nɛ owũsise, klɛ amadi petee nɛ kesukpa nɛa bha na be tsishu.
Ba ba mɔ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ ɔmunɔ nɛ mɛ gɛ ede owũsise nɛ aaba, nɛ kemi anɛ ishubhubhui gbɛgbla mɛ.
Klɛ aba kpɛ yɛ baxwɛdɛ nɛ buxulɔ̃ɛ bubɔ gɛganɛɛ kɛdɔ kukulu, klɛ be be xogo yɛ banɔ nɛ gɛ ebu nɛ alɛ talɛ̃ nɛ mɛ, denɔ owũsise nɛ obekekɔ ɔyɛkɔ vɛnɔ ɔgɔgɔɛkɔ.
“Ɔtsɔ̃ nɛ nɔ kpasɛ kɛdɔ odenɔ kabhɔosi nɛ shu.
Kibe nɔ nɛ gɛ ɔlɛ ɛshɛ nɛ lɛ vuvɔvuvɔ klɛ awulakpa nɛ ekoeyi avuvɔ, no ti sɛ ekpe nɛ etsu aba.
Kɛɛ za na tsyɛ, onu gɛ nɔ mɔ ebuia nɛ petee, no ti sɛ etsu aba nɛ wɔ kedunu nɛ kpɔ̃.
Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, tɛmumɔɛ nɛ mɛ tɛ ba fla ɔdɔ nanɔ kibe lɛ gɛ ebuia nɛ petee aba kɛlɛ mɛ.
Owũsise anɛ kesukpa aba ba fla, pɔ mɛ kibui nɛ tɛ ba fla di.
Anɔnyanɔ Eti Nyi Kiwi Ɔdɔgɔsɛ Kibe “Anɔnyanɔ eti nyi kiwi nɔɔ pɛ ɔdɔgɔsɛ ɔɖɔ nɛ mɛ, baxwɛdɛ nɛ owũsise tsyɛ ti nyi, Kpaya yɛ Eyi nɛ tsyɛ eti nyi, Aka nɛ owũsise nɛ ko yɛe nyi.
Anasɛ gɛ kɛza nɛ Nowa kibe, kana kɛba za nɛ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ tɛ bɛ ba mɛ.
Alasɛ flogo tɛ kesukpa nɛa bha ka ba yɛkɛ buni, banɔa za ŋɛdɔ klɛ ba wɛ̃ dɔ, baa gbanɔ adzɛ klɛ baa yɛkɔ adzɛ akɔ sɛ ba gbanɔ, ɔdɔ nanɔ kibe lɛ gɛ Nowa etsoku otsyokpo nɛ mɛ; klɛ be di ti kibuinyɛbui denɔ kɛ gɛ baa ba nɛ shu, ɔdɔ nanɔ kibe lɛ gɛ buni nɛ ba gbɛgba klɛ bu yɛkɔ balɛ petee ashɛ̃nɔ.
Kana kɛba za nɛ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ tɛ bɛba mɛ.
Banɔ tɛa bha ba za ayakpam; ba ba yɛkɔ terikpo klɛ la ba shɛ̃nahwɛ agɔgɔɛ shu elu.
Badzɛ tɛa bha ba ba za hɔ kɛdɔ nɛ buhɔa bha, ba ba yɛkɔ terikpo klɛ ba shɛnahwɛ abhla nɛ shu elu.
“Kɛlɛ so nɛ nɔ za nɛ awɔ̃, alasɛ no ti nyi kiwi nɔɔ nɛ gɛ klɛa bha wɔnɔ Apalete nɛ aba ba.
Pɔ nu kibui nɛesi sɛ: Otɔ sɛ apalete nɛ eti elishim ɔɖa nɔɔ nɛ mɛ gɛ ezi nɛ aba ba, ata za nɛ awɔ̃ klɛ agɛ ta kɔ sɛ ezi nɛ ebe tsoku bulɛ mɛ.
Kɛlɛ so alasɛ wɔnɔ tsyɛ nɔ za tɛbɛbala mɛ, alasɛ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ aba ba nɛ ɔɖɔ nɔɔ nɛ mɛ gɛ otoo di kidzoe nu.
“Kɛlɛ anee yɛ enu axwɛdɛ gɛ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa lɛ yɛahwɛ klɛ enyi bui, gɛ yɛahwɛ apalete nɛ ayɛkɔ baxwɛdɛ nɛ akpɛ nɛ yɛ bupa nɛ mɛ sɛ tɛ aza kɔa lɛ kɛŋɛŋa nɛ ɔɖɔ dzyɔgo nɛ mɛ?
Kɛ ba pɛ kɔ axwɛdɛ nɔɔ nɛ gɛ yɛ apalete nɛ aba ba mɔ yɛ sɛ aabhɛtɛ kana onu gɛ etsodzi aaba.
Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, aba yɛkɔ yɛ edzu yɛ kɛnɔmɛdɔ petee nu.
Pɔ kɛɛ lɛ sɛ axwɛdɛ nɔa lɛlɛ nɛ kɛtɔkpu mɛ gɛganɛ klɛ aɖɔ nɛ ishum asɛ, ‘Ma palete nɛ aba za ɔklɛ kibe dzidze,’ klɛ aba kpa yɛ baxwɛdɛ glɔa lɛ nɛ tu klɛ aŋa pɛ awɛ̃ dɔ nɛ beluwɛ̃.
Axwɛdɛ nɛ yɛ apalete nɛ aba ba nɛ kiwi nɔ nɛa bha gɛ etee di yɛ dzoenu klɛ nɛ ɔɖɔ nɔɔ nɛ mɛ gɛ etinyi.
Ebe bhui yɛ akpɛ bupɛpɛpɛ mɛ klɛ aba kɔ yɛ kɛxwɛ nɛ betroni nɛ shi, nɛ ɔkɛlɛ gɛ iyuyo nɛ eletɛtã alɛ.
Kɛkpalɛ Denɔ Badzɛ Lɔfɔ Gɛ Betinyi Anyɛ Shu “Nɛ kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ owũsise bukusiɔŋakɔ nɔ bɔ za ansɛ badzɛ lɔfɔ gɛ ba yɛkɔ balɛ bakanɛgbɛ pɛ be koeyi avɛ sɛ tɛ ba da tsyanɔ adzɛenyine.
Batieti edzi bagã klɛ tieti edzi bebuinyi.
Bagɛ eti nyibui na yɛkɔ balɛ bakanɛgbɛ pɔ ba dɛ yɛkɔ bubɔ kanyaka plɛnɔa lɛ.
Bagɛ be nyibui, nɛ xũ, ba yɛkɔ bubɔ akpɛ epulim evunɔ plɛnɔ balɛ bakanɛgbɛ.
Adzɛenyine nɛ aba wɔ kide bɔɛ nɛ yɛ tɛbɛba nɛm, klɛ so ba tɔ klɛ la kpa kɔlɔɛ dɔ klɛ la ba vɛnɔ tra.
“Nɛ elishi nɛ shitibha ogugu oyi sɛ, ‘Adzɛenyine nɛ naa!
No koeyi ɔba tɛ nɔ bɔ tsyanɛ yɛ mɔ!’ “Ɔkɛlɛ badzɛ nɛ gɛ ti nyianyɛ ne vualɔ klɛ le deke balɛ bakanɛgbɛ.
Bagɛ be ti nyibui nɛ etsre bagɛ nyibui nɛ asɛ, ‘Nɔkɔ lɔ wɔnɔ bubɔ nɛ bɔɛ, bulɔ bakanɛgbɛ nɛ eeni.’ Bubite nyinyibui nɛ asɛ, “ ‘Ao,’ ‘bulɔ bubɔ nɛ dɛ kpe kɔɔ lɔ pɛ bu zɛ ba na wɔnɔ tsyɛ.
No tsodzi ɔvɛ, agɛ aadɛ nɛ ɔkɔ tɛ no do bu tuli ɔkɔ shu.’ “Pɔ gɛ be tsodzi atɔ nɔ kidzo avɛ bubɔ nɛ obu kɔ, ko klɛ adzɛenyine nɛ ebe ku.
Bubite nyinyibui nɛ gɛ balɛ ba bala kɔ ishu nɛ bubɔ mɛ nɛ xũ na tsyanɔ adzɛenyine klɛ la ga vɛ adzɛ nɛ ɔgbanɔkɔ nɛ buvugbla nɛ mɛ.
Klɛ ba da opupu.
“Kɛlɛe de mɛ tieti gugɔɛ nɛ tsya ba ba.
Ɔkɛlɛ ba ɖɔ asɛ, ‘Apalete!
Apalete!’ ‘Danɛ opupu nɛ ɔkɔ lɔ!’ “Pɔ be tsre balɛ asɛ, ‘Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, iti nyi nɔ.’ “Kɛlɛ so nɔ za nɛ awɔ̃, alasɛ no tinyi kiwi nɔɔ ɔdɔgɔsɛ ɔɖɔ nɛ mɛ.
Kɛkpalɛ Denɔ Baxwɛdɛ Tɛata Shu “Klɛ kɛ zɛ ba za ansɛ anɔ gɛ aaga kidzo, klɛ eklu yɛ baxwɛdɛ klɛ ayɛkɔ yɛ kɛnɔmɛdɔ nɛ akpɛ ahwɛ kɔa lɛ.
Terikpo akɔ yɛ Sidi Akpãteti, abhla akɔ yɛ Akpãtabha, klɛ agugɔɛ nɛɛ akɔ yɛ Kɛkpãtirikpo, akɔ akanyaka nɛ yɛ tɛzɛzam nu.
Klɛ ashɛ̃ avɛ yɛ kidzo nɛa bha.
Anyɛ nɛ gɛ ayɛkɛ Akpãteti nɛ avɛ ada ayɛkɔ yɛayɛ na kpɛ kɛxwɛ wɛwam klɛ amɔ tieti atrɔ agɛ ba kɔ yɛ nɛa bha.
Kana, aga yɛkɛ Tɛabha nɛ tsyɛ amɔ tɛabha atrɔ agɛ bakɔ yɛ nɛa bha.
Pɔ agɛ yɛ ayɛkɛ kɛkpãtrikpo nɛ xũ ashɛ̃, klɛ ede bu ozi klɛ ayɛkɔ yɛayɛ nɛ ekpu.
“Nɛ kibe dzidze tilie de apalete nɛ ebe de kidzo nɛ mɛ aba klɛ ebe bisi balɛ kana gɛ ba ga nɛ ehoeyi.
Anyɛ nɛ gɛ ayɛkɛ Akpãteti nɛ ayɛkɔ teti bhlatɔ ata amɛna.
Klɛ asɛ, ‘Apalete,’ ‘ɔkɔ mɛ Sidi Akpãteti.
Di, Ɛmɔ teti trɔ yɛa bha.’ Yɛ apalete nɛ asɛ, ‘Wɔ naa bhɛtɛ, axwɛdɛ dzyɔgo gɛ ba ba yɛkɛ wɔa bha ŋa!
Ɔza tɛyɛyɛkɛ ŋa mɛ nɛ kɛdɔ bhli nɛ gɛ ɛkɔ wɔ, ɛba yɛkɔ wɔ idzu ebui anɛ kɛdɔ gelee nu.
Ba tɛ ɔbɔ mɔ same ɔplɛnɔ wɔ apalete!’ “Anyɛ nɛ gɛ ayɛkɛ Akpãtabha nɛ tsyɛ aba.
Asɛ, ‘Apalete,’ ‘ɔkɔ mɛ Sidi Akpãtabha, di, ɛmɔ tabha trɔ.’ “Apalete nɛ asɛ, ‘Ɔnaa bhɛtɛ, axwɛdɛ dzyɔgo gɛ ba ba yɛkɛ wɔa bha ŋa!
Ɔza tɛyɛyɛkɛ ŋam nɛ kɛdɔ bhli nɛ gɛ ɛkɔ wɔ, ɛba yɛkɔ wɔ idzu ebui anɛ kɛdɔ gelee nu.
Ba tɛ ɔbɔ mɔ same ɔplɛnɔ wɔ apalete!’ “Klɛ anyɛ nɛ gɛ ayɛkɛ Sidi Kɛkpãtrikpo nɛ tsyɛ aba.
Klɛ asɛ, ‘Apalete,’ ‘Inyi sɛ anɔ gɛganɛ onu, gɛ oobu kɛdɔ nɛ ɔklɛ gɛ ɔdɛ ɖa kɛdɔ klɛ ɔyalɛ kɛdɔ nɛ ɔklɛ gɛ ɔdɛ hwɛ kɛdɔ.
Kɛlɛ so isi wɔɛ fu klɛ mɛ ɛyɛkɔ ehoeyi nɛ gɛ ɔkɔm nɛ da tsu ozi pɛ ɛyɛkɔ kpɛ.
Di, kɛ gɛ nu wɔɛyɛ nɛ nɛɛ.’ “Apalete nɛ etsre yɛ asɛ, ‘Wɔ kɛtɔkpum gɛganɛ anɔ onu, axwɛdɛ avuvɔ onu!
Kɛlɛ so onyi sɛ ibui dɔ nɛ ɔklɛ gɛ ɛdɛ ɖa kɛdɔ klɛ mɛ yalɛ kɛdɔ nɛ ɔklɛ gɛ ɛdɛ hwɛ dɔ?
Kɛbɔ, anlo ɔtɛ yɛkɔ kɔba nɛ ɔdɔ kpɛ bagɛ baa bala kɔba nɛ ahwɛ, pɛ ata mɔ atrɔ pɛ onu gɛ ide ba pɛ ɛta ba yɛkɛ.
“ ‘Yɛkɛ ehoeyi nɛ yahwɛ tɛ ɔyɛkɔ kɔ agɛ evunɔ Akpã lɔfɔ.
Alasɛ aanɔ gɛ kɛdɔ lɛ yahwɛ ba za ba kɔ yɛ atrɔ, klɛ kɛdɔ ba kpe nɛ yahwɛ.
Aanɔ nɛ gɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ ma yɛ ahwɛ, kibhliyi nɛ gɛ lɛ yahwɛ nɛ tsyɛ ba ba yɛkɛ kɛlɛ nɛ yahwɛ.
Klɛ tɛ ɔyɛkɔ axwɛdɛ zhuzhɔlɛa lɛlɛ nɛ ɔtɛɛ kpɛ ɔtɔ nɛ otumu mɛ, ɔklɛ gɛ iyuyo nɛ eletɛtã alɛ.’ Ibhoshi Nɛ Bepidzya “Onu gɛ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ aaba nɛ yɛ ishu bhuibhui mɛ, pɛ yɛ baxwɛdɛ nɛ peteea lɛ aplɛnɔ yɛ, ebe zhiza yɛ bukusiegbu nɛa bha nɛ owũsise nɛ ishu bhuibhui mɛ.
Amadi nɛ petee le be xogo nɛ yɛ amɛ, klɛ aba tsya banɔ nɛ mɛ ansɛ gɛ ibhoshi agbɛgbanɔ aba tsya ibhoshi ebu nɛ bepidzya nɛɛ shi.
Aba yɛkɔ ibhoshi nɛ elu yɛ kɛŋa mɛ klɛ bepidzya na ba za yɛ kɛbɛtɛkpɛ mɛ.
“Ɔkɛlɛ Ekusi nɛ ebe tsre ɛgɛ li kɛŋa nɛ mɛ asɛ, ‘Nɔ ba, wɔnɔ bagɛ mɛ Aka nɛ atɛ yula, nɔ yɛkɔ wɔnɔ ɔŋakɔ, gɛ bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ gɛ ba bala lu kɔ nɔ denɔ kanɔ nɛ kesikpɛkpɛ.
Alasɛ bubhɛ yim klɛ nɔ kɔ mɛ kɛdɔ mɛ ŋa, oniwɛ ɔtam klɛ nɔ kɔ mɛ kɛdɔ tili mɛ wɛ̃, idzi efu klɛ no kulu mɛ ɔmɛna wɔnɔ mɛ, Ibisi kɛpɔtɛ klɛ nɔ da kɛpɔtɛ ɔkɔ mɛ, ɛɛnya klɛ no di mɛa bha, ɛza buvu klɛ nɔ bɔ sra mɛ odi.’ “Ɔkɛlɛ anɔnɛna nɛ ebe builɛ nu asɛ, ‘Apalete, kibe ɖueɖu lɔ mɔ wɔ gɛ bubhɛ yi wɔ pɛ bu kɔ wɔ kɛdɔ ɔŋa, pɛ ɔdɔgɔsɛ klɛ bu kɔ wɔ kɛdɔ tili sɛ ɔwɛ̃?
Kibe ɖueɖu lɔ mɔ wɔ ansɛ efu pɛ bu yɛkɛ wɔ kpɛ bulɔɛ shi, pɛ ɔdɔgɔsɛ obisi kɛpɔtɛ pɛ bu ba da kɛpɔtɛ kɔ wɔ?
Kibe ɖueɖu mɛ bu mɔ wɔ pɛ ɔɔnya ɔdɔgɔsɛ ɔza buvu pɛ bu ba mɔ wɔ di?’ “Ekusi nɛ ebe bui lɛ nu asɛ, ‘Ítsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, kɛdɔnyɛdɔ nɔ bhɛtɛ kɔ anɔ bhli kanyaka nɛ madzyalɛa nɛ mɛ, mɛ nɔ bhɛtɛ kɔ.’ “Ɔkɛlɛ aba ɖɔ tsre bagɛ bedzi yɛ kɛbɛtɛkpɛ nɛ mɛ asɛ, ‘Nɔ shɛ nɛ mɛ ɔbha, wɔnɔa gɛ ba ɖɔɛ bui akpɛ, ayɛkɔ tɛ̃a kpɛ kifu gɛ tɛba ni di mɛ gɛ ba bala elu kɔ ɔfufɔɛkpã nɛ ɛlɛ baxwɛdɛ.
Alasɛ bubhɛ yi mɛ klɛ nɔ dɛ kɔ mɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ sɛ ɛŋa, oniwɛ ɔta mɛ klɛ nɔ dɛ kɔ mɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ sɛ ɛwɛ̃, Idzi efu klɛ nɔ dɛ yɛkɛ mɛ ɔkpɛ wɔnɔɛ shi, ibisi kɛpɔtɛ nɔ dɛ da kɛpɔtɛ kɔ mɛ, ɛɛnya klɛ mɛ za buvu no dɛ di mɛa bha.’ “Balɛ tsyɛ be be bui lɛ nu aɖɔ sɛ, ‘Apalete, kibe ɖue be bu mɔ gɛ bubhɛ yi wɔ, oniwɛ ɔta wɔ, odzi efu, obisi kɛpɔtɛ, ɔɔnya ɔdɔgɔsɛ ɔza buvu, pɛ bu dɛ plɛnɛ wɔ?’ “Ɛbe bui lɛ nu asɛ, ‘Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, kɛdɔnɔ nɛ gɛ nɔ dɛ bhɛtɛ kɔ anɔ bhli tsyɛ nɛ banɔa nɛ mɛ, nɔ dɛ bhɛtɛ kɔ mɛ naa lɛlɛ.’ “Ɔkɛlɛ la ba shɛ avɛ ede tsoku batɔtɛtɛta mabeke mabeke mɛ, pɔ banɔnɛna na ba vɛ ɛkpã mabeke mabekemɛ.”
Tɛnyɛnya Nɛ Yesu Shu Gɛ Yesu aɖɔ ebuia nɛ petee beke, etsre yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ, “Ansɛ gɛ no nyi, ewi tabha ko ala gɔ kɔ Tɛfɛflawi nɛ tɛŋɛŋa, klɛ la ba yɛkɔ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ akpɛ ahwɛ kɔ la kplasɔ.” Klɛ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ gbla anɛ balɛ banɔ shishe nɛ exogo nɛ Kayafasɛ gɛ enu kpayanɔgbla nɛ teli bupa mɛ, klɛ la nya nɛ Yesu shu asɛ ba ba ga bɔshɛ dzo tilia bha tɛ be yi yɛ.
Ba sɛ, “Pɔ ganɛ kiwiŋɛŋa nɛ mɛ, odinuana eblaebui aba ba nɛ banɔ nɛ shi.” Ba Sra Bubɔ Akɔ Yesu Nɛ Betani Gɛ Yesu aza Betani anyɛ teli gɛ be kulu asɛ Simɔnɛ gɛ aanya bunyadzɛdzã nɛ bupa mɛ, adzɛ teli atɔnɔ aba yɛ ɔbha nɛ bubɔ huhu ŋɛŋaedzi nɛ kɛklãgbuipuli gbɛgbla tili, gɛ ayɛkɔ akɔ abalɛ Yesu ada nɛ mɛ nɛ kibe lɛ gɛ akpasa vɛ kɛwã pɛ edzia ŋɛdɔ.
Gɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ amɔa na, ki kualɛ obulo.
Be bisi asɛ, “Kide dɔ zizi kɛlɛ nui lɛlɛ?” “Ba ta dɛ bubɔ huhuhu nɛ kedziŋɛŋa pɛ ta yɛkɔ ehei nɛ akɔ betsyutsyuini nɛe.” Yesu enyi ana so, etsre alɛ asɛ, “Kide so pɛ nɔɔ kpɛ adzɛ nɛ bunuhu?
Abhɛtɛ kibui gɛ pudi amɛna mɛ ɔkɔe.
Betsyutsyuini nɛ xũa lɛ wɔnɔ bha kibenyɛbe, mɛ pɔ nɛɛ nɔ tɛ bɔ mɔ mɛ kibenyɛbe nɛ wɔnɔ ɔbha.
Bubɔ nɛ gɛ adzɛ na balɛ mɛa bha, bunu sɛ aabala mɛ akɔ tɛvuvubɔ.
Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, ɔkɔnyɔkɔ gɛ baa ɖɔ kibuidzyɔgo nɛ akana nɛ kanɔa nɛ mɛ, kibui nɛ gɛ adzɛ anɛ abhɛtɛ, kana ba ba ɖɔɛ lɛ akana, ayɛkɔ baka yɛ bui nɔ.” Yuɖasɛ Adɛmɛ Asɛ Aba Ga Yesue Si Ɔkɛlɛ banɔ lɔfɔntɛabha nɛ ɔmayɛ teli gɛ be kulu asɛ Yuɖasɛ Iskarɔtɛ nɛ atɔnɔ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ gbla nɛ avɛ klɛ ede bisi asɛ, “Kide nɔ pɛɛ sɛ tɛ nɔ kɔ mɛ onu gɛ ɛyɛkɔ yɛ ɛkpɛ ahwɛ kɔ nɔɔ?” Kɛlɛ shu so ba kla kɔbafufu afata kɔ yɛ.
Denɔ kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ ɔvɛnɔ Yuɖasɛ etenɔ kidzoe nu pɛɛ sɛ tɛ ayɛkɔ Yesu akpɛ ahwɛ.
Apalete Nɛ Owulago Kɛdɔŋɛŋa Nɛ Gbɛgbɛvu nɛ gɛ Bunayekedɔ ma yɛ mɛ Kiwi Ŋɛŋa nɛɛ wi tutɔpu nɛa bha, badɔkpasɛ nɛ ba tɔnɔ Yesu aba klɛ be bisi yɛ asɛ, “Fakɔ ɔpɛɛ sɛ tɛ bubhɛtɛ tɛbɛbala kɔ Tɛfɛflawi nɛ tɛŋɛŋa?” Ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Nɔ tsoku ɔmagbla nɛ mɛ nɛ anyɛ teli ɔkɔ tɛ no tsre yɛ ɔsɛ, ‘Adɔkasɛ nɛ asɛ: Mɛ kibe nɛ tsuu ba.
Ɛɛvɛ tɛ ŋa Tɛfɛflawi bulɔ nɛ mɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ wɔ pa nɛ mɛ.’ ” Kɛlɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ abhɛtɛ ansɛ gɛ Yesu aɖɔ klɛ la bala kɔ Tɛfɛflawi.
Gɛ owulago nɛ ɔna, Yesu akpasa za kɛdɔŋɛŋa nɛ shu anɛ yɛ banɔ Lɔfɔntɛabha.
Klɛ gɛ bedzi aŋa kɛdɔ nɛɛ, aɖɔ asɛ, “Itsre nɔ kɛgba nɛ sɛ, wɔnɔ ɔmɛayɛ teli yɛ aba ga mɛesi.” Kibui lɛ nɛ dɛ kua lɛ same gɛ Yesu aɖɔ so bakpa yɛ ɖɔ tsre yɛ terikpo terikpo asɛ, “Kɛlɛ ganɛ mɛ, Apalete?” Yesu ebu kɛlɛ nu asɛ, “Anɔ nɛ gɛ aakpahwɛ kesugba mɛ nɛ mɛ, yɛ aba ga mɛesi.
Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ aba shɛ ansɛ gɛ ba ŋlɔmɛ elu nɛ yɛ shu.
Pɔ butɔ kɔ anɔɔ nɛ gɛ yɛ aba ga Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛe si!
Anɔa lɛlɛ ba dɛ mɔ yɛ tsyɛ ata pɛ̃ kɔ yɛ adɛ.” Ɔkɛlɛ Yuɖasɛ nɛ gɛ abaa ga yɛesi na ɖɔ asɛ, “Kɛlɛ ganɛ mɛ, Adɔkasɛ?” Yesu ebu lɛ nu asɛ, “Ee, wɔ bɔ ga mɛesi.” Gɛ bedzi aŋa kɛdɔ nɛɛ, Yesu ayɛkɔ gbɛgbɛvu, ehu ahwɛ klɛ aya yɛmɛ, klɛ ayɛkɔ kɔ yɛ badɔkpasɛ, klɛ aɖɔ asɛ, “Nɔ yɛkɛ tɛ nɔ tã, mɛ shuidzya nɛɛ lɛ.” Ɔkɛlɛ ayɛkɔ kantse, ehu ahwɛ klɛ ayɛkɔ kɔa lɛ, klɛ aɖɔ asɛ, “Nɔ wɔɛ̃ kɛdɔ nɛ kalɛm, wɔnɔ petee.
Mɛ dzyosu nɛ naa nɛ onugbunyɛnya mɛ nɛ wɔnɔ, gɛ ba yɛkɔ balɛ esi kɔ banɔ gelee kɔ balɛ buzizi tɛyɛyɛkɔ tsye.
Itsre nɔ, ɛtɛa wɔɛ̃ wayɛ̃ eyuyua denɔ ɔtsɔ̃ ɔdɔ nanɔ kibe lɛ gɛ ɛba wɔɛ̃ yɛ avuvɔ nɛ nɔ nɛ Maka bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ mɛ.” Gɛ ba zha ɔdzɛ nɛ beke, ba shɛ avɛ Olivɛ Butu nɛa bha.
Yesu Aɖɔlu Sɛ Petro Ebe Tsodzi Nɛ Yɛede Ɔkɛlɛ Yesu etsre yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ, “Elishia nɛ mɛ, wɔnɔ petee no bo si ɔlɔ mɛ, alasɛ kɛŋlɔ̃mɛ li sɛ: “ ‘Ɛba hu ibhoshi agbɛgbanɔ nɛɛ dɔ, klɛ ibhoshiha nɛ petee ba hle.’ Pɔ onu gɛ ɛlɔ beke, ɛba putɔ kɔnɔ vɛ Galelia.” Petro asɛ, “Onu gɛ banɔ petee hle nɛ wɔ shu tsyɛ mɛ ɛtɛ ba shɛ.” Yesu ebu kɛlɛ nu asɛ, “Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, ” “elishia nɛ mɛ, flogo tɛ ɔkukɔ ɔbɔ bɔ, wɔ Petro ɔbɔ ɖɔ sɛ oti nyi mɛ aɖɔ tata.” Pɔ nɛ Petro aza trɔ kɛklãgbu asɛ, “Onu gɛ kɛba sɛ tɛ bulɔ nɛ wɔ butsi tsyɛ ɛtɛba shɛ̃nahwɛ wɔ shu di.” Klɛ badɔkpasɛ gɔgɔɛ nɛ petee ba ɖɔ atrɔ.
Kpayakuklu Nɛ Getsemane Ɔkɛlɛ Yesu nɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ na shɛ vɛ ɔkɔ toli gɛ be kulu asɛ Getsemane, klɛ etsre balɛ asɛ, “Za ɔkɛ̃ nɛ mɔ tɛ evɛ da kulukpaya tɛ ɛba.” Agbanɔ Petro anɛ Zebeɖi yɛeyialɛ tɛabha nɛ tsyɛ evunɔ avɛnɔ, klɛ ebe tsoku same mamɔ mamɔ mɛ klɛ awɛ̃ ansɛ kibui tili kɛɛ kpɛ yɛ bunuhu.
Ɔkɛlɛ etsrea lɛ asɛ, “Mɛ ɔfufɔɛ nɛ oyuku nɛ same mamɔ mamɔ ɔyɛkɔ dɔ nanɔ butsi.
Nɔ za nɛ awɔ̃ nɛ ɔkɛ̃ nɛ mɛ.” Gɛ aza ga vɛ otugba kɛbɔɛ, awɔlɛ adɔ klɛ ayɛkɔ amɛnɛmɛ ekumuesi klɛ ekulukpaya sɛ, “Maka, onu gɛ kɛɛ ba za tɛbhɛbhɛtɛ mɛ, kɛlɛ tɛ ɔkɔ kantsea nɛ kafla mɛ nu.
Pɔ ganɛ kana gɛ mɛ ɛpɛɛ, kana gɛ wɔ ɔpɛɛ kɛlɛ ba ba kɛlɛ mɛ.” Ɔkɛlɛ gɛ etsodzi aba yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ ɔbha klɛ aba mɔ be dzi adɔ tra.
Ebisi Petro asɛ, “Kɛlɛ so wɔnɔa nɛ ɔtɛ za nɛ awɔ̃ nɛ mɛ ɔɖɔ torikpo tsyɛ?” “Nɔ za nɛ awɔ̃ tɛ no kulukpaya sɛ tɛ nɔ tɛ bɔ wɔlɛ ku tɛfifeke di mɛ.
Ɔfufɔɛ nɛ xũ ɔpɛɔ sɛ, pɔ ishuidzya nɛ tɔ.” Aza shɛ bubhla avɛ klɛ ede kulukpaya sɛ, “Maka, onu gɛ kɛɛ ta ba kɛlɛ mɛ sɛ tɛ kantsea nɛ kafla mɛ nu, pɛ kɛlɛ sɛ tɛ ɛwɔɛ̃a lɛ, kɛlɛ kɔ la bhɛtɛ wɔ tɛpɛpɛɛ.” Gɛ etsodzi aba, aza ba mɔ badɔkpasɛ nɛ gɛ li aza dɔ tra, alasɛ balɛ awɔ̃hũ nɛ egbiĩ.
So, ashɛ̃ lɔa lɛ klɛ aza vɛ klɛ ede kulukpaya butramɛ, nɛ kibui trikpoɛ lɛlɛ nɛ tɛɖuɖɔ.
Ɔkɛlɛ etsodzi aba badɔkpasɛ nɛ ɔbha klɛ etsre balɛ asɛ, “Nɔ kodzi ɔdɔ tra pɛ no dzi ozo muene?
No di, ɔɖa nɛ mɛ otsuɔba, klɛ ba ga Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛesi akpɛ bagɛ ba bhɛtɛ buzizi nɛ ahwɛ.
Nɔ lɔ, nɔ kɔ lɔ shɛ!
Agɛ aga mɛesi nɛ yɛa baa!” Be Vu Yesu Nɛ kibe lɛ nɛ gɛ eke dzia ɖɔ kaɖɔ, Yuɖasɛ, gɛ enu Kɛfɔntɛabha nɛ ɔmɛayɛ teli, nɛ ebe ku.
Banɔɛza gbla lɛ yɛe de nɛ baa hɛ nɛ busukpogunu, gɛ benu banɔ gɛ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ anɛ beshishe nɛ ba kpɛ yɛe si.
Ɔtsɔ̃ nɛɛ agɛ aba ga yɛe si nɛ atrɔ bushɛ tili nɛ banɔ nɛ asɛ, “Aanɔ nɛ gɛ yɛ onugbu mɛ da mini; no vu yɛ.” Yuɖasɛ aga tɔnɔ Yesu nɛ ɔklɛ, klɛ asɛ, “Adɔkasɛ, Ɛsɛnɛ wɔ!” klɛ emini yɛ onugbu.
Yesu etsre yɛ asɛ, “Ɔbhɛa, bhɛtɛ kɛgɛ kɛlɛ so pɛ ɔba.” Ɔkɛlɛ banɔ nɛ be koeyi aba, ba nyɛna Yesu klɛ be vu yɛ.
Ɔkɛlɛ Yesu yɛ abhla nɛ teli etso ɛhɛ klɛ afatɛ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ nɛ teli axwɛdɛ nɛ butɔ trukpo atɛ̃.
Pɔ Yesu etsre yɛ asɛ, “Yɛkɔ wɔ kɛpamɛ nɛ ɔkpɛ kɛklɔ mɛ, ” “alasɛ anɔnyanɔ gɛ ayɛkɔ kɛpamɛ aba ga kɛpamɛ shu etsi.
Nɔɔ bhɛtɛ kɛtɔkpum sɛ ɛtɛ ba na Maka nɛ owũsise kulu pɛ aba sɛsɛ mɛ yɛ kpayaxwɛdɛ ivulo akpã lɔfɔntabha pɛ ba ba ta keyu nɛ banɔa?
Pɔ kɛlɛ kɛba za pɛ kibui nɛ ba bhɛtɛ ansɛ gɛ ba ŋlɔ̃mɛ lɛ elu nɛ Kpayɛbui keplukpa nɛ mɛ?” Nɛ kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ Yesu etsre banɔɛza nɛ asɛ, “Iputɔ kɔ kititi lulɔ banɔ teli, so pɛɛ nɔ yɛkɔ bupamɛ anɛ busukpogunu pɛ no bo vu mɛ?
Ɛza busɔlɛevu nɛ mɛ kibenyɛbe ɛɛkasɛdɔ, klɛ no di vu mɛ odi.
Pɔ ebuia nɛ petee aba kɛlɛ mɛ sɛ tɛ batɔnu nɛ kɛdɔ nɛ gɛ ba ŋlɔ̃mɛ elu nɛ aba kɛlɛ mɛ.” Kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ petee atɛ pɔɛhle alɔ yɛ.
Yesu Nɛ Bebhuiklu Nɛ Amɛ Ba gɛ evu Yesu nɛ ayɛkɔ yɛ avɛnɔ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ Kayafasɛ, nɛ ɔkɛlɛ gɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ anɛ beshishe nɛ be xogo.
Pɔ Petro yɛa za yɛe de nɛ tɛdzidze tilim, ede ku bubhui oklukɔ.
Etsoku klɛ ezhiaza kesi nɛ bepupo nɛ ɔbha sɛ tɛ amɔ kɛdɔnɔ nɛ gɛ ba de koeyi nɛ kɛlɛ mɛ.
Kpayaɔzakɔanɔ anɛ Bebhuiklu nɛ baa pɛɛ oturo bunubhubhui nɔɔ nɛ gɛ ba ba yɛkɔ nɛ Yesu shu pɛ be be yi yɛ.
Pɔ ba dɛ mɔ kibuinyɛbuia na, nɛ itro nɛ petee gɛ be koeyi ebe hu nɛ mɛ.
Gɔgɔɛ nɛɛ banɔ tɛabha be koeyi aba klɛ be bu aɖɔ asɛ, “Anyɛa nɛ yɛ aɖɔ asɛ, ‘Ɛba na busɔlɛvu nɛ bu yɛɛ klɛ ɛba tsodzini bulɛ ɛbhɔ nɛ ewi tata mɛ.’ ” Ɔkɛlɛ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ nɛ alɔ klɛ etsre Yesu asɛ, “Ɔtɛ bo bu kibui nɛ gɛ be bisi wɔ nɛ nu?
Ebui ɖueɖu di naa nɛ gɛ be be bu dzu wɔa mɛ ana?” Pɔ Yesu adɛ fɔɛ nɛ alɛ.
Kpayaɔzakɔanɔ nɛ etsre yɛ asɛ, “Ɛka atabu nɛ ɛkpã Kpaya nɛ nyi mɛ kɔ wɔ sɛ, Tsre lɔ onu gɛ wo nu Kristo, Kpaya yɛ Eyi.” Yesu ebu aɖɔ asɛ, “Ee, kɛlɛ ansɛ gɛ ɔɖɔ, pɔ itsre nɔ petee sɛ: Nɛ otugba mɛ nɔ bɔ mɔ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ gɛ ezhidzi Agbɛgbladɛ nɛ kɛŋa mɛ gɛ aga ɔmunɔm aaba denɔ owũsise.” Ɔkɛlɛ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ nɛ atsyuɛ yɛ bawi klɛ aɖɔ asɛ, “Aɖɔ ebusobui!
Kide so pɛ kɛlɛ sɛ tɛ bufla zɛɛ pɛɛ ebuimɔɖɔ dɛ ana?
Di, ɔtsɔ̃ no nu yɛ ebusobui nɛ gɛ aɖɔ.
Kide wɔnɔ atɔkpu nɛ mɛ aɖɔ?
Be bui lɛ nu asɛ, “Edzyenɔ kɔ butsi.” Ɔkɛlɛ be bu bututu akpɛ yɛamɛ klɛ be hu yɛ ekpli.
Be teli ba bɔ yɛ dɔ klɛ ba ɖɔ asɛ, “Kristo, mɔ kibui tili ɔɖɔ tsre lɔ.
Ane gɛ ehu wɔɛ dɔ?” Petro Adɛada Nɛ Yesu Shu Ɔtsɔ̃ Petro ebe dzi ɔtɔ nɛ bubhui oklukɔ, klɛ axwɛdɛdzɛ bhli teli aba tɔnɛ yɛ, klɛ aaɖɔ sɛ, “Wɔ tsyɛ ɔza Yesu Galelia eyi nɛe de.” Pɔ nɛ balɛ amɛ Petro adɛ dɛmɛ sɛ yɛ tsyɛ alɛ Yesue de.
Ɔkɛlɛ aaɖɔ sɛ, “Itinyi kɛdɔnɔ nɛ gɛ nɔɔ ɖɔ.” Ɔkɛlɛ ashɛ̃ vɛ ede li kedunu, ɔkɛlɛ adzɛnuvɔɛ teli aza ba mɔɛ klɛ aaɖɔ tsre banɔ nɛ gɛ be li ɔkɛlɛ nɛ asɛ, “Anɔa nɛ gɛ elia nɛ tsyɛ aza Yesu Nazarɛtɛ eyi nɛe de.
” Aza dɛada nɛ atabu asɛ: “Itinyi anyɛ nɛ!” Nɛ kɛlɛe de bɔɛ, banɔ nɛ gɛ be li kititi nɛ ɔkɛlɛ nɛ ba tɔnɔ Petro avɛ klɛ ba ɖɔ asɛ, “Tutuutu wɔ tsyɛ balɛ ɔmayɛ teli onu, alasɛ wɔ kaɖɔ ɖuɖɔ nɛ kebu wɔ akasɛ.” Ɔkɛlɛ akpa ebui ɖɔ kpɛ ishu klɛ aka atabu kɔ banɔ nɛ asɛ, “Mɛ iti nyi anyɛ!” Ko klɛ ɔkukɔ ɔbɔ.
Ɔkɛlɛ Petro abaka ebui nɛ gɛ Yesu aɖɔ etsre yɛ asɛ, “Flogo tɛ ɔkukɔ ɔbɔ bɔ, wɔ ɔbɔ dɛada ada tata sɛ oti nyi mɛ.” Ɔkɛlɛ Petro ekoeyi ashɛ̃ klɛ ede bi iyuyo popoopo.
Yuɖasɛ Akpɛhuioli Nɛ kɛvulɔ nɛ pinii, kpayaɔzakɔanɔ anɛ banɔ anɛ beshishe na ba trɔ asɛ be be yi Yesu.
Klɛ so ba ba nya yɛ klɛ la gbanɔ yɛ avɛnɔ ada kpɛ ahwɛ akɔ Pilatio, gɛ enu anɔ nɛ gɛ aŋa kɛmadi nɛa bha.
Gɛ Yuɖasɛ nɛ gɛ akpɛ yɛ ahwɛ nɛ amɔ asɛ, be bu Yesu butsipɔ, kɛ trɔ yɛa bha klɛ etsodzini kɔbafufu ehoeyi afata nɛ gɛ ba kɔ yɛ nɛ avɛnɔ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ anɛ beshishe.
Klɛ aɖɔ asɛ, “Ɛbhɛtɛ buzizi, ” “alasɛ ɛga dzyosu gɛ adɛ bhɛtɛ buzizi kanyaka nɛe si.” Banɔ nɛ be bisi Yuɖasɛ asɛ, “Bulɔ pɔ, kide kibui lɛ nɛ nu kɔlɔ?” “Wɔ nahwɛ kibui nɛɛ lɛlɛ.” Kɛlɛ so Yuɖasɛ ayɛkɔ kɔba nɛ ada tɛa kpɛ busɔlɛvu nɛ mɛ klɛ ashɛ̃.
Klɛ ashɛ̃ avɛ ada kpɛ kihuioli.
Kpayaɔzakɔanɔ nɛ aba tɔkɛ kɔba klɛ ba ɖɔ asɛ, “Kinu kibui gɛ lɔ kititi nɛ ɔshã nɛ shu sɛ tɛ ba yɛkɔ kɔbaa nɛ ada kpɛ balɛ kɔba shi, alsɛ enu dzyosu kɔba.” So nɛ ba ba trɔɛ lɛ asɛ ba ba yɛkɔ kɔba nɛ ede dzi kesukpa nɛ tisiotsukɔ toli tɛ ba zaa vubɔ befu.
Kɛlɛ so pɛɛ bee kulu ɔkɛlɛ asɛ, Dzyosuesukpa ɔbɔnanɔ nɛ obo.
Ɔkɛlɛ kɛgɛ Yeremia atɔnu nɛ aɖɔ lu kɛ ba kɛlɛ mɛ sɛ, “Ba yɛkɔ kɔba afata, gɛ enu kedzi nɛ gɛ Izraɛlanɛ ba dɛ nɛ yɛ shu, klɛ ba yɛkɔ kɔba nɛ ede dzi kesukpa nɛ tisiotsukɔ, ansɛ gɛ Apalete nɛ akɔ mɛ ɔshã sɛ ɛbhɛtɛ.” Yesu Nɛ Pilatio Amɛ Nɛ kɛlɛ mɛ Yesu eli kititi nɛ ɔma ekusigbla nɛ amɛ, klɛ ebisi yɛ asɛ, “Wo nu Yuɖanɛ ekusi?” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Ee, kɛlɛ ansɛ gɛ ɔɖɔɛ lɛ.” Gɛ kpayanɔgbla nɛ ɔma banɔ shishe nɛ be bisi yɛ ebui nɛ gɛ ba yɛkɔ nɛ yɛ shu, edi bu kibui nyɛbui nu.
Ɔkɛlɛ Pilatio ebisi yɛ asɛ, “Oto nu ebui nɛ gɛ baa yɛkɔ nɛ wɔ shu?” Pɔ Yesu adɛ fɔɛ, klɛ edi bu kibui tirikpo tsyɛ nu, klɛ kɛbhɛtɛ ɔmakuisigbla nɛ bi.
Ɔtsɔ̃ nɛɛ ki nu bugu kɔ ɔmaekusigbla nɛ kiwiŋɛŋa nɛa bha sɛ tɛ ashɛ̃nahwɛ bevuza nɛ terikpo gɛ banɔɛza nɛ ba pɛɛ nɛ shu akɔ alɛ.
Nɛ kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ evuza butɔm gɛganɛ teli gɛ be kulu asɛ Barabasɛ tsyɛ aza buvu.
So gɛ banɔɛza nɛ be ku, Pilatio ebisi alɛ asɛ, “Eɖueɖu shu nɔ pɛɛ sɛ tɛ ɛshɛ̃nahwɛ kɔ nɔ, Barabasɛ pɛnɔɔ Yesu nɛ gɛ be kulu asɛ Kristo?
Alasɛ enyi asɛ kawɔ̃kpɛ mɛ la ga pɛ baa yɛkɔ Yesu nɛ akpɛ ahwɛ kɔ yɛ.
Nɛ kibe lɛ mɛ gɛ Pilatio ezhiedzi yɛ kebhuiegbu nɛa bha, yedzini nɛ asɛsɛ yɛ ɔklasɔ toli asɛ, “Kibuinyɛbui kɛ tɛ za wɔ ahwɛ kɔ anyaa nɛ gɛ buzizi kanyaka ma yɛ shu, alasɛ ɛmɔ butɔ tsutsɔmɔ nɛ yɛ shu nɛ bulɛla mɛ obo.” Pɔ, kpayaɔzakɔanɔ anɛ ɔma banɔ shishe nɛ bakɔ sɛ tɛ banɔɛza nɛ be bisi sɛ tɛ ba shɛnahwɛ Barabasɛ shu tɛ ba yɛkɔ Yesu avɛnɔ ede yi.
Ɔmaekusigbla nɛ bisi balɛ asɛ, “Anee shu nɔ pɛ sɛ eshɛnahwɛ kɔ nɔ nɛ banɔ tɛabha nɛ shi?” Banɔɛza nɛ asɛ, “Barabasɛ lɔ pɛɛ.” Pilatio ebisi asɛ, “Kɛlɛ kidee mɛ ba bhɛtɛ, nɛ Yesu nɛ gɛ bee kulu asɛ Kristo nɛ ɔtsɔ̃?” Banɔɛza nɛ asɛ, “Alasɛ tɛ ɔkɔ la kplaɛasɔ!” Pilato ebisi banɔɛza nɛ asɛ, “Kide so?
Buzizi ɖueɖu abhɛtɛ?” Pɔ, banɔɛza nɛ ba za kpɛ ogugu gɛganɛɛ adɛa na sɛ, “Kɔ la kplaɛasɔ!” Gɛ Pilatio amɔ asɛ eti be ku ɔkɔnyɔkɔ akɔ kibui, pɛ igugu kpɛkpɛ ɛlɛ ba kpɛesi nɛɛ, ayɛkɔ buni klɛ eplu ahwɛ nɛ banɔɛza nɛ amɛ, klɛ aɖɔ asɛ, “Itinyi kibuinyɛbui nɛ anyaa nɛ dzyosu shu, wɔnɔ amɛ lɛ di!” Banɔ nɛ petee be bu klɛ nu asɛ, “Kɔ yɛ dzyosu nɛ aba bulɔ nɛ bulɔeyia lɛ nɛa bha fãa!” Ɔkɛlɛ ashɛ̃nahwɛ Barabasɛ shu akɔ alɛ.
Pɔ akɔ sɛ be tu Yesu, klɛ ayɛkɔ yɛ akpɛ ahwɛ kɔa lɛ kɔ yɛ tɛkpɛkplasɔ.
Keyutugbani Na Kpɛ Yesu Butsɔ Ɔkɛlɛ ɔmaekusigbla nɛ keyutugbani na yɛkɔ Yesu avɛnɔ Ɔmaekusigbla nɛ bupagbla mɛ klɛ ivulo nɛ petee ba kana yɛ atsya.
Ba tsywɛ̃ bawi nɛ yɛ shu klɛ ba yɛkɔ awidzɛdzã akpɛ akɔ yɛ, klɛ ba bhɛtɛ ewikutu klɛ ba yɛkɔ ekumu akɔɛ.
Ba yɛkɔ ovusi akpɛ yɛ kɛŋahwɛ nɛm klɛ be zhi akpla nɛ yɛ otugba klɛ ba kpɛ yɛ butsɔ asɛ, “Obuii, Yuɖanɛ ekusi nɛ naa!” Be bu butu ata yɛ, klɛ ba yɛkɛ ovusi nɛ yahwɛ klɛ ba yɛkɔ ehu yɛ etsodzini ehu.
Gɛ ba kpɛ yɛ butsɔ nɛ beke, be bule kɛdɔ dzɛdzã nɛ yɛ shu klɛ ba yɛkɔ yɛ nahwɛ bawi nɛ akpɛ akɔ yɛ.
Klɛ ba yɛkɔ yɛ avɛnɔ ɔkplasɔ kɔ.
Tɛkpɛkplasɔ Gɛ ba vɛ yɛ ɔkplasɔ kɔ, ba tsyanɔ anyɛ teli gɛ ede Sirene, gɛ be kulu asɛ Simɔnɛ nɛ kidzo nɛ mɛ, klɛ ba trɔ anyɛ nɛa bha sɛ tɛ ayɛkɛ butsiosi nɛ etuku akɔ yɛ.
Be de ku ɔkɔ toli gɛ be kulu asɛ Golgata (Atɔkpuxwa Ɔzakɔ nɛ butu tulia bha).
Ɔkɛlɛ nɛɛ, ba kpɛ bɔwa kɛtɛkɛtɛ nɛ bulu mɛ akɔ Yesu sɛ awɔɛ̃, pɔ gɛ emini bɔlɛ edi, adɛ dɛmɛ awɔɛ̃.
Gɛ ba kplaɛasɔ beke, ba tsyuɛ yɛ bawi na kpɛ aglɔm ganɔ kebisi mɛ.
Klɛ bezhiedzi ɔkɛlɛ klɛ bee po yɛ.
Nɛ yɛ kɛtɔkpu, ba ŋlɔ̃mɛ atrɔ asɛ: Yesu, Yuɖanɛ ekusi nɛ naa.
Ba kpla bezi tɛabha tsyɛ asɔ aplɛnɔ yɛ, teli nɛ yɛ kɛŋam, abhla tsyɛ nɛ yɛ kɛbɛtɛkpɛm.
Baa nɔ nɛ gaa fla nɛ ɔkɛlɛ nɛ baa kula yɛ, klɛ bee shuku balɛ atɔkpu atrɔ pɛ baa ɖɔ asɛ, “Wɔ nɛ gɛ ɔsɛ ɔbɔ yɛ busɔlɛvu, klɛ obo tsodzini bulɛ ɔbhɔ nɛ ewi tata mɛ, bu wɔshue!
Zhi ɔba nɛ butsiosi nɛ shue, onu gɛ onu Kpaya yɛ Eyi!” Kana ke kpayaɔzakɔanɔ, anɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ anɛ banɔshishe tsyɛ ba kpɛ yɛ butsɔ.
Klɛ baa ɖɔ asɛ, “Ebu banɔ, ” “pɔ ataa na yɛshu bu!
Yɛ enu Izraɛlanɛ nɛ Ekusigbla!
Ezhia ba nɛ butsiosi nɛ shue, tɛ bumɔ yɛa bha yɛkɛŋa.
Ayɛkɛ Kpaya kabha ŋa.
Kɔ Kpaya nɛ ebe bu yɛe onu gɛ apɛɛ yɛ, alasɛ aɖɔ asɛ, ‘Mɛ nu Kpaya yɛ Eyi.’ ” Kana bezi nɛ gɛ ba kplasɔ plɛnɔ yɛ nɛ tsyɛ baa kula yɛ nɛ akulatu.
Yesu Tɛtsitsi Denɔ ɛɖa lɔfɔntɛbha mɛ ɔdɔ nanɔ ɔtramɛ nɛ mɛ otumu ɔdɔ nɛ kesukpa nɛa bha petee.
Ansɛ ɛɖa tɛtamɛ ana, Yesu akpɛ ogugu gɛganɛɛ asɛ, “Eloi, Eloi, lama sabaktani?” Gɛ klɛ kesi enu asɛ, “Mɛ Kpaya, Mɛ Kpaya, kide so pɛ ɔshɛnahwɛ mɛ shua na?” Gɛ banɔ nɛ teli gɛ be li ɔkɛlɛ nɛ be nu yɛ ogugu ba sɛ, “Eekulu Eliya.” Ɔkɛlɛ balɛ ɔmayɛ teli esi avɛ ada yɛkɔ ɔkɔɛsa atsakpɛ vinega wayɛ̃ mɛ, klɛ ayɛkɔ sɔ osi toli nu, klɛ ayɛkɔ ada tɔ Yesu onugbu sɛ awɔɛ̃.
Banɔ gɔgɔɛ na sɛ, “Nɔ shɛnahwɛ yɛ shu.
Kɔlɔ di sɛ Eliya nɛ aba ba ebe bui yɛ dza.” Klɛ gɛ Yesu aza kpɛ ogugu nɛɛ, klɛ ebhui ɔfufɔɛ.
Nɛ kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ, busɔlɛvu mɛ kɛpɔtɛ nɛ tsywɛ denɔ kabha ɔbɔ na nɔ kesi.
Kesukpa nɛ ka hwa, klɛ aklãgbu gbɛgbla ayɛɛ.
Idzre danɛ klɛ banɔ dzyɔgo gelee gɛ be ti tsi nɛ tsodzi anyɛmɛ klɛ ba lɔ ba ɛkpãm.
Be koeyi denɔ idzrem, klɛ nɛ Yesu tɛlulɔ nɛe de, be tsoku ɔmagbla nɛ gɛ ɔlɛ shu obhui nɛ mɛ, klɛ ba wɛ̃ nɛ banɔ gelee amɛ.
Gɛ keyutugbani anɛ bepupo nɛ Yesu odzre nɛ shu ba mɔ kesukpahuhwa anɛ ebui nɛ petee gɛ aba kɛlɛ mɛ, kifu kua lɛ tsutsɔmɔ tsɔmɔ, klɛ be bu aɖɔ asɛ, “Kɛgbɛagba Kpaya yɛ Eyi edzi!” Badzɛ gelee ba za odzidzekɔ pɛ bee di kɛdɔ nɛ asɛsɛ.
Ba za Yesue de edenɔ Galelia ke sɛ tɛ ba bhɛtɛ kɛgɛ bazhã nɛ akɔ yɛ.
Badzɛa lɛlɛ nɛ mɛayɛ teli ebe dzi Maria Magdaline, Maria Yakobo yɛeni, anɛ Yosɛfu, anɛ Zebeɖi yɛ eyi anɛ yɛ eni.
Yesu Tɛvuvubɔ Gɛ owulago nɛ ɔna, ehoeyielete teli ede Arimatea, gɛ be kulu asɛ Yosɛfu, gɛ yɛnahwɛ nɛ ebe dzi Yesu adɔkpasɛ.
Atɔnɔ Pilatio avɛ sɛ, ba yɛkɔ Yesu yɛ etsitsi nɛ akɔ yɛ, klɛ Pilatio asɛ ba da yɛkɔ akɔ yɛ.
Yosɛfu ada yɛkɔ anɔ tsitsi, klɛ anya yɛ akpɛ kɛpɔtɛ fufum mɔmɔ, klɛ ayɛkɔ yɛ ada kpɛ kɛklãgbu odzre vuvɔ mɛ gɛ yɛ nahwɛ ebu kɔ shu.
Klɛ eglebe kɛlãgbugbla tili nɛ ɔkɛlɛ nɛ ada odzre nɛ nu klɛ ashɛ̃.
Maria Magdaline anɛ Maria bhla nɛ be zhedzi odzre nɛ ɔbha.
Bepupo Nɛ Odzre Nɛ Shu Kiwi bhla nɛ, kɛgɛ ba nɛ Tɛbɛbala Kiwi nɛe de, kpayaɔzakɔanɔ anɛ Farisianɛ na tɔnɔ Pilatio avɛ.
Klɛ bede tsre yɛ asɛ, “Aka, ” “bu baka sɛ kibe lɛ nɛ gɛ aka lɛ nɛ ɛkpã etronia lɛlɛ na aɖɔ asɛ, ‘Nɛ ewi tata ede ɛba tsodzi lɔ.’ So kɔ ɔshã sɛ tɛ be po yɛ odzre nɛ ɔdɔ nanɔ kiwi tramɛ.
Odinuana yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ be be ti zuru yɛ ebu ka ba sɛ yɛ alɔ denɔ bekpu mɛe.
Otro ɔlɛlɛ nɛ lɔ bɔ tsyɔmɔ dɛ ɔtutɔpu.” Pilatio ebu kɛlɛ nu asɛ, “Nɔ yɛkɔ epupo, ” “Nɔ vɛ odo di odzre nɛa bha ansɛ kana gɛ no nyi.” So, ba vɛ klɛ be de di lɛ ɔkɔ sɛ ba da yɛkɔ kɛdɔ ada odzre, klɛ ba yɛkɔ bepupo edzu ɔkɛlɛ.
Yesu Tɛlulɔ Nɛ Kimuenewi nɛede, nɛ Kiwi tutɔpu nɛ ɔgɔnɛ nɛ mɛ kɛvlɔ nɛ pinii, Maria Magdaline anɛ Maria bhla nɛ ba vɛ asɛ tɛ be de di Yesu odzre.
Kesukpa huhwa gɛganɛɛ abɛ lɛ mɛ, alasɛ Apalete nɛ axwɛdɛ nɛ ede owũsise nɛ aba, klɛ ede tii kɛklãgbugbla nɛ aplɛ nɛ odzre nɛa bha klɛ ezhiaza klɛa bha.
Yɛ tɛwɛ̃wɛ̃ nɛ mɛ za ansɛ subhaɛfu, klɛ yɛ bawi nɛ fuli ansɛ amuklãgbu.
Kifu ku bepupo nɛ tsutsɔmɔ tsɔmɔ nɛ ɔklɛ, klɛ be shuku klɛ le dzi anasɛ banɔ tsitsi.
Kpaya axwɛdɛ nɛ etsre badzɛ nɛ ɔkɛlɛ asɛ, “No ti si kifu, alasɛ inyi sɛ Yesu nɔɔ pɛɛ, agɛ ba kplasɔ.
Avama ɔkɛ, atɛ lɔ, ansɛ gɛ aɖɔ aba fla nɔ.
Nɔ ba tɛ no bo di ɔkɛlɛ gɛ awũsɔ.
Kɛlɛ so nɔ vɛ zia tɛ no do tsre yɛ badɔkpasɛ: ‘Atɛ nyɛmɛ ede nɔ bekpum klɛ eti putɔ kɔ nɔ avɛ Galelia.
Ɔkɛlɛ nɔ bɔ mɔ yɛ.’ Ɔtsɔ̃ iti tsre nɔ.” Kɛlɛ so badzɛ nɛ ba nawɔ̃ klɛ ba shɛ nɛ odzre nɛ shu, nɛ kifu pɔ same aza balɛ mɛ, klɛ be si avɛ ede tsre yɛ badɔkpasɛ.
Nɛ ɔkɛlɛ ɔlɛlɛ nɛ ko Yesu agbla tsyanɔa lɛ.
Asɛ “Ɛsɛnɔ nɔ.” Badzɛ nɛ etsobunɔ yɛ, klɛ ba nyɛna yɛ butsrukpɔ klɛ ba kpɛ kɛtɔkpuesi akɔ yɛ.
Ɔkɛlɛ Yesu etsre balɛ asɛ, “No to si fu.
Nɔ vɛ tɛ no do tsre madzyalɛ nɛ ɔsɛ ba tɔnɔ avɛ Galelia, ɔkɛlɛ la ba mɔ mɛ.” Bepupo Nɛ Kibuiɖuɖɔ Gɛ badzɛ nɛ tsri balɛ kidzoa bha avɛ, bepupo nɛ teli etsoku ɔmagbla nɛ mɛ klɛ ba da ɖɔ kibuinyɛbui di gɛ vɛa bha nɛ etsre kpayaɔzakɔanɔ.
Gɛ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ na ba tɔnɔ banɔshishe, ba bhɛtɛ kɛtɔkpum tili, ba kɔ bepupo nɛ kɔbagbla teli, be tsrea lɛ asɛ, “Alasɛ tɛ nɔ ɖɔ sɛ, ‘Yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ balɛ aba ebe zuru yɛ ebu nɛ odzre nɛ mɛ elishi mɛ nɛ kibe li gɛ bu vɛnɔ tra.’ Onu gɛ kibui nɛ da nanɔ ɔmaekusigbla, kɛ ba ku yɛ awɔ̃ ka bu bu nɔ nɛ kibui mɛe.” Kɛlɛ so, keyutugbani nɛ ba yɛkɛ kɔba klɛ ba bhɛtɛ ansɛ gɛ be tsre alɛ.
Klɛ ɔdzɛdzɛɔ nɛ bata ɔlɛ akana Yuɖanɛ nɛ petee mɛ ɔkɔ bɔ nanɔ obo.
Kɛxwɛ Gbla Ɔkɛlɛ badɔkpasɛ lɔfɔntoli na shɛ avɛ Galelia, nɛ betu nɛa bha gɛ Yesu etsrea lɛ elu.
Gɛ ba mɔ yɛ, ba kpɛ kɛtɔkpuesi akɔ yɛ; pɔ be teli adɛ yɛkɛ aŋa.
Ɔkɛlɛ Yesu aba balɛ ɔbha klɛ asɛ, “Kabhaŋɛŋa petee anɛ owũsise anɛ kesukpa, ba tɛ yɛkɔ akpɛ mɛ ahwɛ.
Kɛlɛ so, nɔ vɛ tɛ nɔ dɔ bhɛtɛ amadi nɛ petee tɛ le dzi badɔkpasɛ, tɛ nɔ kpɛ buni kɔ banɔ nɛ Aka anɛ Eyi nɛ nyi mɛ anɛ Ɔfufɔɛ dzyɔgo, klɛ tɛ nɔ kasɛ dɔ sɛ anɔnyanɔ abhɛtɛ ansɛ gɛ ɛtrɔ kɔ nɔ.
Klɛ kɛlɛ kɛlɛm sɛ ɛlɛ plɛnɔ nɔ kibenyɛbe, ɔkɔ dɔ nanɔ kanɔ nɛ tibibeke.”
Otugbaɛbui Kpaya kibui ansɛ gɛ Marko aŋlɔmɛ nɛ kpɛ kesi sɛ, “Kpaya kibui denɔ Yesu Kristo, Kpaya yɛ Eyi nɛ shu.
” Yesu nɛ awɛ̃ ansɛ anɔ gɛ alɛ kɛxwɛwɛwa mɛ anɛ kabhaŋɛŋa mɛ.
Yɛ kabhaŋɛŋa nɛ kawɛ̃ nɛ yɛ kɛdɔkɛkasɛ nɛ mɛ, yɛ kemi nɛ ɛfufɔɛkpã nɛa bha, anɛ yɛ buzizi tɛyɛyɛkɔtsye banɔ mɛ.
Yesu aɖɔ kaɖɔ edenɔ yɛnahwɛ ishu ansɛ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi ana, gɛ aba sɛ tɛ aba yɛkɔ yɛ ɛkpã nɛ etsye tɛ ebu banɔ edenɔ balɛ buzizi nɛ mɛ.
Marko ebu Yesu shu kibui nɛ akasɛ nɛ kɛlɛ tɛdzyudzyɔ vɛ otugba mɛ, ganɔ bugɛganɛ kidzoa bha, ɔyɛkɔ plɛnɔ tɛɖuɖɔtrɔ yɛ ebui nɛ gɛ abhɛtɛ nɛa bha, ɔyɛkɔdɛ kaɖɔɖuɖɔ anɛ yɛ kɛdɔkɛkasɛ.
Gɛ enyi sɛ badɔkla gelee gɛ ba baa kla yɛ kɛdɔŋuŋlɔmɛ nɛ be di nu Yuɖanɛ so nɛ, nɛ Marko keplukpa nɛ mɛ, ba yɛkɔ atrɔ ishu, klɛ be bu Yuɖanɛ begu nɛ balɛ kesukpa nɛ tɛzɛza mɛ anɛ ebui bhɛbhɛtɛ nɛ kesi mɔɔmɔ.
Nɛ kaɖɔɖuɖɔ bhli denɔ Yohanɛsɛ Enikpɛ nɛ shu, anɛ yɛ bunikpɛkpɛ kɔ Yesu anɛ yɛ tɛfifekedi nɛede, adɔŋlɔmɛ nɛ edi zi kibe flogo pɛ atasɔlɛ Yesu banɔ banya bibeke anɛ yɛ kɛdɔkɛkasɛ nɛ shu ebui ɖuɖɔ.
Nɛ otugba, bagɛ baza Yesue de nɛɛ, bee nu yɛ kesi adɛ kana, pɔ yɛ maɖɔmaɖɔ anɛ kititilulɔ nɛ yɛ shu nɛ xũ kabha ko kɛɛ vɛ.
Nɛ keplukpa nɛ atɔkpu gɔgɔɛ nɛ mɛ, baɖɔ Yesu kanɔ nɛ mɛ ɔgɔnɛ gɔgɔɛ nɛ ɛkpã zɛza nɛ shu kibui, gɛganɛɛ ɔyɛkɔ dɛ nɛ yɛ tɛkpɛkplasɔ nɛ butsiosi nɛ shu, anɛ yɛ tɛlɔlɔ denɔ bekpu mɛ shu.
Bukplo gɔgɔɛ nɛ yɛ kɛdɔŋuŋlɔmɛ nɛ obekekɔ nɛ gɛ kpasɛ ketsuka nɛ mɛ, ganɛ Marko yɛ aŋlɔmɛ klɛ xũ, adɔŋlɔmɛ bhlatɔ yɛ aŋlɔmɛ kɛlɛ.
Kalɛmɛ Ebuilulu Kpaya Kibui nɛ kesikpɛkpɛ :- Yesu Kpaya Kibui nɛ tɛkɛkasɛ nɛ Galelia :—: Denɔ Galelia ɔdɔ nanɔ Yerusalɛm :- Ɔgɔnɛ gɔgɔɛ nɛ Yerusalɛm tɛbubunɔ anɛ yɛ mɛ tɛtsutsoku :—: Yesu tɛnyɛnyɛmɛ denɔ butsi mɛ :- Apalete nɛ tɛwɛ̃wɛ̃ anɛ yɛ tɛshɛshɛ ganɔ ɔmunɔ mɛ :-
Yohanɛsɛ Enikpɛ Nɛ Kidzo Ŋuŋuse Yesu Kristo, Kpayayɛeyi nɛ bui nɛ kesi ɔkpɛkɔ.
Ba ŋlɔmɛ nɛ Yezaya atɔnu nɛ keplukpa nɛ mɛ asɛ, “Ɛba kpɛ mɛ axwɛdɛ nɛ iputɔnɔ kɔ nɔ, yɛ aba be ŋuse wɔnɔɛ dzo ” “anɔ teli ogugu gɛ oklu kɛdɔ denɔ ayakpa mɛ nɔ ɔsɛ, ‘Ŋuse Apalete nɛ dzo, bu kidzo dzyudzyɔ kɔ yɛ.’ ” Klɛ so Yohanɛsɛ aba nɛ bunikpɛkpɛ denɔ ayakpa nɛ mɛ be, klɛ aɖɔ kitem tsyitsyina bunikpɛkpɛ bui kɔ buzizi tɛyɛyɛkɔ tsye.
Banɔ petee gɛ ba kana Yuɖia be ɔyɛkɔ plɛnɔ Yerusalɛm ɔma mɛ banɔ nɛ petee bekoeyi aba tɔnɔ yɛ.
Gɛ be bu balɛ buzizi nɛ aɖɔ beke nɛɛ, ba yɛkɛ bunikpɛkpɛ denɔ yɛ ɔkɔ nɛ Yɔɖan Keni nɛ mɛ.
Yohanɛsɛ akpɛ kipuagatɛka awui, klɛ anya kazaplukpa ɔdzadi, yɛ ŋɛŋa nɛ dzi ahwaye anɛ betsiuni.
Klɛ yɛ kibui nɛ gɛ evunɔ kɛlɛ dzi sɛ, “Mɛe de nɛɛ anɔ teli abaa ba, gɛ alɛ kemi adɛ mɛ, anyɛa lɛlɛ nɛ afukpaohui tsyɛ ɛtɛ ba naa zhikpla kɔ ɔlɛ tɛbublue.
Mɛ nɛɛ ɛkpɛ buni kɔɔ nɔ nɛ buni, pɔ yɛ aba kpɛ buni kɔɔ nɔ nɛ Ɔfufɔɛ Dzyɔgo.” Yesu Bunikpɛkpɛ Anɛ Yɛ Tɛfifekedi Kɛbe lɛlɛ nɛ mɛ gɛ, Yesu ede Nazarɛtɛ nɛ Galelia nɛ aba, klɛ aba yɛkɛ bunikpɛkpɛ denɔ Yohanɛsɛ ɔkɔ nɛ Yɔɖan Keni nɛ mɛ.
Nɛ Yesu tɛ kukoeyi denɔ buni nɛ mɛ ko, amɔ owũsise nɛ gɛ ɔdanɛ klɛ Ɔfufɔɛ Dzyɔgo nɛ ozhiba yɛa bha anasɛ gɔgɔwí.
Klɛ ogugu oyi denɔ owũsise pɛ lɔɔ ɖɔ sɛ, “Wɔ onu Meyi, gɛ ɛdɛmɛ nɔ; wɔ shu mɛ mɔ awɔ̃kuku.” Ɔkɛlɛ nɛ ko, Ɔfufɔɛ nɔ yɛkɔ yɛ ɔvɛ nɔ ayakpam, klɛ aza ayakpa mɛ ewui afɛtalɛ̃, ɔkɛlɛ Satana ebe feke yɛ edi.
Aza bagavuga shi, klɛ kpaya baxwɛdɛ nɛ bee di yɛa bha.
Yesu Badɔkpasɛ Tutɔpu Nɛ Tɛkuklu Gɛ be vu Yohanɛsɛ akpɛ buvu, Yesu ashɛ̃ avɛ Galelia, adaa ɖɔ Kpaya kibui dzyɔgo.
Aɖɔ asɛ, “Kibe nɛ tɛ na,” “Kpaya bukusi nɛ tɛ tso bunɔ lɔ.
So no tsyina kitem tɛ nɔ yɛkɛ kibui dzyɔgo nɛa bha ɔŋa!” Gɛ Yesu agaa fla nɛ Galelia aƒu nɛ shu, amɔ Simɔnɛ anɛ yadzya Andrɛasɛ gɛ ba kpɛ kenim dzikle nɛ kɛvɔ nɛ mɛ, alasɛ be nu banɔ gɛ bee bu kenimɛdzya.
Yesu asɛ, “Nɔ ba, za mɛe de mɔ, ” “Ɛba bhɛtɛ nɔ banɔ gɛ be bu banɔ.” Ɔkɛlɛ nɛ ko, ba gbla shɛ̃nahwɛ balɛ kenim dzikle nɛ shu klɛ ba lɛ yɛe de.
Gɛ aza vɛ otugba nɛ bɔɛ, amɔ Zebeɖi yɛeyialɛ nɛ gɛ be nu Yakobo anɛ yadzya Yohanɛsɛ nɛ keniabha opupu toli mɛ, gɛ be zee ŋuse balɛ kenim dzikle.
Nɛ kibe mazimazi mɛ, Yesu eklu alɛ, klɛ ba gbla lɔ alɛ yɛe de, klɛ ba shɛ alɔ balɛ aka Zebeɖi anɛ yɛ baxwɛwa nɛ opupu nɛ mɛ.
Yesu Akɛka Ɔfufɔɛkpã Ebueyinɔ Ba vɛ Kapenaumɛ, klɛ gɛ Yuɖanɛ Kimuenewi nɛ na, Yesu ede tsoku oxogokɔvu nɛ mɛ klɛ akpa kɛdɔ kasɛ.
Yɛ kɛdɔ kɛkasɛ nɛ yinɔ banɔ, alɛsɛ akasɛ kɛdɔ anasɛ anɔ gɛ kabhaŋɛŋa lɛ yahwɛ ganɛ anasɛ gɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ nɛ baa kasɛ dɔ.
Nɛ kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ, nɛ balɛ oxogokɔvu nɛ mɛ, anyɛ teli gɛ ɔfufɔɛkpã otsri yɛa bha nɛ akpɛ ogugu gɛganɛɛ asɛ, “Kidee wɔ Yesu Nazarɛtɛ eyi nɛ ɔpɛɛ denɔ bulɔ ɔkɔ?
Ɔba sɛ tɛ obo beke lɔ dza?
Inyi anɔ nɛdi gɛ onu, wɔ nu Kpaya Ɔfufɔɛ Dzyɔgo Anɔ!” Yesu asɛ, “Da onugbu!” “Koeyi ɔbɔ fla nɛ anɔ nɛ mɛ!” Ɔfufɔɛkpã nɛ oshuku anyɛ nɛ gɛganɛɛ klɛ lɔ fla koeyi nɛ yɛ mɛ nɛ tɛbubɔ dzyɛɛ.
Yesu tɛbhɛbhɛtɛ nɛ bhɛtɛ banɔ nɛ kibi klɛ bee bisi aglɔ asɛ, “Kide lɔɔ mɔa?
Kɛdɔ kɛkasɛ vuvɔ, klɛ nɛ kabhaŋɛŋa tysɛ ana!
Klɛ ɛfufɔɛkpã tsyɛ ta yɛ atɔ.” Be nu Yesu dɔ zia nɛ Galelia kesukpa nɛa bha petee.
Yesu Ebeke Banɔ Gelee Banya Gɛ ba nya shɛ nɛ oxogokɔvu nɛ mɛ ko, Yesu, Yakobo anɛ Yohanɛsɛ ba shɛ avɛ Simɔnɛ anɛ Andrɛasɛ bupa nɛ mɛ.
Nɛ bupa nɛ mɛ be tsre Yesu asɛ Simɔnɛ yɛ andze nɛ eliesi nɛ buwui.
So Yesu etsoku atɔnɔ adzɛ, klɛ ada nyɛna yɛ ɔhwɛ klɛ evu alɔ.
Buwui nɛ shɛ̃nahwɛ adzɛ nɛ shu klɛ etenɔ balɛa bha di.
Nɛ owulago ɔlɛlɛ nɛ kiwidudɔe de ba gbanɔ banyɛnya nɛ petee anɛ bagɛ ɛfufɔɛkpã tsri balɛa bha nɛ amɛna Yesu.
Ɔma nɛ petee bexogo nɛ bupa nɛ kedunu, klɛ Yesu ebeke banya edidedi nɛ ga za be gelee mɛ.
Klɛ akɛka ɛfufɔɛkpã gelee ebu nɛ banɔ mɛ, pɔ adɛ kɔ ɛlɛ dzo sɛ tɛ lɛ ɖɔ kaɖɔ, alasɛ lɛ nyi anɔ nɛ gɛ enu.
Yesu Eklukpaya Nɛ Okpukpukɔ Nɛ kɛvlɔ nɛ pinii, gɛ kanɔ mɛ eke bhui, Yesu alɔ nɛ bupa nɛ mɛ avɛ okpukpukɔ toli ɔkɛlɛ ede klukpaya.
Klɛ Simɔnɛ anɛ yɛadzyalɛ na daa pɛɛ yɛ, klɛ gɛ ba mɔ yɛ ba kpɛ ogugu aɖɔ asɛ, “Anɔnyanɔ edzi apɛ wɔ!” Yesu etsre alɛ sɛ, “Nɔ kɔ lɔ vɛ ɔkɔ toli tsyɛ, nɛ ɛma bhlibhli nɛ mɛ gɛ tsobunɔ lɔ, sɛ tɛ ɛda ɖɔ Kpayɛbui nɛ ɛkɛlɛ tsyɛ.
Kɛlɛ so pɛ ɛba.” So anyɔ Galelia petee, aɖɔ Kpayabui nɛ oxogokɔevu nɛ mɛ klɛ akɛka ɛfufɔɛkpã.
Yesu Ebeke Anyɛ Teli Bunyadzɛdzã Anyɛ bunyadzɛdzã elete teli aba za ekuisia bha akɔ Yesu, klɛ akɔ yɛ kɛtɔkpu asɛ, “kɛɛ ba dzi wɔ tɛ pɛpɛɛ tɛ oxule bunya nɛ mɛ shu.” Nɛ eshutukubui didi mɛ, Yesu ebu yɛ ɔhwɛ nɛ ehunɔ anyɛ.
“Klɛ aɖɔ asɛ ɛpɛɛ, ” “Wɔ shu bhui!” Ko klɛ anyɛ nɛ bunya dzɛdzã nɛ shɛ kɛshɛ tili.
Yesu akɛka anyɛ nɛ asɛsɛ nɛ ɔshã kpɛkpɛ yɛ gɛganɛɛ asɛ, “Di lɛ ɔkɔ sɛ odi tsre anɔnyanɔ sɛ kana mɛ ibeke wɔ nya.
Pɔ vɛ, yɛ kɔ wɔ shu nɛ ɔdɔ kasɛ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ tɛ ɔdɔ buya kɛdɔnɔ nɛ gɛ lɛ sɛ tɛ ɔbuya anasɛ gɛ Mose ɔshã nɛ ɔɖɔ kɔ wɔ ishu bhuibhui, sɛ tɛ kidzi kibuimɔɖɔ kɔa lɛ.” Nɛ kɛlɛ maza lɛ mɛ ekoeyi avɛ ada ɖɔɛ bui nɛ akana wee.
Nɛ kɛlɛ mɛ, Yesu ada da na ɔma mɛ tsoku awɔɛ̃, pɔ ekoeyi ada za ɛzakɔ gɛ anɔ ama.
Tsyɛ banɔ be de ɔkɔnyɔkɔ atɔnɔ yɛ aba.
Yesu Ebeke Anɔ Gɛ Awɔesukpa Bunya Ewui bhli telie de, gɛ Yesu eze be ku Kapenaumɛ, banɔ nɛ nu yɛ dɔ sɛ aba kepi.
So, banɔ gelee be xogo nɛ yɛ ɔbha, ɔzakɔ ɔdɔ za, ɔyɛkɔ obo yinɔ kedunu nɛ ɔtɔ nɛ petee, klɛ aɖɔ Kpayabui nɛ etsre alɛ.
Banyɛ tɛalɛ̃ teli be tuku anyɛ gɛ awɔesukpa ebe lu kɔ yɛ.
Banɔ nɛ be kpe so ba dɛ na Yesu nanɔ, so be de wu buvu klɛ be de pu ovutɔ klɛ be zhinɔ anyɛnya anɛ oputso nɛ akpɛ Yesu abha.
Amɔ balɛ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa, so aɖɔ etsre anyɛnya nɛ asɛ, “Meyi ba yɛkɔ wɔ buzizi nɛ etsye wɔ.” Kibe lɛlɛ nɛ mɛ, ɛshãdɔkasɛ teli baza kesi nɛ ɔklɛ, ba zaa nyɔ kibui nɛ mɛ edi nɛ ɔhaglɔ asɛ, “Kide so pɛ anyɛa nɛ aaɖɔ kaɖɔa nɛɛ di?
Aaɖɔ ebusobui!
Anee gɛ aba na buzizi ayɛkɔ etsye, gɛ odu nu sɛ Kpaya?” Yesu eti tsiɔ̃ nɛ yɛ ɔfufɔɛ mɛ asɛ kana banɔ nɛ baa ɖɔ nɛ balɛ idzyi mɛ, klɛ etsre alɛ asɛ, “Kide so pɛ no di ebuia nɛ ana?
Kiɖue gɛ lɛ bɔbɔɛbɔɛ dɛ sɛ, tɛ be tsre anɔ gɛ awɔesukpa nɛ asɛ, ‘Ba yɛkɔ wɔ ebuizizi nɛ etsye wɔ,’ anɛ, ‘Lɔ, yɛkɔ wɔ oputso tɛ ɔga?’ Pɔ kɛ lɛ sɛ tɛ no ti sɛ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛɛ kabhaŋɛŋa kalɛ yɛ ahwɛ nɛ kesukpa nɛa bha sɛ tɛ ayɛkɔ buzizi etsye.” Aɖɔ etsre anɔ nɛ gɛ awɔesukpa nɛ asɛ, “Itsre wɔ, vu ɔlɔ, yɛkɔ wɔ oputso tɛ ɔvɛ bupa mɛ.” Evu alɔ, ayɛkɔ yɛ oputso klɛ aga ekoeyi ashɛ nɛ banɔ petee amɛ.
Yesu bui nɛ gɛ abhɛtɛ nɛ yinɔ anɔnyanɔ klɛ banɔnyanɔ nɛ ɔkɛlɛ ba kpɛ Kpaya nɛa bha.
Klɛ baa ɖɔ asɛ, “Bu ka mɔ kibui nɛ di dí!” Yesu Eklu Lewi Yesu aza ba vɛ kɛvɔ nɛ tɔ.
Banɔ gelee aza ba ebe xogo nɛ yɛ ɔbha, klɛ akpa balɛ kɛdɔ kasɛ.
Gɛ aga afla, amɔ Alfeusɛ yɛeyi Lewi gɛ ezhidzi adɔdzyɔ kɛkpako nɛ shu.
Yesu etsre yɛ asɛ, “Za mɛe de,” klɛ Lewi alɔ tɔnɔ yɛ.
Nɛ Lewi bupa nɛ mɛ, Yesu aaŋa owulagoe dɔ, badɔdzyɔ gelee anɛ “bezizi ” ba zaa ŋaɛ dɔ nɛ yɛ anɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ, alasɛ banɔ gelee ba za yɛe de.
Gɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ nɛ gɛ be nu Farisianɛ na mɔ Yesu gɛ aaŋa kɛdɔ nɛ badɔdzyɔ anɛ “banɔzizi ” nɛɛ, be bisi yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ, “Kidee so pɛɛ aŋaɛ dɔ nɛ badɔdzyɔ anɛ ‘banɔzizi’?” Gɛ Yesu enu balɛ ebui nɛ gɛ bee bisi, ebu etsre alɛ asɛ, “Bagɛ ba taa nya na ma kɔ awani, banyɛnya balɛ alɛ kɔ awani.
Bagɛ ba bhɛtɛ buzizi nɛ so pɛ ɛba, ganɛ bagɛ bana.” Be Bisi Yesu Ebui Denɔ Onugbunyɛnya Shu Yohanɛsɛ badɔkpasɛ anɛ Farisianɛ naa nya onugbu.
Banɔ teli ba ba ebe bisi Yesu asɛ, “Kɛde so pɛɛ Yohanɛsɛ badɔkpasɛ anɛ Farisianɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ baa nya onugbu pɛɛ wayɛalɛ xũ na taa nya?” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Kɛlɛ adzɛenyine yɛ befu aba za nya onugbu nɛ kibe lɛ gɛ adzɛnyine nɛ alɛ balɛ ɔbha?
Kɛ tɛ baa za kɛlɛ mɛ kɔa lɛ ana, nɛ kibe lɛ gɛ adzɛenyine nɛ alɛ balɛ ɔbha.
Pɔ kibe tili ba ba gɛ la ba gbanɔ adzɛnyine nɛ ashɛ̃nɔ nɛ balɛ ɔbha klɛ flogo pɛɛ onugbu nyɛnya ɔbɔ za.
“Anɔnyanɔ atɛ yɛkɔ kɛpɔtɛvuvɔ akamɛ atsa nɛ kɛkuku.
Onu gɛ abhɛtɛ ana, kɛpɔtɛvuvɔ nɛ ba nunɔ kɛkuku klɛ kɛba tsyuɛ̃ dɛa na.
Klɛ anɔnyanɔ atɛ yɛkɔ buluvuvɔ abalɛ akpɛ kepulikuku mɛ.
Onu gɛ abhɛtɛ ana kepulikuku nɛ ka ba yɛɛ, klɛ bulu anɛ kepuli nɛ petee be zi.
Buluvuvɔ nɛɛ kepuli vuvɔ mɛ bu ba za.” Apalete Kɔ Kimuenewi Nɛ kimuenewi tilia bha, Yesu aafla nɛ nikpe buya tuli mɛ klɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ be dzyini nikpe nɛ buya nɛ mɛ.
Farisianɛ ne tsre Yesu asɛ, “Di, kidee ɔshã dɛda ebui wɔ badɔkpasɛ nɛ baa bhɛtɛ ana nɛ kimuenewi nɛa bha?” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Nɔ kɔ kla onu di kɛgɛ Daviti abhɛtɛ nɛ kibe lɛ gɛ baza pɛɛ bubhɛ buu yi yɛ nɛ yeshopoa lɛ?
Nɛ Abiata kpayaɔzakɔanɔ gbla nɛ kibe, Daviti etsoku Kpayavu nɛ mɛ ada tã gbɛgbɛvu gɛ be tsyina ahwɛ nɛ lɛ shu, gɛ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ nɛ ko ɔshã kɔɛ dzo sɛ ba tã.
Klɛ akɔ yɛeshopoa lɛ nɛ tsyɛ teli la tã.” Ɔkɛlɛ Yesu etsre alɛ asɛ, “Kimuenewi anɔ ba bhɛtɛ lɛ akɔ, ganɛ anɔ ba bhɛtɛ akɔ Kimuenewi.
So nɛɛ, Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ enu Apalete kɔ Kimuenewi nɛ kruatsyɛ.”
Anyɛ Ɔhwɛsisiku Bunya Tɛbibeke Nɛ kibe bhlatɔ mɛ Yesu aza ba vɛ oxogokɔvu nɛm, klɛ anyɛ teli nɛ ɔhwɛsisiku aza ɔklɛ.
Banɔ teli nɛ ɔkɛlɛ naa pɛ sɛ tɛ be bu buzizi akɔ Yesu so, be vu awɔ̃hũ nɛ yɛ, sɛ tɛ ba mɔ sɛ nɛ, pɔ ebe beke anyɛ nɛ ɔhwɛsisiku bɔnya nɛ Kimuenewi nɛa bha.
Yesu etsre anyɛ ɔhwɛsisiku nɛ asɛ, “Lɔ kititi nɛ anɔnyanɔ amɛ.” Ɔkɛlɛ Yesu ebisi balɛ asɛ, “Kiduwe gɛ lɛ ɔshã mɛ nɛ Kimuenewi nɛa bha: tɛ ɔbhɛtɛ kɛdzyɔgo pɛnɔɔ abhɛtɛ kizizi, tɛ belu ɛkpã pɛnɔɔ be yi anɔ?” Pɔ ba dɔ sɛɛ̃.
Yesu edi banɔ na kana nɛ obulo klɛ, same edi ku yɛ nɛ balɛ idzyim gɛganɛ nɛ shu, so etsre ɔhwɛsisiku anɔ nɛ asɛ, “Bu wɔ ɔhwɛ nɛ oyinɔ, ” Ebu ɔlɛ eyinɔ, klɛ yɛ ɔhwɛ nɛ lo tsodzi okoeyi ɔba.
Klɛ so, Farisianɛ ba shɛ avɛ ada bhɛtɛ terikpo nɛ Heroɖesɛanɛ akɔ Yesu tiyiyi.
Banɔɛza Batɔnɔ Yesu Yesu anɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ ba shɛ avɛ kɛvɔ nɛ shu, klɛ banɔɛza gbla lɔ de Galelia ba za yɛede.
Gɛ be nu yɛ ebui nɛ gɛ alɛ aabhɛtɛ nɛ, banɔ gelee balɔ ede Yuɖia, Yerusalɛm, Idumea, anɛ Yɔdan kibe, ɔyɛkɔ kana Tire anɛ Sidon kɛdɔ nɛ mɛ petee atɔnɔ yɛ aba.
Banɔɛza nɛ so, etsre yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ ba pɛ keniabha opupu bhli toli akɔ yɛ gɛ ebe ti tsoku ɔlɛ mɛ sɛ tɛ banɔ nɛ beti fuekumu yɛ.
Alasɛ eti beke banɔ gelee banya, klɛso bagɛ bakaa nya nee tieku otugba sɛ tɛ be hunɔ yɛ.
Onu gɛ ɛfufɔɛkpã nɛ mɔ yɛ ko lɛ wɔlɛ dɔ nɛ yɛ otugba nɛ igugu kpɛkpɛ sɛ, “Wo nu Kpaya Yeyi.” Pɔ akpɛ ɔshã gɛganɛɛ akɔ ɛfufɔɛkpã nɛ asɛ lɛ tɛ ɖɔ anɔ nɛ di gɛ enu.
Yesu Banɔkpɛkpɛ Lɔfɔntɛabha Nɛ Tɛkukulu Yesu avɛ butu tulia bha klɛ ede klu banɔ nɛ gɛ apɛɛ, klɛ la ba yɛ ɔbha.
Yesu ebu banɔ lɔfɔntɛabha, klɛ edzua lɛ kinyi asɛ Banɔkpɛkpɛ, sɛ tɛ ba za plɛnɔ yɛ tɛ aba kpaa lɛ tɛ bada ɖɔ Kpayɛbui tɛ ba mɔ kabhaŋɛŋa akɔ ɛfufɔɛkpã tɛkɛkɛka.
Banɔ lɔfɔntɛabha nɛ gɛ ekulu nɛ naa: Simɔnɛ (gɛ akɔ kinyi asɛ Petro); Yakobo Zebeɖi yɛeyi anɛ yɛadzya Yohanɛsɛ, (balɛ eklu asɛ Boanerges, gɛ kɛlɛ kesi enu asɛ Subhalɛlɛeyi); Andrɛasɛ, Filipo, Batolomeo, Mateo, Tomasɛ, Yakobo Alfeusɛ yɛeyi, Tadeosɛ anɛ Simɔnɛ Zealɔtɛ ɔha mɛeyi, ɔha nɛ gɛ ɔɔwlɔãkɛ kɔ ishuahwɛ zɛza, anɛ Yuɖas Iskarɔtɛ anɔ nɛ gɛ aba kpɛ yɛ ahwɛ.
Yesu Anɛ Ɛfufɔɛkpã Ekusi Yesu ezɛ de tsoku bupa tuli mɛ gɛ banɔɛza bebe fuekumu alɛ gɛ kɛkɔ sɛ Yesu anɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ ba dɛ mɔ kidzo ada ŋa kɛdɔ tsyɛ.
Gɛ yɛletealɛ nɛ nu kana nɛɛ ba vɛ sɛ tɛ be de di yɛ ɔkɔ, alasɛ baa ɖɔ asɛ, “Ama mɔmɔ.” Klɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ nɛ gɛ be zhi de Yerusalɛm aba naa ɖɔ asɛ, “Bɛlzebul gɛ enu Ɛfufɔɛkpãekusi ɔlɛ otsri yɛa bha.
Ganɔ ɛfufɔɛkpã ekusieyi nɛ kabha yɛ aakɛka ɛfufɔɛkpã.” Klɛ so Yesu eklu balɛ klɛ etsre alɛ nɛ akpalɛ mɛ asɛ, “Kɛlɛ Satana aba kɛka Satana?
Onugɛ bukusi ɔzakɔ tuli ma kpɛ bupɛ tɔbha mɛ, bukusi ɔŋakɔ ɔlɛlɛ nɛ ɔtɛbɔ naa za.
Onu gɛ bupa tuli bu pɔ nɛ aglɔ shu, bupa lɛlɛ nɛ tɛ ba naa za.
Klɛ onu gɛ Satana alɔ kɛtiti nɛ yɛ nahwɛ shu pɛ apɔ, atɛ ba naa za, akasɛ asɛ yɛ kibeke na.
Kɛgbɛagba, anɔnyanɔ atɛ ba na anɔ gɛganɛ bupa mɛ etsoku ede zru, gɛ odunu sɛ evu anɔ gɛganɛ nɛ anya elu.
Klɛ ko aba naa zuru nɛ bupa nɛ mɛ.
Kɛgbɛagba mɛ tsre nɔ, ebuizizi anɛ ebusobui nɛ petee gɛ banɔ abhɛtɛ nɛɛ ba ba yɛkɔ etsye alɛ.
Pɔ aanɔ nɛ gɛ abhɛtɛ buzizi nɛ Ɔfufɔɛ Dzyɔgo nɛ shu nɛɛ ba tɛ ba yɛkɔ etsye yɛ, aŋa buzizi gɛ tɛ ba beke pɔ.” Yesu aɖɔ kibui nɛ, alasɛ baa ɖɔ asɛ “Ɔfufɔɛkpã ɔlɛ otsri yɛa bha.” Yesu Yɛeni Anɛ Yɛadzyalɛ Ɔkɛlɛ Yesu yɛeni anɛ yɛadzyalɛ nɛ be ku.
Be li kititi nɛ ɔtɔɔ, klɛ ba kpɛ anɔ asɛ eklu yɛ akɔ balɛ.
Banɔɛza ba za kana yɛ atsya, klɛ be tsre yɛ asɛ, “Wɔeni anɛ wɔadzyalɛ be li ɔtɔ naa pɛɛ wɔ.” Yesu ebisi asɛ, “bane gɛ enu mɛeni anɛ mɛadzyalɛ?” Klɛ edi banɔ nɛ gɛ bedzi akana yɛ klɛ ehunu asɛ, “Meni nɛ madzyalɛ naa!
Anɔnyanɔ gɛ aabhɛtɛ Kpaya tɛpɛpɛɛ nɛɛ yɛ enu mɛadzya anɛ mɛada anɛ meni.”
Kɛkpalɛ Nɛ Adɔhwɛ Shu Yesu aza ba vɛ yɛ kɛdɔkɛkasɛ nɛa bha nɛ Galelia kɛvɔ nu tɔ.
Banɔɛza nɛ gɛ za ɔkɛlɛ nɛ bekpe kudzɔ.
Kɛkɔsɛ etsoku keniabha opupu nɛ mɛ, nɛ kibe lɛ gɛ banɔɛza na wɔ keni nɛ tɔ.
Akasɛ banɔ nɛ kɛdɔ gelee ganɔ akpalɛ mɛ, klɛ nɛ yɛ kɛdɔ kɛkasɛ nɛ mɛ aɖɔ asɛ, “Nɔ tatɔ mɔ!
Ayadɛ teli avɛ kɛdɔ ɔhwɛ kɔ.
Gɛ ahwɛ kɛdɔ nɛɛ, eyi teli awɔlɛ adɔ kɛdzo nɛ mɛ, klɛ buzhuɔɛ ba tɔkɛ alɛ amunɔ.
Eteli adɔ aklagbua bha, gɛ tisi gelee dɛ za ɔklɛ.
Eyi ne yi zia alasɛ tisi dɛ do nɛ ɔklɛ kɔ alɛ.
Pɔ gɛ buwui ba tã eyi nɛ aba tãyɛ̃, alasɛ igu nɛ dɛ vɛ tisi mɛ.
Abhlatɔ tsyɛ awɔlɛ adɔ ewi mɛ, klɛ ewi nɛ ebe she ada alɛ, so le di yu.
Pɔ tsyɛ eteli adɔ kesukpa dzyɔgo abha.
Alɛ xũ nɛɛ ebe she, le yu gelee; laya nɛ tɛkpikpe afata, afɛtehlo ɔyɛkɔ vɛnɔ kɛfɔɛfɔ mɛ.” Ɔkɛlɛ Yesu asɛ, “Anɔ nɛ gɛ butɔ lɛ yɛ pɛ ebe nu, tɛ enu.” Kɛdɔnɔ Nɛ Gɛ Akpalɛ Nɛ Alɛ Kɔ Gɛ Yesu tite agɔ, yɛ banɔkpɛkpɛ anɛ banɔ gɔgɔɛ nɛ be bisi yɛ ebui denɔ akpalɛ nɛ shu.
Etsre alɛ asɛ, “Ebuikpukpu nɛ gɛ alɛ Kpaya bukusi nɛ mɛ, ba tɛ yɛkɔ akɔ wɔnɔ.
Pɔ banɔ nɛ gɛ ba ma wɔnɔɛshi xũ nɛ kibuinyɛbui ga akpalɛ mɛ kɔ alɛ sɛ tɛ, “ ‘ba za mɔ pɔ batɛ ba mɔ klɛ mɛ, klɛ le be ze nu pɔ be ti be nu klɛesi, odinu sɛ bee be tsyina klɛ la ba yɛkɔ etsyea lɛ!’ ” Yesu Ebu Adɔhwɛ Kɛkpalɛ Nɛesi Klɛ Yesu ehunu etsre alɛ asɛ, “Nɔ di nu kɛkpalɛɛ nɛe si?
Klɛ nɔ bɔ bhɛtɛ pɛ nɔ bo nu kɛkpalɛ tili kesi?
Ayadɛ nɛɛ, Kpayɛbui nɛa hwɛ.
Banɔ teli ba sɔnɔ eyi nɛ gɛ adɔ kɛdzyo nɛ mɛ, nɛ ɔklɛ gɛ ba hwɛ Kpaya bui.
Balɛ gɛ benye nu kibui nɛ ko, Satana aba nyɛna kibui nɛ gɛ ba ɖa nɛ akpɛ ebu nɛ balɛ mɛ.
Babhlatɔ, gɛ dzi ansɛ eyi gɛ ba hwɛ atrɔ ɔklɛ gɛ aklagbu alɛ, be nu kibui, klɛ la gbla yɛkɛɛ lɛ nɛ same.
Pɔ gɛ igu dɛ za alɛ so la dɛ za nɛ ɛkpã dzidze.
Kibe lɛ gɛ butɔ ɔdɔgɔsɛ tɛkpɛkpatɔnɔ ba nɛ kibui nɛ shu ko ba wɔlɛ kplitaa.
Kana ke babhlatɔ tsyɛ teli ba sɔnɔ eyi nɛ gɛ awɔlɛ ku ewi nɛ mɛ, be nu kibui; pɔ kanɔa nɛ mɛ butɔ, ehoeyi anɔ wɛwɛɛ, nɛ kɛnɔmɛdɔ tɛpɛpɛ she da kibui nɛ balɛ mɛ, gɛ kɛ kɔ sɛ kibui nɛ dɛ yu.
Ba ga sɔnɔ eyi nɛ gɛ adɔ kesukpa dzyɔgo nɛa bha, balɛ benu Kpayɛbui klɛ bayɛkɛ kɛlɛ klɛ kɛ yu gelee nɛ, afata, afɛtehlo, ɔyɛkɔ nanɔ kɛfɔɛfɔ nɛ balɛ mɛ ansɛ kana gɛ bahwɛ alɛ.” Kanɛgbɛ Gɛ Etsri Osiabha Yesu ebisi asɛ, “Be deke kanɛgbɛ ayɛkɔ akpɛ ketsukpuesi ɔdɔgɔ sɛ ba yɛkɔ akpɛ apa kesi dza?
Anɛ yɛ osia bha ɔbɔ yɛkɔ ɔtrɔ?
Alasɛ kɛdɔ nyɛdɔ gɛ be kpu nɛɛ kɛ nu kɛdɔ gɛ le be bu eyinɔ, klɛ kɛkanyaka gɛ la ba da klɛ kɛdɔ nɛ kinu kɛdɔ gɛ la ba danɛ kɛdɔ nɛ klɛa bha lu ɔtɔ.
Onu anɔ nɛ gɛ batɔ alɛ yɛ pɛ ebe nu tɛ enu.” Avɛ kɛlɛa bha sɛ, “Lu awɔ̃ nɛ kibui nɛ gɛ oonu nɛ mɔɔ mɔ.” “Kedzyidzyi nɔ gɛ kalɛ shui kɛxwɛ wɔ ɔwa nɛ, kalɛ la ba yɛ kɔ edzyidzyi akɔ wɔ nɔ, klɛ kɛ ba dɛa na.
Aanɔ gɛ kɛdɔ lɛ yɛahwɛ ba ba kɔ yɛ kɛdɔ gelee, agɛ yɛahwɛ kɛma, kɛbhliyi nɔ nɛ gɛ kɛlɛ yɛahwɛ nɛ tsyɛ baa yɛkɛ kɛlɛ nɛ yɛahwɛ.” Kɛkpalɛ Nɛ Kiyi Gɛ She Shu Aza ɖɔ asɛ, “Kana Kpaya bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ odzi.
Anyɛ teli ahwɛ eyi elu kesukpa.
Elishi anɛ kemuze, adɔ tra o alɛ nɛ awɔ̃ o, kiyi nɛ kii yi klɛ kii she, pɔ etinyi kana gɛ kɛɛ bhɛtɛ pɛ kii she.
Kesukpa nɛ kalɛ ishuahwɛ, ka kɔ sɛ kɛdɔ nɛ kiyu.
Putɔnɔ eyuyu nɛ onugbu vuvɔ nɛ obo koeyi nɛ osi nɛ shu, ka kɛklɔ anɛ eyi nɛ gɛ akpasɛ lɛ mɛ nɛ ebe koeyi, flogo pɛ eyuyu nɛ ebe ti she nɛ eyi nɛ mɔɔmɔ.
Kibee lɛ nɛ gɛ kɛdɔyi nɛ she pɛ kɛ kpã ko, ba yɛkɔ kɛpamɛ ko ba da kpa yɛ ayalɛ, alasɛ kɛlɛ kpa be na.” Kɛkpalɛ Nɛ Ɔyurɔpɔɛeyi Shu Yesu ekee hunu asɛ, “Kɛdee lɔ ba ɖɔ sɛ kɛlɛ Kpayakusiɔŋakɔ nɛ odzi ansɛ, klɛ kɛkpalɛ ɖueɖu lɔ ba yɛkɔ shrɔ ɔkɛlɛ?
Kpayakusiɔŋakɔ nɛ odzi anasɛ ɔyurɔpɔɛeyi gɛ baa hwɛ nɛ kesukpa.
Flogo pɛ eeshe edzi osi nɛ ɛshɛgbla dɛ nɛ buka nɛ mɛ, gɛ buzhuɔɛ bu baa dɔ nɛ ɔlɛ mɛ.” Akpalɛa nɛ nɛdi Yesu ayɛkɔ akasɛ Kpaya kibui nɛ nɔ etsre banɔ, nɛ kana gɛ la ba na kibui nɛ kɛlɛe si nu.
Yesu adɛ tsre yɛ banɔ nɛ kibuinyɛbui gɛ adɛ kpɛɛ lɛ kɛkpalɛ.
Pɔ onu gɛ yɛ nɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ tite bee li, adanɛ kibuinyɛbui mɛ petee akɔ balɛ.
Yesu Ayɔ Kɛlɛgɛganɛ Nu Kiwi lɛlɛ nɛ gɛ owulago nɛ ɔna, etsre yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ, “Nɔ kɔ lɔ tsɔkɛ vɛ ogbigbe bhla nɛa bha.” Gɛ ba shɛ̃ alɔ banɔɛza nɛ elu kide, ba gbanɔ yɛ ashɛ̃nɔ ansɛ gɛ aza opupu nɛ mɛ nɛ balɛ.
Keniabha ipupu bhlatɔ tili tsyɛ za plɛnɔ yɛ.
Keniabhalɛ gɛganɛɛ ba kpaa fu, gɛ kɛ kɔsɛ buni nɛ yalɛku opupu nɛ mɛ klɛ buni nɛɛ sɛsɛ vu balɛ.
Kɛbee lɛ nɛ mɛ nɛ, Yesu ada vɛnɔ tra nɛ sumuia bha nɛ opupu nɛ kedeapɛ nɛ mɛ.
Badɔkpasɛ na da nyɛmɛ yɛ klɛ bee tsre asɛ, “Adɔkasɛ, ɔdɛ yɛkɔ nɛ kɛlɛ mɛ onu gɛ keni nɛ kee vu lɔ nɛ dza?” Evua lɔ, akpɛ ozi nɛ kɛlɛɛ nia bha sɛ, “Kɔlenu!
Dɔ sɛɛ̃!” Klɛ kɛlɛɛ nɛ yulɔ fu, klɛ ɔklɛ ɔdɔ sɛɛ̃.
Etsre yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ, “Kidee so pɛ no si kifu kana?
So tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa ka za wɔnɔ ahwɛ nɛ ɔtsɔ̃ nɛɛ dza?” Kifu kua lɛ tsutsɔmɔ tsɔmɔ klɛ bee bisi aglɔ asɛ, “Anee di naa?
Gɛ kɛlɛɛ nɛ bunigiglebe tsyɛ ta yɛa tɔ!”
Ɛfufɔɛkpã Tɛkɛkɛka Bu Nɛ Anyɛ Teli Mɛ Batsɔkɛ kɛvɔ nɛ ede ku Gɛrasɛnisɛ kesi mɛ.
Gɛ Yesu ekoeyi nɛ keniabha opupu nɛ mɛ ko, ɛfufɔɛkpã anɔ teli ekoeyi denɔ idzre nɛ shi aba tsyanɛ yɛ.
Anyɛ anɛ aza idzre nɛ mɛ klɛ anɔnyanɔ atɛ kaa na yɛ nya, onu buɖɛ wɔ yɛkɔ tsyɛ.
Alasɛ nɛ ebea nɛ mɛɛ, baa ganɛ yɛ ɛtsrɛ nɛ ɛhwɛ anya, pɔ apɔ buɖɛ klɛ edzyini ɛɖa nɛ yɛ butsrukpɔ.
Anɔnyanɔ adɛ gɛganɛ gɛ aba ŋa yɛa bha.
Elishi anɛ kemuze akpasɛ idzre nɛ shi, nɛ betushɛ nɛ mɛ, ebhui ishu nɛ aklagbu klɛ akpɛ igugu.
Gɛɛ amɔ Yesu asɛsɛ akpanɛsi klɛ ede dzu ekuisiesi nɛ yɛ etem.
Akpɛ ogugu gɛganɛɛ asɛ, “Yesu, Apaletedɛ nɛ yɛ Eyi, kɛdee wɔ pɛɛ denɔ mɛ ɔkɔ?
Tanɛ Kpaya sɛ ɔtɛ bɔ bhɛtɛ mɛ kibui kpã!” Alasɛ Yesu eti tsre yɛ asɛ, “Koeyi ɔbɔ fla, wɔ ɔfufɔɛkpã nɛ anyɛ anɛ mɛ!” Klɛ Yesu ebisi yɛ asɛ, “Kidee gɛ nu wɔ kinyi?” Ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Mɛ kinyi klɛ nu Ovulo, ” “alasɛ bu kpe.” Klɛ akɔ kɛtɔkpu etsodzini akɔ asɛ, Yesu atɛ kɛka balɛ ebu nɛ ɔkɛlɛ kɛma nɛ mɛ.
Bahɛ kɛhagbla tili zɛɛ ŋa kɛdɔ nɛ betu nɛ shu nɛ ɔkɛlɛ.
Ɛfufɔɛkpã nɛ kɔ kɛtɔkpu Yesu sɛ, “Kɛka lɔ ɔdɔ kpɛ bahɛ nɛ mɛ, kɔ bulɔ kidzo sɛ tɛ butsoku balɛ mɛ.
” Yesu akɔ ɛfufɔɛkpã nɛ dzo klɛ lɛ koeyi da tsoku bahɛ nɛ mɛ, gɛ lɛ koeyi nɛ anyɛ nɛ mɛ.
Bahɛha nɛ ba na ansɛ akpã tabha gɛ la kpanɛ si ada dɔku kɛvɔ nɛ mɛ, klɛ la dɔe ni.
Bagɛ balɛ agbanɔ bahɛha nɛ be si avɛ ɔma nɛ mɛ nɛ ɛbha, ada ɖɔ kɛgɛ vɛa bha nɛ ɔklɛ, klɛ banɔ be si avɛ sɛ tɛ be de di kɛdɔnɔ nɛ gɛ kɛlɛ bɛ lɛ mɛ.
Gɛ banɔ nɛ be ku Yesu ɔbha nɛɛ, ba mɔ anyɛ gɛ yɛa bha ɛfufɔɛkpã ovulo nɛ otsri gɛ ezhidzi ɔkɛlɛ nɛ bawi dzyɔgo mɛ nɛ kibui titi mɛ, kifu ku ba ga mɔ anyɛ nɛ ana.
Bagɛ ba mɔɛ lɛ nɛ aɖɔ kɛgɛ ba ɛfufɔɛkpã anyɛ nɛa bha nɛ etsre banɔ—klɛ ba ɖɔaɖɔ edenɔ bahɛ nɛ tsyɛ shu.
Ɔkɛlɛ banɔ nɛ ba kpa kɛtɔkpuesi kpɛ kɔ Yesu asɛ ashɛ̃ nɛ balɛ kɛma nɛ mɛ.
Gɛ Yesu eetsoku keniabha opupu nɛ mɛ, anyɛ nɛ gɛ ɛfufɔɛkpã nɛ za yɛa bha nɛ tsyɛ asɛ aba tɔnɔ yɛ.
Yesu adɛ kɔ yɛ kidzo, pɔ etsre yɛ asɛ, “Vɛ bupa mɛ tɛ ɔdɔ tsre wɔ beshopo, kana gɛ Apalete nɛ edi wɔ eshutukubui, nɛ kɛdɔnɔ nɛ gɛ abhɛtɛ akɔ wɔ.” So anyɛ nɛ ashɛ̃ avɛ Dekapoli, gɛ enu emagbla lɔfɔ nɛ mɛ, klɛ ada ɖɔ kana gɛ Yesu ayɛkɛ akɔ yɛ.
Klɛ kibui nɛ bhɛtɛ banɔ nɛ petee kibi.
Adzɛnuvɔɛ Tsitsi Nɛ Adzɛ Nyɛnya Teli Gɛ Yesu eze ku opupu nɛ avɛ keni nɛ kapɛ bhla nɛ, banɔ gelee ba za ba kana yɛ atsya nɛ kɛvɔ nu tɔ.
Ɔkɛlɛ anɔgbla teli gɛ eedi oxogokɔ nɛa bha gɛ bee klu asɛ Yairusɛ, nɛ aba ɔkɛlɛ.
Gɛ amɔ Yesu, ezhiadɔ nɛ yɛ otugba klɛ abhɛtɛ tɛbibisi edenɔ yɛ ɔkɔ asɛ, “Mɛeyi adzɛnuvɔɛ bhli nɛ eetsi.
So ɛkɔwɔ kɛtɔkpu, bɔ trɔ ahwɛ nɛ yɛa bha tɛ alɔ tɛ aza nɛ ɛkpã.” So Yesu atɔ nɔ anyɛ nɛ avɛ.
Banɔɛza nɛ zɛ tɔnɔ yɛ, klɛ ba kana yɛ atsya.
Adzɛ teli tsyɛ aza ɔklɛ gɛ dzyosuyiyi bunya za yɛ shu agɔ lɔfɔntabha nyɔɔ.
Atɛ mɔ butɔ nɛ bawani gelee ahwɛmɛ, klɛ yɛ ehoei petee ebeke, tsyɛ buzi ko ekee zi adɛa na akɔ yɛ.
Gɛ enu Yesu kɛdɔ nɛ, yɛ tsyɛ aba klɛ ebeli yɛ kede nɛ kɛma nɛ shu klɛ akpɛ ɔhwɛ ehunɔ Yesu awi dzidze, alasɛ ayɛkɛ aŋa sɛ, “Onu gɛ ihunɔ yɛ awi nɛ ko bunya nɛ ba beke.” Ɔkɛlɛ nɛ ko dzyosuyiyi na dzrɔ klɛ eti nɛ yɛ ishu mɛ asɛ yɛ bunya nɛ beke.
Yesu eti tsiɔ̃ sɛ kemi tieli ke koeyi nɛ yɛ mɛ.
Etsyina klɛ ebisi akana sɛ, “Anee gɛ ehunɔ mɛ awi nɛ?” Yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ be bui lɛ bunu etsre yɛ asɛ, “ɔmɔ kana gɛ banɔɛza nɛ ba kana wɔ atsya, flogo pɛ obisi sɛ ‘Anee yɛ ehunɔ mɛ?’ ” Pɔ Yesu aza kɛlɛ kabha apɛɛ anɔ nɛ gɛ ehunɔ yɛ.
Ɔkɛlɛ adzɛ nɛ gɛ enyi kɛdɔnɔ nɛ gɛ ba yɛa bha so nɛɛ, ekoeyi aba klɛ ebe zhiadɔ nɛ yɛ otugba, klɛ eshuku nɛ kifu, klɛ etsre yɛ kɛ gɛ ba nɛ yɛa bha.
Yesu etsre yɛ asɛ, “Adzɛ wɔ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa nɛ tɛ beke wɔ bunya.
Gavɛ nɛ ishu yuyɔ mɛ tɛ ɔmɔ ɔhwɛ denɔ wɔ butɔ nɛ mɛ.” Kibe lɛlɛ nɛ gɛ Yesu aka za yɛa ɖɔɖuɖɔ nɛa bha nɛɛ, banɔ teli be de Yairusɛ gɛ enu anɔ nɛ gɛ edi oxogokɔvu nɛa bha nɛ bupa mɛ aba.
Klɛ la ba ɖɔ asɛ, “Wɔ eyiadzɛnuvɔ nɛ etsi.” “Kidee butɔ ɔkɔ bɔɔ kpɛ Adɔkasɛ nɛ?” Yesu adɛ yɛkɛ banɔ nɛ kibui so, etsre Yairus asɛ, “Tosi kifu, yɛkɛ ɔŋa ko.” Adɛ kɔ anɔnyanɔ atɔnɔ yɛ ɔyɛkɔ dɛ Petro, Yakobo anɛ yɛadzya Yohanɛsɛ.
Gɛ bede ku agɛ edi oxogokɔvu nɛa bha nɛ bupa nɛ mɛ, Yesu amɔ sɛ bugbudu gbudu anɛ iyuyo anɛ igugu kpɛkpɛ gɛganɛɛ za bupa nɛ mɛ.
Etsoku atɔnɔ balɛ klɛ etsrea lɛ asɛ, “Kɛdee klɛ nu bugbudu gbudu nɛ igugu kpɛkpɛɛ nɛ?
Anuvɔ nɛ edi tsi pɔ adɔ tra.” Pɔ ba mɔɛ yɛ.
Gɛ akɛka balɛ petee ebu beke, agbanɔ anuvɔ nɛ yɛaka, yɛeni anɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ gɛ baza plɛnɔ yɛ, klɛ betsoku ɔkɛlɛ gɛ anuvɔ nɛ eli.
Yesu anyɛna anuvɔ nɛ ɔhwɛ klɛ etsre yɛ asɛ, “Talita Koum!” (Kɛlɛesi enu asɛ, “Adzɛnuvɔɛ bhli, itsre wɔ sɛ, vu ɔlɔ!” Nɛ Hela bunuhu mɛ).
Ɔkɛlɛ nɛ ko adzɛnuvɔɛ nɛ evu alɔ klɛ aaga kana (agɔ lɔfɔntabha alɛ aza yɛ ahwɛ).
Kibui nɛ kɛ bhɛtɛ balɛ kibi.
Akpɛ ɔshã gɛganɛɛ sɛ batɛ kɔ anɔnyanɔ eti kibuinyɛbui nɛ kɛnɛ nɛ shu, klɛ etsre balɛ asɛ bakɔ yɛ kɛdɔ tili tɛ aŋa.
Atɔnu Eti Ku Awɔ̃ Nɛ Yɛ Kepi Yesu aba shɛ nɛ ɔkɛlɛ avɛ kepi, yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ tsyɛ ba za yɛe de.
Gɛ Kimuenewi nɛ kɛ na, Yesu ada kpa kɛdɔ kasɛ nɛ oxogokɔvu nɛ mɛ.
Banɔ gelee gɛ be nu yɛ kɛdɔ, kiyinɔ balɛ.
“Fakɔ anɔa nɛ edenɔ ebuia nɛ gɛ aɖɔ?” “Kide gɛ nu kibui nyinyi nɛ, gɛ ba kɔ yɛa na, gɛ kɔ sɛ abhɛtɛ ebui gɛ eyinɔanɔ tsyɛ!
Ganɛ osiafatɛ nɛ naa?
Ganɛ Maria yɛeyi Yakobo, Yosɛfu, Yuɖas anɛ Simɔnɛ balɛ adzya nɛ naa?
Sɛ yɛadalɛ nɛ balɛ ɔkɛ̃ nɛ bulɔ?” Klɛ banɔ na mɔ obulo nɛ yɛ.
Yesu etsre alɛ asɛ, “Anɔ nɛ gɛ amɔ ebui aɖɔ nɛ yɛshopoa lɛ shi nɛ yɛnahwɛ kepi eti ku awɔ̃.” Adɛ bhɛtɛ ebui yiyinɔanɔ kanyaka nɛ ɔkɛlɛ, ɔyɛkɔdɛ banɔ nyɛnya bhli teli kabha ko atrɔ ahwɛ klɛ ebeke balɛ banya.
Kɛbhɛtɛ yɛ kibi sɛ yɛeletealɛ nɛɛ, tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa ma balɛ mɛ.
Yesu Akpɛ Yɛ Banɔ Lɔfɔntɛabha Nɛ Xwɛ Ɔkɛlɛ Yesu anyɔ akana anɛ yɛ kɛdɔkɛkasɛ denɔ ɛmabhli mɛ ɔvɛnɔ ɛmabhli mɛ.
Gɛ eklu yɛ Banɔkpɛkpɛ nɛ amɛna yɛ ɔbha, akpɛ balɛ asɛsɛ tɛabha tɛabha klɛ akɔa lɛ kabhaŋɛŋa sɛ tɛ ba ŋa ɛfufɔɛkpã nɛa bha.
Yɛ ɛshã ɛlɛ dzi sɛ, “Nɔ tɛ yɛkɔ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ kɔ wɔnɔ kidzo gɛga nɛ ɔyɛkɔdɛ ovusi, nɔ tɛ yɛkɔ kɛŋɛŋa, nɔ tɛ yɛkɔ ɔkpɛtɛ nɛ kɔba nɛ ɔdzadi mɛ.
Nɔ kpɛ ɔtsrɛklɔ pɔ nɔ tɛ yɛkɔ awidzidze bhla.
Bupa nɔɔ nɛ mɛ gɛ nɔɔ dɔ ya, nɔ za bulɛ mɛ ɔdɔ nanɔ kibe lɛ gɛ nɔ bɔ shɛ̃ nɛ ɔmaa lɛ nɛ mɛ.
Ɔkɛlɛ gɛ noo ku pɛ baa dɛ yɛkɛ wɔnɔ, klɛ ba dɛ taa nɔ batɔ, no xule osumududu nɛ wɔnɔ butsrukpɔ nɛ olu tɛ nɔ shɛ̃, tɛ kidzi kibuimɔɖɔ nɛ balɛ shu.” Ba vɛ ada kasɛ kɛdɔ sɛ tɛ banɔ nɛ be tsyina kite mɛ.
Ba kɛka ɛfufɔɛkpã, ba balɛ bubɔ nɛ banɔ nyɛnyɛa bha, klɛ be beke balɛ banya.
Be Bhui Yohanɛsɛ Enikpɛ Nɛ Kɛtɔkpu Ekusi Heroɖesɛ ebe nu kibui, alasɛ le be ti Yesu kinyi nɛ mɔmɔ.
Banɔ teli asɛ, “Yohanɛsɛ Enikpɛ nɛ yɛ aza nyɛmɛ edenɔ bekpu mɛ, klɛ so gɛ ebuiyiyinɔ anɔ kemia nɛ di kaa wa kɛxwɛ nɛ yɛ mɛ ana.” Banɔ teli asɛ, “Eliya.” Klɛ banɔ bhlatɔ tsyɛ asɛ, “Enu atɔnu, anasɛ batɔnu nɛ gɛ ba za klibe nɛ teli.” Pɔ gɛ Heroɖesɛ enu ana nɛɛ, asɛ, “Yohanɛsɛ, agɛ yɛ tɔkpu ibhui ba flanɔ, yɛ aza nyɛmɛ edenɔ bekpu mɛ!” Alasɛ Heroɖesɛ nahwɛ atɛ kɔ ɔshã sɛ bevu Yohanɛsɛ, ba nya yɛ tɛ bakɔ ada kpɛ buvu.
Abhɛtɛ kibui nɛ alasɛ Heroɖias, gɛ enu yadzya Filipo yedzini nɛ gɛ ayɛkɛ agbanɔ nɛ so.
Alasɛ Yohanɛsɛ aganɛ aɖɔ etsre Heroɖesɛ asɛ, “Ɔshã ɔdɛ kɔ kidzo sɛ tɛ ɔyɛkɛ wadzya yedzini.” Kibui lɛlɛ nɛ so Heroɖiasɛ evu Yohanɛsɛ akpɛ ɛyam klɛ atrɔ sɛ ebe yi yɛ.
Pɔ adɛ mɔ kidzo nɛ yɛ shu, alasɛ Heroɖesɛ eesi Yohanɛsɛ kifu, so nɛ akpɛ buka akpɛ yɛ, gɛ enyi yɛ asɛ anɔnɛna klɛ yɛshu bhui.
Onu gɛ Heroɖesɛ enu Yohanɛsɛ ebuiɖuɖɔ nɛ eshuku, tsyɛ apɛ asɛ tɛ ezee nu yɛ ebui.
Gugɔɛ nɛɛ, kibe dzyɔgo ba kɔ yɛ.
Nɛ yɛ kɛmɔwi ŋɛŋa nɛa bha atɔ kɛdɔ, eklu yɛ shu banɔ gbɛgbla, yɛ keyutugbani baka nɛ otugba banɔ nɛ Galelia.
Gɛ Heroɖiasɛ yɛ eyiadzɛ nɛ ebe yu kivu nɛ, yɛ kivuyuyu nɛ ku Heroɖesɛ nɛ yɛ be fu nɛ same.
Ekusi nɛ etsre adzɛnuvɔɛ nɛ asɛ, “Bisi kɛdɔnyɛdɔ gɛ ɔpɛɛ tɛ ɛbhɛtɛ kɔ wɔ.” Klɛ aka atabu atrɔ kɛlɛ kabha sɛ, “Kɛdɔnyɛdɔ gɛ obisi mɛ ko eba kɔ wɔɛ lɛ, ɔkɔ nanɔ mɛ bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ kapɛ zɛzɛ.” Klɛ adzɛnuvɔɛ nɛ ekoeyi avɛ yɛeni ɔbha klɛ ede bisi yɛ asɛ, “Kidee mɛ ɛba bisi?” Yɛeni nɛ etsre yɛ asɛ, “Yohanɛsɛ Enikpɛ nɛ yɛ tɔkpu.” Adzɛnuvɔɛ nɛ anawɔ̃ avɛ ada tɔnɔ Ekusi Heroɖesɛ nɛ tɛbibisi nɛ asɛ, “Ɛpɛɛ Yohanɛsɛ Enikpɛ nɛ kɛtɔkpu nɛ kɛtɛa bha ɔtsɔtsiɔ̃.” Tɛbibisi nɛ kɛ trɔ Ekusi nɛa bha piim, pɔ atabu, anɛ yɛ befu nɛ so adɛ pɛa sɛ tɛ atɛ yɛkɛ adzɛnuvɔɛ nɛ tɛbibisi.
Kɛlɛ so akpɛ yɛ atɔkpubhui nɛ teli sɛ ada mɛna Yohanɛsɛ kɛtokpu zia.
Anyɛ na vɛ ede bhui Yohanɛsɛ kɛtɔkpu nɛ buvu nɛ mɛ, klɛ ayɛkɔ atrɔ kɛtɛ kabha amɛna.
Ayɛkɔ kɛlɛ akɔ adzɛnuvɔɛ klɛ yɛ tsyɛ ada yɛkɔ akɔ yɛeni.
Gɛ Yohanɛsɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ nui bui nɛɛ, ba tɔnɔ aba klɛ la ba yɛkɔ yɛ ishuidzya nɛ ede lu odzrem.
Yesu Anyunɔ Banɔ Akpã Teti Banɔkpɛkpɛ nɛ be xogo nɛ Yesu ɔbha klɛ be tsre yɛ ebui nɛ gɛ bada bhɛtɛ nɛ kɛdɔ nɛ gɛ bakasɛ nɛ petee.
Kɛlɛ gɛ banɔ gelee ba vɛ pɛ baa ba balɛ ɔbha nɛ so, ba dɛ mɔ kibe gɛ la ba ŋa kɛdɔ, Yesu etsre balɛ asɛ, “Nɔ tɔnɔ mɛ ɔba wɔnɔnahwɛ tɛ bu vɛ ɔkranakɔ toli tɛ nɔ do muene kɛbɔɛ.” Kɛlɛso, be ku keniabha opupu toli balɛ nahwɛ klɛ ba shɛ avɛ ede ku ɔkranakɔ toli.
Pɔ nɛɛ, banɔ gelee ba mɔ balɛ edzyesi, so bakpanɛ kisi edenɔ ɛma nɛ mɛ petee eputɔ kɔ balɛ ede ku ɔklɛ.
Kibe lɛ nɛ gɛ Yesu ede ku pɛ amɔ banɔɛza nɛ piim, eshutukubui eku yɛ nɛ balɛ, alasɛ baza kɔ yɛ anasɛ ibhoshi gɛ agbɛgbanɔ ama kɔ ɛlɛ.
So etenɔ balɛ kɛdɔ edidedi kasɛ.
Nɛ ɔɖa lɛlɛ nɛ mɛ keli kaa vɛ obelekɔ, so yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ be tsuebunɔ yɛ.
Klɛ baa ɖɔ sɛ, “Ɔkɛŋ nɛ onu okpukpukɔ, ” “klɛ keli eti bele.
Shɛnahwɛ banɔ nɛ shu tɛ bamɔ kɛshɛ vɛ ɛma nɛ gɛ kana balɛ nɛ mɛ, tɛ balɛnahwɛ bada mɔ kɛdɔ tili edzi tɛ ba ŋa.” Pɔ ebu kɛlɛ bunu asɛ, “Wɔnɔ nɔ pɛɛ dɔ tili ɔkɔ balɛ tɛ ba ŋa.” Be tsre yɛ asɛ, “Anɔ wele tɛasuɛ kɛbhɛ ko klɛ ba nyunɔ banɔ kplumua!
Kɛ lɛ sɛ tɛ bɔ vɛ da zi kɔba nɛɛ di nyɔɔ kɔ balɛ kɛŋɛŋa dza?” Ebisi balɛ asɛ, “Gbɛgbɛvu ɛgbaa tɛshɛ ɛlɛ lɛ wɔnɔ ahwɛ?” “Nɔ vɛ tɛ no do di.” Gɛ ba vɛ ede di nɛɛ, ba ɖɔa sɛ, “Titi anɛ kenimɛdzya tɛbha.” Klɛ Yesu etsre badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ ba kɔ anɔnyanɔ ezhi aza kesi nɛ etsu etsu mɛ nɛ tɛwa wuwɔ nɛa bha.
Klɛ so ba za kesi nɛ kɛfɔɛfɔ etsum anɛ afeti etsu mɛ.
Gɛ ayɛkɔ ɛgbaa titi anɛ kenimɛdzya tɛbha, ebu amɛ akpɛ owũsise, ehu ahwɛ klɛ aya ɛlɛ mɛ.
Klɛ ayɛkɔ kpɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ ahwɛ sɛ tɛ ba ya kɔ anɔnyanɔ nɛ ɔkɛlɛ.
Kana dzuku ba ya kenimɛdzya tɛbha nɛ akpɛ balɛ mɛ.
Banɔ nɛ petee ba ŋa klɛ be xui, klɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ be xogo kɛgɛ wɔlɛ li kesukpa klɛ tsyɛ na ashwɛ lɔfɔntabha.
Banɔnyɛ nɛ gɛ ba ŋa kɛdɔ nɛ tɛkɛklamɛ za akpã teti.
Yesu Aga Keniabha Kibe dɛ dze ko Yesu akɔ sɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ be de tsoku kenia bha opupu nɛ mɛ eputɔ kɔ yɛ avɛ Betsaiɖa, flogo pɛ akpɛ banɔɛza gugɔɛ nɛ dzo.
Gɛ Yesu ashɛ̃ nɛ balɛ ɔbha, ewu avɛ butu tulia bha kɔ kpayakuklu.
Gɛ owulago nɛ ɔna, opupu nɔ za keni nɛ kishitɛbha, klɛ Yesu terikpo agɔ nɛ ogbigbe nɛa bha.
Yesu evu awɔ̃hũ asɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ be dzi aza mɔ butɔ nɛ opupu nɛ tigige nɛ keni nɛa bha, alasɛ kɛ lɛɛ nɛ lɔ kititi nɛ tɛvɛvɛ nɛm.
Ansɛ olizatɔ ɛɖa tɛlɛ mɛ ana ekoeyi aaga keni nɛa bha atɔnɔ balɛ aavɛ.
Abhɛtɛ ansɛ aafla balɛ dza, pɔ gɛ ba mɔ yɛ gɛ aaga keni nɛa bha, balɛ kɛtɔkpu nɛ mɛ tsre alɛ asɛ ekpu.
Ba kpɛ ogugu, alasɛ balɛ petee ba mɔ yɛ klɛ besi kifu tsutsɔmɔɔ tsɔmɔ.
Aɖɔ sɛsɛ alɛ zia sɛ, “Nɔ kpɛ kite!
Mɛ nɔɔ mɔ!
Nɔ ti si kifu.” Ɔkɛlɛ ewoku opupu nɛ mɛ atɔnɔ balɛ, ko klɛ kɛlɛɛ nɛ yulɔ fu.
Tɛbhɛbhɛtɛ nɛ kɛ bhɛtɛ balɛ kibi petee, alasɛ gbɛgbɛvu nɛ kibui nɛ tsyɛ beke nu klɛ kesi, balɛ idzyi mɛ agɛganɛ.
Kibe lɛ gɛ ba tsɔkɛ, ba da dzrɔ nɛ Genesarɛt klɛ le dzu opupu nɛ kesi nɛ ɔklɛ.
Kibe lɛ gɛ benye koeyi nɛ opupu nɛ mɛ ko, banɔ nɛ ba kpɛ Yesu kɛxawũ.
Banɔ besi edenɔ kibee lɛlɛ nɛ mɛ petee klɛ ba yɛkɔ balɛ banyɛnya nɛ etuku nɛ iputso abha atɔnɔ Yesu avɛ ɔklɛ gɛ bee nye nu yɛ kɛdɔ sɛ alɛ ko.
Klɛ ɔkɔnyɔkɔ gɛ avɛ ko, ɛma bhlibhli, ɛmagbla, anɛ idubha nɛ petee mɛ, ba yɛkɔ banyɛnya nɛ ebe lu budzi nɛm.
Ba kɔ kɛtɔkpu asɛ, Yesu akɔ balɛ be hunɔ yɛ awi nɛ butɔ tite ko, klɛ bagɛ be hunɔ yɛ nɛ petee balɛ banya nɛ be beke.
Bagɛ Balɛ Ishu Bhui Nɛ Bagɛ Balɛ Ishu Di Bhui Farisianɛ anɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ teli gɛ be de Yerusalɛm nɛ be xogo nɛ Yesu ɔbha klɛ ba mɔ Yesu badɔkpasɛ teli gɛ be dzi aŋa kɛdɔ nɛ ahwɛ gɛ alɛ ishu “edibhui ” alasɛ bedi plu alɛ.
.
So Farisianɛ anɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ nɛ be bisi Yesu asɛ, “Kide so pɛɛ wɔ badɔkpasɛ nɛ ba taa bhɛtɛ bakakuku nɛ begu nɛa bha pɛ balɛ baa ŋa kɛdɔ nɛ ahwɛ gɛ alɛ shu edi bhui?” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Yezaya kibui dzyɔ nɛ ebui nɛ gɛ aɖɔ elu nɛ wɔnɔ shu sɛ no nu baa nɔ gɛ nɔtɔɔ ɖɔ kibui kɛwɔ̃hu; ansɛ gɛ ba ŋlɔmɛ elu asɛ: “ ‘Banɔa nɛ baɖɔ mɛ nɛ balɛ inugbu, pɔ balɛ idzyi mɛ aga ɔtɔ nɛ mɛ shu.
Ba kpɛ kɛtɔkpuesi kɔ mɛ kito; balɛ kɛdɔ kɛkasɛ nɛ nu banɔdzyrame eshã gɛ bakpɛ elu.’ Nɔ shɛnahwɛ Kpaya ɛshã nɛ shu olu klɛ nɔ dɔ lɛ banɔdzyrame begu nɛ ede.” Klɛ etsre balɛ asɛ, “Edzo dzyɔgo alɛ wɔnɔ ahwɛ gɛ nɔ ga pɛ nɔɔ yɛkɔ plɛ Kpaya ɛshã nɛ olu kɛwã sɛ tɛ nɔ mɔ wɔnɔ nahwɛ begu nɛ bu gu!
Alasɛ Mose aɖɔ asɛ, ‘Kpɛ kɛtɔkpu kesi kɔ wɔaka anɛ wɔeni,’ klɛ ‘Anɔnyanɔ gɛ aɖɔ kibui akpɛ yɛeni nɛ yɛaka, alasɛ tɛ be yi yɛ.’ Pɔ nɔ sɛ onu gɛ anɔ teli etsre yɛaka ɔdɔgɔsɛ yɛeni asɛ, ‘Tɛpɛplɛnɔ nɔɔ nɛ gɛ aba yɛkɛ denɔ yɛ ɔkɔ nɛ, kinu kɛdɔ gɛ ba yɛkɔ etsye Kpaya,’ klɛ so kɛ tɛa kɔ sɛ anɔ afla bhɛtɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ akɔ yɛaka pɛ ɔdɔgɔsɛ yɛeni.
Kɛ kɔ sɛ no xule Kpaya kibui ganɔ wɔnɔ begu nɛ gɛ nɔ nyɛna ovunɔ nɛ mɛ.
Klɛ nɔɔ bhɛtɛ ebui gelee kana.” Yesu eze klu banɔɛza nɛ amɛna yɛ ɔbha klɛ etsre alɛ asɛ, “Nɔ ta mɛ batɔ, anɔnyanɔ, tɛ no nu kibui nɛ kesi.
Kɛdɔnyɛdɔ gɛ kɛ lɛ ɔtɔ pɛ kɛ tsoku anɔ ishu mɛ nɛ kɛtɛ ‘tutru’ anɔ.
Pɔ, kɛ gɛ koeyi nɛ anɔ mɛ kɛ lɛ ‘tutru’ anɔ.” Anɔ nɛ gɛ batɔ alɛ yɛ tɛ enu.
Kibe lɛ gɛ ashɛ̃ alɔ banɔɛza nɛ beke pɛ ede tsoku bupa nɛ mɛ, yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ be bisi yɛ ebui edenɔ kɛkpalɛ nɛ shu.
Ebisi asɛ, “Klɛ so wɔnɔ atɔkpu nɛ egble tsi kana lo?” “So nɔ tɔɔ mɔ sɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ gɛ kitsoku anɔ mɛ denɔ ɔtɔ nɛɛ kɛtɛ tutru anɔ?
Alasɛ kɛ tɛɛ tsoku yɛ idzyi nɛ mɛ, eya nɛ mɛ lɛɛ vɛ, flogo pɛ kɛ ba tɛ koeyi nɛ yɛ ishu mɛ.” (Nɛ kibui lɛ nɛ tɛ ɖuɖɔ mɛ nɛ, Yesu atrɔ ahwɛ kɛlɛa bha sɛ kɛdɔŋɛŋa kanyaka di ko kɛlɛ shu bhui.)
Avɛ klɛa bha sɛ: “Kɛdɔ nɔɔ nɛ gɛ koeyi nɛ anɔ mɛ, klɛ tutru anɔ.’ Alasɛ denɔ anɔdzyrame idzyi mɛ, klɛ kɛtɔkpum kpã kii de, anyɛ anɛ adzɛ tɛzɛzam kpã, buzi, anɔyiyi, aglɔbui, kɛdɔgbla pɛpɛ kɔshu, ɔhayɛ shu zizi, anɔ wɛwɛɛ, bu mabhui mabhui, kawɔ̃kpɛ, anɔshu zizi, buwɔ̃dzu anɛ buzizi.
Ebui zizi anɛ petee le de koeyi nɛ anɔ mɛ, klɛ ala bhɛtɛ anɔ pɛ yɛ ishu ‘iti bhui.’ ” Sirofoenisian Dzi Teli Nɛ Yɛ Tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa Yesu ashɛ̃ nɛ ɔkɛlɛ klɛ avɛ Tire kibee.
Ede tsoku bupa tuli mɛ gɛ adɛ pɛ sɛ anɔnyanɔ eti, pɔ adɛ na yɛ ɔkɛlɛ tɛzɛza nɛ bu kpu.
Nɛ kɛgbɛagba mɛ, adzɛ teli gɛ ɛfufɔɛkpã tsri yɛ eyia bha, gɛ enye nu yɛ kɛdɔ ko klɛ ebe zhiadɔ nɛ yɛ etem.
Adzɛ nɛ enu Griki dzi, gɛ ba mɔ nɛ Sirianɛ Fonesia.
Edzu kɛtɔkpu kesi akɔ Yesu sɛ akɛka ɔfufɔɛkpã nɛ ebu nɛ yɛeyi adzɛ nɛ mɛ akɔ yɛ.
Etsre adzɛ nɛ asɛ, “Putɔnɔ nɛɛ kɔ beyi nɛ aŋa kɛdɔ nɔɔ gɛ ba pɛɛ nɛ petee, ” “alasɛ kɛdɛ kɔ kidzo sɛ tɛ ba yɛkɔ banuvɔ nɛ ŋɛŋa nɛ atɛɛ elu akɔ balɛ bukudzɔgɛ.” Adzɛ nɛ ebu kɛlɛ nu asɛ, “Yoo, Apalete, ” “pɔ bukudzɔgɛ nɛ gɛɛ za kɛdɔŋa ɔkplɔ̃ nɛ kesi nɛ, butɔkɛ kiwili wili nɛ gɛ kɛ wɔlɛ nɛ xũ nɛ aŋa.” Klɛ etsre adzɛ nɛ asɛ, “Nɛ wɔ kibu nɛ gɛ obu kibui nɛ bunu so nɛ, gavɛ faã, ɔfufɔɛkpã nɛ oti koeyi nɛ wɔ eyiadzɛ nɛ mɛ.” Gɛ adzɛ nɛ ashɛ̃ avɛ ede ku bupa nɛ mɛ nɛ amɔ yɛ eyiadzɛ nɛ gɛ eli kesi nɛ oputsoa bha, klɛ ɔfufɔɛkpã nɛ okoeyi ɔshɛ.
Batɔpu Anɛ Omumu Toli Banya Tibibeke Klɛ Yesu ashɛ̃ nɛ Tire kibee klɛ ada ga Sidɔn, ede zhi atɔnɔ Galelia Aƒu klɛ ede tsoku Dekapoli.
Ɔkɛlɛ banɔ teli ba gbanɔ anɔ teli gɛ etee nu klɛ kaɖɔ ɖuɖɔ tsyɛ ka gɛganɛ akɔ yɛ, klɛ la ba kpɛ kɛtɔkpu kesi akɔ Yesu asɛ atrɔ ahwɛ nɛ anɔ nɛa bha tɛ yɛ bunya nɛ bu beke.
Gɛ ebu anyɛnya nɛ eyinɔ kide nɛ banɔ nɛ kishi beke nɛ, Yesu ayɛkɔ yɛ ahwɛ nɛ akpɛ anyɛ nɛ batɔ mɛ.
Klɛ ebu bututu klɛ ayɛkɔ ala anyɛ nɛ kɛnɛkɛ.
Ebu amɛ akpɛ owũsise klɛ afɔɛ vuu, klɛ aɖɔ etsre anyɛ nɛ asɛ, “Efata!” (klɛ kesi asɛ “Danɛ!”).
Nɛ ɔklɛ nɛ, anyɛ nɛ batɔ nɛ adanɛ, yɛ kɛnɛkɛ nɛ mɛ kibule, klɛ akpa kaɖɔ ɖɔ wee.
Yesu akpɛ ɔshã akɔ balɛ asɛ ba tɛ da ɖɔ etsre anɔnyanɔ.
Pɔ kɛkpɛ nɛ gɛ akpɛ ɔshã nɛ, kana ke baa ɖɔ kaɖɔ nɛ kibui nɛ shu.
Kɛ bhɛtɛ banɔ nɛ kibi.
Klɛ baa ɖɔ asɛ, “Abhɛtɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ klɛ kɛ na.” “Akɔa sɛ bagɛ betee nu tsyɛ be nu, bagɛ ba taa ɖɔ kaɖɔ na ɖɔ kaɖɔ.”
Yesu Anyunɔ Banɔ Akpã Talɛ Nɛ ewi alɛlɛ nɛ mɛ banɔɛzagbla bhlatɔ zɛ ba xogo.
Gɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ kɛdɛ za balɛ ahwɛ gɛ ba baŋa, Yesu eklu yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ ebunɔ ishu klɛ asɛ, “Eshutukubui ekum nɛ banɔa nɛ, ewi tata naa gɛ la ba lɛ mɛ ɔbha gɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ ma balɛ ahwɛ gɛ la ba ŋa.
Onu gɛ ɛsɛ ba shɛ vɛ bapam nɛ bubhɛ, bee ti tsi abhɛbhɛ nɛ kidzo nɛ mɛ, alasɛ beteli idekɔ nɛ dze.” Yɛ Badɔkpasɛ nɛ be bui lɛ bunu asɛ, “Klɛ nɛ okpukpu kɔɔ nɛ, fakɔ anɔ ebe denɔ kɛŋɛŋa kɔ banɔ kplumua?” Yesu ebisi asɛ “gbɛgbɛvu egbaa tɛshɛ gɛ lɛ wɔnɔ ahwɛ?” Be bui lɛ nu sɛ, “Tigene.” Etsre banɔɛza nɛ asɛ ba za kesi nɛ kesukpa.
