Gɛ ayɛkɔ egbaa tigene nɛ ehu ahwɛ, klɛ aya ɛlɛ mɛ, klɛ ayɛkɔ ɛlɛ akpɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ ahwɛ sɛ ba ma kɔ banɔ, klɛ balɛ tsyɛ ba bhɛtɛ ansɛ gɛ aɖɔ.
Kenimɛdzya bhli tili tsyɛ za balɛ ahwɛ, ehu ahwɛ nɛ alɛ tsyɛ kɛtɔkpu klɛ etsre badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ ba ma lɛ.
Banɔ na tã klɛ be xui.
Kɛlɛ de badɔkpasɛ na tɔkɛ kiwiliwili nɛ gɛ gɔ nɛ ashwɛ tegene.
Banyɛ ansɛ akpã talɛ balɛ aza ɔkɛlɛ.
Klɛ gɛ akpɛ banɔ nɛ kidzo beke, ede woku keniabha opupu nɛ mɛ nɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ klɛ ba shɛ avɛ Dalmanuta kibee.
Farisianɛ na ba klɛ ba kpa ebui bisi Yesu.
Tɛ ba yɛkɔ efeke yɛ edi nɔ, be bisi yɛ asɛ abhɛtɛ kɛdɔmumɔ tili gɛ kide owũsise.
Afɔɛ vuu klɛa sɛ, “Kide so pɛ ɔtsɔ̃ nɛ mɛ banɔ nee bisi ebui gɛ eyiyinɔ anɔ sɛ tɛ ba mɔ?
Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, ba tɛ ba kasɛ kɛdɔmumɔ kanyaka nɛ kɛlɛ shu.” Klɛ ashɛ̃ lɔ balɛ, ede tsoku keniabha opupu nɛ mɛ klɛ atsɔkɛ avɛ ogbigbe bhla nɛa bha.
Farisianɛ Anɛ Heroɖesɛ Bunɛyekedɔ Badɔkpasɛ nɛ ba dzɛkɛ ba dɛ yɛkɔ kɛŋɛŋa kanyaka, ɔyɛkɔ dɛ gbɛgbɛvu ɔgbaa torikpo gɛ lɔ za balɛ ahwɛ nɛ opupu nɛ mɛ.
Yesu etsre alɛ asɛ, “Nɔ dii mɔ.” “No vu awɔ̃hũ nɛ Farisianɛ anɛ Heroɖesɛ bunɛyekedɔ.” Ba nyɛna kibui nɛ edi nɛ aglɔ mɛ klɛ ba ɖɔ asɛ, “Alasɛ gɛ gbɛgbɛvu kanyaka kɛma blɔ ahwɛ nɛ so.” Gɛ enu balɛ ebui nyɛnyɛnadi nɛ, Yesu ebisi alɛ asɛ, “Kidee so pɛ gbɛgbɛvu nɛ gɛ ma wɔnɔ ahwɛ nɛ kibui no dzi ɔɖɔ?
So ɔbɔ nanɔ ɔtsɔ̃ nɛ, nɔ kɔ mɔ, pɛ kibuiesi no bo nu dza?
Wɔnɔ idzyi nɛ mɛ aza gɛganɛ atrɔ?
Anhũ alɛ wɔnɔ ahwɛ flogo pɛ nɔ tɔɔ mɔ, klɛ batɔ alɛ wɔnɔ ahwɛ, pɛ nɔ sɛ no too nu dza?
Klɛ nɔ tɔɔ baka?
Gɛ ɛya gbɛgbɛvu ɛgba titi nɛ ɛkɔ banɔ akpã teti, be wiliwili nɛ ashwɛ tashɛ̃ nɔ tɔkɛ?” Be bu klɛ nu asɛ, “Kɛfɔntabha.” “Klɛ gɛ ɛyɛ ɛgbaa tigene nɛ ɛkɔ banɔ akpã talɛ̃, bewiliwili ashwɛ tashɛ̃ nɔ tɔkɛ?” Be bu klɛ nu asɛ, “Tegene.” Etsre balɛ asɛ, “So nɛ ɔtsiɔ̃ nɛɛ nɔ kɔ nu klɛesi dza?” Anhũpuelete Teli Anhũdɛdanɛ Nɛ Besaɛda Ba ebe ku Besaɛda, klɛ banɔ teli agbanɔ anyɛ awɔ̃hũ pupu elete teli amɛna klɛ ba kpɛ kɛtɔkpu kesi akɔ Yesu asɛ tɛ ehunɔ yɛ.
Anyɛna awɔ̃hũ pupu elete nɛ ɔhwɛ klɛ agbanɔ yɛ ebu avɛ nɔ ɔmabhli nɛe de.
Kibe lɛ nɛ gɛ ebu bututu na kpɛ anyɛ na awɔ̃hũ nɛ mɛ, pɛ atrɔ ahwɛ nɛ yɛa bha nɛ, Yesu ebisi yɛ asɛ, “Ɔmɔ kɛdɔ tili dza?” Edi kabha klɛ asɛ, “Ɛmɔ banɔ; baa wɛ̃ anasɛ isi gɛ lɛ gaa fla.” Yesu aza trɔ ahwɛ nɛ anyɛ nɛ awɔ̃hũ nɛa bha.
Ko klɛ yɛ awɔ̃hũ nɛ adanɛ, yɛ tɛmumɔ nɛ tsodzi ba kɔ yɛ, klɛ amɔ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ wee.
Yesu asɛ gavɛ bupa mɛ, klɛ etsre yɛ asɛ, “Tɔɔ vɛ Besaɛda.” Petro Adanɛ Kristo Shu Yesu anɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ ba shɛ avɛ ɛmabhli nɛ gɛ kana Sizeria Filipi nɛ mɛ.
Gɛ baa vɛ nɛ kidzo nɛ mɛ, Yesu ebisi alɛ asɛ, “Anee banɔ baa ɖɔ sɛ inu?” Be bu klɛ nu asɛ, “Banɔ teli asɛ Yohanɛsɛ Enikpɛ; be teli asɛ, Eliya; klɛ babhlatɔ teli tsyɛ asɛ, batɔnu nɛ ɔmɛayɛ teli.” Ebisi asɛ, “Pɔ wɔnɔ xũ xɔ̃?” “Anee wɔnɔ ɔsɛ inu?” Petro ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Wo nu Kristo.” Yesu akpɛ balɛ ɔshã sɛ, batɛ ɖɔ yɛ shuibui etsre anɔnyanɔ.
Yesu Aɖɔ Yɛ Titsitsi Nɛ Shuibui Elu Ɔkɛlɛ akpa kɛdɔ kasɛ balɛ asɛ, Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi alasɛ tɛ atɔ nɛ ebui gelee mɛ klɛ beshishe na tɛ ba yɛkɛ yɛ, kpayaɔzakɔanɔ anɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ, klɛ kɛba za sɛ tɛ be yi yɛ klɛ nɛ ewi tataede ebe tsodzi alɔ.
Aɖɔ kaɖɔ adanɛ kibuinyɛbui mɛ, klɛ Petro agbanɔ yɛ eyinɔ kide klɛ ada ka yɛ amɛ.
Pɔ gɛ Yesu etsyina edi yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ, aka Petro amɛ asɛ, “Tsu ɔvɛ nɛ mɛ ɔbha, Satana!” “Kpaya ebui nɛ ama wɔnɔ kɛtɔkpu mɛ, banɔdzyrame ayɛ nɛ ala lɛ wɔnɔ mɛ.” Ɔkɛlɛ eklu banɔɛza anɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ amɛna yɛ ɔbha klɛ asɛ, “Onu anɔ teli asɛ mɛ kede yɛ aba za nɛ, klɛ ashɛ̃nahwɛ yɛ ishu nɛ shu, tɛ yɛnahwɛ ayɛkɔ yɛ butsiosi tɛ aza mɛ kede.
Alasɛ anɔnyanɔ gɛ aba pɛ sɛ tɛ ebu yɛ ɛkpã nɛ, aba lɛla ɛlɛ, pɔ anɔ nɛ gɛ aba lɛla yɛ ɛkpã nɛ akpɛ mɛ anɛ kibuidzyɔgo nɛ so ebe bui lɛ.
Kɛdɔ dzyɔgo ɖue anɔ aba mɔ sɛ tɛ kanɔ nɛ petee kedzi yɛa yɛ tɛ ada lɛla yɛ kɛtɔwi?
Klɛ kidee anɔ aba naa yɛkɔ atsrakɛ yɛ kɛtɔwi nɛ nɔ?
Onu gɛ mɛ anɛ kibui nɛ ba ku anɔ teli kɛwɛ̃, nɛ aglɔbui anɛ buzizi kanɔa nɛ mɛ, klɛ anɔɔ nɛ tsyɛ ebe ku Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ kɛwɛ̃ onu gɛ ebe ku nɛ yɛ Aka nɛ kabhakpɛkpɛ mɛ ɔplɛnɔ kpayaxwɛdɛ nɛ gɛ balɛ shu bhui.”
Klɛ etsre balɛ asɛ, “Itsre nɔ sɛ kɛgba lɛ nu sɛ, banɔ teli gɛ beli kititi nɛ ɔkɛ̃ nɛ batɛ ba mɔ butsi flogo pɛ Kpaya Bukusiɔzakɔ nɛ ɔbɔ ba nɛ kemi.” Ishu Tsɛtsrakɛ Nɛ ewi tehloe de, Yesu agbanɔ Petro, Yakobo anɛ Yohanɛsɛ aplɛnɔ ishu klɛ ba vɛ butu ɖɛɖama tulia bha, gɛ anɔnyanɔ ama ɔkɛlɛ.
Ɔkɛlɛ yɛ tɛzɛza mɛ tsyina nɛ balɛ amɛ.
Yɛ bawi nɛ gɛ akpɛ nɛ petee baa tã frɛɖɛɛ ɖɛ ɔyɛkɔ dɛ kɛdɔ fufu kanyakaɛ di nɛ kanɔa nɛ mɛ, gɛ anɔnyanɔ atɛba na kɛlɛ bu plu pɛ kɛba fuli dɛ kana.
Klɛ ba mɔ Eliya anɛ Mose gɛ be dzi aɖɔ kaɖɔ nɛ Yesu.
Petro etsre Yesu asɛ, “Adɔkasɛ, kɛpɛ sɛ bu ba ɔkɛ̃.
Kɔ lɔ dzu bugba tɔta nɛ ɔkɛ̃, wɔayɛ tierikpo, Mose yɛayɛ tierikpo, anɛ Eliya yɛayɛ tierikpo.” (Edi ti kibui nɔɔ nɛ gɛ aba ɖɔ, kifu kua lɛ tsutsɔmɔ tsɔmɔ.)
Klɛ ɔmunɔ toli ɔbɔ dɔ kana balɛ, klɛ ogugu toli oyi denɔ ɔmunɔ nɛ mɛ sɛ, “Mɛ Eyi naa, gɛ ɛdɛmɛ yɛ kibui.
Nɔ ta yɛ batɔ!” Ɔtsɔlɛ gɛ be lu awɔ̃ edi balɛ ɔbha nɛ, ba daa mɔ anɔnyanɔ ɔyɛkɔ dɛ Yesu nɛ ɔkɛlɛ.
Gɛ be zhi butu nɛ pɛ baa ba, Yesu akpɛ balɛ ɔshã sɛ be ti tsre anɔnyanɔ kɛdɔnɔ gɛ ba da mɔ nɛ ɔkɛlɛ, ɔdɔ nanɔ kibelɛ gɛ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ aba nyɛmɛ edenɔ bekpu mɛ.
Be kpu kibui nɛ balɛ kpɛkpa nɛ kishi, klɛ be bisi nɛ aglɔm asɛ kide “tɛlulɔ denɔ bekpu mɛ nu.” Klɛ bee bisi Yesu asɛ, “Kidee so pɛ bagɛ baa kasɛ ɛshã na sɛ kɛ lɛ sɛ tɛ Eliya eputɔ aba?” Yesu asɛ, “Tɛ bu ka nɛ klɛa bha nɛ, kɛ lɛ sɛ tɛ Eliya aba eputɔnɔ, kɔ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ tɛŋuŋuse.
Klɛ kidee so pɛ ba za ŋlɔmɛ elu asɛ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ alasɛ tɛ aba tɔ gelee tsyɛ tɛ batɛ yɛkɛ yɛ?
Pɔ itsre nɔ, Eliya atɛ ba, klɛ ba bhɛtɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ gɛ ba pɛɛ nɛ yɛ, anasɛ gɛ ba ŋlɔmɛ elu nɛ yɛ shu.” Ɔfufɔɛkpã Tɛkɛkɛkabu Nɛ Anyɛnuvɔɛ Teli Mɛ Gɛ le be ku badɔkpasɛ gugɔɛ nɛ ɔbha, ba mɔ banɔɛza gɛ kana lɛ, klɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ nɛ be dzi awlãkɛ ebui nɛ balɛ.
Gɛ banɔ petee amɔ Yesu ko same ekua lɛ klɛ be si ada sɛnɛ yɛ.
Yesu ebisi badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ, “Kidee shu nɔ wlãnkɛ kibui nɛ balɛ?” Anyɛ teli nɛ banɔɛza nɛ mɛ na ɖɔ asɛ, “Adɔkasɛ, ɛmɛna wɔ mɛ eyianyɛ gɛ ɛfufɔɛkpã kɔ sɛ eku omumu.
Onu gɛ lɔɔ dɔ yɛa bha nɛ loo bu yɛ obho.
Yɛ onugbu nɛ mɛ ɔtsa kɛfɔ, atã ele klɛ yaa nunɔ.
Ibisi wɔ badɔkpasɛ nɛ sɛ ba kɛka kana mɛ ɔfufɔɛ nɛ ebu nɛ yɛ mɛ pɔ ba dɛ na.” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “O ɔtsɔ̃ nɛ banɔ nɛ gɛ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa ma balɛ mɛ,” “ɔdɔ na nɛ kibe ɖueɖu mɛ ɛba za wɔnɔ bha?
Klɛɛ za mɛ ba za wɔnɔ ɔbha da tɔnɔ?
Gbanɔ anyɛnuvɔɛ nɛ ɔmɛna mɛ.” So, ba gbanɛ yɛ amɛna.
Gɛ ɔfufɔɛ nɔ mɔ Yesu ko, lɔ kpɛ anuvɔ nɛ bunuvɔnya mɛ.
Klɛ awɔlɛ adɔ kesukpa klɛ eglebe atsya, nɛ kɛfɔ denɔ yɛ onugbu nɛ mɛ.
Yesu ebisi eyi nɛ yaka nɛ asɛ, “Kibe ɖueɖuibe ke anuvɔ nɛ abhɛtɛ kana?” Eyiaka nɛ aɖɔ asɛ, “Denɔ kɛnuvɔbe mɛ ke.” “Bunya nɛɛ ganɛ yɛ bu tii kpɛ kifu anɛ buni mɛ sɛ tɛ bu yi yɛ.
Pɔ onu gɛ ɔbɔ na kɛdɔ tili ɔbhɛtɛ, klɛ tɛ odi bulɔ eshutukubui tɛ ɔplɛnɔ bulɔ.” Yesu asɛ, “ ‘Ɔsɛ onu gɛ ɛba na dza?’ Kibui nyɛbui lɛ bɔbɔɛbɔɛ kɔ anɔ nɛ gɛ ayɛkɛ aŋa.” Ko klɛ Aka nɛ akpɛ ogugu asɛ “Ɛyɛkɛ ɛŋa, plɛnɔ mɛ tɛ ɛŋa mɛ kabha mayɛkɛ mayɛkɛŋa nɛa bha!” Gɛ Yesu amɔ banɔɛza nɛ gɛ ba yalɛ aba sɛ tɛ le be di kɛdɔnɔ nɛ gɛ kɛlɛ vɛ kabha nɛ, alɛɛ nɛ ɔfufɔɛkpã nɛa bha.
“Wɔ batɔpu anɛ omumu ɔfufɔɛ,” “Ɛkpɛ ɔshã kɔ wɔ, fla okoeyi nɛ anuvɔ nɛ mɛ, tɔɔ ba obo tsoku yɛ mɛ kiwinyɛwi.” Ɔfufɔɛ nɛ ɔxlɔ̃, klɛ lɔ hwa nɛ yɛ gɛganɛɛ, klɛ lɔ fla okoeyi.
Anuvɔ nɛ awɛ̃ nɛ banɔ nɛ amɛ ansɛ anɔ tsitsi.
So banɔ gelee aɖɔ sɛ, “Etsi.” Pɔ Yesu anyɛna anuvɔ nɛ ɔhwɛ klɛ efeke yɛ edzu yɛ ɛtsrɛa bha, klɛ alɔ kititi.
Klɛɛ de mɛ gɛ Yesu etsoku buvu nɛ mɛ, yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ be bisi yɛ nɛ tɛkpukpu mɛ asɛ, “Kidee so pɛ bulɔ bu dɛ na ɔfufɔɛ nɛ bu kɛka bu?” Yesu asɛ, “Ɔnɛ nɛ kidi nɛ ganɔ Kpaya kuklu anɛ onugbu nyɛnya mɛ ko lo bo koeyi.” Ba shɛ nɛ ɔkɛlɛ ada ga Galelia.
Yesu adɛ ka pɛɛ sɛ anɔnyanɔ eti ɔkɛlɛ gɛ ba lɛ, alasɛ aakasɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ kɛdɔ.
Etsre balɛ asɛ, “Ba baa ba ga Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ kesi ayɛkɔ akpɛ banɔ ahwɛ.
Ba ebe yi yɛ, klɛ nɛ ewi tata kede nɛ ebe tsodzi alɔ.” Pɔ be di nu kibui nɔ nɛ gɛ aɖɔ nɛ kesi, klɛ kifu kua lɛ sɛ tɛ be bisi klɛ kesi enu.
Anee Yɛ Enu Agbɛgbla Dɛ Ba ebe ku Kapenaum.
Gɛ beli bupa nɛ mɛ, Yesu ebisi balɛ asɛ, “kibui ɖue nɔ wlãnkɛ nɛ kidzo nɛ mɛ?” Pɔ badɔ sɛɛ̃ alasɛ baa wlãnkɛ anɔ nɛ gɛ ebe dzi agbɛgbla nɛ adɛ.
Gɛ aza kesi beke nɛ, Yesu eklu yɛ banɔ lɔfɔntɛabha klɛ aɖɔ asɛ, “Onu gɛ anɔ teli aaba pɛ asɛ tɛ edzi atutɔpu, klɛ ebe dzi agɔgɔɛ anɛ axwɛdɛ kɔ balɛ petee.” Agbanɔ anuvɔ bhli teli amɛna klɛ akɔ yɛ alɔ kititi nɛ balɛ kishi.
Gɛ agbanɔ yɛ akpɛ ete mɛ beke nɛ, klɛ etsre alɛ sɛ, “Aanɔ nɛ gɛ ayɛkɛ banuvɔ bhlia nɛ ɔmɛayɛ teli nɛ mɛ kinyi mɛ, mɛ ayɛkɛ, klɛ anɔɔ nɛ gɛ ayɛkɛ mɛ nɛ ganɛ mɛ ayɛkɛ, agɛ akpɛ mɛ nɛ ayɛkɛ.” Aanɔ Nɛ Gɛ Aadɛ Lɔ Kititi Nɛ Bulɔ Shu Alɛ Kɔ Bulɔ Yohanɛsɛ aɖɔ asɛ, “Adɔkasɛ,” “Bu mɔ anyɛ teli gɛ akɛka ɛfufɔɛkpã nɛ wɔ kinyi mɛ klɛ bu tsre yɛ sɛ ataa bhɛtɛ, alasɛ edi nu blɔmɛayɛ teli.” Yesu asɛ, “Nɔ tɛ dzu ahwɛ nɛ yɛa bha.” “Anɔnyanɔ ama gɛ abhɛtɛ kibui yiyinɔ anɔ nɛ mɛ kinyi mɛ, pɛ ebe tsyina aɖɔ kibui kpã nɛ mɛ shu, alasɛ aanɔ nɛ gɛ aadɛ lɔ kititi nɛ bulɔ shu nɛ enu bulɔa yɛ.
Itsre nɔ kibuigba sɛ, anɔnyanɔ gɛ akɔ nɔ buniatse nɛ mɛ kinyi mɛ sɛ no nu Kristo ayɛ so, yɛ ahwɛhuhu nɛ atɛba lɛla.
Tɛtitikpɛ Kibuikpã Bhɛbhɛtɛ Mɛ “Klɛ so aanɔ nɛ gɛ aba kɔ sɛ banuvɔ bhli anɛ teli gɛ ayɛkɛ mɛ kabha aŋa nɛ awɔlɛ ku buzizi mɛ, onugɛ ba yɛkɔ buhɔgbla anya plɛnɔ yɛ oli pɛ ba yɛkɔ wɔ ada tɛɛ akpɛ aƒu mɛ tsyɛ, aba pɛ akɔ yɛ adɛ.
Onu gɛ wɔ ɔhwɛ toli ɔkɔ sɛ oku buzizi mɛ, bhui ɔlɛ ɔtɛɛ̃.
Abɔ kɔ wɔ sɛ tɛ ɔhwɛ torikpo ɔza wɔ ahwɛ nɛ ɛkpã mɛ, ɔyɛkɔ dɛ sɛ tɛ ɔyɛkɔ ɛhwɛ tɛbha ɔvɛnɔ butsutsɔmɔ mɛ, nɛ ɔklɛ gɛ kifu tii ni.” [Nɛ ɔklɛ gɛ asɔ̃ eti be tsi edi, klɛ kifu nɛ tsyɛ tɛ ba ni di.]
Onu gɛ wɔ ɔtsrɛ toli ɔɔkɔ sɛ oku buzizi mɛ, bhui ɔlɛ ɔtɛ̃ɛ.
Kɛ ba pɛ sɛ tɛ otsoku ɛkpã mɛ nɛ ɔtsrɛ torikpo, ɔyɛkɔ dɛ sɛ tɛ ɔza ɛtsrɛtɛbha kabha tɛ ba yɛkɔ wɔ ada tɛɛ̃ akpɛ butsutsɔmɔ mɛ.
[Nɛ ɔkɛlɛ gɛ asɔ̃ eti be tsi edi, klɛ kifu tsyɛ tɛ ba ni di.]
Klɛ onu gɛ wɔ kɛwɔ̃hũ tili kɔ sɛ ɔbhɛtɛ kibuikpã, kpa kɛlɛ obu.
Kɛpɛ kɔ wɔ sɛ tɛ otsoku Kpaya bukusi ɔŋakɔ nɛ kɛwɔ̃hũ tirikpo ɔyɛkɔ dɛ sɛ tɛ awɔ̃hũ tabha aza wɔ ahwɛ tɛ ba yɛkɔ wɔ ada tɛɛ̃ akpɛ kifu gɛ tɛ ba ni di mɛ.
ɔklɛ gɛ “ ‘balɛ asɔ̃ nɛ etee tsi, klɛ kifu tsyɛ tii ni.’ Baa yɛkɔ kifu eplu anɔnyanɔ shu klɛ la ba yɛkɔ bumɔɛ akpɛ anɔnyanɔ sɛ tɛ eti zi.
“Bumɔɛ nɛ kɛdɔ dzyɔgo bu nu, pɔ onu gɛ bu lɛla bulɛ ɔdzyɛ, klɛ ɔzɔ bɔ kɔ sɛ ɔdzyɛ ɔza lɛ?
Nɔ kɔ bumɔɛ za nɔ mɛ, tɛ nɔ za ishu yuyɔ mɛ nɛ wɔnɔ hayɛalɛ.”
Anyɛ Anɛ Adzyɛ Aglɔ Shu Shɛshɛ̃nahwɛ Yesu ashɛ̃ nɛ ɔklɛ aba fla vɛ Yuɖua kɛdɔ nɛ mɛ, klɛ ada tsɔkɛ Yɔɖan keni.
Kana ke banɔɛza nɛ zɛ ba yɛ ɔbha, klɛ anasɛ gɛ aabhɛtɛ, akasɛ balɛ kɛdɔ.
Farisianɛ teli be feke yɛ edi klɛ be bisi yɛa sɛ, “Kɛ lɛ ɔshã mɛ sɛ tɛ anyɛ ashɛ̃nahwɛ yɛedzini shu dza?” Ebisi balɛ asɛ, “Ɔshã ɖueɖu Mose akpɛ kɔ nɔ?” Ba ɖɔ asɛ, “Mose akɔ kidzo sɛ anyɛ aŋlɔmɛ adzɛ shu shɛshɛ̃nahwɛ keplukpa tɛ ayɛkɔ akpɛ yɛ dzo nɔ.” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Alasɛ wɔnɔ idzyi nɛ mɛ agɛganɛ so pɛ Mose akpɛ ɔshã nɛ akɔ wɔnɔ,” “Pɔ denɔ kanɔ nɛ kesi kpɛkpɛ mɛ, Kpaya ‘abhɛtɛ alɛ anyɛ anɛ adzɛ.’ Nɛ kɛlɛ shu so, anyɛ aba shɛ alɔ yɛaka anɛ yɛeni avɛ ada bhɛtɛ terikpo nɛ yɛedzini, klɛ baa tɛa bha nɛ bebe dzi ishuidzya tirikpo.
Kɛlɛ so be deke nu banɔ tɛa bha, pɔ be dzi anɔ terikpoo.
Kana mɛ so, kɛdɔnɔ nɛ gɛ Kpaya atsa abhɛtɛ tirikpo, kɔ anɔnyanɔ eti bule kɛlɛ.” Gɛ be ke li bupa nɛ mɛ nɛɛ, Badɔkpasɛ nɛ be ze bisi Yesu ebui denɔ kibui nɛ shu.
Ebu lɛ nu asɛ, “Anyɛnyanyɛ gɛ ashɛ̃nahwɛ yedzini shu pɛ aza da gbanɔ adzɛ bhlatɔ nɛɛ, abhɛtɛ aglɔbui avɛnɔ adzɛ nɛ ɔkɔ.
Klɛ onu gɛ adzɛ tsyɛ ashnahwɛ yɛenyine shu pɛɛ aza da zanɔ anyɛ bhlatɔ nɛɛ, yɛ tsyɛ abhɛtɛ aglɔbui.” Banuvɔ Bhli Anɛ Yesu Banɔ baa mɛna banuvɔ bhli sɛ tɛ Yesu atrɔ ahwɛ nɛ balɛa bha tɛ ayula alɛ, pɔ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ ba kpaa lɛ.
Gɛ Yesu amɔ kibui nɛ, amɔ obulo.
So etsre balɛ asɛ “Nɔ kɔ bunuvɔɛbhli na ba mɛ ɔbha, klɛ nɔ tɔɔ kɛka lɛ, alasɛ banɛ nɛɛ di nɛ ɔzakɔ ɔlɛ nu Kpaya bukusiɔŋakɔ.
Itsre nɔ kɛgbɛagba sɛ, anɔnyanɔ gɛ atɛ ba yɛkɛ Kpaya bukusiɔŋakɔ ansɛ anuvɔ bhli, atɛ ba na bulɛ mɛ etsoku.” Klɛ Yesu ayɛkɛ bunuvɔɛ na kpɛ etem, klɛ atrɔ ahwɛ nɛ balɛa bha klɛ ayula balɛ.
Anyɛsɔ Ehueielete Teli Gɛ Yesu agaa vɛ, anyɛ teli aba tɔnɔ yɛ klɛ ezhiakpla nɛ yɛ otugba.
Ebisi asɛ, “Adɔkasɛ Dzyɔgo,” “kidee mɛ ɛba bhɛtɛ pɛ ɛba mɔ ɛkpã gɛ tɛ ba beke?” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Kide so pɛ oklu mɛ ɔsɛ anɔ dzyɔgo?” “Anɔnyanɔ adɛ na, dɛ Kpaya trikpo.
Sɛ no nyi ɛshã, Ti yi anɔ, tɛbhɛtɛ aglɔbui, tɛ zuru, tɛ ɖɔ kibuinɔ nɛ gɛ otinyi, tɛ wɛɛ anɔ ozru, bubɔ shu kɔ wɔaka nɛ weni.” Anyɛ na ɖɔ sɛ, “Adɔkasɛ, ” “anɛ nɛ petee ɛbhɛtɛ alɛ denɔ mɛ anyɛnuvɔɛ dzibe ke.” Yesu edi yɛ klɛ yɛ kibui za yɛ buli.
Klɛ asɛ, “Kibui tirikpo gɔ kɔ wɔ,” “Vɛ, dɔ dɛ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ gɛ lɛ wɔ ahwɛ tɛ ɔyɛkɔ kɔ betsyutsyuini, klɛ kɛba kɔ sɛ kɛnɔmɛdɔ kɛ ba za wɔ ahwɛ nɛ owũsise.
Tɛ otsodzi ɔba tɛ ɔbɔ za mɛe de.” Nɛ kɛnɛ nɛ mɛ anyɛ nɛ ezhinɔ amɛesi.
Kibui nɛ dɛ kui same, alasɛ kɛnɔmdɔ lɛ yɛ ahwɛ gelee.
Yesu elu awɔ̃ edi klɛ etsre yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ, “Kɛ ba gɛganɛ kɔ ehoeyielete sɛ tɛ etsoku Kpaya bukusi ɔŋakɔ!” Ebui nɛ gɛ aɖɔ nɛ abhɛtɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ kibi.
Pɔ Yesu aza ɖɔa sɛ, “Beyi mɔ, Kpaya bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ mɛ vɛvɛ no nu kibui gɛganɛ Kɛ ba za bubɔɛbɔɛ kɔ kipuaga sɛ aga kɛtsa ozi mɛ afla ɔyɛkɔ dɛ sɛ tɛ ehoeyielete etsoku Kpaya bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛ mɛ.” Kibui nɛ zɛ bhɛtɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ kibi dɛ kana, klɛ baa ɖɔ nɛ aglɔmɛ asɛ, “Kɛlɛ anee di yɛ aba mɔ ɛkpã?” Yesu edi alɛ klɛ aɖɔ asɛ, “Nɛ anɔdzyrame kapɛ mɛ kɛ ma bɔbɔɛbɔɛ, pɔ ganɛ kɔ Kpaya xũ, kibuinyɛbui lɛ bubɔɛbɔɛ kɔ Kpaya.” Petro etsre yɛ asɛ, “Bu tɛ shɛnahwɛ bulɔ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ shu klɛ bu ba lɛ wɔ kede!” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Itsre nɔ kɛgba,” “anɔnyanɔ ama gɛ ashɛ̃ nɛ kepi, ayɛlɔ yɛadzyalɛ, anɛ yɛadalɛ, anɛ yɛeni, anɛ yɛaka, anɛ yɛeyialɛ, anɛ yɛ kaya akpɛ mɛ Kibui Dzyɔgo nɛ so, pɛ ata yɛkɛ kɛdɔ gelee adɛ nɛ kɛfɔɛfɔ mɛ nɛ ɛkpã nɛ mɛ, (bapa, badzya, bada, beni, beyi nɛ kaya kapɛ mɛ— klɛ ɔyɛkɔ plɛnɔ alɛ kititilulɔ) klɛ nɛ agɔ gɛ aba tɛ ba nɛ mɛ, ɛkpã gɛ tɛba beke ba za.
Pɔ be gelee gɛ be putɔ nɛ be dzi bagugɔɛ, klɛ bagɔgɔɛ nɛ be dzi batutɔpu.” Yesu Aza Ɖɔ Kaɖɔ Elu Nɛ Yɛ Butsi Nɛ Shu Baza kidzoa bha ewua aavɛ Yerusalɛm, nɛ kibe lɛ gɛ Yesu eputɔ kɔ balɛ, yɛ ebui nɛ eyinɔ yɛ badɔkpasɛ, klɛ kifu ku bagɛ ba za yɛe de.
Aza gbanɔ kɛfɔntɛabha nɛ eyinɔ kide klɛ etsre balɛ kɛgɛ baa ba yɛa bha.
Etsre balɛ asɛ, “Bu vɛ Yerusalɛm,” “klɛ la ba tɛ ga Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛesi akɔ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ anɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ.
Bee bu yɛ butsipɔ klɛ la ba yɛkɔ yɛ akpɛ ahwɛ kɔ bagɛ edi nu Yuɖanɛ, gɛ la ba kpɛ yɛ butsɔ klɛ le be bu bututu ata yɛ, klɛ la ba mɛna yɛ kishi klɛ le be yi yɛ.
Nɛ ewi tata kede nɛ aba lɔ.” Yakobo Anɛ Yohanɛsɛ Tɛbibisi Ɔklɛ Yakobo anɛ Yohanɛsɛ gɛ benu Zebeɖi yɛeyialɛ nɛ ba tɔnɔ yɛ aba.
Klɛ ba ɖɔ asɛ, “Adɔkasɛ, bu pɛɛ sɛ tɛ ɔbhɛtɛ kɛkanyaka gɛ bu bisi nɛ ɔkɔ lɔ.” Ebisi asɛ “Kide nɔ pɛɛ sɛ ɛbhɛtɛ kɔ nɔ?” Be bui lɛ nu asɛ, “Kɔ bulɔmɛayɛ teli aza wɔ kɛŋa mɛ tɛ abhla nɛ aza wɔ kɛbɛtɛkpɛ mɛ nɛ wɔ same ɔzakɔ.” Yesu etsre alɛ asɛ, “No ti nyi kɛdɔnɔ nɛ gɛ noo bisi.” “Nɔ bɔ na mɛ butɔantse nɛ gɛ ɛba wɛ̃ nɛ ɔwɛ̃ pɛ, ɔdɔgɔsɛ tɛ ba kpɛ buni akɔnɔ nɛ buni nɛ di gɛ bakpɛ kɔ mɛ nɛ dza?” Be bu klɛ nu asɛ, “Bu ba na.” Klɛ Yesu etsre alɛ asɛ, “Nɔ bɔ wɛ̃ mɛ katse nɛ gɛ ɛwɛ̃, klɛ nɔbɔ yɛkɛ bunikpɛkpɛ nɛ gɛ ɛkpɛ nɛ di, pɔ tɛ ɔza mɛ kɛŋa mɛ nɛ kɛbɛtɛkpɛ mɛ xũ nɛ, ganɛ mɛ ba kɔ kɛlɛ.
Ɛzakɔɛ lɛ nɛ lɛ kɔ bagɛ ba bala ɛlɛ elukɔ.” Gɛ badɔkpasɛ lɔfɔ gɔgɔɛ nɛ nu kibui nɛ gɛ baa ɖɔ nɛ, ba mɔ obulo nɛ Yakobo nɛ Yohanɛsɛ.
Yesu eklu alɛ exogo klɛ etsre balɛ asɛ, “No nyi sɛ, banɔ nɛ gɛ bee di ansɛ balɛ aŋa bagɛ edi nu Yuɖanɛ nɛa bha, naa trɔ balɛa bha, klɛ balɛ banɔgbla nɛ tsyɛ ba wa balɛ kabhaŋɛŋa nɛ shui kɛxwɛ nɛ balɛa bha.
Wɔnɔ kɛma kɔnɔ kana.
Pɔ wɔnɔ, ɔmɛayɛ nɔɔ nɛ gɛ apɛ asɛ tɛ edzi agbɛgbla nɛ wɔnɔ kishi nɛ, klɛ alasɛ tɛ yɛ edzi axwɛdɛ, klɛ anɔɔ nɛ gɛ apɛ asɛ tɛ edzi otugbanɔ nɛɛ, alasɛ tɛ yɛ edzi balɛ petee axwɛwa.
Alasɛ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ krua tsyɛ adɛ ba sɛ tɛ anɔ aba dɛ kɛxwɛ akɔ yɛ, pɔ yɛ aba sɛ tɛ aba dɛ kɛxwɛ, tɛ ayɛkɔ yɛ ɛkpã nɛ abuya kɛbhɛ nɛ banɔ gelee tɔkpu.” Batimeo Anhũpu Amɔ Anhũ Dɛdanɛ Ɔkɛlɛ bede ku Yeriko.
Gɛ Yesu anɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ, anɛ banɔɛza, nɛ be koeyi nɛ ɔmagbla nɛ mɛ, awɔ̃hũpuelete, Batimeo (gɛ klɛesi nu sɛ Timeos Yeyianyɛ), ezhiaza kidzo nɛ butɔ klɛ eebisi kɛdɔ.
Gɛ enu asɛ Yesu Nazarɛtɛ eyi nɛ yaa fla nɛ, etenɔ ogugu kpɛ asɛ, “Yesu Daviti yɛ Eyi, di mɛ eshutukubui!” Banɔ gelee ba kpa anyɛ klɛ be tsre yɛ asɛ aza kɛdzyɛɛ, pɔ aza kpɛ ogugu nɛ adɛa na sɛ, “Daviti Yɛeyiee, di mɛ eshutukubui!” Yesu adzrɔ klɛ asɛ, “No klu yɛ ɔmɛna.” Kɛlɛso nɛ be tsu ebunɔ awɔ̃hũpuelete, “Mɔ same!
Lɔ kititi!
Eklu wɔ.” Anyɛ nɛ ebu yɛ kabha awidzidze nɛ atɛɛ̃, klɛ alɔ zia ada tɔnɔ Yesu.
Yesu ebisi yɛ asɛ, “Kide wɔ sɛ ɛbhɛtɛ kɔ wɔ?” Anhũ pupuelete na sɛ, “Adɔkasɛ!
Ɛpɛɛ sɛ tɛ ɛmɔ.” Yesu asɛ, “Gavɛ,” “wɔ tɛyɛyɛkɛŋa nɛ tɛ beke wɔ bunya.” Kɛɖɔ nɛ gɛ ɛɖɔa nɛɛ, awɔ̃hũ nɛ agbla danɛ, klɛ alɔ alɛ Yesu kede nɛ kidzo nɛa bha.
Yerusalɛm Tɛtsutsoku Nɛ Kabhaŋɛŋa Gɛ be bunɔ Yerusalɛm pɛ le be ku Betfage nɛ Betania nɛ Olivɛ Butu nɛa bha, Yesu akpɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ tɛabha, etsre alɛ, “Nɔ vɛ ɔmabhli nɛ gɛ oli wɔnɔ otugba nɛ mɛ, onu gɛ no tsoku ɔlɛ mɛ ko, nɔ bɔ mɔ Kitukuagaeyi teli nɛ ohwi mɛ, gɛ anɔnyanɔ aka za yɛa bha edi, no bule yɛ tɛ nɔ yɛkɔ mɛna ɔkɛ̃.
Onu gɛ anɔ teli ebisi wɔnɔ sɛ ‘Kidee pɛ nɔɔ bhɛtɛ ana?’ No tsre yɛ ɔsɛ, ‘Apalete nɛ ya pɛɛ yɛ, klɛ le be tsodzinɛ yɛ amɛna nɛ kibe kplitaa mɛ.’ ” Ba vɛ bada mɔ kitukuagaeyi nɛ kidzo nu tɔ, gɛ ba kpaka nɛ kedunu.
Kibe lɛ gɛ be bule yɛ nɛ, banɔ teli gɛ be li ɔkɛlɛ nee bisi asɛ, “Kide nɔɔ bhɛtɛ, pɛ noo bule kitukuagaeyi nɛ?” Be bu ishu nu ansɛ gɛ Yesu etsre alɛ sɛ ba ɖɔ, klɛ banɔ na kɔ balɛ kidzo klɛ ba shɛ.
Gɛ ba yɛkɔ kitukuagaeyi nɛ amɛna Yesu pɛ ba yɛkɔ balɛ bawidzidze nɛ atrɔ yɛa bha beke, Yesu ewoku yɛa bha.
Banɔ gelee be bule balɛ bawidzidze nɛ elu kidzo nɛa bha, klɛ beteli ba yɛkɔ awɔlakpa gɛ be dzyini edenɔ ayakpa mɛ nɛ elu kesi akɔ yɛ.
Ba gɛ be putɔ nɛ bagɛ balɛ yɛe de naa kpɛ igugu asɛ, “Hosiana!” “Ba yula anɔ nɛ gɛ aaba nɛ Apalete nɛ kinyi mɛ!” “Bayula bulɔ aka Daviti bukusiŋɛŋa nɛ gɛ buba ba!” “Hosiana nɛ Ɔɖɛɖamakɔdɛ!” Yesu eku Yerusalɛm klɛ avɛ Kpayavu nɛ mɛ.
Elu awɔ̃ edi kɛdɔnyɛdɔ, pɔ gɛ keli kefli bele so, ekoeyi nɛ yɛ banɔkpɛkpɛ lɔfɔntɛabha nɛ avɛ Betani.
Yesu Akɛka Badɔdɛ Nɛ Ebu Nɛ Busɔlɛvu Nɛm Kelizɛza nɛ gɛ baa shɛ nɛ Betani nɛ, Bubhɛ baa yi Yesu.
Amɔ kabhɔ nɛ kalɛ awulakpa teli asɛsɛ nɛ odzidzekɔ, avɛ asɛ tɛ ede di asɛ eyuyu teli akpasɛ ɔlɛ mɛ dza.
Gɛ eku ɔlɛ ɔbha nɛ, awulakpa ko amɔ, alasɛ kibee lɛ nɛ dɛ nu osi nɛ kiyu be.
Klɛ etsre osi na sɛ, “Anɔnyanɔ atɛa ŋa wɔ eyuyu denɔ ɔtsɔ̃ nɛ ɔyɛkɔ vɛ nɔ.” Klɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ be nu kibui nɛ gɛ aɖɔ.
Gɛ be de ku Yerusalɛm nɛɛ, Yesu etsoku busɔlɛvu buka nɛ mɛ, klɛ akpa bagɛ aba dɛ kɛdɔ anɛ bagɛ bee dzi dɔ nɛ ɔkɛlɛ.
Etsyina bagɛ balɛ atsrakɛ ehoeyi nɛ baa kplɔ̃ nɛ ekumu, anɛ bagɛ bala dɛ bagɔgɔwi nɛ bugbu dzidze petee ekumu.
Adɛ kɔ kidzo sɛ anɔnyanɔ aflanɔ kɛdɔ dɛdɛ kanyaka nɛ busɔlɛvu buka nɛ mɛ.
Gɛ aakasɛ balɛ kɛdɔ, aɖɔ asɛ, “Sɛ ba ŋlɔmɛ elu asɛ, “ ‘Bee klu mɛ bupa nɛ asɛ amadi nɛ petee kpaya oklukɔ?’ Pɔ nɔ yɛkɔ ɔklɛ ɔbhɛtɛ ‘bezi ɔzakɔ.’ ” Gɛ Kpayaɔzakɔanɔ anɛ eshãdɔkasɛ nɛ be nu ana, ba kpa kidzo pɛ nɛ yɛ shu kɔ tiyiyi, alasɛ bee si yɛ kifu, alasɛ yɛ kɛdɔ kɛkasɛ nɛ yinɔ banɔɛza nɛ petee.
Gɛ owulago nɛ ɔna, be koeyi nɛ ɔmagbla nɛ mɛ.
Kabhɔ Tsitsi Nɛ kɛvulɔ nɛ mɛ, gɛ baa fla nɛ, ba mɔ kabhɔ nɛ gɛ ketsi denɔ kalɛ igu nɛ mɛ.
Petro abaka klɛ etsre Yesu asɛ, “Adɔkasɛ, di!
Kabhɔ nɛ gɛ ɔɖɔɛbuiɔkpɛ nɛ ke tsi!” Yesu aɖɔ sɛ, “Yɛkɛ Kpaya kabha ɔŋa.” “Itsre nɔ kibuigba sɛ, onu gɛ anɔ teli ebe tsre butu nɛ asɛ, ‘Vɛ tɛ ɔdɔ tɛɛku aƒu mɛ,’ klɛ ɔyɛkɛ ɔŋa nɛ idzyim sɛ kɛ gɛ aɖɔ nɛ kɛ ba bhɛtɛ nɛ, kɛ ba ba klɛ mɛ kɔ wɔ.
Klɛso nɛ itsre wɔnɔ sɛ, kɛdɔnyɛdɔ gɛ wɔ anɔ obo klu Kpaya obisi nɛ, yɛkɛ ɔŋa sɛ ɔtɛ yɛkɛ kɛlɛ, klɛ kɛba dzi wɔɛ yɛ.
So, onu gɛ oli pɛ oklukpaya, pɛ anɔ teli kibui zizi kpasɛ wɔ ishu mɛ, yɛ kɔ otsye yɛ, tɛ wɔ aka nɛ owũsise tsyɛ ayɛkɔ wɔ buzizi nɛ etsye wɔ.” [Pɔ onu gɛ nɔ dɛ yɛkɔ otsye, klɛ wɔnɔ aka nɛ owũsise tsyɛ atɛ ba yɛkɔ wɔnɔ buzizi nɛ etsye nɔ.]
Yesu Kabhaŋɛŋa Nɛ Shu Ebui Bibisi Be ze be ku Yerusalɛm, klɛ gɛ Yesu aaga nɛ busɔlɛvu buka nɛ mɛ, kpayaɔzakɔanɔ anɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ anɛ beshishe ba ga ebunɔ yɛ.
Be bisi Yesu asɛ, “Kabhaŋɛŋa ɖuweɖu mɛ ɔyɛkɔ bhɛtɛ ebui anɛ?” “Klɛ anee yakɔ wɔ kabhaŋɛŋa nɛ asɛ tɛ ɔbhɛtɛ ebui anɛ?” Yesu ebu aɖɔ sɛ, “Ɛba bisi wɔnɔ kibui tirikpo.
Nó bui lɛ nu ɔkɔ mɛ, klɛ ɛba tsre wɔnɔ ɔkɛlɛ gɛ idenɔ kabhaŋɛŋa pɛ ɛbhɛtɛ ebuia nɛ petee.
Yohanɛsɛ bunikpɛkpɛ nɛ, owũsise bu de pɛnɔɔ banɔdzyrame ɔkɔ?
Nɔ tsre mɛ!” Ba nyɛna kibui nɛ aglɔm klɛ laa ɖɔ asɛ, “Bu ɖɔ sɛ, ‘Kpaya ɔkɔ nɛɛ,’ ebe bisi asɛ, ‘Kɛlɛ kide so pɛ bu dɛ yɛkɛ yɛ kabha ŋa?’ Pɔ onu gɛ buɖɔ sɛ, ‘Kide banɔdzyrame ɔkɔ’....” (Bee si banɔ, alasɛ anɔnyanɔ ayɛkɛ aŋa sɛ Yohanɛsɛ nɛ atɔnu yɛ edzi.)
So bebu klɛ nu akɔ Yesu asɛ, “Bu tinyi.” Yesu asɛ, “Mɛ tsyɛ ɛtɛ ba tsre wɔnɔ ɔkɔ nɔɔ nɛ gɛ idenɔ mɛ kabhaŋɛŋa nɛ gɛ ɛyɛkɔ bhɛtɛ ebui nɛ nɔ.”
Kɛkpalɛ Nɛ Bagɛ Bedi Buya Kabha Shu Yesu etenɔ kaɖɔ ɖɔ tsre alɛ ganɔ akpalɛ mɛ, “Anyɛ teli adɛ vãyɛ̃ buya.
Abhɔ kidri akana buya, ebu kizi kɔ bulu nɛ tɛkɛka klɛ edzu opokɔvu.
Klɛ ayɛkɔ buya nɛ akpɛ ahwɛ kɔ bayadɛ teli klɛ aga kidzo.
Nɛ kɛdɔɛ gɔ be, akpɛ axwɛdɛ teli asɛsɛ bagɛ balɛ ahwɛ mɛ buya nɛ kpasɛ nɛ asɛ, ba yɛkɛ eyuyu teli edenɔ buya nɛ mɛ amɛna yɛ.
Pɔ be vu yɛ, be tu yɛ klɛ ba kɛka yɛ ashɛ̃nɔ nɛ ahwɛ kpɛkpa.
Klɛ aza kpɛ axwɛdɛ bhlatɔ asɛsɛ balɛ, anyɛ alɛlɛ nɛ xũ be hu yɛ kɛdɔ nɛ kɛtɔkpu, klɛ ba kpɛ yɛ butsɔ.
Aza kpɛ abhlatɔ, klɛ yalɛlɛ nɛ be yi yɛ.
Aza kpɛ banɔ gelee bhlatɔ, balɛlɛ nɛ mɛ beteli tsyɛ be tua lɛ, beteli be yi alɛ.
“Anɔ terikpo aka gɔ gɛ aba kpɛ, gɛ enu yɛ eyianyɛ nɛ gɛ adɛmɛ yɛ bui.
Aba kpɛ yɛ gɔgɔɛ, klɛ aɖɔ asɛ, ‘Baa yɛkɛ yɛ ansɛ mɛ eyi.’ “Pɔ baxwɛwa nɛ aɖɔ nɛ aglɔmɛ asɛ, ‘Agɛ yɛ abaa za yɛ kinyi mɛ nɛ naa.
Nɔ ba nɔ kɔ lɔ yi yɛ, tɛ ɔŋakɔ nɛ obo dzi bulɔ yɛ.’ So be vui klɛ be yi yɛ, klɛ ba yɛkɔ atɛ̃ akpɛ buya nɛe de.
“Kidee klɛ lɛ sɛ tɛ Ayalete nɛ abhɛtɛ?
Aba ba ebe yi baxwɛwa lɛlɛ klɛ aba yɛkɔ buya nɛ akpɛ ahwɛ kɔ banɔ bhlatɔ.
Nɔ kɔ kla kibui nɛ Kpaya keplukpa nɛ mɛ odi sɛ, “ ‘Kɛklãgbu nɛ gɛ bevudzu na dɛ pɛɛ nɛ klɛ ba dzi ɔxãkɔɛ kɛklãgbu.
Apalete nɛ ya bhɛtɛ kɛlɛ kana, ki yinɔ lɔ nɛ bulɔ kɛdɔmumɔ nu.’ ” Klɛ banɔ na kpa kidzo pɛɛ nɛ yɛ shu kɔ tɛvuvu, alasɛ benyi asɛ balɛ shu akpɛ kɛkpalɛ.
Pɔ bee si banɔɛza nɛ ɔkɛlɛ nɛ kifu, so ba shɛnahwɛ yɛ shu klɛ ba shɛ.
Kadzyɔ Kɔ Kaɛzaro Klɛe de nɛ ba kpɛ Farisianɛ anɛ Heroɖesɛanɛ teli sɛ tɛ be de vu Yesu aganɔ yɛ ebui ɖuɖɔ shu.
Ba ebe ku yɛ ɔbha klɛ la ɖɔ asɛ, “Adɔkasɛ, bunyi sɛ onu anɔ gɛ ɔna.
Anɔdzyrame ataa na wɔ tsyina, alasɛ wɔ otoo di banɔ nɛ di gɛ be nu nɛ ɔkɔ, pɔ ɔkasɛ Kpaya kidzo nɛ kɛgbɛagba nɛ nu.
Kɛbɔ sɛ tɛ ba kɔ kadzyɔ Kaɛzaro pɛnɔɔ kɛmɛtã?
Bu buya pɛnɔɔ bɔtɛ buya?” Pɔ Yesu enyi balɛ butsutsɔmɔ.
Ebisi alɛ asɛ, “Kide so pɛ nɔ tɔ kɛgba kɔ mɛ?” “Nɔ yɛkɔ wɔnɔ kɔba nɛ tili ɔmɛna tɛ idi.” Ba yɛkɔ kɔba nɛ amɛna, klɛ ebisi alɛ asɛ, “Anee kɛtɔkpu klɛ tsri yɛa bha?
Klɛ anee kɛdɔ ŋuŋlɔmɛ klɛ tsri?” Be bu klɛ nu asɛ, “Kaɛzaro yɛ.” Klɛ Yesu etsre balɛ asɛ, “Kɛgɛ nu Kaɛzaro yɛ tɛ nɔ yɛkɔ kɔ Kaɛzaro tɛ nɔ yɛkɔ kɛgɛ nu Kpaya yɛ nɛ ɔkɔ Kpaya.” Klɛ kɛ bhɛtɛ alɛ bi.
Adzɛ Gbɛgbanɔ Nɛ Kɛlɔwi Ɔkɛlɛ Sarusianɛ, gɛ baa ɖɔ sɛ tɛlulɔ ma, na ba tɔnɔ yɛ nɛ tɛbibisi.
“Adɔkasɛ, ” “Mose aŋlɔmɛ ɔhsã kɔ bulɔ sɛ onu anɔadzya etsi alɔ yɛedzini gɛ yɛ nɛ yɛ ba dɛ mɔ eyinyeyi, alasɛ tɛ adzya nɛ gɛ alɛ nɛ ayɛkɔ adzɛ nɛ agbanɔ tɛ ba mɔ beyi akɔ agɛ eti tsi.
Ɔtsɔ̃ nɛ badzya tiegene teli ba za.
Atɛtɔpu na gbanɔ adzɛ klɛ ebe tsi eyi mamɔ-mamɔ.
Abhla na yɛkɔ adzɛ nɛ agbanɔ, klɛ yɛ tsyɛ ebe tsi, adɛ mɔ eyi nɛ adzɛ nɛ shu.
Atramɛ nɛ tsyɛ kana kɛ za kɔ yɛ.
Kɛgba nɛ, banyɛ tiegene nɛ petee akanyaka adɛ mɔ eyi elu.
Gugɔɛ nɛ, adzɛ nɛ tsyɛ ebe tsi.
Nɛ balɛ kɛlɔwi nɛa bha ane yɛedzini adzɛ nɛ ebe dzi, gɛ balɛ petee ba tɛ gbanɔ adzɛ nɛ edi?” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Ganɛ kitoe bui nɔ zɔ ɖɔa, alasɛ no ti nyi Kpaya kibuieplukpa ɔdɔgɔsɛ yɛ kemi?
Onu gɛ be tsitsi nɛ ba lɔ, aglɔ gbɛgbanɔ atɛa za, ɔdɔgɔsɛ ba yɛkɔ anɔ akɔ sɛ bagbanɔ, baba za ansɛ Kpaya baxwɛdɛ nɛ owũsise.
Ɔtsɔ̃ nɛɛ, nɛ anɔ tsitsi tɛlulɔ shu, nɔ dɛ kla nɛ Mose keplukpa nɛ mɛ, denɔ yɛ ayakpa mɛ zɛza shu, nɛ kana gɛ Kpaya aɖɔ etsre yɛ asɛ, ‘Mɛ nu Abraham Kpaya, Isakɛ Kpaya, anɛ Yakobo Kpaya,’ Edinu betsitsi nɛ Kpaya, pɔ be lulu na yɛ enu.
Nɔ ta kesi tsutsɔmɔ tsɔmɔ!” Ɔshã Gbɛgbla Dɛ Ɔshãdɔkasɛ nɛ teli ebe nu kana gɛ bedzi atsrakɛ ebui nɛ akpɛ aglɔ nɛ mɛ.
Gɛ amɔ sɛ Yesu akɔ balɛ kibui nu bubu dzyɔgo nɛ, ebisi yɛ asɛ, “Nɛ ɛshã nɛ petee mɛ, oɖuweɖu ɔlɛ ɖamadɛ ɔkanyaka?” Yesu ebui lɛ bunu asɛ, “Ɔgɛ ɔlɛ ɖamadɛ,” “ɔlɛ nu sɛ, O Izraɛl, ‘Taatɔ, Apalete blɔ Kpaya, Apalete terikpoo ko enu.
Dɛmɛnɛ Apalete wɔ Kpaya nɛ wɔ idzyi petee, anɛ wɔ ɔfufɔɛ anɛ wɔ kɛtɔkpumɛ anɛ wɔ kemi nɛ petee.’ Ɔbhla nɛ ɔlɛ onu sɛ, ‘Dɛmɛnɛ wɔhayɛ ansɛ wɔ ishu.’ Ɔshã gbɛgbla kanyaka ɔvɔ ma gɛ lɔ ɖama ɔdɛ ɛnɛɛ.” Anyɛ nɛ ebui lɛ nu asɛ, adɔkasɛ, “Ɔɖɔ kɛlɛ mɔmɔ,” “Wɔ kibui nɛ na gɛ ɔɖɔ sɛ Kpaya nɛ terikpoo ko enu klɛ akanyaka ava ma ɔyɛkɔ dɛ yɛ.
Tɛ ɔdɛmɛnɛ yɛ nɛ wɔ idzyi petee, nɛ wɔ kibuiesi nunu petee, anɛ wɔ bugɛganɛ petee, tɛ ɔdɛmɛnɛ wɔhayɛ ansɛ wɔnahwɛ ishu, kɛɖama dɛ ɔŋa nɛ butã tɛkukɔ Kpaya.” Gɛ Yesu amɔ sɛ anyɛ nɛ ebu kibui nɛ bunu mɔmɔ nɛ, etsre yɛ asɛ, “Wɔ ɔdɛ vɛ odzidzekɔ nɛ Kpaya bukusi ɔŋakɔ nɛ mɛ.” Klɛ denɔ kibelɛ nɛ ɔyɛkɔ ɔvɛnɔ nɛɛ, anɔnyanɔ adaa na yɛ kibuinyɛbui bu bisi.
Anee Yɛ Eyi Yɛ Enu Kristo?
Kibee lɛ nɛ gɛ Yesu akasɛ kɛdɔ nɛ busɔlɛvu ka nɛ mɛ, ebisi asɛ, “Kɛlɛ lɛ lɛ so pɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ nɛ baɖɔ sɛ Kristo nɛ enu Daviti yɛeyi?
Deviti nahwɛ nɛ, yɛ kaɖɔɖuɖɔ ganɔ Ɔfufɔɛ Dzyɔgo nɛa bha nɛ, ebu aɖɔ sɛ, “ ‘Apalete na ɖɔ etsre mɛ Apalete nɛ asɛ, “Za mɛ kɛŋa nɛ mɛ ɔdɔ nanɔ kibee lɛ gɛ ɛba yɛkɔ baga dɛ pɛɛ wɔ nɛ ɛkpɛ wɔ butsrukpɔ kesi.” Daviti nahwɛ eklu yɛ asɛ, ‘Apalete.’ Klɛɛ dzi Yesu eze be dzi yɛ eyi?” Banɔɛza nɛ bata yɛ kibui nɛ batɔ nɛ same.
Nɛ yɛ kɛdɔ kɛkasɛ nɛ mɛ Yesu aɖɔ asɛ, “No vu awɔ̃hũ nɛ ɛshãbadɔkasɛ.
Kinu balɛ tɛpɛpɛ sɛ tɛ baza balɛ bawi dzidze nɛ mɛ tɛ baza mɔ balɛ asɛnɔ nɛ budzi nɛ mɛ, tɛ bamɔ ɛzakɔ gbɛgbla nɛ ixogokɔvu nɛ mɛ, nɛ kinyibgla ɛzakɔ nɛ kɛdɔŋakɔ.
Ba yɛɛ bagɛ be tsi banyɛ nɛ bapa, klɛ tɛ ba yɛkɔ akasɛ ishu so nɛ, baa za Kpayakuklu kabha dzrororo.
Banɔ balɛlɛ nɛɛ di nɛ ba la mɔ batɔtɛtɛta adɛ petee.” Anyɛtsi Kɛdɔ Kukɔ Yesu aza kesi nɛ ɔklɛ gɛ kɛdɔ kukɔ nɛɛ vɛ kabha nɛ kapɛ bhla, klɛ evu awɔ̃hũ nɛ banɔɛza nɛ kɛdɔkukɔ nɛ busɔlɛvu kakputɔ nɛ mɛ.
Behoeyilete gelee ba kpɛ kɔba gbɛgbla nɛ kɛdɔ dzyudzyɔ kesugba nɛ mɛ.
Pɔ anyɛtsi etsyutsyuini teli, kɔba bhli tɛabha ko evunɔ aba za ansɛ kapleapɛ aba kpɛ kɛkpɛtɛ nɛm.
Gɛ Yesu eklu yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ amɛna yɛ ɔbha nɛ, klɛ etsre alɛ asɛ, “Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, Anyɛtsi etsyutsyuini nɛ kɔba gɛ akpɛ nɛ kakputɔ nɛ mɛ na ŋaedzi adɛ anɔnyanɔa yɛ.
Banɔ nɛ petee gɛ bakɔ kɛdɔ nɛ balɛ ehoeyi gelee zɛza anɔ ahwɛ nu, pɔ nɛ yɛ kitsyui nɛ nu, ayɛkɔ yɛ kɛdɔ nɛ gɛ kɛ lɛ yɛ ahwɛ nɛ ada kpɛ, kɛ gɛ kɛlɛ shu aba za nɛ petee nɛ kiwi lɛlɛ nɛm.”
Kɛdɔmumɔ Anɛ Kanɔ Nɛ Tɛbibekem Kibe lɛ nɛ gɛ Yesu ekoeyi nɛ busɔlɛvu nɛ mɛ, yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ teli etsre yɛ asɛ, “Di, Adɔkasɛ!
Kide aklãgbu alɛ nu agbɛgbla nɛɛ di!
Kide bevu balɛ enu bagbɛgbla nɛ di!” Yesu ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Sɛ nɔɔ mɔ bevu gbɛgbla nɛ petee?” “Batɛ ba shɛnahwɛ kɛklãgbu kanyaka atrɔ klɛ ɔhayɛa bha gɛ ba tɛ ba tsɛ atɛ̃ɛ.” Gɛ Yesu ezhiedzi Olivɛ Butu nɛa bha nɛ busɔlɛvu nɛa pɛ bhla, Petro, Yakobo, Yohanɛsɛ anɛ Andrɛasɛ be bisi Yesu nɛ tɛkpukpumɛ asɛ, “Tsre bulɔ, kibee nɔ nɛ gɛ ebuia nɛ aba ba klɛ mɛ?
Klɛ kide gɛ ba dzi kɛdɔmumɔ sɛ, kibe nɛ kɛna gɛ ebuia nɛ aba ba klɛ mɛ?” Yesu etsre alɛ asɛ, “No lu awɔ̃ sɛ tɛ anɔnyanɔ atɛ ba wɛɛ wɔnɔ.
Banɔ gelee baba ba nɛ mɛ kinyi mɛ, baba ɖɔ asɛ, ‘mɛ nu yɛ,’ klɛ la ba wɛɛ banɔ gelee.
Kibelɛ gɛ nɔ kpa buyu kɛdɔ nu, anɛ buyushu buɖɔ nu, nɔ tɛ hwa.
Ebui alɛ nɛɛ di nɛɛ ala sɛ tɛ laba klɛmɛ, pɔ kanɔ nɛ obekekɔ nɛ ɔkɔlɛ gɛ ɔbɔ ba.
Kɛmadi ba lɔ kititi nɛ kɛmadi shu, klɛ bukusiɔŋakɔ ɔbɔ lɔ kititi nɛ bukusiɔŋakɔ shu.
Busukpa ba hwa nɛ ɛzakɔ gelee, klɛ bubhɛ ba dɔ.
Alɛlɛ nɛ petee lenu ansɛ gɛ ɛyatɛtã kpɛ ayamunɔ kesi.
“No di wɔnɔ shua bha.
Baa yɛkɔ wɔnɔ akpɛ ahwɛ kɔ bamani klɛ le be tu wɔnɔ nɛ ixogokɔvu nɛm.
Mɛ so, nɔ bɔ wɛ̃ nɛ bekusi anɛ ɛshãletegbla nɛ amɛ, klɛ no bo dzi ansɛ bebuimɔɖɔ kɔ balɛ.
Klɛ alasɛ tɛ baɖɔ Kibui Dzyɔgo nɛ akpɛ otugba nɛ amadi nɛ petee mɛ.
Kibe nɔɔ nɛ gɛ be vu wɔnɔ avɛnɔ kebhui nɛ, nɔ tɛ ganɛ awɔ̃ oputɔnɔ nɛ kibui nɔɔ nɛ gɛ nɔ bɔ ɖɔ.
Nɔ ɖɔ kibui nɔɔ nɛ gɛ ba kpɛ wɔnɔ nu nɛ kibee lɛ nɛ mɛ, alasɛ ganɛ wɔnɔ ɖɔ kaɖɔ, Ɔfufɔɛ Dzyɔgo ɔlɛ ɔɖɔ.
“Adzya aba yɛkɔ yɛadzya akpɛ ahwɛ kɔ butsi, klɛ aka aba yɛkɔ yɛ eyi akpɛ ahwɛ.
Beyi baba lɔ kititi nɛ balɛ eni nɛ aka shu, klɛ la ba kɔ sɛ be yi balɛ.
Banɔ petee baba lɔ kititi nɛ wɔnɔ shu akpɛ mɛ so, pɔ aanɔ nɛ gɛ aza mahwa-mahwa ɔyɛkɔ vɛnɔ tɛbibeke mɛ nɛ, aba mɔ tɛyɛyɛkɛ.
“Kibee lɛ gɛ nɔɔ mɔ ‘ebusobui nɛ gɛ mɛna tɛkɛkɛka’ gɛ kɔ sɛ ɔdɔ za ɔklɛ gɛ ɔklɛayɛ odinu—kɔ adɔkla nɛ enu klɛesi—klɛ tɛ bakɔ sɛ bagɛ balɛ Yuɖia nɛ ba kpɛsi avɛ betu nɛa bha.
Nɔ tɛ kɔ anɔnyanɔ gɛ etsri yɛ ovutɔ nɛ ezhi aba kesi, ɔdɔgɔsɛ etsoku buvu nɛ mɛ sɛ tɛ ada yɛkɔ kɛdɔnyɛdɔ ebu eyinɔ.
Nɔ tɛ kɔ anɔnyanɔ gɛ alɛ ayakpa mɛ nɛ, etsodzi aba bupa mɛ asɛ, abaa yɛkɔ yɛ kabhawi.
Klɛɛ gɛganɛ lɛ ba za kɔ bayamunɔ anɛ bamumɔvuvɔ nɛ kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ!
No klukpaya sɛ tɛ kibee lɛ nɛ tɛ dzi bublɔɛ be, alasɛ ewi alɛlɛ nɛ be dzi ewi tsutsɔmɔ gɛ alɛ kidi aka za edi, denɔ gɛ Kpaya ebu kanɔ pɛ kakpɛ kesi ɔbɔ nanɔ ɔtsɔ̃, klɛ butsutsɔmɔ kanyaka tɛa za ansɛ bulɛlɛ nɛ di.
Otɔsɛ Apalete nɛ adɛ tsɛ ewi alɛlɛ nɛa bha nɛ, anɔdzyrame agɛ ta gɔ.
Pɔ akpɛ yɛ bekuklu nɛ gɛ eti klu nɛ so, ebhui ewi nɛa bha.
Nɛ kibee lɛ nɛ mɛ anɔnyanɔ etsre wɔ asɛ, ‘Di, Kristo nɛ naa!’ Ɔdɔgɔsɛ asɛ, ‘Di, yɛ eli ɔklɛa nɛ!’ Tɛ yɛkɛ klɛa bha ɔŋa.
Alasɛ Kristo itroayɛ anɛ batɔnu itroa yɛ nɛ be koeyi klɛ ba baa bhɛtɛ ebuimumɔ anɛ ebuiyiyinɔ anɔ, sɛ tɛ ba yɛkɔ awɛɛ bagɛ be kulu, onu gɛ kɛɛ ba za bɔbɔɛbɔɛ.
So no di ishua bha, ɛtɛ ɖɔ kibuinyɛbui tsre wɔnɔ kpɛ otugba.
“Pɔ nɛ ewi alɛlɛ nɛ mɛ, nɛ butɔ lɛlɛ nɛe de, “ ‘kiwi nɛ ba dɔ otumu, klɛ wele tsyɛ atɛ ba tã; Awɛ̃wɛ̃ na ba wɔlɛ denɔ kɛlɛm, klɛ owũsise mɛ dɔ nɛ ba hwa.’ “Nɛ kibee lɛ nɛ mɛ banɔ aba mɔ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ gɛ aaba denɔ ɔmunɔ nɛ mɛ nɛ kemi gɛganɛɛ nɛ same mɛ.
Klɛ aba kpɛ yɛ kpaya baxwɛdɛ klɛ la baa ba ebe xogo yɛ bagɛ eklu edenɔ kanɔ nɛ bupɛ tɔlɛ, denɔ kesukpa nɛ ibekekɔ ɔdɔ tɔnɔ iwũsise nɛ ibekekɔ.
“Ɔtsɔ̃ nɛ nɔ kpasɛ kɛdɔ denɔ kabhɔ osi nɛ shu, kibelɛ nɛ gɛ ɔlɛ ɛshɛ nɛ nya wɛ̃ avuvɔ klɛ awulakpa nɛ anya tɔɛ ko, no ti sɛ subha kɛdɔbe nɛ tsuu ba.
Kɛlɛso tsyɛ, nɔɔ mɔ ebuia nɛ petee gaa ba klɛ mɛ nɛ, no ti sɛ kibe nɛ tsuu ba, nɛ kedunu nɛ kpɔ̃.
Itsre nɔ kɛgba nɛ sɛ, tɛmumɔɛ nɛ mɛ tɛ baa ba fla ɔdɔ tɔnɔ kibe lɛ gɛ ebuia nɛ petee aba ba kɛlɛ mɛ.
Owũsise anɛ kesukpa nɛ bunu ba fla, pɔ mɛ ebui nɛ atɛ ba fla di.
Kiwi Anɛ Ɔɖa Nɛ Mɛ Ɔma Tititim “Anɔnyanɔ eti nyi kibui edenɔ kiwi lɛ nɛ shu pɛ ɔdɔgɔsɛ ɔɖa nɛ mɛ, kpayaxwɛdɛ nɛ owũsise tsyɛ beti nyi, pɛ yɛ Eyi nɛ yɛ ebe ti, pɔ Aka nɛ ko.
No di ishua bha!
Nɔ za nɛ awɔ̃!
No ti nyi kibelɛ nɛ gɛ ɔɖa lɛlɛ nɛ mɛ ɔbɔ ba.
Edzi ansɛ anyɛ teli gɛ ekoeyi aavɛ, klɛ ayɛkɔ yɛ bupa nɛ akpɛ yɛ baxwɛdɛ nɛ ahwɛ, akanyaka nɛ yɛ kɛxwɛ, klɛ etsre agɛ eli kedunu na sɛ epo ɔkɛlɛ.
“Klɛ so nɛ zo po alasɛ oti nyi kibe nɔɔ nɛ gɛ apalete nɛ aba ba, tɛ owulago mɛo, elishiteti mɛo, ɔkukɔ tɛ bubɔ mɛo, tɛ olizatɔ mɛo, oti nyi.
Onu gɛ kɛɛ ba klɛ mɛ sɛ aba kɛba tili nɛɛ, tɛ kɔ amɔ wɔ sɛ ɔdɔ tra.
Kɛ gɛ itsre wɔ, klɛ ko mɛɛ tsre anɔnyanɔ, “Zanawɔ̃!”
Ba Sra Bubɔ Kɔ Yesu Nɛ Betani Gɛ agɔ ansɛ ewi tabha ko tɛ Yuɖanɛ ba ŋa balɛ Ɔmɛwi gɛ nu Tɛfɛflãwi nɛ Gbɛgbɛvu gɛ ba dɛ kpɛ lɛ bunɛyekedɔ kiwi nɛ, ɛshãdɔkasɛ anɛ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ nɛ baa pɛ bushɛdzo nɔɔ nɛa bha gɛ la ba ga pɛ ba ebe vu Yesu pɛ le be yi yɛ.
“Pɔ basɛ ganɛ kiwi ŋɛŋa nɛ mɛ,” “odibhi banɔ na ba kpɛ ebla.” Kibee lɛ nɛ gɛ aza Betani nɛ, aza ŋa kɛdɔ nɛ anyɛ teli gɛ bee klu asɛ Simɔnɛ gɛ enu bunya dzɛdzãelete nɛ bupa mɛ nɛ, adzɛ teli aba ɔklɛ nɛ bubɔ huhuhu ŋɛŋa kedzi tuli gɛ kpasɛ aklãgbu kɛbɔplui mɛ.
Adzɛ nɛ adanɛ bubɔ klɛ ayɛkɔ abalɛ akpɛ Yesu ada nɛ mɛ petee.
Banɔ teli gɛ baza ɔklɛ nɛ, kibui nɛ dɛ za balɛ buli so nɛ, baa ɖɔ nɛ aglɔ mɛ asɛ, “Kide bubɔ zizi ebui naa?
Ba taa dɛ bubɔ nɛ kedziŋɛŋa, gɛ aba fla kɛgɔ zɛzɛ bhɛ pɛ la ba yɛkɔ edi bee tsyuitsyuini nɛa bha nɔ.” So nɛ, ba kpa adzɛ nɛ tsutsɔmɔɔ tsɔmɔ.
Yesu asɛ, “nɔ shɛnahwɛ yɛ shu mɔ.” “Kidee pɛ nɔɔ kpɛ yɛ bunuhu?
Abhɛtɛ kibui pupudi amɛna mɛ ɔkɔe.
Betsyutsyuini nɛ xũ nɛ balɛ wɔnɔ ɔbha kibenyɛbe, gɛ nɔ bɔ plɛnɔa lɛ onu gɛ nɔɔ pɛɛ.
Pɔ mɛ ɛtɛ ba za wɔnɔ bha kibenyɛbe.
Adzɛ nɛ abhɛtɛ kɛgɛ aba naa bhɛtɛ.
Edzuawɔ̃ asra bubɔ kɔ mɛ tɛvuvubɔ.
Itsre nɔ kɛgba sɛ, ɔkɔnyɔkɔ gɛ ba ɖɔ Kpayɛbui nɛ kanɔ nɛ mɛ petee, kɛgɛ adzɛ nɛ abhɛtɛ ba ba ɖɔɛ lɛ tsyɛ, ayɛkɔ abaka yɛbui nɔ.” Ɔklɛ Yuɖas Iskarɔtɛ, gɛ enu Yesu Kɛfɔntɛabha nɛ teli nɛ ashɛ̃ atɔnɔ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ nɛ asɛ tɛ ada kpɛ Yesu ahwɛ.
Same ku kpayaɔzakɔanɔ gɛ be nu ana, klɛ batrɔ sɛ tɛ ba kɔ yɛ ehoeyi.
So, abaa pɛɛ kidzo nɔɔ nɛa bha gɛ aba ga pɛ aba yɛkɔɛ akpɛahwɛ kɔa lɛ.
Apalete Nɛ Owulago Kɛdɔŋɛŋa Nɛ Gbɛgbɛvu manyɛnya-manyɛnyawi nɛ kiwi tutɔpu nɛa bha nɛ, gɛ ki nu bugu sɛ tɛ bebhui Tɛfɛflãwi obhoshieyi, Yesu badɔkpasɛ nɛ bisi yɛ asɛ, “Fakɔ ɔpɛɛ sɛ tɛ bu vɛ da bala kɔ wɔ kɔ Tɛfɛflãwi nɛ tɛ ŋɛŋa?” Klɛso nɛɛ akpɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ tɛabha, etsre alɛ asɛ, “No tsoku ɔmagbla nɛm, klɛ anyɛ teli gɛ etuku bunie tsukpu aba tsyanɛ wɔnɔ.
Nɔ za yɛe de.
Nɔ ɖɔ tsre apalete nɛ bupa nɛ mɛ gɛ anyɛ nɛ ebe tsoku nɔ sɛ, ‘Adɔkasɛ nɛ yɛ ebisi asɛ: Mɛ ɔyakɔ vu nɛ xɔ̃, ɔkɛlɛ gɛ ɛba ŋa Tɛfɛflãwi nɛ mɛ badɔkpasɛ?’ Aba kasɛ wɔnɔ kabha buvugbla tuli, gɛ batɛ bala elu.
Bhɛtɛ tɛbɛbala kɔɔ lɔ nɛ ɔklɛ.” Badɔkpasɛ nɛ ashɛ̃, ede tsoku ɔmagbla nɛm klɛ ba da mɔ ebui nɛ ansɛ gɛ Yesu eti tsrea lɛ.
So ba bala Tɛfɛflãwi nɛ dɔ ŋɛŋa.
Gɛ owulago nɛ ɔna, Yesu ebe ku nɛ yɛ Kɛfɔntɛabha.
Kibee lɛ gɛ bedzi pɛ baa ŋa kɛdɔ nɛɛ, Yesu asɛ, “Itsre wɔnɔ kɛgba, wɔnɔ mɛayɛ teli aba yɛkɔ mɛ akpɛ ahwɛ edzi aŋa kɛdɔ nɛ mɛ.” Badɔkpasɛ nɛ shuku, klɛ terikpo terikpo ba ɖɔ tsre yɛ asɛ, “Ɛdɛ yɛkɛ ŋa sɛ mɛ.” Ebui lɛ nu asɛ, “Kɛfɔntɛabha nɛ ɔmɛayɛ teli,” “agɛ yɛa kpɛahwɛ kesugba tierikpo mɛ nɛ mɛ.
Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ aba shɛ ansɛ gɛ ba ŋlɔmɛ elu nɛ yɛ shu.
Pɔ butɔ kɔ aanɔ nɛ gɛ yɛ aba kpɛ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ ahwɛ!
Aba pɛ̃ kɔ anɔa lɛlɛ nɛ adɛ onu gɛ ba dɛ mɔɛ.” Kibe lɛ gɛ be dzia ŋa kɛdɔ nɛɛ, Yesu ayɛkɔ gbɛgbɛvu, ehu ahwɛ klɛ aya lɛ, klɛ ayɛkɔ akɔ yɛ badɔkpasɛ, aɖɔ asɛ, “Nɔ tã yɛ; mɛ ishuidzya nɛ lɛ.” Ɔkɛlɛ ayɛkɔ kantse, ehu ahwɛ, klɛ ayɛkɔ akɔa lɛ, klɛ balɛ petee awɛ̃.
Etsre alɛ asɛ, “Mɛ onugbu nyɛnya dzyosu nɛ naa, gɛ be bu abalɛ lu kɔ banɔ gelee.” “Itsre nɔ kɛgba, ɛtia fla wɛ̃ vãyɛ̃ eyuyu mɛ ni ɔdɔ na nɔ kibe lɛ gɛ ɛba tɛ wɛ̃ yɛ avuvɔ nɛ Kpaya bukusiɔŋakɔ nɛm.” Gɛ ba zha ɔdzɛ toli beke, klɛ be koeyi ashɛ̃ avɛ Olivɛ Butu nɛa bha.
Yesu Aɖɔ Elu Sɛ Petro Aba Dɛada Sɛ Eti Nyi Yɛ Yesu etsre badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ, “Nɔ bɔ shɛ ɔlɔm petee,” alasɛ ba ŋlɔmɛ lɛ elu asɛ, “ ‘Ɛba hu ibhoshi agbɛgbanɔ nɛ ibho, klɛ ibhoshi nɛ ba kɛka.’ Pɔ onu gɛ ɛba lɔ, ɛba putɔ kɔnɔ tsoku Galelia.” Petro ebu aɖɔ asɛ, “Onu gɛ anɔnyanɔ ehle tsyɛ mɛ ɛtɛ baa shɛ.” Yesu etsre yɛ asɛ, “Kɛgba mɛ itsre wɔnɔ,” “obo— ee, elishia— tɛ ɔkukɔ ɔbɔ bɔ abɔ tabha, wɔ Petro nahwɛ nɛ ɔbɔ dɛada ada tata sɛ oti nyi mɛ.” Pɔ Petro atrɔ kɛklãgbu asɛ, “Onu kɛ dzi sɛ itsi plɛnɔ wɔ, ɛtɛ ba shɛnahwɛ wɔshu di.” Klɛ badɔkpasɛ gɔgɔɛ nɛ petee aɖɔ atrɔ ana.
Getsemane Ba shɛ avɛ ɔkɔ toli gɛ bee klu asɛ Getsemane, klɛ Yesu etsre yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ, “Nɔ za kesi nɛ ɔkɛ̃ tɛ ɛda klukpaya.” Agbanɔ Petro, Yakobo anɛ Yohanɛsɛ evunɔ avɛnɔ, klɛ ebe tsoku butɔ nɛ awɔ̃ gɛganɔ mɛ.
Yesu etsre alɛ asɛ, “Mɛ ɔfufɔɛ nɛ oyuku nɛ butɔ ɔdɔ tɔnɔ butsi,” “Nɔ dzrɔ nɛ ɔkɛ̃ tɛ nɔ za nɛ awɔ̃.” Gɛ aza ga vɛ otugba nɛ bɔɛ ko, awɔlɛ adɔ kesukpa klɛ eklukpaya sɛ onu gɛ kɛba za bubɔɛbɔɛ tɛ ɔɖɔ nɛm ɔfla mɛ.
Yesu asɛ, “Aba, Aka,” “kibuinyɛbui lɛ bubɔɛbɔɛ kɔ wɔ.
Tsunɔ butɔ katsea nɛ mɛ nu.
Pɔ anɛ kɛgɛ mɛ ɛpɛɛ, pɔ kɛgɛ wɔ ɔdɛmɛ.” Ɔkɛlɛ etsodzi avɛ yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ ɔbha klɛ ada mɔa lɛ le dzi adɔ tra.
“Simɔnɛ,” ebisi Petro asɛ, “tra no dzi ɔdɔ?
So nɔ tɛ bɔ na awɔ̃ za ɔɖa tɛta torikpo tsyɛ?
Nɔ za nɛ awɔ̃ nɛ kpayakuklu mɛ sɛ tɛ nɔ tɛ bɔ dɔ ku tɛfifekedi mɛ.
Ɔfufɔɛ nɛ ɔɔpɛ ɔsɛ, pɔ ishuidzya nɛ ɛtɔ.” Bu vɛ turukpo plɛnɔ aza shɛ avɛ klɛ ede kulukpaya nɛ kibui lɛ nɛ shu.
Gɛ ede aba, aza ba mɔa lɛ le dzia dɔ tra, alasɛ balɛ awɔ̃hũ nɛ egbĩĩ.
Ba dɛ mɔ kibui nɔɔ nɛ gɛ le be tsre Yesu.
Gɛ eze de aba butramɛ, etsre alɛ asɛ, “No ko dzi ɔdɔ tra klɛ no muene?
Abɔ!
Kibe nɛɛ na.
No di, ba yɛkɔ Anɔdzyrame Yi nɛ ada kpɛ bezizi nɛ ahwɛmɛ.
Lɔ!
Nɔ kɔ lɔ shɛ!
Agɛ ada kpɛ mɛ ahwɛ nɛ yɛa baa!” Be Vu Yesu Gɛ Yesu azaa ɖɔaɖɔ nɛ ko, Yuɖasɛ Kɛfɔntɛabha nɛ ɔmɛayɛ teli aba wɛ̃.
Yɛ anɛ banɔɛza tili gɛ ba bala shu nɛ bupamɛ anɛ busukpogunu, gɛ ba kpɛ edenɔ bakpayanɔgbla, ɛshãdɔkasɛ anɛ beshishe nɛ ɔkɔ.
Ɔtsɔ̃ nɛ agɛ akpɛahwɛ nɛ abhɛtɛ tɛtɛtrɔ tili nɛ banɔ: “Anɔ nɛ gɛ yɛ onugbu mɛ eba mukɔ yɛ nu anɔ; no vu yɛ tɛ nɔ gbanɛ yɛ ɔshɛnɔ nɛ tɛpupoe si.” Yuɖasɛ aga tɔnɔ Yesu tsiɔɔ̃, klɛ eklu yɛ asɛ, “Adɔkasɛ!” klɛ amukɔ yɛ onugbu.
Banɔɛza nɛ be ge ku Yesu mɛ, klɛ be vu yɛ.
Ɔkɛlɛ teli gɛ eli ebunɔ ɔkɛlɛ nɛ etso yɛ kɛpamɛ klɛ afatɛ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ nɛ teli yɛ axwɛdɛ nɛ batɔ.
Yesu ebisi balɛ asɛ, “Iputɔ nɛ banɔ gɛ balɔ kititi nɛ wɔnɔ shu so pɛ nɔ yɛkɔ busukpogunu nɛ bupa mɛ sɛ no bo vu mɛ nɔ?
Ɛza plɛnɔ wɔnɔ kiwinyɛwi, ɛkasɛ kɛdɔ nɛ basɔlɛvu nɛ baka mɛ, klɛ no di vu mɛ.
Pɔ alasɛ tɛ Kpayaeplukpa mɛ kibui ba bhɛtɛ lɛ tɛ kɛnaa.” Ɔkɛlɛ anɔnyanɔ ashɛ̃nahwɛ yɛ shu klɛ le si ashɛ̃.
Anyɛayɛsɔ teli, gɛ edi nyumu kɛdɔnyɛdɔ pɔ akpɛ akraɖa awi, klɛ aza Yesue de.
Gɛ bevu yɛ, esi ashɛ̃ nɛ alagba, ashɛ̃nahwɛ kɛdɔ nɛ gɛ enyumu nɛ shu elui de.
Yesu Nɛ Bebhuiklu Nɛ Amɛ Ba yɛkɔ Yesu avɛnɔ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ ɖɛɖama nɛ amɛ klɛ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ, beshishe anɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ nɛ petee be xogo.
Petro aza Yesue de nɛ odzidzekɔɛ bɔɛ, ede tsoku kpayaɔzakɔanɔ ɖɛɖama nɛ bubhui oklukɔ.
Ɔkɛlɛ ede zhiaza plɛnɔ bagɛ be po ɔkɛlɛ, klɛ edzi aŋanɛ kifu.
Kpayaɔzakɔanɔ anɛ Bebhuiklu nɛ petee ba pɛɛ kibui nɔ nɛ gɛ la ba yɛkɔ ebhui Yesu nu nɔ pɛ le be yi yɛ, pɔ ba dɛ mɔ kibuinyɛbui.
Begelee be hu itro sɛ tɛ ba yɛkɔ etii yɛ akpɛ kibuim, pɔ balɛ ebui nɛ adɛ ŋa.
Ɔkɛlɛ beteli aba lɔ kititi klɛ be hu itro nɛ yɛ shu asɛ, “Bunu gɛ aɖɔ asɛ, ‘Ɛba yɛ busɔlɛvu gɛ nɔ bhɔ nɛ ahwɛ, klɛ nɛ ewi tata mɛ, ɛba bhɔ bubhlatɔ, gɛ budɛ nu anɔdzyrame yɛ bhubhɔ.’ ” Pɔ kɛlɛlɛ nɛ mɛ tsyɛ balɛ ebuimɔɖɔ nɛ adɛ ŋa.
Ɔkɛlɛ balɛ kpayaɔzakɔanɔ nɛ alɔ nɛ balɛ amɛ klɛ ebisi Yesu asɛ, “Ɔtɛ bo bu shu nu?
Kidee gɛ nu ebuimɔɖɔa nɛɛ di gɛ banɔ nɛ baa yɛkɔ nɛ wɔ shu?” Pɔ Yesu adɔ sɛɛ̃ klɛ edi bu shu nu.
Kpayanɔgbla nɛ eze bisi Yesu asɛ, “Wo nu Kristo, Kpaya yɛ Eyi Yuyula?” Yesu ebui lɛ bunu asɛ, “Mɛnu Kristo.” “Klɛ nɔ bɔ mɔ Anɔdzyrame yɛ Eyi nɛ gɛ ezhiedzi Agbɛgbladɛ nɛ kɛŋam gɛ aaba denɔ ɔmunɔ nɛ mɛ nɛ owũsise.” Kpayaɔzakɔanɔ nɛ atsyuɛ yɛ bawi nɛ ishu.
Ebisi asɛ, “Kidee so pɛ bu zɛ ba pɛɛ bebuimɔɖɔ gelee dɛa na nɛ Yesu shu?” “No nu ebusobui.
Kide wɔnɔ kɛtɔkpu nɛ mɛ tsre nɔ?” Balɛ petee be bu yɛ kɛpɔ gɛ dzyenɔ butsi.
Ɔkɛlɛ be teli ba kpa bututu bu ta yɛ; banya yɛ amɛ, be hu yɛ ekpli, klɛ baa ɖɔ asɛ, “Mɔɛbuiɔɖɔ!” Klɛ bepupo na gbanɔ yɛ klɛ be de tu yɛ.
Petro Asɛ Eti Nyi Yesu Kibee lɛ nɛ gɛɛ Petro adzrɔ nɛ kesiɔkɔ nɛ kebhui buka nɛ mɛ, kpayaɔzakɔanɔ anɛ yɛ axwɛdɛ adzɛnuvɔɛ teli abaa fla. Gɛ amɔ Petro gɛ edzi aŋanɛ kifu, evu awɔ̃hũ nɛ yɛ mɔɔ mɔ.
Klɛ aɖɔ asɛ, “Wɔ tsyɛ ɔza Nazarɛtɛ eyi Yesu nɛe de.” Pɔ Petro adɛ dɛmɛ lɛ.
“Iti nyi, klɛ mɛ tii nu kibui nɔ nɛ gɛ ɔɔɖɔ nɛesi,” klɛ ekoeyi avɛ ede li kedunu.
Gɛ adzɛnuvɔɛ nɛ aza mɔ yɛ asɛsɛ nɛ ɔkɛlɛ, aza ɖɔ etsre bagɛ li kititi nɛ ɔkɛlɛ, “Anyɛa nɛɛ balɛ ɔmɛayɛ teli enu.” Aza dɛ dɛmɛ lɛ.
Nɛ kɛlɛede bɔɛ ko, banɔ nɛ gɛ beli titi nɛ ebunɔ Petro ne tsre yɛ asɛ, “Kɛlɛlɛm sɛ balɛɔmayɛ teli onu, alasɛ Galeliaeyi onu.” Petro etenɔ ebui ɖɔkpɛ shu, klɛ atanɔ kɛdɔ kɔa lɛ asɛ, “Iti nyi anyɛa nɛ gɛ yɛ bui nɔɔ ɖɔ.” Ɔklɛ nɛ ko klɛ ɔkukɔ ɔzɔ bɔ bubhla.
Ɔkɛlɛ Petro abaka Yesu ebui nɛ gɛ aɖɔ tsre yɛ asɛ, “Flogo tɛ ɔkukɔ ɔbɔ bɔ abɔ tabha nɛɛ obɔ dɛada ada tata sɛ oti nyi mɛ.” Klɛ Petro ezhidɔ nɛ iyuyo.
Yesu Aba Wɛ̃ Nɛ Pilato Amɛ Nɛ kɛvlɔ nɛ pinii, kpayaɔzakɔanɔ, anɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ anɛ ɔhamɛ bebhuiklu afɛtegene nɛ petee na ba dɛmɛ atrɔ kibui tirikpoa bha.
Banya Yesu, klɛ ba gbanɛ yɛ ada kpɛ ahwɛ akɔ Pilato.
Pilato ebisi Yesu asɛ, “Wɔ nu Yuɖanɛ ekusi dza?” Yesu asɛ, “Ee, kɛlɛ ansɛ gɛ ɔɖɔ.” Kpayaɔzakɔanɔ nɛ ayɛkɔ ebui kpi nɛ yɛ shu.
So Pilato eze bisi yɛa sɛ, “Ɔtɛ bɔ bu kibui nɛ nu?
Di ebuia nɛ nyɔɔ gɛ ba yɛkɔ nɛ wɔ shu.” Pɔ tsyɛ Yesu eze di bu kibuinyɛbui nu, klɛ kɛ bhɛtɛ Pilatio bi.
Ɔtsɔ̃ nɛ kinu bugu sɛ tɛ ba shɛ̃nahwɛ evuza terikpo gɛ banɔ nɛ ba pɛɛ nɛ shu nɛ Tɛfɛflãwi ŋɛŋa nɛa bha.
Anyɛ teli gɛ bee kulu asɛ Barabasɛ nɛ aza vu plɛnɔ anɔ dzyidzyeaga teli gɛ eyi anɔ nɛ kititilulɔɛ be tilim.
Banɔɛza na ba tɔnɔ Pilato sɛ abhɛtɛ kɛgɛ aabhɛtɛ tsã nɛ akɔ balɛ.
Pilato ebisi alɛ asɛ, “Nɔ pɛɛ sɛ ɛshɛnahwɛ Yuɖanɛ ekusi nɛ shu kɔnɔ?” Enyi asɛ ganɔ kawɔ̃kpɛ mɛ kpayaɛzakɔanɔ nɛ ba yɛkɔ Yesu akpɛ yɛ ahwɛ.
Pɔ kpayaɛzakɔanɔ nɛ ba kpɛahwanɔ banɔɛza nɛ asɛ tɛ be tui lɛ akpɛ tɛ Pilato ashɛ̃nahwɛ Barabasɛ shu.
Pilato ebisi banɔ nɛ asɛ, “Kidee mɛ ba bhɛtɛ ɔtsɔ̃, nɛ agɛ noo kulu sɛ Yuɖanɛ ekusi?” Ba kpɛ igugu asɛ, “Kplayɛɔsɔ!” Pilato ebisi asɛ, “Kidee so?
Buzizi ɖuweɖu abhɛtɛ?” Pɔ ba za kpɛ igugu nɛ gɛganɛɛ adɛa na sɛ, “Kplãyɛɔsɔ!” Sɛ tɛ Pilato eku banɔ nɛ awɔ̃ so nɛ, ashɛ̃nahwɛ Barabasɛ shu akɔa lɛ.
Akɔ ba mɛna Yesu kɛtamu, klɛ ayɛkɔ yɛ akpɛahwɛ kɔa lɛ sɛ ba da kplasɔ.
Keyutugbani Na Kpɛ Yesu Butsɔ Keyutugbani na gbanɔ Yesu ebu eyinɔ avɛnɔ ada kpɛ bukusi bupagbla nɛm (gɛ nu Praɛtorium keyutugbani ivulo nɛ oxogokɔ) klɛ be kulu ivulo nɛ petee ebe xogo.
Ba kpɛ awi dzɛdzã akɔ yɛ, klɛ be tro bɔkpɔewi abhɛtɛ kikutu pɛ ba yɛkɔ ekumu akɔ yɛ.
Klɛ la kpa yɛ dzɔ sɛ, “Hee, Yuɖanɛ ekusi nɛ naa!” Be hu yɛ kesukpogunu nɛ kɛtɔkpu nɛ etsodzini ehu klɛ be bu bututu ata yɛ.
Be dzu ekuisiesi akɔ yɛ, sɛ tɛ ba yɛkɔ akpɛ yɛ butsɔ nɔ.
Klɛ gɛ ba kpɛ yɛ butsɔ nɛ beke, be bu awi dzɛdzã nɛ yɛ shu, klɛ ba yɛkɔ yɛnahwɛ bawi nɛ akpɛ kɔ yɛ.
Ɔkɛlɛ ba gbanɔ yɛ ebueyinɔ sɛ tɛ ba da kplasɔ.
Yesu Tɛkpɛkplasɔ Anyɛ teli gɛ ede Sirene, Simɔnɛ, gɛ enu Alɛksanda anɛ Rufusɛ alɛ aka, abaa fla denɔ yɛ dzogɛga bha ebe tsoku ɔma nɛ mɛ, klɛ banɔ nɛ ba trɔ yɛa bha sɛ ayɛkɛ butsiosi nɛ etuku.
Ba gbanɔ Yesu ede kunɔ ɔklɛ gɛ be kulu asɛ Golgata (atɔkpuxwa ɔzakɔ).
Nɛ ɔklɛ nɛ ba hɔ aɖuɖo akpɛ bulu mɛ akɔ Yesu sɛ awɛ̃, pɔ adɛ wɛ̃.
Klɛ ba kplayɛasɔ.
Be dzyidzyidɔ nɛ yɛ bawi nɛ tɔkpu tɛ bamɔ kapɛ nɔɔ nɛ gɛ anɔnyanɔ aba yɛkɛ.
Ɔɖa ɔtramɛ nɛ mɛ la kplayɛasɔ.
Ebui nɛ gɛ ba yɛkɔ nɛ yɛ shu, ba ŋlɔmɛ alɛ ata yɛ asɛ, Yuɖanɛ ekusi.
Ba kpla bezi tɛabha teli tsyɛ asɔ aplɛnɔ yɛ, terikpo nɛ yɛ kɛŋa nɛm, teli tsyɛ nɛ yɛ kɛbɛtɛkpɛm.
[Klɛ kibui ŋuŋlɔmɛ nɛ ba klɛ mɛ sɛ, “Kplayɛasɔ akpɛ banɔ nɛ gɛ ata bhɛtɛ ɔshã bha nɛ shi.”] Banɔ nɛ gɛ aba fla nɛ balɛ akulatu nɛ yɛa bha, ba hwanɔ atɔkpu atrɔ pɛ ba ɖɔ sɛ, “Klɛ so!
Wɔ nɛ gɛ ɔsɛ ɔbɔ yɛ busɔlɛvu pɛ obo tsodzini ɔbhɔ nɛ ewi tata mɛ, zhiɔba nɛ butsiosi nɛ shu tɛ obu ishue!” Kana ke kpayaɛzakɔanɔ anɛ ɛshãdɔkasɛ petee baa kpɛ Yesu butsɔ nɛ aglɔmɛ.
Klɛ baa ɖɔ asɛ, “Ebu banɔ,” “pɔ ataa na shu bu!
Nɔ kɔ Kristoanɛ, Izraɛlanɛ Ekusia nɛ, ezhi ɔtsɔtsiɔ̃ aba nɛ butsiosi nɛ shu, tɛ bu mɔ tɛ bu yɛkɛ yɛabha ŋae.” Bagɛ yɛnalɛ ba kplasɔ nɛ tsyɛ ba yalɛ akulatu abalɛ akpɛ yɛa bha.
Yesu Tɛtsitsi Nɛ kemuze ɛɖa lɔfɔntɛbha mɛ otumu ɔdɔ nɛ kesukpa nɛa bha ɔdɔ nanɔ owulago ɛɖa tɛta mɛ.
Nɛ ɛɖa tɛta nɛ mɛ, Yesu akpɛ ogugu gɛganɛɛ asɛ, “Eloi, Eloi, Lama Sabaktani?” Gɛ klɛ kesi enu asɛ, “Mɛ Kpaya, Mɛ Kpaya, kidee so pɛ ɔshɛnahwɛ mɛshu ana?” Gɛ banɔ nɛ gɛ be li ɔklɛ nɛ be nu kaɖɔ nɛ gɛ Yesu aɖɔ nɛ butsiosi nɛ shu, klɛ baa ɖɔ asɛ, “Nonu mɔ, eklu Eliya.” Anyɛ teli akpɛsi, ada yɛkɔ ɔkɔɛsa akpɛ bulu gɛganɛ mɛ, klɛ ayɛkɔ asɔ osi shu, klɛ ayɛkɔ akɔ Yesu sɛ tɛ awɛ̃.
“Ɔtsɔ̃ nɛ nɔ shɛnahwɛ yɛ shu.
Kɔlɔ di sɛ Eliya aba ba ebe zhinɔ yɛ edzu dza.” Nɛ ogugu gɛganɛɛ, Yesu afɔɛ yɛ ɔfufɔɛ gɔgɔɛ.
Busɔlɛvu mɛ kɛpɔtɛ nɛ tswɛ denɔ kabha ɔbɔ nanɔ kesi nɛ wa.
Klɛ gɛ keyutugbani Ovuloaka, gɛ aza kititi nɛ Yesu otugba, nɛ enu yɛ ogugu klɛ amɔ kana gɛ etsi nɛɛ, aɖɔ asɛ, “Kɛlɛlɛm sɛ anyɛa nɛɛ enu Kpaya yɛ Eyi!” Badzɛ teli aza odzidzekɔ pɛ bee di ɔklɛ asɛsɛ.
Balɛ mɛ banɔ balɛ enu Maria Magdaline, Maria Yakobo yɛeni gɛ enu anuvɔ kɔ Yosesɛ, anɛ Salomɛ.
Nɛ Galelia, badzɛa nɛ balɛ aza Yesue de kɔ kɛdɔnɔ nɛ gɛ ba zhã kɔ yɛ.
Badzɛ gelee bhlatɔ gɛ ba za yɛe de aba Yerusalɛm nɛ tsyɛ ba za ɔklɛ.
Yesu Tɛvuvubɔ Kiwi lɛlɛ nɛ dzi Tɛbɛbala Kiwi (gɛ putɔkɔ Kimuenewi nɛ gɛ nu Sabatɛ).
So gɛ owulago nɛ ɔɔna nɛɛ, Yosɛfu Arimatiaeyi, anɔgbla nɛ Beshisheha nɛ shi, gɛ yɛ nahwɛ nɛ eedi kidzoe nu kɔ Kpaya bukusiɔŋakɔ, atɔnɔ Pilato avɛ nɛ awɔ̃dzudzum klɛ ede bisi asɛ ayɛkɔ Yesu ishuidzya tsitsi nɛ akɔ yɛ.
Kiyinɔ Pilato sɛ Yesu etigble tsi.
Eklu Ovuloaka nɛ ebisi asɛ Yesu nɛ eti tsi dza.
Gɛ Pilato enu denɔ Ovuloaka nɛ ɔkɔ sɛ Yesu etsi kɛgba, ashɛ̃nahwɛ yɛ shu akɔ Yosɛfu.
Klɛ Yosɛfu ede bhui kɛpɔtɛ fufu, klɛ ede zhinɔ Yesu tsitsi klɛ ayɛkɔ yɛ anya kpɛ kɛlɛ mɛ, klɛ ayɛkɔ yɛ ada vubɔ nɛ kɛklãgbu odzrem.
Klɛ ayɛkɔ kɛklãgbugbla bhlatɔ ada ɔlɛ nu.
Maria Magdaline nɛ Maria Yoses yeni nɛ ba mɔ ɔklɛ gɛ ba vubɔ Yesu.
Yesu Tɛlulɔ Denɔ Bekpum Gɛ Kimuenewi nɛ ba fla, Maria Magdaline anɛ Maria Yakobo yɛeni, anɛ Salomɛ bede dzi bawa huhuhu sɛ tɛ ba yɛkɔ ada sra Yesu ishu.
Kɛvulɔ nɛ pinii, nɛ ɔgɔnɛ nɛ kiwi tutɔpu nɛa bha, nɛ kiwiyɛyɛ nɛe de ko, batɔnɔɛ dzo aavɛ odzre nɔ bha, klɛ bee bisi ɔhaglɔ asɛ, “Anee gɛ ebe glebe kɛklãgbu nɛ atsɛ nɛ odzre nɛa bha?” Pɔ gɛ be vu awɔ̃hũ, ba mɔ sɛ kɛklãgbu, nɛ gɛ tri, be ti glebe lɛ ashɛ̃nɔ.
Gɛ be tsoku odzre nɛ mɛ, bamɔ anyɛnuvɔɛ gɛ akpasɛ kɛdɔ fufu mɛ pɛ ezhidzi odzre nɛ kɛŋamɛa pɛ, klɛ kɛ wa kɛxwɛ nɛ balɛa bha.
Anyɛnuvɔɛ nɛ asɛ, “Nɔ tɛ ganɛ awɔ̃,” “Nɔɔ pɛɛ Yesu Nazarɛtɛ eyi, gɛ ba kplasɔ.
Atɛ lɔ ekoeyi!
Ava ma ɔkɛ̃.
No di ɔkɛlɛ gɛ be lu yɛ.
Pɔ nɔ vɛ, no tsre yɛ badɔkpasɛ anɛ Petro sɛ, ‘Eti putɔ kɔnɔ avɛ Galelia.
Ɔkɛlɛ nɔ bɔ mɔ yɛ, ansɛ gɛ etsre nɔ.’ ” Ganɔ tɛshushuku mɛ anɛ awɔ̃nyunyɔ mɛ, badzɛ nɛ koeyi klɛ be si ashɛ̃ nɛ odzre nɛ shu.
Ba dɛ ɖɔ kibuinyɛbui etsre anɔnyanɔ, alasɛ kifu kua lɛ.
Gɛ Yesu alɔ kɛvulɔ nɛ pinii nɛ ɔgɔnɛ nɛ kiwi tutɔpu nɛa bha, eputɔ awɛ̃ nɛ Maria Magdaline amɛ, agɛ yɛ mɛ akɛka ɛfufɔɛkpã tigene nɛ ebu.
Adzɛ na shɛ avɛ ede tsre banɔ petee gɛ baza aplɛnɔ yɛ, pɛ be tsishu pɛ be bi iyuyo.
Kibelɛ gɛ be nu sɛ Yesu alɛ nɛ ɛkpã, klɛ yɛ atɛ mɔ yɛ, ba dɛ yɛkɛ kɛlɛa bha ŋa.
Kɛlɛede mɛ Yesu aba wɛ̃ nɛ tɛzɛza bhlatɔ mɛ kɔ balɛ tɛa bha nɛ kibe lɛ nɛ mɛ gɛ ba ga afla nɛ ɔma nɛm.
Banɔa nɛ tsodzi avɛ klɛ la da ɖɔɛ lɛ etsre bagɔgɔɛ; pɔ balɛ tsyɛ adɛ yɛkɛ balɛa bha ŋa.
Kɛlɛede mɛ Yesu aba wɛ̃ nɛ Kɛfɔntoli nɛ amɛ gɛ baa ŋɛ dɔ; Yesu etsrenɔalɛ nɛ balɛ mayɛkɛ mayɛkɛŋa nɛ shu nɛ balɛ tɛmadɛmɛ gɛganɛ sɛ tɛ ba yɛkɛ baga tɛ mɔ yɛ nɛ tsyɛa bha ŋa sɛ atɛ lɔ.
Yesu etsre yɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ asɛ, “No tsoku kanɔ nɛm petee tɛ nɔ ɖɔ kibui dzyɔgo nɛ otsre kanɔ nɛ petee.
Anɔnyanɔ gɛ ayɛkɛ aŋa pɛ nɔɔ kpɛ buni ɔkɔ yɛ nɛ ebe dzi anɔ gɛ be bu, pɔ anɔnyanɔ gɛ adɛ yɛkɛ aŋa be be bu yɛ butsipɔ.
Klɛ ebuimumɔa nɛ aba ga plɛnɔ bagɛ ba yɛkɛ aŋa: Nɛ mɛ nyi mɛ ba ba kɛka ɛfufɔɛkpã ebu; baba ɖɔa ɖɔ nɛ anɛkɛ vuvɔm; bee vu beblidzya nɛ ahwɛ; klɛ onu gɛ ba wɛ̃ aɖii tsyɛ etibe bhuia lɛ, baa trɔ ahwɛ nɛ banyɛnya bha, klɛ balɛ banya nɛ be beke.” Gɛ Apalete Yesu aɖɔ ebuia nɛ etsrea lɛ beke nɛɛ, baa yɛkɔ yɛ avɛnɔ owũsise klɛ ede zhiaza Kpaya kɛŋam, Ɔklɛ badɔkpasɛ nɛ koeyi ashɛ̃, klɛ la da ɖɔ Kpayɛbui nɛ ɔkɔnyɔkɔ, klɛ Apalete nɛ awa kɛxwɛ nɛ balɛ klɛ trɔ kɛklãgbu nɛ yɛ kibui nɛa bha ganɔ kɛdɔmumɔ nɛ gɛ za kɛlɛe de.
